#Author:Devapāla
#Text:Kāṭhagṛhyasūtrabhāṣya
#Comments:Kāṭhakagṛhyasūtra
#Edition:Kashmir Series of Texts and Studies, No. XLIX (1923)
#Data entry:Oliver Hellwig
#Notes:Currently covers only the first half of the mūla text.



1.1.[1]	vrataśabdo yamaniyamavācakaḥ /
1.1.[2]	tatra prasaktipratiṣedhātmakā yamāḥ amāṃsabhakṣaṇādayaḥ /
1.1.[3]	niyamāstu aprāptyaṅgaparipūrakā bhaikṣavṛttyādiviṣayāḥ /
1.1.[4]	‘ahiṃsāsatyāsteyabrahmacaryāparigrahāḥ’ yamāḥ /
1.1.[5]	‘śaucasantoṣatapaḥsvādhyāyeśvarapraṇidhānāni’ niyamāḥ /
1.1.[6]	iti tu yamā niyamāśca tairuktāste'pi yathāsaṃbhavamiha nirdhāryante /
1.1.[7]	upanayanādārabhya ā vedādhyayanaparisamāptevratacaraṇaśīlo bhavet // 1 //
1.2.[1]	syādityanuṣaṅgaḥ /
1.2.[2]	uttaratrāpi yojyamevaitat /
1.2.[3]	mṛgasyedaṃ mārgaṃ sāmānyaśabdenāpyeṇasyeti viśeṣo vakṣyamāṇatvāt /
1.2.[4]	vaste ācchādayatīti vāsaḥ paridhānam /
1.2.[5]	tacca mṛgacarma, mārgaṃ vāso yasyeti mārgavāsāḥ syāt // 2 //
1.3.[1]	hantirhiṃsākarmā /
1.3.[2]	samyak kṣureṇa natu kartaryādinā apasāritāḥ keśā yasya muṇḍitaśirā ityarthaḥ, tena muṇḍanena vakṣyamāṇena paunaruktyamityāhuḥ /
1.3.[3]	athavā saṃhatā ekarūpāḥ keśā yasya saḥ /
1.3.[4]	etaduktaṃ bhavati ‘muṇḍo jaṭilo śikhī vā’ iti vakṣyati, tatraikasya traivarṇikasya brahmacāriṇaḥ kālabhedena vikalpanivṛttyarthaṃ niyamābhidhānametat ekarūpā evaikaikena keśāḥ kartavyāḥ, jaṭī cenna muṇḍī śikhī veti /
1.3.[5]	evaṃ muṇḍādiṣu // 3 //
1.4.[1]	bhikṣāṇāṃ samūho bhaikṣam /
1.4.[2]	ācāryastu ‘upanīya tu yaḥ śiṣyam’ ityādilakṣaṇaḥ /
1.4.[3]	bhaikṣeṇaiva brahmacāriṇā śarīraṃ saṃdhāraṇīyamiti niyamaḥ /
1.4.[4]	ācāryādhīnā cāsya vṛttiḥ sthitirūpā śarīrapoṣaṇarūpā ca syāt /
1.4.[5]	ācāryo hi prerya kāṃścidbhikṣāṃ dāpayatītyācāryeṇāpi tasya śarīrapoṣaṇalakṣaṇā vṛttiranyaceṣṭāvadupapadyate, anyato vā kadācidbhaikṣasyālābhe ācārya eva bhojanādikaṃ dadātīti // 4 //
1.5.[1]	iha sāmānyābhidhāne'pi daṇḍaḥ pālāśādiḥ yathāyathaṃ vakṣyamāṇaḥ /
1.5.[2]	saha śalkena tvacā vartamāno daṇḍo yasya sa saśalkadaṇḍaḥ syādityanuṣaṅga eva // 5//
1.6.[1]	saptabhirmuñjavyaktibhistrivṛttyāvṛttībhavati tāṃ mekhalāṃ dhārayet /
1.6.[2]	atra mehanasaṃbandhinaḥ khasya mālā mekhaleti nirvacanaṃ kurvanti /
1.6.[3]	mayūravyaṃsakāditvātsādhu kila /
1.6.[4]	miha secane, mihyate sicyate vīryādikamaneneti mehanamānandendriyaṃ tasyopari nābheradhobhāge yatkhaṃ tasya mālā // 6//
1.7.[1]	mākṣikaṃ māṃsaṃ na bhakṣayediti tṛptyarthatayā prasaktasya pratiṣedhaḥ /
1.7.[2]	madhu madyamapi tat kṣatriyavaiśyayorniṣidhyate ityupākhyānamekīyam /
1.7.[3]	tanna, prasaktyabhāvāt ‘tasmādbrāhmaṇarājanyau vaiśyaśca na surāṃ pibet /’ iti trayāṇāmapi na niṣedhaḥ syāt // 7 //
1.8.[1]	kṣāraṃ ca tallavaṇamauṣaraṃ sāmudrikādi tadvarjī tadvarjanaśīlaḥ /
1.8.[2]	saindhavasauvarcalādikaṃ bhakṣayedeva /
1.8.[3]	kṣāradravyaṃ sarvaṃ ca lavaṇaṃ varjayediti kecit // 8 //
1.9.[1]	anukūla ityarthaḥ // 9 //
1.10.[1]	āstāmadhyayanādikam, kriyāmātramapyācāryānujñayā vinā na kuryādityarthaḥ // 10 //
1.11-12.[1]	śayanādikamāśrite gurau utthātukāme prathamamevottiṣṭhet, śayanāvasthite cācārye tatpādasaṃvāhanādikaṃ ca kṛtvā paścāt śayanādikaṃ saṃviśet /
1.11-12.[2]	jaghanyasaṃveśītyasyāyamarthaḥ - yadācāryaḥ khaṭvāyāṃ tiṣṭhati tadā brahmacāriṇā khaṭvāyāḥ sakāśādyajjaghanyamāsanaṃ paṭṭatalaśayyādikaṃ tatra saṃveśanīyam /
1.11-12.[3]	evaṃ śayyāmāsīne gurau tato nimna ityādyanumantavyam // 11, 12 //
1.13.[1]	yat suvarṇādikaṃ kilainamupeyādāgacchet tat brahmacārī asmai ācāryāya dadyāt // 13 //
1.14.[1]	yadyapi brahmacārī sakalavedavedāṅgopāṅgajñānārthaṃ yathāyogyaṃ krameṇa bahūnācāryānupāste, tathāpi yat yasya saṃnidhau nivasaṁllubheta tattasmai dadyāt, natu sarvadā sarvaṃ sarvebhyo vibhajyetyarthaḥ // 14 //
1.15.[1]	yasyāṃ śayyāyāmācāryaḥ sthitastāmapāṭavādidaśāyāṃ kāruṇyāt snehātiśayādvāpāṭave vācāryānujñāto'pi nādhitiṣṭhedityarthaḥ /
1.15.[2]	tena jaghanyasaṃveśītyanena paunaruktyābhāvaḥ // 15 //
1.16.[1]	asyetyanuṣaṅgaḥ /
1.16.[2]	ayamapyanujñātasya pratiṣedhaḥ /
1.16.[3]	anye tu śayyāgrahaṇamācāryādhiṣṭhitāsanayānādyupalakṣaṇārthaṃ rathavākyaṃ varṇayanti, rathagrahaṇaṃ tu karituragādyupalakṣaṇārthaṃ varṇayanti, ‘na saṃvastrayeta’ ityatra ca sthitena dvitīyena nañā tantreṇāvṛttyā vā saṃbandhayanti rathaṃ na samārohenna kiṃ tarhi grāmādikaṃ gacchannasamartho vāhanāntaraṃ ca na labhate tadācāryānujñātastenādhiṣṭhitamapi karituragaṃ samārohedevetyarthaḥ //16//
1.17.[1]	samānaṃ vastraṃ na kuryāt, ācāryaparihitaṃ vastraṃ na paridadhīta /
1.17.[2]	nāpyācāryavastreṇa saha samāne karaṇḍādibhāṇḍe svavastraṃ saṃśritaṃ kuryāt // 17 //
1.18.[1]	saṃsparśanimittāni yāni pāṇigrahaṇābhyañjanādīni karmāṇi tāni sarvāṇyeva sarvābhiḥ strībhiḥ saha varjayet /
1.18.[2]	‘gurāviva tatputradāreṣu vartanīyam’ ityasyāḥ smṛterapyayamapavādaḥ pādasaṃvāhanādiviṣayaḥ // 18 //
1.19.[1]	muṣitāmiva nagnāṃ na paśyedityarthaḥ // 19 //
1.20.[1]	vihāraḥ krīḍā tadarthaṃ parihāsādikaṃ na vadet /
1.20.[2]	athavā ‘sarvakāryāsvatantraḥ’ ityanena sarvakriyāsvācāryānujñā grahaṇapūrvikāyāṃ pravṛttau sthitāyāṃ vihāraṃ mūtramalotsargamāha vihārārthaṃ na jalpedanujñāgrahaṇāya // 20 //
1.21.[1]	rucirdīptiḥ ratiḥ prītiśca /
1.21.[2]	tadarthaṃ dravyaviśeṣādikaṃ na saṃgṛhṇīyāt alaṅkaraṇaṃ krīḍādikam // 21 //
1.22.[1]	rucyarthamityanuvartate // 22 //
1.23.[1]	ayamarthaḥ - rucyarthaṃ snānaṃ niṣiddhaṃ, nityaṃ tu kartavyameva ‘nityaṃ snātvā śuciḥ kuryādevarṣipitṛtarpaṇam /’ ityādinā brahmacāriṇo'pi vidhānāt /
1.23.[2]	tatra ca vikalpaḥ snānaṃ kadācinmantrasaṃskṛtenodakena prokṣaṇaṃ kadācinmajjanam /
1.23.[3]	tatrādyamanenoktam ‘udakaṃ vābhyupeyāt’ iti // 23 //
1.23.[4]	majjanamadhikṛtyāha
1.24.[1]	yadiśabdaḥ pratibaddho vidhāyako'nuvādaṃ prārthayate ‘yadi śāliṃ bhuñjīta tadā dadhyupasiñcet’ ‘yadi rathantarasāmā somaḥ syāt aindravāyavāgrān grahān gṛhṇīyāt’ ityādivat /
1.24.[2]	tenāyamarthaḥ yadā majjanarūpaḥ snānapakṣastadā brahmacāriṇā daṇḍenevāpsu pariplavamātraṃ kartavyam /
1.24.[3]	natu kāntyādisiddhaye malāpasāraṇādinā yatanīyam // 24 //
1.25.[1]	muṇḍaḥ śikhārahitaḥ // 25 //
1.26.[1]	sakalādityopalakṣitaḥ kālo divasaḥ /
1.26.[2]	ādityaśūnyakālo rātriḥ /
1.26.[3]	ardhoditenārdhāstaṃgatena cādityenopalakṣitaḥ kālaḥ sandhiḥ /
1.26.[4]	sandhau bhavā sandhyā /
1.26.[5]	tāmubhayīmapi pratyahamupāsīta /
1.26.[6]	upāsanaṃ sevā // 26 //
1.26.[7]	kathamupāsītetyāha
1.27.[1]	pūrvāhṇabhāgagatāṃ tiṣṭhet nivṛttagatiḥ pūrvāṃ prāṅmukho japannavatiṣṭheta sanakṣatrakālādārabhya ā sūryajyotirdarśanāt // 27 //
1.28.[1]	aparāhṇasaṃnihitāmupaviṣṭaḥ pratyaṅmukhaḥ sabhāskarakālādārabhya japannāsīta ā tārakajyotirdarśanāt āsītottarāṃ saṃdhyākālasyātisūkṣmatvādevaṃ tadupāsanamiṣṭam // 28 //
1.29.[1]	diṅmātradarśanametat /
1.29.[2]	brāhma muhūrte'bhyutthāyānuṣṭhitaśarīradharmaḥ, “atyantamalinaḥ kāyo navacchidrasamanvitaḥ /
1.29.[3]	sravatyeṣa divā rātrau prātaḥstrānaṃ viśodhanam //” iti smaraṇāt mukhyaṃ gauṇaṃ vā snānaṃ vidhāya, “trirācamya dvirunmṛjya khānyupaspṛśya prāṇāyāmaistribhiḥ pūtastata oṃkāramarhati” iti smaraṇāt trīnprāṇāyāmān pañcadaśamātrāparimāṇānsmārtoktānkṛtvā pratipraṇavayuktavyāhṛtisaptakānvitasaśiraskasāvitryā trirabhyāsena paricchinnāṃstrīnprāṇāyāmānkṛtvā aghamarṣaṇādisūryopasthānāntaṃ bhūrbhuvaḥ svariti mahāvyāhṛtitrayayuktāṃ tatsavituriti sāvitrīmabhyastāṃ japet /
1.29.[4]	sāvitrīmanvāhetyanuśabdo'bhyāsārthaḥ /
1.29.[5]	tatsavituriti pratīkaḥ savitṛdevatākatve'pi “ākṛṣṇena rajasā” ityādīnāṃ sāvitrāntarāṇāṃ nivṛttyarthaḥ // 29 //
1.30.[1]	anastaṃgate bhānau grāmānniṣkramyāṣṭau samidho agnisamindhanārthaṃ haritavarṇā ārdrā āharedyo vedādhyayanatadarthānuṣṭhānādisamṛddhilakṣaṇaṃ kāmayate /
1.30.[2]	etaddhi śrutyāveditaṃ śrutimūlatvātsmṛteḥ // 30 //
1.31.[1]	sāyaṃprātaḥ saṃdhyopāsanārthaṃ grāmādbahirniḥsaraṇaṃ kartavyam /
1.31.[2]	sāyaṃprātaśca bhaikṣācaraṇaṃ kartavyam /
1.31.[3]	ubhayakālaṃ hi bhojanamāmnātam “sāyaṃprātarmanuṣyāṇāmaśanaṃ devanirmitam /” iti /
1.31.[4]	evamagnisamindhanaṃ kāladvaye'pi kartavyam /
1.31.[5]	catasraḥ prātaḥ catasraḥ sāyaṃ samidho hotavyāḥ /
1.31.[6]	evamanyakālaviśeṣavidhānārthānyetāni trīṇi vākyāni /
1.31.[7]	pūrvaśca madhyāhnāt prātaḥkālaḥ uttaraśca sāyaṃkālaḥ // 31 //
1.32.[1]	“sāyamevāgnisamindhanam” ityekeṣāṃ vedavidāṃ matam /
1.32.[2]	atra ca pakṣe catasraḥ samidha āhartavyāḥ // 32 //
1.33.[1]	upalakṣaṇametat /
1.33.[2]	bhaikṣasyācaraṇe agneścāsamindhane saṃdhyālopādike ca doṣaḥ pratyavāyo bhavati vihitātikramaṇāt /
1.33.[3]	yathoktam “nopatiṣṭhati yaḥ pūrvā nopāste yaśca paścimām /
1.33.[4]	sa śūdrabahiḥkāryaḥ sarvamādvijakarmaṇaḥ //” iti /
1.33.[5]	atha saṃdhyopāsanabhraṃśe bhaikṣārthamacaraṇe anaṭane agneścāsamindhane sati yatpāpaṃ bhavati tasya vināśāya avakīrṇivrataṃ prāyaścittamācaret /
1.33.[6]	avakaraṇamavakīrṇo'vidhānotsargaḥ kāmato brahmacāriṇo retasa utsargaḥ /
1.33.[7]	avakīrṇaṃ vidyate yasya so'vakīrṇī /
1.33.[8]	tasya vratamāmnātam /
1.33.[9]	“saptāgāraṃ caredbhaikṣaṃ svakarma parikīrtayan /
1.33.[10]	tebhyo labdhena bhaikṣeṇa vartayedekakālikam //
1.33.[11]	upaspṛśaṃstriṣavaṇamabdena sa viśuddhyati /” iti /
1.33.[12]	etatsandhyopāsanādikamakṛtvā avakīrṇivratamācaret /
1.33.[13]	kiṃ paripūrṇamābdikameva ? netyāha saptarātramiti /
1.33.[14]	anye tu vyācakṣate saṃdhyopāsanādikaṃ saptarātramakṛtyā avakīrṇivrataṃ caret paripūrṇameveti /
1.33.[15]	saptarātrānyūnādhike vā avakaraṇaṃ nyūnamadhikaṃ ceti /
1.33.[16]	yājñavalkya āha “bhaikṣāgnikārye tyaktvā tu saptarātramanāturaḥ /
1.33.[17]	kāmāvakīrṇa ityābhyāṃ hutvā cājyāhutidvayam //
1.33.[18]	nairṛtaṃ gardarbhaṃ vaitatsaṃvatsaravrataṃ caret /” iti /
1.33.[19]	atrāpi pūrvavadyojanā // 33 //
2.0.[1]	brahmacāriṇo'gnīndhanamuktam /
2.0.[2]	tatretikartavyatāmāha
2.1.[1]	samiditi dvitīyāmityādau sarvatra samidhamādadhātīti saṃbandhaḥ /
2.1.[2]	eṣo'sīti pratīkena edhiṣīmahītyantasya grahaṇam, evaṃ samidasītyanena samedhiṣīmahītyantasya, idamahamityanena bhavāmītyantasya /
2.1.[3]	caturthaḥ sakalaḥ paṭhitaḥ //
3.0.[1]	brahmacaryavratasyācāryapūjāvidhidvāreṇāvadhimāha
3.1.[1]	chandasi vede ṛgyajuḥsāmalakṣaṇe mantrabrāhmaṇārthavādanāmadheyabhedayukte ye vyavasthitā arthā dvādaśādhyāyanirṇeyāstān buddhvā tadyogyatvāt, snāsyan dāraparigrahārthaṃ snātakadharmān grahītumicchan ācāryamadhīṣya gāṃ madhuparkārthaṃ kārayet svadhanaṃ dattvā arhayet /
3.1.[2]	sā madhuparkopayoginī satī gurave dāsyate /
3.1.[3]	ācāryo hi śiṣyāya siṣṇāsave madhuparkaṃ dadāti, śiṣyaścācāryāya dakṣiṇāmiti kecit /
3.1.[4]	anye tu goprabhavo madhuparko gośabdena vivakṣita iti vyācakṣate /
3.1.[5]	tenācāryamadhīṣya madhuparko me dīyatāmiti madhuparkaṃ kārayedityarthaḥ /
3.1.[6]	gṛhītamadhuparkaśca brahmacārī ācāryamarhayeddakṣiṇādinā yathāśaktyā pūjayet /
3.1.[7]	apare tu sūtrabhedena vyācakṣate - chandasyarthān buddhvā snāsyan gāṃ kārayedityekam, ācāryamarhayediti dvitīyam /
3.1.[8]	ācāryamadhīṣyādāvātmane gāṃ madhuparkaṃ ca dāpayedityādyasyārthaḥ /
3.1.[9]	ācāryeṇa ca pūjito gṛhītadakṣiṇaḥ san brahmacārī paścādācāryamarhayet dakṣiṇādānādinā /
3.1.[10]	brahmacāriṇaṃ hi samyagadhītāvabuddhavedamācāryaḥ pūrvaṃ pūjayatīti /
3.1.[11]	tathāca smṛtiḥ “taṃ pratītaṃ svadharmeṇa brahmadāyaharaṃ pituḥ /
3.1.[12]	sragviṇaṃ talpa āsīnamarhayetprathamaṃ gavā //” iti /
3.1.[13]	taṃ brahmacāriṇaṃ, svadharmeṇa śiṣyadharmeṇa, pratītamabhimukhamāgatam, ācāryasya brahmaharaṃ piturdāyaharaṃ, sragviṇaṃ mālādhāriṇaṃ, talpe khaṭvāyāmāsīnamupaviṣṭaṃ gavā pūjayedācāryaḥ /
3.1.[14]	tasmādgṛhītavidyo guruṇānujñātaḥ snāyāt, snātvā ca bhāryāmadhigacchet /
3.1.[15]	anutsṛṣṭastu vīryaṃ hitvā upāvartate /
3.1.[16]	tathāca śrutiḥ “indro vai prajāpatau brahmacaryamuvāsa sa vā anutsṛṣṭo vīryaṃ hitvopāvartata //” iti /
3.1.[17]	“ācāryo brahmacāriṇaḥ prajāpatiḥ /” iti ca // 1 //
3.1.[18]	dvividho brahmacārī - upakurvāṇo yo brahmacaryaṃ caritvā snānadāraparigrahādikaṃ saṃśrayate, naiṣṭhiko yo brahmacaryeṇa niṣṭhāṃ gamayati /
3.1.[19]	tatropakurvāṇakasya sāvadhikaṃ brahmacaryamiti tadapekṣayoktaṃ “chandasyarthān” ityādi /
3.1.[20]	naiṣṭhikāpekṣayā tvidamucyate
3.2.[1]	anyo naiṣṭhiko brahmacārī /
3.2.[2]	śrotriyo vedādhyāyī /
3.2.[3]	“śrotriyaṃ chando'dhīte” iti śrotriyaśabdo vedādhyāyini nipātitaḥ /
3.2.[4]	vedādhyāyīti punarvacanamavadhāraṇārthaṃ vedādhyāyyeva, na snānādyācarati nidhanāvadhikamasya brahmacaryavratamityarthaḥ // 2 //
3.2.[5]	ata eva spaṣṭārthamāha
3.3.[1]	tasyānantarottasya naiṣṭhikasya snānaṃ nāstītyarthaḥ // 3 //
3.3.[2]	yasya tūpakurvāṇakasya snānādikamasti, tasya snānakartavyatāmāha
3.4.[1]	gosamūho vrajaḥ, tena parihitamadhiṣṭhitaṃ deśaṃ prapādya praveśya prayojakakarturācāryasyāyaṃ nirdeśaḥ /
3.4.[2]	yathāsaṃbhavaṃ jaṭilapakṣe jaṭānāṃ vāpanam śikhipakṣe keśānām /
3.4.[3]	tena jaṭādikamabhisaṃhāryāpasārya vāpayitvā āpo hi ṣṭhetyādibhistisṛbhiḥ saṃmārjanaṃ kurvantaṃ snāyāt snāpayet majjayet /
3.4.[4]	hiraṇyavarṇā iti dvābhyāṃ dvitīyaṃ majjanaṃ kuryāt, “śaṃ na āpa” iti dvābhyāṃ tṛtīyam /
3.4.[5]	atra ca śmaśrugrahaṇenauṣṭhoparigatakeśānāmapi grahaṇam /
3.4.[6]	lomagrahaṇena guptasthānagatānāṃ grahaṇaṃ natu bhrvādivṛttīnāmāryaprasiddhivirodhāt // 4 //
3.4.[7]	tatastriḥ snātaḥ pavitrībhūta idamidaṃ kuryādityāha
3.5-21.[1]	atra sūtragaṇe pāṭhakramādarthakramasya balīyastvāt uktānuktapadārthānāmarthavaśena kramaviśeṣayojanā kartavyā /
3.5-21.[2]	tathāhi triḥsnātasya jalāśayānnadyāderuttīrṇasya caraṇaprakṣālanādayo'nuktāḥ, sūtritāśca dhautavastraparidhānādayo yathākrameṇa jñeyāḥ /
3.5-21.[3]	dyauste pṛṣṭhamityādimantreṇa cchatraṃ dhārayeta, yathāvibhavānusāreṇa imamagna ityādinā kaṭakakuṇḍalādi hiraṇyam /
3.5-21.[4]	pratiṣṭhe stha ityādinā vārāhyopānahau pratimuñcate paridhatte /
3.5-21.[5]	varāhaśabdo varāhacarmaṇi vartate /
3.5-21.[6]	varāhacarmaṇā nirvṛtta ityaṇ, tasya “aṇiñoranārṣayorgurū pottamayoḥ ṣyaṅ gotre” iti ṣyaṅ, “yaṅaścāpū” vārāhye ca te upānahau vārāhyopānahau /
3.5-21.[7]	varāhaḥ sūkaraḥ /
3.5-21.[8]	varāhopānahau ca rājasūyādāvarthavādādikādavagamyete /
3.5-21.[9]	anye tu vārāhyaśabdaṃ saṃniveśaviśiṣṭopānadvācakaṃ vyācakṣate catuṣkacchāditavat /
3.5-21.[10]	apare lakṣaṇayā carmamātramayatvaṃ varṇayanti, nahi kaścidā cāryaḥ sūkaracarmamayyāvupānahau paridadhaddṛśyate /
3.5-21.[11]	kecittu paṭhanti vārāhyupānahāviti /
3.5-21.[12]	tatra vārāhī upānahī iti dve pade /
3.5-21.[13]	“chandovatsūtrāṇi bhavanti” iti prathamapadadvivacanasya luk pūrvasavarṇādeśo vā “supāṃ suluk pūrvasavarṇa” ityādinā /
3.5-21.[14]	dvivastro'ta ūrdhvam, ato brahmacaryādūrdhvaṃ dvivastraḥ /
3.5-21.[15]	brahmacārī hyekavastra āsīt, mṛgājinaṃ hi tenopari dhāritam, naca tatra loke vastraśabdaprayogo'sti /
3.5-21.[16]	tataśca vastradvayaṃ vibhavānusāreṇotkṛṣṭaṃ bhartavyam /
3.5-21.[17]	tathāca śrutiḥ “tasmācchobhanaṃ vāso bhartavyam” iti /
3.5-21.[18]	veṇoḥ saṃbandhinaṃ ca daṇḍaṃ dhārayate tacchīlo vaiṇavadaṇḍadhārī/ nityamiti natvavaṣṭambhanādyarthitayaiva kadācideveti /
3.5-21.[19]	evaṃ chatradhārī /
3.5-21.[20]	apanthadāyī nānyasmai panthānaṃ dadyāt dṛṣṭaprayojanavyatirekeṇa /
3.5-21.[21]	apathadāyīti tu yuktaḥ pāṭhaḥ /
3.5-21.[22]	yataḥ “rājñā tu śrotriyāya panthā deyaḥ” iti gautamādibhiruktamataḥ kathamayaṃ śrotriyaviśeṣaḥ sannanyasmai prāṇimātrāya panthānaṃ dadyāt /
3.5-21.[23]	adattaharaṇaṃ pratiṣiddhaṃ - parakīyaṃ yaddravyaṃ tatpareṇādattaṃ na gṛhṇīyāt “na parasvamapaharet” iti śrutyādiniṣiddhatvāt /
3.5-21.[24]	aparayā dvārā niḥsaraṇam /
3.5-21.[25]	pratiṣiddhamiti kāṇḍikāntaṃ yāvadanuṣaṅgaḥ /
3.5-21.[26]	prasiddhamavigarhitaṃ yaddvāraṃ, tato'nyayā dvārā aprasiddhayā guptāntaḥpurādiniḥsaraṇapraveśāya parikalpitayā niḥsaraṇaṃ praveśanaṃ ca pratiṣiddham /
3.5-21.[27]	malavadvāsāḥ śvapacādiḥ, tena saha saṃbhāṣaṇaṃ pratiṣiddham /
3.5-21.[28]	tathā rajovāsasā rajasvalayā udakyāparaparyāyayā saha śayanaṃ pratiṣiddhaṃ, snānasya vivāhopakramatvādevamucyate, itikartavyatayā hi snānasya vivāhamṛte nāsti prasaktiḥ /
3.5-21.[29]	gurormānyasya “vittaṃ bandhurvayaḥ karma vidyā bhavati pañcamī /
3.5-21.[30]	etāni mānyasthānāni garīyo yadyaduttaram //” ityādikasya, duṣṭaṃ paruṣādi vacanaṃ pratiṣiddham /
3.5-21.[31]	asthāne gurustrījanādau smayanaṃ hasanaṃ pratiṣiddham /
3.5-21.[32]	evaṃ saraṇaṃ gamanamasthāne rahasyagurujanādhiṣṭhite /
3.5-21.[33]	evaṃ gāyanaṃ gītaṃ nartanaṃ cāsthāne pratiṣiddham, natūtsavādau samānaśīlamadhyagatasya guptasthāne /
3.5-21.[34]	tathāca mahāvrate gītavādyanartanakartavyatāvacanam /
3.5-21.[35]	“tamudgātā vācayitvā prastotre prayacchati prastotādhvaryave'dhvaryuranyasmai brāhmaṇāya /” ityādivīṇāvādanuvacanaṃ śrūyate /
3.5-21.[36]	yājñavalkya āha “vīṇāvādanatattvajñaḥ śrutijātiviśāradaḥ /
3.5-21.[37]	tālajñaścāprayāsena yogamārgaṃ nigacchati //” iti /
3.5-21.[38]	tasya ca nṛttagītāderasthāne'vekṣaṇaṃ pratiṣiddhaṃ natūtsavādau /
3.5-21.[39]	“āpo hi ṣṭhā” ityādayo vyākhyātāḥ /
3.5-21.[40]	hiraṇyavarṇā iti śākhāntarīyatvāt samastāḥ sūtrakṛtā paṭhitāḥ //
3.5-21.[41]	dyauste pṛṣṭhaṃ pṛthivī sadhasthamātmāntarikṣaṃ samudro yoniḥ /
3.5-21.[42]	vikhyāya cakṣuṣā tvamabhitiṣṭha pṛtanyataḥ //
3.5-21.[43]	bṛhatī /
3.5-21.[44]	aśvastutau viniyuktā /
3.5-21.[45]	iha cchatrastutāvapi tulyā /
3.5-21.[46]	tava dyauḥ svargalokaḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ pṛṣṭhe upari /
3.5-21.[47]	pṛthivī sadhasthaṃ samānasthānam /
3.5-21.[48]	ātmāntarikṣaṃ chatrāvayavino mahattvastutiḥ /
3.5-21.[49]	samudra udakaṃ yoniḥ kāraṇam “apsujo'śvaḥ” iti saṃstavāt aśvayoniḥ sarvasyodakaprabhavatvānnetravastrādeśchatramapi tathā evaṃ cenmahāprabhāvastvamataścakṣuṣā vikhyāya nirīkṣyābhitiṣṭha ākrāma abhibhava /
3.5-21.[50]	kān /
3.5-21.[51]	pṛtanyataḥ pṛtanā senā tāmicchanti ye te pṛtanyantaḥ, tān pṛtanyataḥ //
3.5-21.[52]	imamagna āyuṣe varcase kṛdhi tigmamojo varuṇa saṃśiśādhi /
3.5-21.[53]	mātevāsmā adite śarma yaccha viśve devā jaradaṣṭiryathāsat //
3.5-21.[54]	he agne imaṃ suvarṇālaṅkāramāyuṣe cirajīvanāya, varcase ca dīptaye kṛdhi kuru /
3.5-21.[55]	he varuṇa tvamapi ojo balaṃ tigmaṃ tīvraṃ samyak saṃpādaya/ he adite devamātaḥ asmai snātakāya śarma sukhaṃ yaccha prayaccha māteva jananīva /
3.5-21.[56]	he viśve devāḥ sarvadivaukasaḥ jaradaṣṭirjarāvyāptiryathā yena prakāreṇa asadbhavati, tathā kuruta jarājarjaritaśarīrā yathā saṃpadyāmahe tathā kurutetyarthaḥ //
3.5-21.[57]	pratiṣṭhe stho devate mā mā hiṃsiṣṭam //
3.5-21.[58]	he devate upānahau supratiṣṭhe sthaḥ śobhanaprasthāne bhavatam /
3.5-21.[59]	mā mā hiṃsiṣṭaṃ mama hiṃsā mā kārṣṭam //
4.1.[1]	vyākhyāsyāma ityadhyāhāraḥ /
4.1.[2]	vratamiti ca prastāvādgamyate /
4.1.[3]	caturṣu vedeṣu yadaṣṭācatvāriṃśasaṃvatsaraiḥ saṃmitaṃ paricchinnaṃ vratamuktaṃ, tasya pratinidhibhūtaṃ saṃvatsaranirvartyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ /
4.1.[4]	yasya vedamadhīyānasya yathākālavihitaṃ vrataṃ na saṃpannaṃ tena caitatkartavyamadhītavedacatuṣṭayena ca /
4.1.[5]	ata eva traividyakavratamidamucyate /
4.1.[6]	snānādanantaraṃ cāsyābhidhāne prayojanaṃ - snātakabhūtenāpyetatkartavyaṃ prāgvivāhāditi /
4.1.[7]	anye tu yathākālavihitavratasaṃpattāvapi etadvārṣikaṃ vrataṃ tapo'tiśayasiddhyarthaṃ kartavyatayā anena vidhīyate iti vyācakṣate /
4.1.[8]	athaśabdo vratapūraṇārthaḥ /
4.1.[9]	yathoktam “maṅgale pūraṇe hetāvānantaryādhikārayoḥ /
4.1.[10]	ṣaṭsvartheṣyathaśabdo'yaṃ smṛtaḥ prākprastute'pi ca //” anyo'picārtho yathāsaṃbhavaṃ yojyaḥ /
4.1.[11]	ataḥśabdo hetvarthaḥ /
4.1.[12]	yato'dhyayanakāle yathāvihitavratāsaṃpattiḥ kasyacitsaṃbhāvyate, ato hetoḥ pratinidhibhūtaṃ vratāntaraṃ vakṣyāma iti // 1 //
4.2.[1]	ucyata iti śeṣaḥ // 2//
4.3.[1]	sthānāsanādikān vakṣyamāṇānniyamān ācāryamādāya kuryāt /
4.3.[2]	ācāryaprādhānyena ca vedaguṇanārthābhyāsāvanuvartete // 3 //
4.4.[1]	śītātapabhīto nilayārthī bhūtvā yūnabaddhaṃ miśraveṇuvīraṇakāṇḍādinibaddhaṃ kuṭīśālāparṇādikavāsaviśeṣaṃ na praviśet // 4 //
4.5.[1]	na kevalaṃ paranirmitamāśrayaviśeṣaṃ na praviśet, yāvatā svayaṃ nilayamātramapi na kurvītetyarthaḥ // 5 //
4.5.[2]	yadyevaṃ vātyākarakadṛṣṭyādyupaplavāddehabhaṅgaḥ syādityāśaṅkyāha
4.6.[1]	vṛkṣādikamāśrayedityarthaḥ /
4.6.[2]	valmīkaṃ valmīkabhūmyādi // 6 //
4.7.[1]	tanturveṇuriti kecit, śītādyupahato vaṃśanirmitavyatirekeyāśrayāntaraṃ viśet /
4.7.[2]	rajjustanturityanye, rajjvādibandhairyannivṛttaṃ śālādi, tattāntavam // 7 //
4.8.[1]	yatpūrvamuktamekaṃ vāsaḥ, tadevātrāpi /
4.8.[2]	iyāṃstu viśeṣa: - iha śāṇī kutapaṃ vā /
4.8.[3]	śāṇī varāsiḥ, na punaḥ kṣaumī prasiddhā, klinnakuṭṭitadarbhanirmiteti tvanye /
4.8.[4]	ajalomanirmitaṃ kutapam // 8 //
4.8.[5]	asya vāsasaḥ parimāṇamāha
4.9.[1]	urasa ārabhya jānunoruparibhāgaṃ yāvadvyāpnoti, tāvatparimitametatkartavyamekameva traividyena /
4.9.[2]	adhyayanakāle tu adhobhāge paṭolikā tvāsīdupari tu mārgaṃ carma, tacca vāsa iti nocyate loke ityuktam // 9 //
4.10.[1]	“sāyaṃ prātarmanuṣyāṇāmaśanaṃ devanirmitam /” iti bhojanakālaḥ /
4.10.[2]	tatra prathamadinasya sāyaṃprātarlakṣaṇaṃ kāladvayaṃ, dvitīyadinasya ca prātaḥkālaṃ varjayitvā sāyaṃ caturthe kāle bhojanapāne kuryādityeke /
4.10.[3]	ekadinavyavadhānena ekakālaṃ bhuñjītetyarthaḥ /
4.10.[4]	anye tvāhuḥ pīyate iti pānaṃ kṣīratakrādi tadeva caturthakāle paścimaprahare bhakṣo'syeti, kṣīrādipānīye bhakṣaśabdo dṛṣṭaḥ “abbhakṣo vāyubhakṣaḥ” iti //
4.11.[1]	hiraṇyādisaṃcayaṃ na kurvītetyarthaḥ // 11 //
4.12.[1]	bhikṣāṇāṃ samūho bhaikṣam /
4.12.[2]	pūrveṇa bhikṣāṇāmapi saṃcayasya pratiṣedhe prāpte pratiprasavo'nena kriyate /
4.12.[3]	pratidinaṃ bhaikṣamaśnīyāt /
4.12.[4]	śarīrāpāṭave tu kadācidekāmapi bhikṣāmaśnīyāt, aṭitumaśaktaḥ saktukaṇikādikaṃ vā /
4.12.[5]	tāvanmātraṃ saṃcinuyādityanenābhiprāyeṇa vāśabdaḥ // 12 //
4.13.[1]	kālādhvanoratyantasaṃyoge ahaḥśabdāddvitīyā /
4.13.[2]	ahani tiṣṭhedeva ūrdhva evāsītetyarthaḥ /
4.13.[3]	rātrāvāsītopaviśet /
4.13.[4]	atiśrāntaḥ svapyādapi kadācidantarā manāk /
4.13.[5]	atyantasaṃyogābhāvāt dvitīyāvirahaḥ // 13 //
4.14.[1]	ubhayamahorātraṃ vāksaṃyamaṃ kuryāt /
4.14.[2]	munīnāṃ vratametat // 14 //
4.15.[1]	bhārgavastu cyavano manyate stryādibhireva na saṃbhāṣeta, natu sarvaiḥ /
4.15.[2]	saṃbhāṣayeteti svārthe ṇicū “rāmo rājyamakārayat” itivat /
4.15.[3]	patitāstraivarṇikā api /
4.15.[4]	rabhasā apṛṣṭavaktāro bhaṇḍavandiprabhṛtayaḥ /
4.15.[5]	rajasvalāstu ye raktena śarīramavalipya bhojanādikaṃ dāpayanti // 15 //
4.16-17.[1]	asamarthāpekṣametat /
4.16-17.[2]	saṃvatsarasyobhayorārambhasamāptilakṣaṇayoḥ pārśvayordvādaśarātrametatsthānāsanavāgyamaprabhṛtikaṃ kuryāt paurṇamāsīmamāvasyāṃ ca /
4.16-17.[3]	tena saṃvatsaramadhye aṣṭācatvāriṃśaddināni bhavanti /
4.16-17.[4]	upakramopasaṃhārayodvadaśarātradvayaṃ, dvādaśa paurṇamāsyaḥ, dvādaśāmāvasyāḥ // 16 //
4.18.[1]	yā brahmacāriṇo nityāḥ samidhaḥ, tā iha pālāśyaḥ /
4.18.[2]	palāśālābhe pratinidhiḥ, pratinidhāne ca paridhivṛkṣāṇāṃ vā, paridhivṛkṣāṇāṃ saṃbandhinyo grāhyāḥ /
4.18.[3]	paridhivṛkṣāśca yūpyāḥ bilvakhadirapalāśarohītakodumbarabadhiraprabhṛtayaḥ /
4.18.[4]	tathāca brāhmaṇaṃ śrutiśca “bailvo vā khādiro vā pālāśo vā rauhītako vā saumyasyādhvarasya yūpaḥ syāt /
4.18.[5]	audumbaro yūpo bhavati //” “khādire badhnāti pālāśe badhnāti rauhītake badhnāti //” iti /
4.18.[6]	yajñiyā vā sarve paridhivṛkṣāḥ /
4.18.[7]	śrūyate hi paridhibrāhmaṇam “tasyendraḥ paridhīnyajñiyebhyo vṛkṣebhya ājahāra” iti /
4.18.[8]	paridhivṛkṣatvādeva pālāśīnāṃ siddheḥ pṛthaggrahaṇaṃ tāsāṃ nityatvārthaṃ tathāceha nityagrahaṇam /
4.18.[9]	nanu mūlaprakṛtāveva kasmānnoktam /
4.18.[10]	sādhūcyate bhavatā kiṃtu jñāpakārthaṃ bhaviṣyati yathā sādyaskra evamuktaṃ madhyamāyāṃ saṃsthitāyāṃ yūpakarmeti, prakṛtau coktamupasatsu yūpakarmeti /
4.18.[11]	tatra kālākāṅkṣāyāṃ satyāṃ vikṛtirapi prakṛtiṃ gṛhṇāti ityetamarthamavabodhayitumevaṃ sūtritavānācāryo virodhābhāvāt /
4.18.[12]	evamanyatrāpi tulyanyāyatvādyojyam /
4.18.[13]	tenāṃhomugbhiḥ samiddāne'pyevaṃ jānīyādeva “tasyendro yajñiyebhyo vṛkṣebhyaḥ paridhīnājahāra /” iti // 17 //
4.19.[1]	kuryāditi śeṣaḥ /
4.19.[2]	medhāṃ mahāmaṅgirasa ityādibhirmantraiḥ dvābhyāṃ nābherārabhyordhvaṃ brahmadvāraparyantaṃ mārjanaṃ nigharṣaṇātmakaṃ kṛtvā ‘nābherurdhvameva pāṇinā unmārṣṭi’ iti smṛteḥ prātaḥsavane madhyandinasavane tṛtīyasavane iti savanatraye'pi rātribhāgatraye'pyevamudakopasparśanaṃ kuryāt /
4.19.[3]	upasparśanamiha snānam /
4.19.[4]	upasparśanaśabdo hyācamanasparśanasnāneṣu dṛṣṭaḥ, ‘upaspṛśya svastyayanaṃ bhavati’ ityādāvācamane, na kulyādyantarāgamananimittaprāyaścittabhūte sadācārādisiddhe; ‘upaspṛśya somamālabheran’ ityatra sparśe; ‘ālabhya copaspṛśeyuḥ’ ityatrāpyudakācamanamātre; ‘rathyādāvupaspṛśet’ ityādau snāne /
4.19.[5]	tatra prakaraṇavaśādviśeṣavyavasthā /
4.19.[6]	yathā saindhavaśabdāderaśvalavaṇamanuṣyeṣu /
4.19.[7]	divā vātārkasaṃyogādrātrau nakṣatramārutaiḥ /
4.19.[8]	sandhyayoragnivātābhyāṃ pavitraṃ sarvadā jalam //
4.19.[9]	tatra cāgniṃ pratiṣṭhāpya suvarṇaṃ saṃnidhāyeti vadanti /
4.19.[10]	astamite vasatīvarīgrahaṇavat ‘agnirvai vāk’ ityabhedāt anyabhāve'pi vāguccāryā evaṃ rātrāvācamanādyapi kuryāt // 18 //
4.19.[11]	evaṃ snātvā
4.20.[1]	etā evaṃ devatāstarpayannudakena tarpayannamaḥśabdāvacchinnairmantraiścaturbhirupasparśanaṃ kuryāditi saṃbandhaḥ /
4.20.[2]	āditya evopādhyavacchinno'trānekadevatārūpo'bhimataḥ /
4.20.[3]	tathāca hama ādityo gantṛtvena stūyate /
4.20.[4]	‘dramahammamīmṛgatau’ iti hammeḥ rūpaṃ hama iti /
4.20.[5]	‘mīñ hiṃsāyām’ ityasya tvapratyaye rūpaṃ chāndasam, mohamāyeti andhakārāpasārakāyetyarthaḥ /
4.20.[6]	tapatīti tapaḥ /
4.20.[7]	tapaścacāreti tāpasaḥ āditya eva prajāpatirūpeṇa stutaḥ /
4.20.[8]	tapyate iti tapaḥ brahmāṇḍādisargaḥ, taṃ tanoti utpādayatīti tapantaḥ ‘sarve vidhayaśchandasi vikalpyante’ iti supo luk /
4.20.[9]	vindate cetayate iti vinduḥ, vindyate cetyate iti vindaḥ cetyacetayitṛrūpaḥ prajāpatistasmai namaḥ vasu vindate vasuvindaḥ, evaṃ sarvavindaḥ tayorviśeṣaṇasamāsaḥ /
4.20.[10]	‘pāratīrakarmasamāptau pārayatīti pāraḥ /
4.20.[11]	pārayantaṃ tanoti pārayantaḥ /
4.20.[12]	ūrmīnraśmikallolānarhatīti ūrmyaḥ /
4.20.[13]	evaṃ sūrmyaḥ /
4.20.[14]	cyāvayatīti cyavanaḥ /
4.20.[15]	bhṛjjati pācayati bhūtānīti bhṛguḥ tasyāpatyaṃ bhārgavaḥ bhānurevātra // 19 //
4.21.[1]	eṣa brahmacārī snātako vā prakṛtaḥ saṃvatsaramuktaṃ vrataṃ caritvā, vimalo rāgādimalaśūnyo vigatapāpaśca bhavati // 20 //
4.21.[2]	pāpābhāvapradarśane nādhyayanāṅgatvavihitādhyayanakālavratākaraṇanimittaprāyaścittatāmasya saṃvatsaravratasya darśayati
4.22.[1]	yadyanyadvrataṃ vedādhyayanakāle na kurute, tadāsmiṃstatpratinidhibhūte saṃvatsaravrate kṛte sati caturṇāmapi vedānāmadhītānāṃ caritabrahmacaryaḥ saṃpadyate vrataparipūrṇaṃ vedacatuṣṭayādhyayanamasya saṃpadyata ityarthaḥ /
4.22.[2]	ye tu svatantramevedaṃ saṃvatsaravrataṃ traividyakasya tapotiśayārthaṃ varṇayanti, ta evaṃ vyācakṣate - pūrveṇa sahāsyaikavākyatā, eṣa saṃvatsaravrataṃ caritvā sarveṣāṃ vedānāṃ caritavrataḥ san vimalo vipāpaśca bhavati, yadi tanmadhye'nyanniṣiddhācaraṇaṃ na kurute // 21 //

4.23.[2]	khalurniścaye // 22 vaidikatvaprasiddhidyotanāya ca phalāntaramāha /

4.24-25.[1]	etasminvrate samāpte, pūrvoktadevatābhyo'naṃ juhoti taṇḍulalakṣaṇaṃ sthālīpākaṃ vā /
4.24-25.[2]	‘chandovatsūtrāṇi bhavanti’ iti subvyatyayaḥ /
4.24-25.[3]	annaśabdo hi kṛte'kṛte vipakve ca dṛṣṭaḥ ‘heṣibhiḥ nidhanaṃ kuryādannakāmāya’ ityakṛtavacanaḥ, ‘annaṃ prayauti ghṛtaṃ madhu taṇḍulān’ ityādau kṛtavacanaḥ, ‘yo'nnamaśnīyāt’ ityādau vipakvavacanaḥ /
4.24-25.[4]	trividhamapi vrīhitaṇḍulasthālīpākarūpaṃ paryāyeṇa yathāsvaṃ nirvāhyam //
4.24-25.[5]	medhā mahyamaṅgiraso medhāṃ saptarṣayo dadhuḥ /
4.24-25.[6]	medhāmagniśca vāyuśca meghāṃ dhātā dhātu me // 1 //
4.24-25.[7]	medhāṃ me varuṇo rājā medhāmagnirdadhātu me /
4.24-25.[8]	medhāmiṃdraśca sūryaśca medhāṃ devī sarasvatī // 2 //
4.24-25.[9]	yā medhā apsarassu gandharveṣu ca yanmanaḥ /
4.24-25.[10]	daivī manuṣye yā medhā sā māmāviśatādiha // 3 //
4.24-25.[11]	śarīraṃ me vicakṣaṇaṃ vāṅme madhumadduhe /
4.24-25.[12]	niśāmitaṃ niśāmaye mayi śrutam // 4 //
4.24-25.[13]	yanme'nūktaṃ tadramatāṃ śakeyaṃ yadanubruve /
4.24-25.[14]	priyāḥ śrutasya bhūyāsma medhayā saṃvidhīmahi // 5 //
4.24-25.[15]	namo hamāya mohamāya //
4.24-25.[16]	sayajuṣkaḥ paṃcarcaḥ /
4.24-25.[17]	agiraso devāḥ mahyaṃ medhāṃ buddhiṃ dadhurdadhatu madarthaṃ kurvantu dadatu vā mahyam /
4.24-25.[18]	kaśyapādayaśca saptarṣayo medhāṃ dadhatu /
4.24-25.[19]	tathāgnirvāyuḥ dhātā prajāpatirmedhāṃ me dadhātu /
4.24-25.[20]	evaṃ rājā varuṇo'gnirindraśca sūryaśca mahyaṃ medhāṃ dadhātu devī ca sarasvatī /
4.24-25.[21]	tathāpsaraḥsu ca yā medhā sthitā, gandharveṣu ca yat manaḥ sthitaṃ, tadubhayamihaiva mānuṣaśarīre sati māmāviśatātpraviśatu /
4.24-25.[22]	yā ca manuṣyaviśeṣe daivī amānuṣī medhā, sāpi māmāviśatāt /
4.24-25.[23]	mama ca śarīraṃ vicakṣaṇaṃ vipaścit sakalakalākovidamastu /
4.24-25.[24]	vāk sarasvatī trayīrūpā me mama madhumat madhuravipākaṃ svargāpavargādikaṃ phalaṃ duhe dogdhu /
4.24-25.[25]	yacca mayi śrutaṃ jātaṃ, niśāmitaṃ cāvabuddhaṃ mayāsīt, tata niśāmaye niśāmayeya smaraṇaśaktistatra mamāstvityarthaḥ /
4.24-25.[26]	yacca mamānūktaṃ guruṇā nigaditaṃ, tadramatāṃ śataśākhaṃ śiṣyapraśiṣyādīn prasaratu phalaparyavasāyi sat /
4.24-25.[27]	yaccānubruve nigaditumicchāmi tacchaknuyām /
4.24-25.[28]	tathā vayaṃ śrutasya priyāḥ bhūyāsma śrutamasmākaṃ phaladānaprasādaparamastu /
4.24-25.[29]	medhayā ca saṃvidhīmahi sambadhyemahi vayam /

8.0.[1]	sarveṣāṃ kṛcchravratānāṃ dvādaśāhādadhikatvaṃ, gauṇatvaṃ tu dvādaśāhasyeti tena tadīyā eva mantrādayo'tra guṇatvena yojayitavyā ityabhiprāyeṇa guṇaviśeṣamāha
8.1.[1]	eteṣu samasteṣu kṛcchreṣu atra yatpūrvaṃ vratamuktaṃ vrataniyamāśceti tasyopāyanaṃ grahaṇopāya itikartavyatā dvādaśāhādityucyate, tyāgopāyaśca tata eveti jñeyam // 1 //
8.2.[1]	prathamasya trirātrasya prathame'hani snātvāgnisamīpe ‘vasavo vratapatayaḥ’ ityādibhirmantrairvrataṃ gṛhṇīyāt /
8.2.[2]	’vasavo vratapatayo vratamālabhe tadvaḥ prabravīmi tacchakeyaṃ tenardhyāsam /’ ityādimatraliṅgāddhi saṃsiddhyantavratagrahaṇānujñāsiddhaye devatābhyarthanaṃ pratīyate /
8.2.[3]	tathā vratānte vratatyāgaḥ kartavyaḥ ‘vasavo vratapatayo vratamacāriṣaṃ tadaśakaṃ tadvaḥ prabrūmastanno gopāya’ ityādibhiḥ /
8.2.[4]	evametaiścaturbhirmantrairvratamālabhya prathame trirātre adbhirvasūnpratyahaṃ tarpayet, dvitīye rudrān, tṛtīye ādityān /
8.2.[5]	caturthe trirātre marudaṅgirasa udakena santarpayet // 2 //
8.3.[1]	prathame tryahe'hanyahani caruṇā mantradvayena vasubhyo homaḥ kāryo brahmacārisnātakābhyāṃ laukike'gnau, gṛhasthenāhavanīye gṛhye'gnau vā // 3 //

8.7.[1]	havyavāhamityādimatreṇa sviṣṭakṛtaṃ juhuyādaviśeṣeṇa sarveṣu tryaheṣu // 7 //

8.7.[4]	rudrā vratapatayo vratamālabhe tadvaḥ prabravīmi tacchakeyaṃ tenardhyāsam //
8.7.[5]	pūrvavyākhyānenaiva gatārthaḥ /

8.7.[19]	yajñaśca vīryavānmāṃ viśatu /

8.7.[21]	sahasraśabdo'tibhūyastvopalakṣaṇārthaḥ /

8.7.[27]	ādityā rudrā vasavaśca mama sadasi bhavāḥ sadasyāḥ bhavantu /

8.7.[30]	teṣāṃ sahasrayojane'va dhanvāni tanmasi // 1 //
8.7.[31]	agniprakaraṇe rudrābhidhānāḥ ṣaḍanuvākāḥ paṭhyante ‘namaste rudra manyave’ ityādyāḥ /
8.7.[32]	tanmadhye ete daśa mantrāḥ /
8.7.[33]	sarveṣu teṣvanuvākeṣu devānāmārṣam /
8.7.[34]	tathāca śrūyate ‘rudraṃ vai devā yajñānnirabhajan /
8.7.[35]	sa devānāyatayā āyāmavatyā senayābhiparyāvartata /
8.7.[36]	ete devā bhītā etacchatarudriyamapaśyaṃstenainamaśamayanyacchatarudriyaṃ juhoti tenaitaṃ rudraṃ vitatadhanvānaṃ saṃhateṣu manyumantaṃ mahābāhuṃ śamayati /’ iti /
8.7.[37]	ye bhūmyāmadhi pṛthivyāmīśvaratvenāntarvartamānā vyavasthitā rudrā asaṃkhyātā sahasrāṇi asaṃkhyāni sahasrāṇi ‘śeśchandasi bahulam’ iti śerluk aparimitā rudrā ityarthaḥ, teṣāṃ kupitānāmāropitaguṇadhanuṣkāṇāṃ hananodyatānāṃ satāṃ dhanvāni dhanūṃṣi avatanmasi avatanumaḥ idanto masiḥ, avatāritaguṇāni kurmaḥ stutidvārakakopapraśāntyā sahasrayojane atidūre sthitāḥ santaḥ /
8.7.[38]	‘ūṣa so'naṅ’ ‘dhanuṣaśca’ ityanaṅ /
8.7.[39]	ye'sminmahatyarṇave'ntarikṣe bhavā adhi /
8.7.[40]	teṣāṃ sahasrayojane'va dhanvāni tanmasi // 2 //
8.7.[41]	ye'sminpratyakṣe sarveṣāmantarikṣe ākāśe arṇave samudre ākāśaṃ hi sūkṣmasamudrayuktamityāhuḥ rātryādāvavaśyāyādirūpajalapatanadarśanāt, athavā ye samudre'ntarikṣe ca mahati adhi bhavā adhipatitvena vartamānāḥ, teṣāṃ dhanūṃṣi avaropitajyāni dūrādeva kurma iti pūrvavat //
8.7.[42]	ye nīlagrīvāḥ śitikaṇṭhā divaṃ rudrā upāśritāḥ /
8.7.[43]	teṣāṃ sahasrayojane'va dhanvāni tanmasi // 3 //
8.7.[44]	ye rudrā nīlagrīvā aśuklagalāśca divaṃ svargamupāśritāḥ /
8.7.[45]	śeṣaṃ pūrvavat //
8.7.[46]	ye nīlagrīvāḥ śitikaṇṭhāḥ śarvā adhaḥ kṣamācarāḥ /
8.7.[47]	teṣāṃ sahasrayojane'va dhanvāni tanmasi // 4 //
8.7.[48]	ye śarvā rudrā adhaḥkṣamācarāḥ pātālacarāḥ //
8.7.[49]	ye vaneṣu śaṣpiṃjarā nīlagrīvā vilohitāḥ /
8.7.[50]	teṣāṃ sahasrayojane'va dhanvāni tanmasi // 5 //
8.7.[51]	ye vipineṣu tarugulmalatāvitānatṛṇādigahaneṣu sthitāḥ śaṣpavat komalatṛṇavat piṃjarāḥ kapilāḥ nīlagrīvāśca, tathā vilohitā nitāntaraktāḥ //
8.7.[52]	ye'nneṣu vividhyanti pātreṣu pibato janān /
8.7.[53]	teṣāṃ sahasrayojane'va dhanvāni tanmasi // 6 //
8.7.[54]	ye cānneṣu bhujyamāneṣu, pīyamāneṣu kṣīrādiṣu pracchannarūpeṇāntargatāḥ santo bhoktṝn pātṝṃśca janān vividhyanti tāḍayanti vyathayanti //
8.7.[55]	ye bhūtānāmadhipatayo viśikhāsaḥ kapardinaḥ /
8.7.[56]	teṣāṃ sahasrayojane'va dhanvāni tanmasi // 7 //
8.7.[57]	ye bhūtānāṃ pṛthivyādīnāṃ devaviśeṣāṇāṃ vādhipatayo rakṣakāḥ /
8.7.[58]	viśikhāso muṇḍāḥ /
8.7.[59]	kapardino jaṭilāḥ //
8.7.[60]	ye pathīnāṃ pathirakṣaya aiḍamṛdā yavyudhaḥ /
8.7.[61]	teṣāṃ sahasrayojane'va dhanvāni tanmasi // 8 //
8.7.[62]	ye pathīnāṃ adhvanyānāṃ pathirakṣaya adhvanyāḥ santo rakṣakā ādityarūpā ityarthaḥ /
8.7.[63]	iḍā annaṃ tatsamūha aiḍaṃ, tanmṛdnanti komalīkurvanti iti aiḍamṛdāḥ /
8.7.[64]	yudhi saṃgrāme yuvanti miśrībhavantīti yavyudhaḥ yoddhāra ityarthaḥ //
8.7.[65]	ye tīrthāni pracaranti sṛkāvanto niṣaṅgiṇaḥ /
8.7.[66]	teṣāṃ sahasrayojane'va dhanvāni tanmasi // 9 //
8.7.[67]	ye tīrthāni pracaranti tapotiśayasiddhaye sṛkāvantaḥ sātiśayabuddhiyuktāḥ, niṣaṅgāḥ khajāstadyuktāḥ //
8.7.[68]	ya etāvanto vā bhūyāṃso vā diśo rudrā vitaṣṭhire /
8.7.[69]	teṣāṃ sahasrayojane'va dhanvāni tanmasi // 10 //
8.7.[70]	ye rudrā etāvanta iyattayā avadhṛtā, bhūyāṃso vā iyattayā anavadhṛtā diśo vitaṣṭhire dikṣu vividhaṃ sthitāḥ //
8.7.[71]	kadācana starīrasi nendra saścasi dāśuṣe /
8.7.[72]	upopennu maghavanbhūya innu te dānaṃ devasya pṛcyate // 1 //
8.7.[73]	aindrī /
8.7.[74]	bṛhatī /
8.7.[75]	eka upaśabdaḥ pādapūraṇaḥ ‘asamupodaḥ pādapūraṇe’ iti pāṇinivacanāt /
8.7.[76]	‘starī hiṃsāyāṃ’ /
8.7.[77]	he indra tvaṃ na kadācana naiva kadācit starīrhiṃsako yajamānasya bhavasi, pratyuta saścasi dāśuṣe /
8.7.[78]	saścatiranugrahakarmā /
8.7.[79]	dāśuṣe iti dvitīyāsthāne vyatyayena caturthī /
8.7.[80]	dāśvāṃsaṃ dātāraṃ yajamānamanugrahṇāsi phalena yojayasi /
8.7.[81]	eko nuśabdaḥ kṣipravacanaḥ, dvitīyo niścayārthaḥ /
8.7.[82]	icchabdo'vadhāraṇārtha ekaḥ, upedityatra tu pādapūraṇārthaḥ /
8.7.[83]	maghamannaṃ dhanaṃ ca vidyate yasya sa maghavā /
8.7.[84]	he maghavan dhaneśa te tava devasya dānādiguṇayuktasya sambandhi dānaṃ dīyamānaṃ svargādiphalaṃ bhūyaḥ pracuraṃ kṣiprameva upapṛcyate ‘pṛcī samparke' sambadhyate /
8.7.[85]	kena /
8.7.[86]	arthāddāśuṣā yajamānena /
8.7.[87]	‘dāśvānsāhānmīḍhāṃ’ iti dāśvāñchabdo nipātitaḥ ‘dāṭa dāne’ ityasya //
8.7.[88]	kadāca na prayucchasyubhe nipāsi janmanī /
8.7.[89]	turīyāditya savanaṃ ta indriyamātasthā amṛtaṃ divi // 2 //
8.7.[90]	‘idi paramaiśvarye’ ityasyendraḥ /
8.7.[91]	saca pūrvamaṃtre'pi āditye pravṛttaḥ ādityānāṃ sthālīpāke viniyogāt /
8.7.[92]	ādityo vātrendro brahmā prajāpatistasyaiva prakāśavibhavatvāt /
8.7.[93]	‘yuccha pramāde’ /
8.7.[94]	he indra evaṃ samyak pūjitaḥ san na kadācit prayucchasi pramādyasi yajñe phalavaiguṇyādirūpeṇa /
8.7.[95]	yata ubhe devamānuṣajanmanī nipāsi nitarāṃ rakṣasi /
8.7.[96]	he turīya tvaramāṇa yadvā caturthagāyatrīpādātmakaparabrahmasvabhāva āditya te tava sambandhi savanaṃ sūyamānaṃ kriyamāṇaṃ karma sūyate'nena phalamiti savanamiti karma, indriyamindradṛṣṭaṃ, divi dyusthānamamṛtamamaraṇadharmakamātasthau āsthitaṃ yajamānaṃ tatra prāpayatītyarthaḥ //
8.7.[97]	yajño devānāṃ pratyeti sumnamādityāso bhavatā mṛḍayantaḥ /
8.7.[98]	ā vo'rvācī sumatirvavṛttyādaṃhościdyā varivovittarāsat //3// triṣṭup /
8.7.[99]	ādityadaivatyā /
8.7.[100]	ādityā evādityāsaḥ ‘ājjaserasuk’ /
8.7.[101]	bhavatā iti subvyatyayaḥ /
8.7.[102]	mṛḍayanta iti tṛcaḥ sthāne śatṛ /
8.7.[103]	he ādityā yato bhavanto mṛḍayitāraḥ sukhayitāraḥ ‘mṛḍa sukhane’ ato hetorayaṃ bhavaddaivatyo yajño devānāṃ yajamānānāṃ sumnaṃ sukhaṃ pratyeti sukhābhimukho gacchati sukhaṃ sādhayatītyarthaḥ /
8.7.[104]	kiṃca vaḥ yuṣmāke sambandhinī sumatiḥ kalyāṇī buddhiḥ arvācī abhimukhā satī āvavṛttyāt asmadabhimukhā āvartatāṃ punaḥpunarasmākaṃ kalyāṇī matirbhavatvityarthaḥ /
8.7.[105]	kīdṛśī matiḥ /
8.7.[106]	aṃhościdyā varivovittarāsat /
8.7.[107]	cicchando'pyarthe /
8.7.[108]	asat bhavati /
8.7.[109]	varivo dhanam /
8.7.[110]	yā aṃhorapi pāpiṣṭhasyāpi varivovittarā dhanalabdhitarā bhavati //
8.7.[111]	vivasva ādityaiṣa te somapīthastasminmandasva /
8.7.[112]	yā divyā vṛṣṭistayā tvā śrīṇāmi // 4 //
8.7.[113]	tamāṃsi vivāsayatīti kṛtvā vivasvān /
8.7.[114]	he vivasvan āditya aditerapatya eṣa te tava somapīthaḥ somapānaṃ somagrahe viniyogāt jyotiṣṭome somapīthaḥ somarasaḥ ihatu ūhenopacāreṇa vā somapīthaḥ sthālīpākastasminsthālīpāke mandasva tṛptiṃ bhajasva /
8.7.[115]	anenaiva karmānuṣṭhānena yā divyā vṛṣṭiḥ, tathā tvāṃ śrīṇāmi miśrīkaromi meghādidvāreṇa vṛṣṭyā saṃyojayāmītyarthaḥ //
8.7.[116]	adabdhemiḥ savitaḥ pāyubhiṣṭvaṃ śivebhiradya paripāhi no gayam /
8.7.[117]	hiraṇyajihvaḥ suvitāya navyase rakṣā mākirno aghaśaṃsa īśata // 5 //
8.7.[118]	he savitaḥ adyāsminnahani naḥ asmākaṃ gayaṃ gṛhaṃ paripāhi paripālaya /
8.7.[119]	kaiḥ /
8.7.[120]	pāyubhiḥ pālanaśīlaiḥ pānaśīlairvā raśmibhiḥ /
8.7.[121]	adabdhebhiḥ anupahiṃsitaiḥ /
8.7.[122]	yatastvaṃ hiraṇyajihvaḥ satyavādī, tena suvitāya phalaprasavanāya yajñāya navyase navāya gayaṃ gṛhaṃ rakṣa /
8.7.[123]	kiṃca mā naḥ asmān kiḥ kaścit aghaṃ pāpaṃ śaṃsatītyaghaśaṃsaḥ pāpiṣṭha īśata prābhūt //
8.7.[124]	sāntapanā idaṃ havirmarutastajjujuṣṭuna /
8.7.[125]	yuṣmākotī riśādasaḥ // 1 //
8.7.[126]	he marutaḥ idaṃ haviḥ yuṣmākaṃ, tattasmāt jujuṣṭana juṣata bhajadhvaṃ, ūtī rakṣāścāsmākaṃ kuruta /
8.7.[127]	samyak tāpayanti vighnakāriṇo rakṣaḥprabhṛtīniti sāntapanāḥ /
8.7.[128]	yato riśādasaḥ riśatirhiṃsākarmā ‘dasu upakṣaye’ hiṃsākāriṇāmupakṣayakāriṇaḥ //
8.7.[129]	yo no marto maruto durhaṇāyustiraścittā vo vasavo jighāṃsat /
8.7.[130]	druhaḥ sapāśaṃ pratiṣūmucīṣṭa tapiṣṭhena tapasā hantanā tam // 2 //
8.7.[131]	he marutaḥ yo naḥ asmān marto maraṇadharmā manuṣyo, duṣṭaṃ hṛṇaṃ kāryamapakāraṃ kāmayamānaḥ, tiraḥ nikaṭe vartamānaḥ guptarūpo vā cittā cittena tiraścitto vā aspaṣṭacittaḥ jighāṃsat jighāṃset vaḥ yuṣmākaṃ sambandhī yuṣmānapi vā yo jighāṃset he vasavaḥ vāsayitāraḥ anyacca kīdṛśo martaḥ, druhaḥ svabhāvena hiṃsakaḥ taṃ pratiṣūmucīṣṭa suṣṭhu pratimuṃcata badhnīta /
8.7.[132]	tathā hantana hiṃsata /
8.7.[133]	kena /
8.7.[134]	tapiṣṭhena tapasā atiśayena tapasā /
8.7.[135]	kīdṛśaṃ tam /
8.7.[136]	sapāśaṃ pāśayati pāśaḥ putradārādiḥ svavargaḥ, saha pāśena vartamānaṃ sapaśubāndhavamityarthaḥ //
8.7.[137]	gṛhamedhā riśādaso maruto māpabhūtana /
8.7.[138]	pramuñcanto no aṃhasaḥ // 3 //
8.7.[139]	gāyatrī /
8.7.[140]	he marutaḥ gṛhamedhā asmākaṃ bhavata gṛhaṃ medhayantīti gṛhamedhāḥ /
8.7.[141]	kīdṛśāḥ santaḥ /
8.7.[142]	riśādasaḥ hiṃsānāṃ kṣayakāriṇaḥ, asmān aṃhasaḥ pāpāt pramuñcantaḥ santaḥ /
8.7.[143]	mā apabhūtana asmākaṃ abhibhavaṃ mā kārṣuḥ //
8.7.[144]	pra budhnayā va īrate mahāṃsi pra nāmāni prayajyavastiradhvam /
8.7.[145]	sahaśriyaṃ damyaṃ bhāgametaṃ gṛhamedhīyaṃ maruto juṣadhvam // 4 //
8.7.[146]	triṣṭup /
8.7.[147]	he marutaḥ etaṃ bhāgaṃ havirlakṣaṇaṃ sthālīpākaṃ juṣadhvaṃ bhajadhvam /
8.7.[148]	gṛhamedhīyaṃ gṛhadevatārhaṃ prayājānuyājahīnam /
8.7.[149]	etena ca bhāgena prayajyavaḥ ijyamānāḥ santaḥ asmabhyaṃ damyaṃ damanārhaṃ abhinavakarituragaprabhṛtikaṃ pratiradhvaṃ dadata sahaśriyaṃ kanakamaṇimuktākalāpādilakṣmīyuktam /
8.7.[150]	mahāṃsi ca tejāṃsi nāmāni ca ‘yajvāno'mī dhārmikāḥ satputrāḥ’ ityādīni pratiradhvam /
8.7.[151]	yato budhne bhavā budhnyā bhūmiloke vartamānā janā vo yuṣmān pra īrate prerate upasarpanti yuṣmadadhīnāḥ siddhiṣvityarthaḥ //
8.7.[152]	krīḍaṃ vaśśardho mārutamanarvāṇaṃ ratheśubham /
8.7.[153]	kaṇvā abhipragāyata // 5 //
8.7.[154]	he prakṛtā marutaḥ vaḥ yuṣmākaṃ sambandhi śardhaḥ balaṃ krīḍaṃ krīḍayatvasmān /
8.7.[155]	kaṇatiḥ śabdakarmā, kaṇantīti kaṇvā vāyavaḥ yūyameva mārutaṃ marutāṃ sambandhi śardhaḥ pragāyata kathayata yādṛśaṃ taditi /
8.7.[156]	kīdṛśaṃ śardhaḥ /
8.7.[157]	ratheśubhaṃ rathavimānādīnāmanukūlaṃ gamane, tathānarvāṇaṃ liṃgavyatyayaḥ /
8.7.[158]	anarva apracyutamityarthaḥ //
8.7.[159]	atyāso na ye marutaḥ svañco yakṣadṛśo na śubhayanta maryāḥ /
8.7.[160]	te harmyeṣṭhāḥ śiśavo na śubhrā vatsāso na prakrīḍinaḥ payodhāḥ // 6 //
8.7.[161]	triṣṭup /
8.7.[162]	atantītyatyā aśvāḥ /
8.7.[163]	naśabdaḥ sarvatropamārthīyaḥ /
8.7.[164]	ye marutaḥ aśvā iva svañcaḥ śobhanagatayaḥ, ye ca yakṣadṛśa iva śubhayantaḥ śubhamicchantaḥ samyagavalokanaṃ kurvanti yakṣā yajvānaḥ maryā martyāḥ, te harmyeṣṭhā bhavantu yajñamaṇḍapasthā bhavantu tatra krīḍantvityarthaḥ /
8.7.[165]	śiśava iva śubhrā anāhāryaśobhāyuktāḥ /
8.7.[166]	prakrīḍanaśīlā vatsā iva vatsāsaḥ, ata eva prakrīḍanaśīlāḥ /
8.7.[167]	payodhāḥ payo dhayanti pibanti ye te payodhāḥ abhinavāḥ /
8.7.[168]	te hi prakrīḍanaśīlā bhavanti vatsāḥ śiśavaśca //
8.7.[169]	tvāmagne aṃgiraso guhāhitamanvavindañchiśriyāṇaṃ vane vane /
8.7.[170]	sa jāyase mathyamānaḥ saho mahattvāmāhuḥ sahasasputramaṃgiraḥ /
8.7.[171]	he agne tvāmaṃgirasaḥ guhāhitaṃ aṃgāreṣu guptamanvavindan lebhire vane vane śiśriyāṇaṃ teṣāṃ vanaspatyādīnāṃ vaneṣvāśritam /
8.7.[172]	saho mahat mahatā sahasā balena mathyamānastvaṃ jāyase /
8.7.[173]	yasmātsa tvamevaṃbhūtaḥ, tasmāttvāmṛṣayaḥ sahaso balasya putramāhuḥ /
8.7.[174]	aṃgiraḥ aṃgāreṣu jātaḥ //
8.7.[175]	vāyuragregā yajñaprīssākaṃ ganmanasā yajñam /
8.7.[176]	śivo niyudbhiḥ śivābhiḥ //
8.7.[177]	vāyureva sarvadevatānāmagre gacchati yasmāt, tasmātsa eva prathamaṃ yajñaprīḥ yajñe prīyate tarpyate /
8.7.[178]	tena ‘aṃgirobhyo dīyamāne haviṣi tanmadhye vāyave'pi havirdīyate’ iti liṃgādvāyorapi devatātvaṃ pratīyate yato vāyureva manasā sākaṃ saha yajñaṃ gat gacchati /
8.7.[179]	śivaḥ śāntaḥ /
8.7.[180]	rūpeṇa yajñopakāriṇā niyujyante iti niyutaḥ aśvāḥ tābhiraśvābhistulyaṃ kṛtvā gacchati //
8.7.[181]	havyavāhamabhimātiṣāhaṃ rakṣohaṇaṃ pṛtanāsu jiṣṇum /
8.7.[182]	jyotiṣmantaṃ dīdyutaṃ purandhimagniṃ viṣṭakṛtamāhuvema //
8.7.[183]	vayamagnimāhuvema āhvayāmaḥ havyavāhaṃ yo devānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca havyaṃ vahati tam /
8.7.[184]	abhimanyate iti abhimāḥ śatruḥ, taṃ prasahate abhibhavati yastamabhimātiṣāham /
8.7.[185]	rakṣasāṃ hantāram /
8.7.[186]	pṛtanāsu parasenāsu jayanaśīlam /
8.7.[187]	jyotiṣmantaṃ jvālākarālam /
8.7.[188]	dīdyutaṃ atiśayena dyotamānam /
8.7.[189]	puraṃ samūhaṃ dhatte dhayati vā purandhistam /
8.7.[190]	yajanamiṣṭaṃ śobhanamiṣṭaṃ karotīti sviṣṭakṛt tam //
8.7.[191]	vastūṃstarpayāmi rudrāṃstarpayāmi ādityāṃstarpayāmi marudaṃgirasastarpayāmi //
8.7.[192]	vasavo vratapatayo vratamacāriṣaṃ tadaśakaṃ tadvaḥ prabrūmastanno gopāyata //
8.7.[193]	rudrā vratapatayo vratamacāriṣaṃ tadaśakaṃ tadvaḥ prabrūmastanno gopāyata //
8.7.[194]	ādityā vratapatayo vratamacāriṣaṃ tadaśakaṃ tadvaḥ prabrūmastanno gopāyata //
8.7.[195]	marudaṅgiraso vratapatayo vratamacāriṣaṃ tadaśakaṃ tadvaḥ prabrūmastanno gopāyata //
8.7.[196]	he vasavaḥ vāsayitāraḥ vratapatayo vratasya pālayitāraḥ yuṣmatprasādādahaṃ vratamacāriṣaṃ caritaṃ sampāditaṃ mayā vratam /
8.7.[197]	tadvratamahamaśakaṃ yuṣmatprasādādaśaknavaṃ śakitaṃ pāritaṃ mayā vratamityarthaḥ /
8.7.[198]	tattasmādvayaṃ vaḥ yuṣmān brūmaḥ tadvratamāsmākīnaṃ vrataṃ yūyaṃ gopāyata rakṣata /
8.7.[199]	etenaivānyadapi mantratrayaṃ vyākhyātam //
9.1.[1]	atra ‘antevāsināṃ yogamicchan’ iti vakṣyamāṇaṃ sambandhanīyam /
9.1.[2]	yadyadadhyayanādhyāpanāṃgaṃ smaryate, tattatkila vaktavyam /
9.1.[3]	upākaraṇaṃ cādhyayanādhyāpanayorapyaṃgam /
9.1.[4]	tathāca ‘antevāsināṃ yogamicchan’ ityato'dhyetuḥ phalasambandhaḥ pratīyate /
9.1.[5]	‘amuṣmai kāmāyāyuṣe tvā’ ityataśca mantraliṃgādupākartrācāryeṇa prayujyamānāddvayorapi śiṣyācāryayoraviśeṣeṇa phalaṃ pratīyate /
9.1.[6]	tatra traividyakatvasiddhyarthaṃ vedādhyayanāṃgabhūtāni vratāni pratipāditāni /
9.1.[7]	adhītavedasyāpi ca śiṣyasyāṃgopāṃgagrahaṇārthaṃ gurorvāsa iṣyate śilpādiśikṣārthaṃ ca /
9.1.[8]	tathāca smṛtiḥ ‘kṛtaśilpo'pi nivasetkaṃcitkālaṃ gurorgṛhe /
9.1.[9]	antevāsī... //’ ityādi /
9.1.[10]	tatrāntevāsināṃ yogaṃ sambandhamicchannācārya upākaraṇaṃ vedānāṃ kuryāt /
9.1.[11]	upākaraṇaṃ svīkaraṇaṃ, manasā saṃkalpanaṃ, etatsthānakaviśeṣādi mayā asmai śiṣyāya pravaktavyamiti /
9.1.[12]	śiṣyo hi śilpāṃgopāṃgaparijñānāyāpi gurau vasan sthānakaviśeṣādikamapi guroḥ sakāśādadhīte, tamadhyāpayatā guruṇā upākaraṇaṃ kartavyam /
9.1.[13]	śiṣyo yadi kasmaicidadhyāpayati, tadā tenāpi kartavyam /
9.1.[14]	so'pihi śiṣyasya guruḥ /
9.1.[15]	naca vaktavyaṃ śiṣyasyācāryavṛttitvāmnānādbrahmacāriṇi gurau kathaṃ vṛttistasya bhojanāstaraṇādidānasāmarthyābhāvāditi, yato bhaikṣavṛttitvamapyāmnātam /
9.1.[16]	sambhavati ca traividyakasya brahmacāriṇo'pi dhanaviśeṣaprāptyā jñānādinā vā svaśiṣyapoṣaṇasāmarthyam /
9.1.[17]	tasmāttenāpyupākaraṇaṃ kartavyaṃ yathāsaṃbhavam /
9.1.[18]	śrāvaṇabhādrapadau māsau varṣāḥ /
9.1.[19]	tatra yat prathamameva śravaṇanakṣatraṃ, tatraivopākaraṇaṃ kartavyaṃ prathamaparityāge kāraṇābhāvāt ‘prathamaṃ vā niyamyeta kāraṇādatikramaḥ syāt’ iti nayena /
9.1.[20]	kiṃ kurvatā /
9.1.[21]	antevāsināṃ sāṃgopāṃgādiśikṣārthaṃ gurau nivasatāṃ yogaṃ sambandhamadhyāpayitradhyāpyalakṣaṇamicchatā antevāsinaśca prajñātiśayasambandhamicchateti phalato vyākhyā // 1 //
9.2.[1]	sa juhoti ya upākaroti ‘apavā nāmāsi’ ityādibhiryajurbhiḥ /
9.2.[2]	anyāstisraḥ /
9.2.[3]	eteṣu yajuṣuḥ prathama mantrasthaṃ ‘tasyāste’ ityetadanuṣajyate vākyaparipūraṇasāmarthyāt anuṣaṃgo vākyasamāpti sarveṣu tulyayogitvāditi nayena /
9.2.[4]	tena ‘rantirnāmāsi tasyāste’ ityādīni trīṇi vākyāni bhavanti /
9.2.[5]	samastapāṭhaḥ śākhāṃtarīyatvāt // 2 //
9.3.[1]	antevāsināṃ yogamicchanniti pratyekaṃ sambadhyate // 3 //
9.4.[1]	‘dadhi krāvṇa’ iti mantraḥ sakṛt /
9.4.[2]	dadhibhakṣaṇamevāvartate triḥ /
9.4.[3]	sāvitrī savitṛdevatyā tatsaviturityādikaiva mahāprabhāvatvāt /
9.4.[4]	nānyā ‘ākṛṣṇena rajasā’ ityādikā /
9.4.[5]	ādāvāditaḥ ye trayo'nuvākāḥ ‘iṣe tvā’ ityādirekaḥ, ‘devasya tvā’ ityādirdvitīyaḥ, ‘vasoḥ pavitramasi’ ityādistṛtīyaḥ /
9.4.[6]	‘kastvā yunakti’ iti cāśvamedhe paridhiniyojane niyuktaḥ /
9.4.[7]	ubhayatrānvāhetyanuṣaṃgaḥ // 4 //
9.5.[1]	tasyādhyāpayituradhyetuścānadhyāya ucyate // 5 //
9.6.[1]	vartamāna nirdeśāttātkālikametadanadhyayanam /
9.6.[2]	vidyotamāne vaidyute tejasi /
9.6.[3]	stanayati garjati meghe // 6 //
9.7.[1]	ākālikaṃ samānakālamucyate /
9.7.[2]	ya evādiḥ sa eva cedanto bhavati, tasya vacane ākālikaśabdo nipātitaḥ ‘ākālikaḍāyantavacane’ iti sūtreṇa, ṭakāro ṅībarthaḥ /
9.7.[3]	ākālikī vidyut, ya evopakramakālaḥ sa eva vināśakālo vidyuta ityarthaḥ /
9.7.[4]	evamihāpi yasminprathamārthapraharādau devatumulādikamutpadyate sa tasyādikālaḥ sa eva dvitīya divase'ntakālo bhavati etadākālikaśabdenoktam /
9.7.[5]	etaduktaṃ bhavati yāvati kāle devatumulādikamutpadyate, tāvatyeva kāle dvitīyadivase'dhyayanayogyatā bhavati antarā tvanadhyāyaḥ /
9.7.[6]	ye tvākālikaśabda ‘na vidyotamāne na stanayati ākālikam’ ityevaṃ pūrveṇa sambandhayanti, yāvaddevatumulādi śrūyate tāvanmātrakālaṃ cānadhyayanamiti vyācakṣate; teṣāmuttaratrāhorātrikamanadhyayanaṃ śabdataḥ prayojyaṃ, vartamānanirdeśalabdhasya ca punarvacanaṃ punaruktam /
9.7.[7]	tatrāntarikṣe gītavādyātmakaṃ gandharvādikṛtaṃ devatumulam /
9.7.[8]	vidyuditi vidyutpāto vivakṣito'trāhorātrādikādhyayanāvasare, dhanvaśabdenāpīndradhanurvarṣākālādanyatra /
9.7.[9]	varṣāsu tātkālikatvaṃ sadācārarūḍham /
9.7.[10]	ulkayāpi mahatyā ulkāyāḥ pāto vivakṣitaḥ /
9.7.[11]	tārakāmā trapatane'pi hyulkāśabdaprayogo'sti // 7 //
9.8.[1]	anye'pyanadhyayanahetava ācārādhyāyoktā anusartavyāḥ bhūkampacandrārkoparāganṛpatimahāpuruṣapramayaprabhṛtayaḥ // 8 //
9.9.[1]	atikrāntā akṣarāṇi atyakṣarāḥ śabdāḥ nirghātahuṃkāratalāsphoṭanaprabhṛtayaḥ /
9.9.[2]	santatasya valīkasya prasrāvo, natu prastrāvamātraṃ tasya prāyeṇa bhāvāt /
9.9.[3]	etadvayamākālikasyānadhyayanasya nimittam // 9 //
9.10.[1]	ardhaṃ paṃcamo yeṣāṃ te'rdhapaṃcamā māsāḥ sārdhacatvāraḥ /
9.10.[2]	evamardhaṣaṣṭhāḥ sārdhapaṃca /
9.10.[3]	māsānuktavidhinādhītyādhyayanārthaprayojakavyāpārādhyayanaṃ nirvartya adhyāpyeti yāvat, utsṛjate adhyāyān utsargasaṃkalpanaṃ karotītyarthaḥ, naca vedādhyayanasya tyāgo'sti, anadhyāyaviśeṣebhyo'pivā utsarge mantradvayasambandhamāha ‘utsṛjāmahe’ ityādi // 10 //
9.11.[1]	ayamanyo'nadhyāyaḥ /
9.11.[2]	pakṣāvivobhayapārśvavartitayā amāvasyāyāścaturdaśī pratipacca /
9.11.[3]	yadyapicācārādhyāye dve paurṇamāsyau dve amāvasye iti caturdaśīsahite paurṇamāsyamāvasye ukte, tathāpi pratipadvidhānārthā punaḥ śrutiḥ /
9.11.[4]	taduktaṃ ‘guṇārthena punaḥ śrutiḥ‘ iti // 11 //
9.12.[1]	ata utsargādūrdhvamabhradarśanamātre'pi sati nādhyetavyaṃ, kā kathā vidyotamānādiṣu //
9.12.[2]	apavā nāmāsi tasyāste joṣṭrīyaṃ gameyamahamiddhamedhaḥ pari medhāmṛtasya jagṛhurahaṃ sūrya ivājani svāhā //
9.12.[3]	rantirnāmāsi, yuktirnāmāsi, yogo nāmāsi, yuje svāhā udyuje svāhā yuktyai svāhā yogāya svāhā //
9.12.[4]	brāhmī vidyā devatā /
9.12.[5]	pavate svarūpāccyavate iti pavā adhruvā, tatpratiṣedhena apavā dhruvā vidyā /
9.12.[6]	kecida‍pveti paṭhanti, tatrāpyayamevārthaḥ /
9.12.[7]	apavā nāmāsi nityānandā, tasyāstava sambandhi yadedhaḥ iddhaṃ rūpaṃ, tadahaṃ gameyaṃ prāpnuyām /
9.12.[8]	iddhamedha iti punarvacanamanāditvakhyāpanārtham /
9.12.[9]	kīdṛśamedhaḥ /
9.12.[10]	joṣṭrīyamatiśayena sevanīyam /
9.12.[11]	etasya amṛtasya maraṇarahitasya brahmamayasya vidyārūpasya medhāṃ parijagṛhurvipaścitaḥ medhāvanto vidyāsvarūpaṃ brahma lebhire ityarthaḥ athavā ṛtasya satyasya brahmaṇo medhāṃ parijagṛhurvipaścitaḥ /
9.12.[12]	ataścāhamapi sūrya ivājani sūrya ivāhamuttamaprakāśo brahmarūpanikaṭaḥ syāmityarthaḥ /
9.12.[13]	svāhā suhutamastu //
9.12.[14]	ramate krīḍati jagadvivartādinā iti rantiḥ brahmamayī vidyā /
9.12.[15]	yujyate loke vivartapariṇāmaśaktibhiriti yuktiḥ /
9.12.[16]	evaṃ yogo, yuk, udyugityādi vyākhyeyam /
9.12.[17]	punarvacanaṃ stutyartham //
9.12.[18]	dadhi krāvṇo akāriṣaṃ jiṣṇoraśvasya vājinaḥ /
9.12.[19]	surabhi no mukhā karatpra ṇa āyūṃṣi tāriṣat //
9.12.[20]	anuṣṭup /
9.12.[21]	asyāśca ṛcaḥ surabhimatīti nāma /
9.12.[22]	tathāca śrutiḥ /
9.12.[23]	‘ṛtvijo yajamānāśca surabhimatīmṛcamanvāhurvācameva punate’ iti /
9.12.[24]	anyatrāśvasaṃskārottarakālamṛtvigyajamānayordadhibhakṣaṇasamayādāviyamabhyarthanā ihāpi yathāyogyatvaṃ yojayitavyā /
9.12.[25]	krāmatīti krāvā /
9.12.[26]	jayanaśīlo jiṣṇuḥ /
9.12.[27]	vyāptyarthasya aśnoteraśvaḥ, vejanavānvājī anyatrāśvaḥ, iha tu prajāpatiḥ /
9.12.[28]	yatkrāvṇo jiṣṇoraśvasya vājinaḥ aśvasya saṃskārakāle aślīlābhibhāṣaṇena mukhāṇyapavitrībhūtāni dadhi dadhnā pavitrāṇi akāriṣaṃ vyatyayenaikavacanaṃ uttaratra ca bahuvacanadarśanāt vayaṃ akāriṣma /
9.12.[29]	prajāpatervā sarvātmakasya vedātmano vā ajñānenāpabhāṣaṇena bālyāditayā apavitrāṇi mukhā mukhāni ‘śeśchandasi bahula’miti luk naḥ asmākaṃ surabhi surabhīni pavitrāṇi karat loḍarthe leṭ ‘itaśca lopaḥ parasmaipadeṣu’ iti terikāralopaḥ ‘leṭo'ḍāṭau’ ityaḍāgamaḥ karotu /
9.12.[30]	kiñva aśvaḥ prajāpatirvā asmākamāyūṃṣi pratāriṣat prataratu karotu /
9.12.[31]	‘tṛ plavanataraṇayoḥ’ pūrvavatpaṃcamalakārādi ‘sip bahulaṃ leṭi’ iṭ guṇaḥ varṇavyatyaye nākāraḥ //
9.12.[32]	iṣe tvorje tvā vāyavassthopāyavasstha devo vassavitā prārpayatu śreṣṭhatamāya karmaṇe //
9.12.[33]	āpyāyadhvamaghnyā devabhāgaṃ prajāvatīranamīvā ayakṣmā //
9.12.[34]	mā vasstena īśata māghaśaṃsaḥ pari vo rudrasya hetivṛṇaktu //
9.12.[35]	dhruvā asmingopatau syāta bahvīryajamānasya paśūnpāhi yajamānasya paśupā asi // 1 //
9.12.[36]	devasya tvā savituḥ prasave'śvinorbāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāmādade goṣadasi pratyuṣṭaṃ rakṣaḥ pratyuṣṭārātiḥ preyamagāddhiṣaṇā barhiraccha manunā kṛtā svadhayā vitaṣṭā //
9.12.[37]	urvantarikṣaṃ vīhīndrasya pariṣūtamasi mādho mopari parusta ṛddhyā samācchettā te mā riṣat //
9.12.[38]	deva barhiśśatavalśaṃ viroha sahasravalśā vi vayaṃ ruhema //
9.12.[39]	adityā rāsnāsīndrāṇyāssannahanaṃ pūṣā te granthiṃ grathnātu sa te mā sthādindrasya vā bāhubhyāmudyacche bṛhaspatestvā mūrdhnāharāmi devaṃgamamasi //
9.12.[40]	tadāharanti kavayaḥ purastāddevebhyo juṣṭamiha barhirāsade // 2 //
9.12.[41]	vasoḥ pavitramasi śatadhāraṃ vasūnāṃ pavitramasi sahasradhāram //
9.12.[42]	ayakṣmā vaḥ prajayā saṃsṛjāmi rāyaspoṣeṇa bahulā bhavantīḥ /
9.12.[43]	madhumaddhṛtavatpinvamānā jīvā jīvantīrupa vassadema //
9.12.[44]	mātariśvano gharmo'si dyaurasi pṛthivyasi viśvadhāyāḥ pareṇa dhāmnāhutāsi mā hvāssā viśvāyussā viśvavyacāssā viśvadhāyā hutasstoko huto drapso'naye bṛhate nākāya svāhā dyāvāpṛthivībhyām //
9.12.[45]	sampṛcyadhvamṛtāvarīrūrmiṇā madhumattamāḥ /
9.12.[46]	maṃdrā dhanasya sātayaḥ //
9.12.[47]	indrasya tvā bhāgaṃ somenātanacmyadhastamasi viṣṇave viṣṇo havyaṃ rakṣasvāpo jāgṛta // 3 //
9.12.[48]	‘iṣe tvā’ ityādayo mantrā dārśapaurṇamāsayoḥ śākhācchedanādau viniyuktāḥ śrutiliṃgādibhiḥ /
9.12.[49]	tatra parameṣṭhinaḥ prājāpatyasyārṣam śākhādirabhidheyo devatā /
9.12.[50]	yajuṣāṃ chando nāstītyeke /
9.12.[51]	kecittu vaiśeṣikaṃ chanda icchanti piṃgalaparipaṭhitaṃ daivyekamityādi /
9.12.[52]	tatra ca sarvasaṃkhyāyā vyavahāraḥ pāda ityadhikārāt /
9.12.[53]	iṣe tvā //
9.12.[54]	devī, anuṣṭup, tryakṣarā, śākhācchedane viniyuktā /
9.12.[55]	‘iṣe tveti cchindanti’ iti /
9.12.[56]	‘iṣu icchāyāṃ’ kip tādarthye caturthī ‘sāvekācastṛtīyādirvibhaktiḥ’ ityantodāttam ‘iṣe’ iti padam, athavā iḍvidyate yasya sa iṣaḥ iṣyamāṇo'nnādiḥ /
9.12.[57]	akāraḥ pratyayaḥ /
9.12.[58]	nimittātkarmasaṃyoge saptamī /
9.12.[59]	‘ādguṇaḥ’ /
9.12.[60]	‘ekādeśa udāttenodāttaḥ’ ityantodāttatvam /
9.12.[61]	‘tvā’ iti karmapadaṃ yuṣmadādeśaḥ karma ca kriyāyām /
9.12.[62]	tatra kriyāyā aśravaṇādviniyogabalācchindanti ityadhyāhāraḥ /
9.12.[63]	annādisiddhaye tvāṃ chindantīti samudāyārthaḥ /
9.12.[64]	annādinimittatvaṃ tu ‘agnerdhūmo jāyate dhūmādabhramabhrādvṛṣṭiḥ /’ ityādiśrutikathitapraṇālikayā //
9.12.[65]	ūrje tvā //
9.12.[66]	‘ūrja balaprāṇanayoḥ’ kvibantaḥ annasya balasya ca nāmadheyatvena prasiddhaḥ /
9.12.[67]	śākhāsannamane parimārjane ca dvipadasyāsya mantrasya tryakṣarāyā daivyā anuṣṭubho viniyogaḥ /
9.12.[68]	parimārjmi sannamayāmīti paryāyeṇādhyāhāraḥ /
9.12.[69]	balārthaṃ tvāṃ parimārjmi sannamayāmīti vākyārthaḥ //
9.12.[70]	vāyavasthopāyavasstha //
9.12.[71]	anuṣṭup /
9.12.[72]	vatsadaivatyā /
9.12.[73]	catasṛṇāṃ gavāṃ sambandhino vatsān śākhayopaspṛśan deśāddeśāntaraṃ nayati kṛtaprasravaṇān /
9.12.[74]	he vatsāḥ vāyavaḥ iva stha bhavata kṛtaprasravaṇāḥ santo vegenāpasarata yāvadahaṃ kṣīraṃ gṛhṇāmi, upāyavasstha upagacchata mātuḥ samīpe anusarata punaḥ kṣīraṃ pātumityarthaḥ //
9.12.[75]	devo vaḥ savitā prārpayatu śreṣṭhatamāya karmaṇe //
9.12.[76]	dhṛtiśchandaḥ, gāvo devatā, anena dhenūḥ prācīṃ gamayati /
9.12.[77]	he dhenavaḥ vo yuṣmān devo dānādiguṇakaḥ, savitā karmaṇo'nujñātā phalaprasavitā vā prārpayatu śarīrāntarasambandhaṃ samarpayatu deśāntaraṃ prāpayatu, natvahaṃ mānuṣamātra ityarthaḥ /
9.12.[78]	kimartham /
9.12.[79]	śreṣṭhatamāya karmaṇe yajñārthaṃ ‘yajño vai śreṣṭhatamaṃ karma’ iti śrutiḥ //
9.12.[80]	‘āpyāyadhvaṃ’ ityādi yajuḥ /
9.12.[81]	he aghnyāḥ ahantavyāḥ aghasya pāpasya hantryo vā devasyendrasya sambandhinaṃ bhāgaṃ bhajanīyaṃ sānnāyyalakṣaṇamāpyāyadhvam ‘pyāyī vṛddhau’ vardhayata /
9.12.[82]	yato yūyaṃ prajāvatīḥ prajāvatyaḥ putravatyaḥ, anamīvā ‘ama roge’ ityasyāmīvāśabdaḥ vyādhiviśeṣaśūnyāḥ, ayakṣmāḥ yakṣmo vyādhiviśeṣaḥ rājayakṣmākhyastacchūnyāḥ, athavā ayanamayaḥ kṣmāyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ yāsāṃ tāḥ ayakṣmāḥ /
9.12.[83]	‘mā vasstena īśata’ vaḥ yuṣmākaṃ stenaścauro mā prābhūt /
9.12.[84]	‘māghaśaṃsaḥ’ - aghaṃ pāpaṃ śaṃsatītyaghaśaṃsaḥ cāṇḍālādiḥ mā vaḥ īśata /
9.12.[85]	‘pari vo rudrasya hetivṛṇaktu’ parivṛṇaktu parivarjayatu /
9.12.[86]	‘dhruvā asmingopatau syāta bahvīḥ’ asminyajamāne sthirā bhavata bahvīḥ bahvyaśca bhavatāsmin /
9.12.[87]	‘yajamānasya paśūnpāhi yajamānasya paśupā asi /’ anena śākhāṃ sthāpayati, he śākhe yatastvaṃ svabhāvenaiva yajamānasya paśupāḥ ato yajamānasya paśūnpāhi //
9.12.[88]	prathamo'nuvākaḥ // 1 //
9.12.[89]	devasya tvā savituḥ prasave'śvinorbāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāmādade //
9.12.[90]	anena havirnidadhāti /
9.12.[91]	saṃkṛtiśchandaḥ /
9.12.[92]	he dhānyādika devasya saviturādityasya prasave'nujñāyāṃ vartamānastena prakāśadvāreṇa karmasu pravartanāt, aśvinoḥ sambandhibhyāṃ bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇaśca hastābhyāṃ natu svakābhyāṃ carmādimayābhyāṃ tvāmādade /
9.12.[93]	pratigrahādāvapyasya viniyogaḥ //
9.12.[94]	goṣadasi //
9.12.[95]	barhirlavaṇīmaśvapaśūnāmāha gāvaḥ sīdantyasyāmiti goṣat tathā barhirlavaṇyā gāvo vartante ityevamuktam //
9.12.[96]	‘pratyuṣṭaṃ rakṣaḥ pratyuṣṭārātiḥ’ ityagnimabhyarthayate paśūṃstāpayan /
9.12.[97]	‘uṣa dāhe’ rakṣaḥ rākṣasa upalakṣaṇametat rākṣasapiśācādikaṃ pratidagdhamastu /
9.12.[98]	na vidyate rātiḥ dhanaṃ yatra so'rātirarthābhāvaḥ alakṣmīrityādiparyāyaḥ, adānaṃ kārpaṇyaṃ vā arātiḥ, śatrurvā arātiḥ sa dagdho bhavatu //
9.12.[99]	barhirlavanāyottiṣṭhannāha preyamagāddhiṣaṇā barhiraccha manunā kṛtā svadhayā vitaṣṭā //
9.12.[100]	iyaṃ mama dhiṣaṇā buddhiḥ barhiḥ karmabhūtaṃ accha prāgāt ābhimukhyena gantuṃ pravṛttā /
9.12.[101]	‘acchābheḥ śākapūṇiḥ’ ityacchaśabdo'bherarthe ābhimukhye vartate /
9.12.[102]	kīdṛśī dhiṣaṇā /
9.12.[103]	manunā prajāpatinā kṛtā, tathā svadhayā annena vitaṣṭā tīkṣṇīkṛtā //
9.12.[104]	barhiḥsthānaṃ gacchati urvantarikṣaṃ vīhi //
9.12.[105]	he caraṇayugalaka uru vistīrṇamantarikṣaṃ vīhi gaccha //
9.12.[106]	darbhastambaṃ triḥ parilikhati indrasya pariṣūtamasi //
9.12.[107]	he darbhastamba tvamindrasya kṛte pariṣūtaṃ jātaḥ //
9.12.[108]	pakvaṃ madhyena yojayati //
9.12.[109]	mādho mopari paruste //
9.12.[110]	he darbhastamba te tava paruḥ parva adhaḥ upari mā bhūt paraśudhārāsāmyena vartatāmityarthaḥ //
9.12.[111]	lunāti ṛddhyā samācchettā te mā riṣat //
9.12.[112]	‘ruṣa riṣa hiṃsārthaḥ’ te tava samācchettā lavitā ṛddhiṃ mā riṣat mā hiṃsīt yajñasādhanaśaktiṃ mā cchaitsīdityarthaḥ /
9.12.[113]	ṛddhyeti vyatyayena tṛtīyā //
9.12.[114]	chinnaśeṣāṇi bhūmilagnāni punaḥprarohaṇasamarthāni barhirmūlāni abhimṛśati deva barhiḥ śatavalśaṃ viruha sahasravalśā vi vayaṃ ruhema //
9.12.[115]	he deva barhiḥ tvaṃ jātaṃ sat śatavalśaṃ śataśākhaṃ viruha vardhasva, vayamapi tvatprasādāt sahasravalśāḥ sahasraśākhāḥ viruhema vardhiṣīmahi //
9.12.[116]	bandhanārthaṃ rajjuṃ karoti adityā rāsnāsi //
9.12.[117]	asi tvaṃ adityāḥ pṛthivyā rāsnā rajjuḥ //
9.12.[118]	barhiḥ sannahyati indrāṇyāḥ sannahanaṃ pūṣā te granthiṃ grathnātu sa te mā sthāt //
9.12.[119]	yatastvamindrāṇyāḥ sannahanaṃ bandhanamataste pūṣā indro granthiṃ grathnātu te barhiṣaḥ, tvāmindro badhnātvityarthaḥ /
9.12.[120]	saca granthirmathitaḥ san tava ciraṃ mā sthāt śīghrameva tava vimuktasya yajñopayogo'stvityarthaḥ //
9.12.[121]	udyacchati barhiḥ indrasya tvā bāhubhyāmudyacche //
9.12.[122]	he barhiḥ tvāmahamindrasya sambandhibhyāṃ bāhubhyāmudyacchāmi, natu svakābhyāṃ carmādimayābhyāmiti //
9.12.[123]	protsāhena uddhṛtaṃ mūrdhni nidhatte bṛhaspatestvā mūrdhnāharāmi //
9.12.[124]	tvāmahaṃ bṛhaspateḥ sambandhinā mūrdhnā śirasāharāmi dhārayāmīti //
9.12.[125]	pūrvadbarhirāha devaṅgamamasi //
9.12.[126]	asi tvaṃ barhirdevaṅgamaṃ devārthaṃ tava nayanamityarthaḥ //
9.12.[127]	na kevalaṃ vayameva devārthaṃ tvā nayāmaḥ, pūrvairapyevamanuṣṭhitamityāha tadāharanti kavayaḥ purastāt //
9.12.[128]	kavayaḥ krāntadarśanāḥ samyagviditānuṣṭhitasakalavedārthāḥ tadbarhirevamevāhṛtavanta iti tātparyārthaḥ //
9.12.[129]	vedyāmāsādayati devebhyo juṣṭamiha barhirāsade //
9.12.[130]	idaṃ barhidevebhyo juṣṭamiti rucitamiha vedyāmāsādayāmīti //
9.12.[131]	dvitīyo'nuvākaḥ // 2 //
9.12.[132]	kṣīrapāvanārthaṃ darbhapavitraṃ karoti vasoḥ pavitramasi śatadhāraṃ vasūnāṃ pavitramasi sahasradhāram //
9.12.[133]	he pavitra vasordhanasya kṣīrasya tvaṃ pavitraṃ pāvanaṃ asi /
9.12.[134]	śatasahasragrahaṇamaparimitatvopalakṣaṇārtham, aparimitacchidratvādaparimitadhāramityarthaḥ /
9.12.[135]	vasūnāmiti āstāmidamekayajamānasambhṛtamalpaṃ payaḥ, yāvajjagatīgatānāmitarayajamānasambhṛtānāṃ payasāṃ pāvanamasi /
9.12.[136]	yadvātra maruto vasava ucyante indrasāhāyyena vartamānāḥ, te hi vasate ācchādayantīti vasavaḥ /
9.12.[137]	tathāca brāhmaṇam ‘vasūnāṃ vā etadbhāgadheyam’ iti //
9.12.[138]	vatsaiḥ saṃgṛhyamāṇā gā anumantrayate ayakṣmā vaḥ prajayā saṃsṛjāmi rāyaspoṣeṇa bahulā bhavantīḥ //
9.12.[139]	he ayakṣmāḥ vyādhiviśeṣahīnāḥ avadhyadhanā vā vo yuṣmān prajayā saṃsṛjāmi /
9.12.[140]	rāyo dhanasya bhakṣyaviśeṣātmakasya poṣeṇa bahulāḥ pravṛddhadehā bhavantīḥ, yadvā dhanapuṣṭyā saha bahulāḥ pracurāḥ bhavantīḥ //
9.12.[141]	duhyamānāsu japati madhumadghṛtavatpinvamānā jīvā jīvantīrupa vaḥ sadema //
9.12.[142]	he gāvaḥ vo yuṣmānvayamupasadema anavaratamityāśāsmahe /
9.12.[143]	kīdṛśīḥ /
9.12.[144]	jīvantīḥ dīrghāyuṣaḥ, jīvāḥ prāṇayutā balavatīrityarthaḥ kiṃ kurvatīḥ /
9.12.[145]	madhumat madhurarasasaṃyuktaṃ ghṛtavaccātisnigdhaṃ kṣīraṃ pinvamānāḥ sravantyaḥ //
9.12.[146]	gārhapatyādaṃgārarāśiṃ pṛthakkaroti mātariśvano gharmo'si //
9.12.[147]	he aṃgārarāśe tvaṃ mātariśvano vāyoḥ gharmaḥ tejaḥ /
9.12.[148]	tathāca brāhmaṇam ‘antarikṣaṃ vai mātariśvano gharmaḥ /’ iti /
9.12.[149]	atrāntarikṣaśabdaḥ tātsthyādantarikṣasthe bhānutejasi vartate //
9.12.[150]	uddhṛte'ṅgārarāśau ukhāmadhiśrayati dyaurasi pṛthivyasi viśvadhāyāḥ pareṇa dhāmnāhutāsi mā hvāḥ //
9.12.[151]	‘upastautyevaināmetat’ iti śrutiḥ /
9.12.[152]	yadā divaḥ patitenodakena sampādyate tadā dyauriti stūyate /
9.12.[153]	pṛthivyavayavanirmitatvātpṛthivīti /
9.12.[154]	viśvaṃ sarvaṃ dhatte iti viśvadhā pṛthivī, tasyāḥ sambandhinā pareṇotkṛṣṭena dhāmnā tejasā sāreṇa asi tvaṃ ahutā ‘hvṛ kauṭilye’ akuṭilā /
9.12.[155]	yataśca tvamakuṭilā, ataḥ mā hvāḥ dravyadhāraṇe vyāpṛtā satī kuṭilā mā bhūḥ //
9.12.[156]	tisṛṣu dhenuṣu dugdhāsu kāṃ dugdhavānasīti praśne amūmiti cottare dogdhrābhihite adhvaryurāha sā viśvāyuḥ sā viśvavyacāḥ sā viśvadhāyā //
9.12.[157]	yā prathamaṃ dugdhā, sā viśvāyuḥ sarvasyāyuṣo dhātrī kṣīrādidvāreṇa /
9.12.[158]	tathāca śrutiḥ ‘āyurghṛtam’ iti /
9.12.[159]	yā dvitīyasthānadugdhā, sā viśvavyacāḥ ‘vyaca sambhave’ viśvaṃ tataḥ sambhavati yajñadvāreṇa /
9.12.[160]	yā tṛtīyasthānadugdhā, sā viśvadhāyā viśvaṃ dhāpayatīti viśvadhāyā sarvasya kṣīreṇa tṛptiṃ karotītyarthaḥ //
9.12.[161]	pṛthagbhavato dugdhavipruṣo'numantrayate hutaḥ stoko'huto drapso'gnaye bṛhate nākāya svāhā dyāvāpṛthivībhyām //
9.12.[162]	yaḥ stoko binduḥ, yaśca drapsaḥ sthūlo bhūmau patitaḥ sa sarva evāhuto'pi huto'stu kasmai /
9.12.[163]	agnaye, bṛhate mahate, tathā nākāya nāsmin akaṃ duḥkhamastīti kṛtvā svargāya /
9.12.[164]	dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ ca svāhā suhutamastu //
9.12.[165]	dyaurantarikṣamiti yatra pātre dohaḥ kṛtastasmādukhāyāṃ kṣīre āsikte sati yatkiṃcana dohabhāṇḍe lagnaṃ, tadadbhiḥ prakṣālya sthālyāṃ nikṣipati sampṛcyadhvamṛtāvarīrūrmiṇā madhumattamāḥ /
9.12.[166]	mandrā dhanasya sātayaḥ //
9.12.[167]	he āpaḥ saṃpṛcyadhvaṃ payasokhāsthena /
9.12.[168]	ṛtāvarīḥ satyavatyaḥ, yajñavatyo vā tatsādhanatvāt /
9.12.[169]	kena /
9.12.[170]	ūrmiṇā kallolaiḥ /
9.12.[171]	madhumattamā madhuratamarasasaṃyuktāḥ /
9.12.[172]	maṃtrāḥ ‘madī harṣe’ mādayitryaḥ, tathā dhanasya sātayaḥ sādhikāḥ //
9.12.[173]	dugdhe dadhyāsiñcati indrasya tvā bhāgaṃ somenātanacmi //
9.12.[174]	he payaḥ tvāṃ somena dadhnā ātanacmi saṃkocayāmi, tañciḥ saṃkocanārthaḥ /
9.12.[175]	kīdṛśaṃ tvām /
9.12.[176]	indrasya bhāgaṃ bhajanīyam //
9.12.[177]	gārhapatyasamīpe payaḥ sthāpayati adastamasi viṣṇave //
9.12.[178]	‘dasu upakṣaye’ adastamanupakṣīṇaṃ he payaḥ yatastvaṃ viṣṇave viṣṇvarthaṃ yajñopayogītyarthaḥ /
9.12.[179]	‘yajño vai viṣṇuḥ’ iti śrutiḥ //
9.12.[180]	havirabhimantrayate viṣṇo havyaṃ rakṣasva //
9.12.[181]	he viṣṇo idaṃ havyaṃ havanīyaṃ rakṣasva //
9.12.[182]	sajalena dārupātreṇa ukhāṃ pidadhāti āpo jāgṛta //
9.12.[183]	he āpaḥ jāgṛta rakṣārthaṃ jāgarūkā bhavata //
9.12.[184]	tṛtīyo'nuvākaḥ // 3 //
9.12.[185]	kastvā yunakti sa tvā yunaktu viṣṇustvā yunaktvasya yajñasya //
9.12.[186]	yajñādikaṃ prastutaṃ karmaivamucyate /
9.12.[187]	kaḥ prajāpatiḥ, he karman, tvāṃ yunakti saṃpādayati phalena vā yojayati /
9.12.[188]	sa ityapi prajāpatereva nirdeśaḥ parokṣarūpeṇa /
9.12.[189]	abhyāse bhūyāṃsamarthaṃ manyante yathā aho ramaṇīyā aho ramaṇīyeti /
9.12.[190]	viṣṇuryajñaḥ, saca prajāpatireva /
9.12.[191]	yajñastvā yunaktu phalena saṃvardhayatu /
9.12.[192]	kimartham /
9.12.[193]	asya prārabdhasya yajñādikasya karmaṇaḥ samṛddhyai māhātmyāya /
9.12.[194]	sāvitryanuvākavadanuvacanamasya //
9.12.[195]	amuṣmai kāmāyāyuṣe tvā prāṇāya tvā vyānāya tvāpānāya tvā vyuṣṭyai tvā rayyai tvā rādhase tvā poṣāya tvā ghoṣāya tvārāddhoṣāya vā pracyutyai tvā //
9.12.[196]	atra pratyekaṃ tarpayāmītyadhyāhṛtya yojanīyam /
9.12.[197]	amuṣmai kāmāya tvāṃ prajāpatiṃ tarpayāmi /
9.12.[198]	asāvityukte nāma pratīyāt /
9.12.[199]	tena ‘amuṣmai’ ityasmātkāmyamānapaśuputrādiphalaviśeṣanāmāni pratyetavyāni /
9.12.[200]	āyuṣe āyurarthaṃ tvāṃ tarpayāmi /
9.12.[201]	sarvatra tādarthye caturthī /
9.12.[202]	vyuṣṭyai tvāṃ tarpayāmi ‘uṣa dāhe’ viśeṣeṇa avidyāsmitārāgadveṣābhiniveśalakṣaṇānāṃ kleśānāṃ uṣṭiḥ, tadartham /
9.12.[203]	rayirdhanaṃ, tadartham /
9.12.[204]	rādho'nnam /
9.12.[205]	poṣastattvajñānasya, tadartham /
9.12.[206]	prakarṣeṇa cyutiḥ saṃsārasya, tadarthaṃ tvāṃ prajāpatiṃ tarpayāmi //
9.12.[207]	agnaye vāyave sūryāya brahmaṇe indrāya prajāpataye bhavāya śarvāya īśānāya īśvarāya viṣṇave bṛhaspataye yajurvedāya cchandobhya ṛṣibhyo vedebhyo brāhmaṇebhyaḥ somebhyaḥ somapebhya ācāryebhyo namo namaḥ //
9.12.[208]	ityudakatarpaṇamācārādhyāyoktamado'pyadhyāyopākaraṇam //
9.12.[209]	iti navamī kāṇḍikā // 9 //
10.1.[1]	śiṣyā ucyante iti śeṣaḥ /
10.1.[2]	adhyāyopākaraṇānantaramadhyayanaprasaṃgenopaniṣad śāstraṃ ye'rhanti, te upaniṣadarhāḥ śiṣyāḥ naiṣṭhikabrahmacāryādaya ucyante // 1 //
10.2.[1]	brahmacārī naiṣṭhikabrahmacaryayuktaḥ, sucaritamasyāstīti sucaritī sadācāro gṛhasthādirapi /
10.2.[2]	medhāvī grahaṇadhāraṇaśaktiyuktaḥ /
10.2.[3]	karmakṛt nityanaimittikakarmānuṣṭhānarataḥ guruparicaryācaraṇakārī ca /
10.2.[4]	dhanadaḥ pracuradhanadāne samarthaḥ grahaṇānte gurudakṣiṇāvasāne, natu pūrvaṃ niṣiddhatvāt ‘na pūrvaṃ gurave kiñcidupakurvīta dharmavit /’ iti /
10.2.[5]	priyaḥ putrādiḥ sadācāraḥ /
10.2.[6]	yaśca vidyayā vidyāntaramāditsate, tāni brahmaṇastīrthāni vedasya rahasyarūpasya dāne nipānāni grahaṇe copāyā ityarthaḥ /
10.2.[7]	tīrthaṃ hi nipānaṃ smṛtam /
10.2.[8]	‘tīrthāmidhānamicchanti tritayaṃ kṛtabuddhayaḥ /
10.2.[9]	śāstraṃ caiva nipānaṃ ca vāri cāpyṛṣisevitam //’ iti // 2 //
11.1.[1]	adhyāhitāgniṃ vakṣyati /
11.1.[2]	tatsaṃbaddhamidamanāgatāvekṣaṇenābhidhīyate /
11.1.[3]	sahadharmacāriṇīmudvoḍhukāmastasmindeśaviśeṣe śaraṇaṃ kārayet sthapatyādibhirvivahanātpūrvameva /
11.1.[4]	kīdṛśaṃ śaraṇam /
11.1.[5]	prādvāraṃ dakṣiṇadvāraṃ vā /
11.1.[6]	tathā navaṃ anyānupayuktadārvādinirmitam /
11.1.[7]	navāvasānaṃ avasānaṃ bhūpradeśaḥ navapradeśamityarthaḥ /
11.1.[8]	samamanimnonnatam /
11.1.[9]	samūlaṃ praśastakrīḍākusumādimūlayuktam /
11.1.[10]	samavasrāvaṃ samo'vasrāvo yatra tatsamavasrāvaṃ, udakaṃ prakṣiptaṃ yatra samaṃ kṛtvā sravati sañcarati, tatsamavasrāvaṃ, atiraścīnamityarthaḥ /
11.1.[11]	samavasrāvaṃ yadbhūmaṃḍalaṃ tasminniti saṃbandhaḥ /
11.1.[12]	samavasrutya vā yasmātprāgudīcyaḥ āpo nirdraveyuḥ, pratyagudīcyo vā nirhareyuḥ nirgaccheyuḥ /
11.1.[13]	athavā pratīcīmudīcīṃ vā yatrāpo gacchanti, tasmiṃstiraścīne'pi śaraṇaṃ kārayet // 1 //
11.2.[1]	madhyamāyāḥ sthūṇāyāḥ stambhasya sambandhini karte ‘kṛtī cchedane’ kṛtyate iti kartaḥ khātaḥ gartastasmin, prāgagrānudgagrānvā svastikasanniveśabhājo darbhānāstīrya, teṣveva darbheṣvadhikaraṇabhūteṣu sthūṇāṃ stambhaṃ madhyamamavadadhāti prakṣipati //
11.2.[2]	prakṣepe cedaṃ mantratrayamāha dhruvāmityādi he sthūṇe tvāṃ dhruvāṃ dṛḍhāṃ kṛtvā sinomi prakṣipāmi garte /
11.2.[3]	tvaṃ hi amṛtasya amaraṇadharmakasya patnī pālayitrī /
11.2.[4]	ataḥ kṣeme tiṣṭha kṣemanimittaṃ tiṣṭha /
11.2.[5]	kiṃ kurvatī /
11.2.[6]	ghṛtamukṣamāṇā dadatī ghṛtagrahaṇaṃ sarvasampadupalakṣaṇārtham /
11.2.[7]	yata evaṃ bhūtāsi, atastāṃ tvāṃ he sthūṇe vayamāviśemetyāśāsmahe /
11.2.[8]	praviṣṭāśca santastvadāyattaṃ gṛhamihaiva janmani sarvavīrāḥ bahuputrāḥ suvīrāḥ suputrāḥ, ariṣṭavīrāḥ anupahiṃsitaputrāśca syāma //
11.2.[9]	he sthūṇe ihaiva sthāne amṛtenāvināśinā rūpeṇopalakṣitā satī roha rūḍhā bhava /
11.2.[10]	kīdṛśī satī /
11.2.[11]	aśvāvatī aśvayuktā /
11.2.[12]	evaṃ gomatī /
11.2.[13]	amṛtaiśca gṛhamānuṣairyuktā satī /
11.2.[14]	sūnṛtaṃ satyaṃ vaidikaṃ ca karma yāgādikaṃ, tadvatī /
11.2.[15]	ūrjasvatī ‘ūrja balaprāṇanayoḥ’ prāṇayantī balavatī vetyarthaḥ /
11.2.[16]	payasvatī kṣīravatī /
11.2.[17]	sarvasamṛddhiyuktamasmadgṛhaṃ kurvityarthaḥ /
11.2.[18]	ata evāha ‘asmānsthūṇe payasābhyāvavṛtsva’ he sthūṇe asmān payaḥprabhṛtinā ābhimukhyena vartamānena āvavartayasva //
11.2.[19]	kiṃca tvāṃ karmabhūtāṃ kumārastaruṇa āviśatu, vatsaśca āviśatu /
11.2.[20]	ekavacanaṃ vyatyayena bahuvacanasthāne /
11.2.[21]	jagatā jaṃgamena garbhavāsādinā parisrutaḥ parivṛto dugdhasya kumbhastvāviśatu ayaṃ dadhnaḥ kalaśaiḥ saha // 2 //
11.3.[1]	mantramāha ṛtena sthūṇāmiti virāṭa /
11.3.[2]	he vaṃśa ṛtena satyena apātinā rūpeṇa tvaṃ sthūṇāmadhiroha stambhasyopari tiṣṭha /
11.3.[3]	kīdṛśaḥ /
11.3.[4]	ugraḥ anabhibhavanīyaḥ san viśeṣeṇa rājamānaḥ /
11.3.[5]	anyacca apasedha nāśaya śatrūn ātmīyān sthitipratibandhahetubhūtān, āsmākāṃśca /
11.3.[6]	stambhādhiṣṭhātrī devataivamabhidhīyate /
11.3.[7]	evaṃ ca śatrūn asmadarīṃścābhibhūya niścintaṃ gṛhādhiṣṭhātari tvayi sthite sati, athā anantaraṃ tava vayameva sarvavīrāḥ bahuputrayuktāḥ rayiṃ dhanaṃ bhaviṣyāmaḥ pratidinaṃ havirdānena vayameva hi te svabhūtāḥ /
11.3.[8]	itiśabdo mantrasamāptipratīkaḥ /
11.3.[9]	madhyamavaṃśastambhayoḥ mantraviniyogāditarastambhavaṃśānāmamantrakaṃ tūṣṇīmevārohaṇaṃ śasyate //
11.4.[1]	‘prāñcaṃ vaṃśaṃ samāropayati’ iti ‘prāgdvāraṃ dakṣiṇadvāraṃ vā śaraṇaṃ kārayet’ iti coktam /
11.4.[2]	tatra prāgdvāratāpakṣe pūrvāgratā vaṃśasamādhānasya bhāvayitavyaitadarthamidaṃ sūtram /
11.4.[3]	samādhānaṃ samyagādhānaṃ vaṃśasyāropaṇaṃ kuḍyakoṭiṣu //
12.1.[1]	atha vivāhe kṛte vaivāhanāgnau praveśite'nantaramadhyāhitāgniko vāstvāviśet //
12.1.[2]	vasantyasminniti vāstu gṛham /
12.1.[3]	kiṃ kṛtvā praviśet /
12.1.[4]	vāstoṣpatīyasya sthālīpākasyeṣṭvā /
12.1.[5]	vāstorgṛhasya patiradhiṣṭhātrī devatā vāstoṣpatiḥ mayūravyaṃsakāditvātsupo'luṅgipātanam /
12.1.[6]	vāstoṣpatirdevatā yasya sa vāstoṣpatīyaḥ ‘vṛddhācchaḥ’ vyatyayena ṣaṣṭhī sthālīpākeneṣṭvā avayavāvayavisambandhena vā, nahi samasto'sau hūyate bhakṣyasaṃrakṣaṇāt /
12.1.[7]	nanu ceṣṭvā āviśedityuktamayuktaṃ praviśya yajanāt? satyaṃ, kintvadhyavasāyapaurvakālyena netre sammīlya hasatītyādivat /
12.1.[8]	yājayitveti vā ṇijartho yojanīyaḥ /
12.1.[9]	nirvāpasyāmantrakasyeṣṭatvāt ‘amī vahāḥ’ ityādinā ‘catasṛbhiḥ’ ityantena śiṣyahitārthaṃ catasraḥ paṭhitvārpayati //
12.1.[10]	amī vahā vāstoṣpate viśvā rūpāṇyāviśan /
12.1.[11]	sakhā suśeva edhi naḥ // 1 //
12.1.[12]	vāstoṣpate pratijānīmānsvāveśo'namīvo bhavā naḥ /
12.1.[13]	yattvemahe prati tanno juṣasva śanno bhava dvipade śaṃ catuṣpade //
12.1.[14]	vāstoṣpate prataraṇo na edhi gayasphāno gobhiraśvebhirindo /
12.1.[15]	ajarāsaste sakhye syāma piteva putrānprati no juṣasva // 3 //
12.1.[16]	vāstoṣpate śagmayā saṃsadāte sakṣīma hiraṇvayā gātumatyā /
12.1.[17]	pāhi kṣema uta yoge varanno yūyaṃ pāta svastibhiḥ sadā naḥ // 4 //
12.1.[18]	prathamā gāyatrī /
12.1.[19]	anyāstriṣṭubhaḥ /
12.1.[20]	vāstoṣpatirantarikṣanivāsī vāyuḥ, yadvā prāṇaḥ /
12.1.[21]	he vāstoṣpate gṛhasvāmin viśveṣāṃ sarveṣāmasmatparijanānāṃ rūpāṇi svarūpāṇi āviśan adhitiṣṭhan amī amūn parijanānāvaha prāpaya pūrvametāneva gṛhaṃ praveśaya /
12.1.[22]	prathamaṃ parijanasya gṛhapraveśamanujānīhi paścādasmākamiti bhāvaḥ /
12.1.[23]	evamevānutiṣṭhanno'smākaṃ sakhā mitraṃ supraveśanīyo bhava //
12.1.[24]	he vāstoṣpate pratijānīhyasmān gṛhapatiḥ paramaḥ san asmānapyavāntarasvāmitayāṃgīkurvityarthaḥ /
12.1.[25]	svāveśaḥ sukhapraveśaśca no'smākaṃ bhava /
12.1.[26]	tathānamīvo vyādhiśūnyo'smākaṃ bhava /
12.1.[27]	kiṃca yattubhyaṃ kiñciddadmo havirādikaṃ, tanno'smākaṃ sambandhi juṣasva bhajasva /
12.1.[28]	tathā śaṃ sukhaṃ no bhava dvipade mānuṣarūpe, catuṣpade gavāvādike //
12.1.[29]	he vāstoṣpate naḥ asmākaṃ prataraṇaḥ prakarṣeṇa saṃsārasāgarakleśataraṇaḥ edhi bhava /
12.1.[30]	‘asa bhuvi’ loṭ, sipi hyādeśaḥ ‘hujhalbhyo iti dhitvaṃ ‘ghvasoreddhāvabhyāsalopaśca’ /
12.1.[31]	gayasphānaḥ gayaṃ gṛhaṃ, gṛhe sphītaḥ san gobhiraśvaiśca sahitaḥ he indo parameśvara te tava sakhye vartamānā vayamajarāsaḥ ajīrṇāḥ syāma /
12.1.[32]	tvaṃ ca no'smānpratijuṣasva prīṇīhi /
12.1.[33]	ka iva kān /
12.1.[34]	piteva putrān //
12.1.[35]	he vāstoṣpate yā tvāṃ saṃsadāte sevate vibhūtistayā vayamapi sakṣīma ‘ṣaca samavāye’ yujyemahi /
12.1.[36]	kīdṛśyā /
12.1.[37]	śagmayā sukharūpayā, hiraṇvayā hitaramaṇīyayā hiraṇyayuktayā vā, gātumatyā kīrtirūpagānayuktayā udgātṛgītayutayā ca /
12.1.[38]	yaccāsmākaṃ kiñcidvaramutkṛṣṭaṃ tvatprasādopanataṃ, tatsarvaṃ pāhi rakṣa /
12.1.[39]	kiṃ kurvan /
12.1.[40]	alabdhalābhātmake yoge, prāptaparirakṣaṇarūpe ca kṣeme vartamānaḥ /
12.1.[41]	utaśabdaścārthe /
12.1.[42]	kiṃvā viśeṣeṇa vāstoṣpatireva prārthyate /
12.1.[43]	he gṛhadevatāḥ evaṃ sarvā eva yūyaṃ no'smān svastibhiravināśaiḥ pāta rakṣata sarvakālam // 1 //
12.2.[1]	tasmin gṛhe brāhmaṇān bhojayet /
12.2.[2]	tasya ca karmaṇo vaṃśodvīkṣaṇikamiti nāma /
12.2.[3]	te hi vaṃśānudvīkṣamāṇā bhuñjate // 3 //
13.1.[1]	sahadharmacāriṇyā sārdhaṃ yo gṛhapraveśaḥ, tadnantaraṃ pākayajñāḥ kartavyāstadanuṣṭhānāvasaralābhāt /
13.1.[2]	pākanirvartyā yajñāḥ pākayajñāsteṣāmāsūtraṇamātramiha kriyate, vistareṇa te vakṣyante //
13.2.[1]	bahuvacanenopakrāntānāmihaikavacanaṃ yajñatvasāmānyāpekṣayā ekasyaiva cāturvidhyaṃ pratyakṣasyeva cākṣuṣādibhedeneti pradarśanāya /
13.2.[2]	caturṇāmevāvāntarabhedāḥ ṣaṭ /
13.2.[3]	yānāha gautamaḥ ‘aṣṭakā: pārvaṇaśrāddhaṃ śrāvaṇyāgrahāyaṇī caitrī āśvayujī ca /’ iti ‘ṣaṭpākayajñasaṃsthāśca’ iti /
13.2.[4]	tatra huto havananirvartyo vaiśvadevādiḥ /
13.2.[5]	ahutastvahavanasādhyo balyupahārādiḥ /
13.2.[6]	yasya tu prārambhe havanaṃ, sa prahuto'nvaṣṭakādiḥ /
13.2.[7]	prakṛṣṭenāśanena nirvartyate yo'tithibrāhmaṇabhojanādiḥ, sa prāśitaḥ /
13.2.[8]	sarvaścāyaṃ yāgo devatoddeśena dravyasaṃkalpanāt //
13.3.[1]	prakṛtiriti śeṣaḥ /
13.3.[2]	ihatyānāṃ hutānāṃ vaidiko homaḥ prakṛtirityarthaḥ /
13.3.[3]	yataḥ itikartavyatopajīvyate, sā prakṛtiḥ /
13.3.[4]	yopajīvati, sā vikṛtiḥ /
13.3.[5]	tathāca vaiśvadeve prākṛtāḥ samūhanaparyukṣaṇaparistaraṇasvāhākārānnaprakṣepādayaḥ kriyāḥ kriyate // 3 //
13.4.[1]	vaidika upahāro'tratyānāmupahārāṇāṃ prakṛtiḥ /
13.4.[2]	atropāgni viṣṭaramāstīryāvāhanaṃ kṛtvā srajo gandhāṃścopahṛtya dhūpaṃ pradāya balyupakalpanamiti itikartavyatā // 4 //
13.5.[1]	vaidikaḥ piṇḍapitṛyajño'tratyānāṃ prahutānāṃ prakṛtiḥ /
13.5.[2]	vaiśvadevaśeṣapiṃḍapratipattitvāttadīyapiṇḍamantrā grāsāsanadānādayaśca taddharmā bhavantyatideśāt // 4 //
13.6.[1]	prāśitā dvividhā atithibhojanadānātmāno brāhmaṇabhojanavitaraṇātmānaśca /
13.6.[2]	tatrātithibhojanādāvasyātithye vaidiko yo madhuparkaḥ, sa prakṛtiḥ /
13.6.[3]	tatra ca śrotriyāṇāṃ pādyārghyamadhuparkapūrvaṃ māṃsapradhānaṃ bhojanamityādirvidhyantaḥ /
13.6.[4]	devatāviśeṣoddeśena tu brāhmaṇabhojanadāne ādhānavihito brahmaudanaḥ prakṛtiḥ, tatrāpi barhiryukteṣvāsaneṣu upaveśanaṃ arghyadānādikaṃ saghṛtamannaṃ devatāyai saṃkalpya ‘prāśnantu bhavantaḥ’ ityanujñānapūrvakaṃ cāśanamityādiritthaṃbhāvaḥ // 5 //
13.7.[1]	sādhāraṇetikartavyatātideśo'yam /
13.7.[2]	asādhāraṇāstu pūrvamitikartavyatā nidarśitāḥ // 6 //
13.7.[3]	dārśapaurṇamāsike vidhyaṃte aviśeṣeṇa prāpte kvacidapavādamāha
13.8.[1]	āvṛt kriyā /
13.8.[2]	upacāro'nuṣṭhānam /
13.8.[3]	tūṣṇīṃ nirvāpāvaghātādikriyānuṣṭhānamamantrakamityarthaḥ //
13.9.[1]	yalluptārthaṃ niṣprayojanaṃ, tatprakṛtau dṛṣṭamapi na kartavyaṃ vikṛtāvamantrakamapi /
13.9.[2]	yathā peṣaṇakapālopadhānādi sthālīpāke niṣprayojanam /
13.9.[3]	evaṃ sāmidhenīnāṃ luptatvāt samidādhānaṃ luptārthatvānna kartavyaṃ prayājābhāvāccopabhṛt /
13.9.[4]	sāmidhenyādyabhāvastu vakṣyamāṇātparisaṃkhyānāt /
13.9.[5]	nacaitāvatā darvihomagṛhamedhīyādivadapūrvatvaṃ pākayajñānāṃ kiṃ darśapūrṇamāsaprakṛtitvābhidhāneneti vācyaṃ juhūhomādidharmopajīvanāt // 13 //
14.1.[1]	‘snātvā bhāryāmadhigacchet’ iti snānānantaraṃ bhāryānveṣaṇakālaḥ /
14.1.[2]	bharaṇamarhatīti bhāryā ‘arhe kṛtyatṛcaśca’ iti ṇyat /
14.1.[3]	vindeta labheta paśyedityarthaḥ /
14.1.[4]	udgayane ādityasya dakṣiṇadigbhāgāduttaradigbhāgābhimukhagamane sati uttarāyaṇa ityarthaḥ // 1 //
14.1.[5]	nakṣatrāṇyāha
14.2.[1]	kṛttikā ca svātiśca pūrvāṇi ca tairvarayet kaṃcitprayuñjīta, natu svayaṃ vṛṇuyādityaucityaṃ ṇicā darśayati // 2 //
14.3.[1]	hastādilakṣaṇavedinā lakṣaṇāni śubhasūcakāni parīkṣayet /
14.3.[2]	pāṭhakramādarthakramasya balīyastvādyathārthaṃ kramo jñeyaḥ lakṣaṇaparīkṣaṇapūrvakaṃ varaṇamiti // 3 //
14.3.[3]	lakṣaṇālābhe parīkṣāyāḥ karaṇāntaramāha
14.4.[1]	apiśabda upāyāntarābhyupagame /
14.4.[2]	vāśabdo vikalpe /
14.4.[3]	piṇḍairvā bhāgyāni parīkṣayet bhartaryanukūlatvāpādanāni pūrvoktālābha ityarthaḥ //
14.5.[1]	yajñārthā vediḥ prasiddhā /
14.5.[2]	sītā halotkhātā bhūmiḥ /
14.5.[3]	aśoṣyaḥ padmādyākaro jalāśayo hradaḥ /
14.5.[4]	goṣṭhaṃ gavāśrayo gokulādiḥ /
14.5.[5]	ādīvyantyasminnādevanaṃ kitavasthānam /
14.5.[6]	ādahyante'sminnityādahanaṃ śmaśānam /
14.5.[7]	svastikākāreṇa sambadhyamānaṃ mārgadvayaṃ catuṣpathaḥ /
14.5.[8]	iriṇaṃ ūṣarapradeśaḥ /
14.5.[9]	etebhyaḥ pratyekaikaṃ piṇḍaṃ gṛhṇīyāt /
14.5.[10]	saṃbhāryaṃ ca navamam, aṣṭabhyo'pi vedyādibhyo leśaṃ leśaṃ mṛdaḥ saṃbhṛtya, navamaṃ kuryādityarthaḥ //
14.5.[11]	vedyādibhya uddhṛtānāṃ piṇḍānāmanumatraṇe mantramāha ṛtameveti /
14.5.[12]	itiśabdaḥ sarvapratīkārthaḥ /
14.5.[13]	parameṣṭhī prajāpatiḥ /
14.5.[14]	ṛtaṃ satyaṃ nātyeti nātivartate kimapi /
14.5.[15]	ataḥ so'tra sannihito bhūtvā satyaṃ dyotayatu /
14.5.[16]	iyamapi vedyādirūpā pṛthivī ṛte āśritā /
14.5.[17]	asāvityukte nāma pratīyāt /
14.5.[18]	kanyā ucyate asau śobhāvatyādisaṃjñitā /
14.5.[19]	iyaṃ pratyakṣatvena vartamānatvāt /
14.5.[20]	idaṃ bhūyaḥ satyaprakāśayoḥ // 5 //
14.6-8.[1]	vedisītāhradagoṣṭhoddhṛtānāmanyatamaṃ gṛhṇīyāccettadodvahedenām, itaragrāhiṇīṃ tu varjayet /
14.6-8.[2]	‘vedipiṇḍe hi vedārthakriyā sāhāyyamāvahet /
14.6-8.[3]	prajāvatīti sītāyāṃ goṣṭhapiṇḍe gavādikam //
14.6-8.[4]	hradapiṇḍe hṛdodbhūtakusumābharaṇocitā /
14.6-8.[5]	tṛptidā caityahetuśca bhartṛjīvanakāriṇī //
14.6-8.[6]	śmaśāne vidhavāvaśyaṃ dyūtabhūmau kalipriyā /
14.6-8.[7]	iriṇe nityasaṃtaptāvakīrṇā ca catuṣpathe /’
14.9.[1]	manyante ityadhyāhāraḥ /
14.9.[2]	gṛhṇatīmupayacchedityanuṣaṃgaḥ // 7 //
14.10.[1]	upayamaḥ svīkāraḥ, tatraivānukūlāni nakṣatrāṇi etānītyarthaḥ //
14.11.[1]	puṇyoktaṃ jyotiḥśāstroktaṃ yathāsambhavamanusartavyamityarthaḥ //
15.1.[1]	brāhmena vidhinā yā dīyate sā brāhmadeyā /
15.1.[2]	tasyāḥ prakṛṣṭe dāne vidhimitikartavyatāṃ vakṣyāmaḥ /
15.1.[3]	athetyadhikārārthaḥ /
15.1.[4]	brāhmo daiva ārṣaḥ prājāpatya āsuro gāndharvo rākṣasaḥ paiśāca ityaṣṭau vivāhāḥ /
15.1.[5]	tatra brāhmāsuravyatirekiṇāṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ vidhānaṃ suprathitaṃ neha vacanamarhati /
15.1.[6]	tena brāhmāsurayorevetikartavyatoktā /
15.1.[7]	tathāhi prasahyāpahārāt rākṣaso vivāhaḥ, tatra kiṃ prakārābhidhānena /
15.1.[8]	evamasaṃvijñātopagamātpaiśāco'pi prakāravacanānarho'tipāpatvāt /
15.1.[9]	svayamicchantyā sahecchāvataḥ saṃyogo gāndharvaḥ, tatrāpyasādhāraṇetikartavyatā /
15.1.[10]	saha dharmaścaryatāṃ, sahāpatyamutpādyatāṃ, dharme cārthe ca kāme ca na vyabhicaritavyamiti prājāpatyavidhiḥ prathitaḥ /
15.1.[11]	alaṃkṛtya kanyāntarvedi ṛtvije pradīyate, iti daivo vivāha uktaḥ smṛtikāraiḥ /
15.1.[12]	gomithunaṃ kanyāvate dadyādityārṣasya vidhānam // 1 //
15.2.[1]	śuklapakṣasya sambandhini praśaste jyotiḥśāstraviśuddhe divase parvaṇi vā paurṇamāsīrūpe, viṣṭaraviśeṣe pavitrārthamuttaradigagrāndarbhānāstīrya, teṣu tayordātṛpratigrahītrorupaviśet prāṅmukho bhūtvā /
15.2.[2]	kaḥ /
15.2.[3]	pratigrahītā /
15.2.[4]	kīdṛśaḥ /
15.2.[5]	sāmātyaḥ parijanasahitaḥ /
15.2.[6]	pradātā punaḥ pratyaṅmukha upaviśet tathaiva sāmātyo darbhānāstīryodagagrān // 2 //
15.3.[1]	tayordātṛpratigrahītrordakṣiṇadeśe uttarābhimukha upaviṣṭaḥ san ṛtvigviśeṣaḥ ācāryastayoḥ upayamanaṃ dātṛpratigrahītṛsambandhaṃ kārayet /
15.3.[2]	kiṃ kṛtvā /
15.3.[3]	dātṛpratigrahītrormadhye prāgagrānudagagrāṃśca darbhānāstīrya, teṣu ca darbheṣu kāṃsyapātryāmudakaṃ sannidhāya, tatrodakamadhye vrīhiḥ yavasthāvapanaṃ kṛtvā /
15.3.[4]	atha ‘udakaṃ sannidhāya’ iti sāmānyavacanātkaṃsasya kuto lābhaḥ? ‘kaṃse hiraṇyaṃ samupya’ iti darśanāt // 3 //
15.4.[1]	sameteṣu saṅghaṭiteṣu dātṛpratigrahītṛbandhuṣu satsu ṛtvigbrūyāt, dātustāvadidaṃ brūyāt kanyāsmai pradīyatāmiti, pratigrahītuḥ kanyāsmātpratigṛhyatāmiti /
15.4.[2]	tato dadāni te, dadāni te, dadāni te iti triruccārayeti dātāraṃ bodhayet /
15.4.[3]	dātā ca tathaiva kuryāt /
15.4.[4]	evaṃ pratigṛhṇāmi ityapi ṛtvijāveditaḥ pratigrahītā brūyāt /
15.4.[5]	‘triḥsatyā hi devāḥ’ iti śrutiḥ, ‘trirabhihitaṃ na vyabhicāri bhavati’ iti triruccāraṇamiṣṭamata eva sameteṣvāhetyuktam /
15.4.[6]	bahujanasannidhau dattāṃ pratigṛhītāṃ ca nāpahartuṃ tyaktuṃ vā śakṣyatīti // 4 //
15.5.[1]	etaddānapratigrahakarma yuṣmākaṃ satyamavyabhicaritamastviti laukikoktyā ṛtvika ‘samānā’ ityādi ṛgdvayaṃ japati, ubhau dātṛpratigrahītārau vīkṣamāṇaḥ //
