15.5.[2]	samānā va ākūtāni samānā hṛdayāni vaḥ /
15.5.[3]	samānamastu vo mano yathā vaḥ susahāsati // 1 //
15.5.[4]	saṃ vo manāṃsi saṃ vratā samu cittānyākaram /
15.5.[5]	amī ye vivratāḥ sthana tānna sannamayāmasi // 2 //
15.5.[6]	anuṣṭubhau /
15.5.[7]	he dātṛpratigrahītārau vaḥ yuṣmākaṃ sambandhīnyākūtānyabhiprāyāḥ samānāstulyānyekarūpāṇi āsati santu, kasyacidapi kanyāpahārādyabhiprāyo duṣṭo mābhūdityarthaḥ /
15.5.[8]	evaṃ manaḥ samānamastu, ahaṃ ca vo yuṣmākaṃ tathā ā akaraṃ karomi japena, yathā su saha asati suṣṭu vaḥ sahabhāvo bhavati, tathā manāṃsi samākaraṃ, vratāni ca saṃmilitāni karomītyarthaḥ /
15.5.[9]	evaṃ cittāni caitanyāni samākaramiti yojyam /
15.5.[10]	ye ca yuṣmākaṃ madhye vivratā viruddhācārāḥ yūyamiti kecit, amī iti pratyakṣaṃ tāneva mukhavikārādinā durācārāndarśayati, sthana bhavatha, tānna sannamayāmasi netivarṇopajanaḥ tānvayaṃ sannayāmaḥ samyak natān kurmaḥ sadācārān saṃpādayāma ityarthaḥ // 5 //
16.1.[1]	pradānavidhirucyate iti śeṣaḥ /
16.1.[2]	śulkena mūlyena dīyate yā, sā śulkadeyā // 1 //
16.2.[1]	suvarṇaṃ vijigīṣayā parasparaṃ dadato dātṛpratigrahītārāvasuratvāt, dasyuvijigīṣupradhānatvāccāsurāṇāṃ rājasatvenānyonyopacāraṃ kuruta iti śasyate /
16.2.[2]	kanyāmūlyabhūtaṃ tu suvarṇaṃ vyatiharato niścinuto dvau dātṛpratigrahītārau sambhūyetyarthadvayaṃ tantreṇāvagamyate // 2 //
16.3.[1]	tatprakṛtaṃ hiraṇyaṃ prajābhyastvetyanena dadāti varaḥ kanyāyāḥ pitre, he hiraṇya prajārthaṃ tvāmahaṃ dadāni // 3 //
16.4.[1]	kanyāyāḥ pitā /
16.4.[2]	rāyaspoṣāya tvāṃ pratigṛhṇāmi // 4 //
16.5.[1]	tatkanyāmūlyabhūtaṃ hiraṇyaṃ pratigṛhītaṃ kāṃsyapātre nidhāya jalayuktaṃ ‘hiraṇyavarṇāḥ’ iti ṛgbhiścatasṛbhiḥ samavamṛśante upaspṛśanti ghorapāpaviśuddhaye /
16.5.[2]	bahuvacanaṃ sarvabaṃdhvapekṣaṃ sa rveṣāṃ pāpabhāgitvapradarśanāya /
16.5.[3]	hiraṇyavarṇā ityādyāḥ saṃmārjanāvasare vyākhyātāḥ // 5 //
16.5.[4]	prajābhyastvā dadāni /
16.5.[5]	rāyaspoṣāya vā pratigṛhṇāmi //
16.5.[6]	ityetāvantāveva mantrau kecitprayuñjate vākyaparisamāpteriṣe tvetyādivat, anyamate tu prajābhyastvānuprāṇantu tvaṃ ca prajāḥ anuprāṇihīti prathamasya, suprajārthaṃ ca vīryārthaṃ ca tvāmahaṃ pratigṛhāmīti dvitīyasya śeṣaḥ //
17.1.[1]	pāṭhakramādarthakramasya balīyastvāttadanusāreṇa vyākhyā kartavyā yathā jātaṃ janinā juhoti jātamatiprāṇitīti, tathāgnihotreṇa juhoti yavāgūmadhiśrayatīti /
17.1.[2]	tenāyamarthaḥ pādacatuṣṭayayukte bhadrapīṭhe śobhane āsane prāṅmukhyā upaviṣṭāyāścatasṛṣu dikṣu catasro'vidhavā bhavanti, vāmabhāge mātā, dakṣiṇabhāge pitā, agre guruḥ saṃskārasya kartā saptamaḥ /
17.1.[3]	teṣu yathāsanniveśaṃ sthiteṣu godāne bhavā gaudānikāstanmantraistāṃ guruḥ kanyāṃ sahasracchidrayuktena pavitreṇa pāvanena vastraviśeṣeṇa suprajastvāya gaudānikaireva mantraiḥ kaṭakakeyūrādibhiryathāvibhavamalaṃkṛtyāhatenānupabhuktena vāsasā pracchādya sthālīpākena gururjuhoti /
17.1.[4]	atra pallavacatuṣṭayaṃ vastrasya pavitrasya catasro'vidhavā avaṣṭabhnanti /
17.1.[5]	pitarau jalamabhiṣiñcataḥ /
17.1.[6]	gurumaṃtrapāṭhaṃ karoti /
17.1.[7]	snāpane'laṃkaraṇe ca gurureva prayojakakartā, tena homena samānakartṛkatvam /
17.1.[8]	ye tvalaṃkaraṇaṃ viparītalakṣaṇayā keśavapanaṃ vyācakṣate, amāṅgalikāste /
17.1.[9]	sthālīpākasyetyupādīyamānagatatvādekatvaṃ vivakṣitaṃ paśugataikatvavat /
17.1.[10]	juhotītyekavacanaṃ eka eva homo navasvapyāhutiṣu, iti pratyabhijñānabalena sūcayati, tenaivāhutīrnigadati /
17.1.[11]	viśvāvasave gandharvarājāyetyekaivāhutistena nava bhavanti /
17.1.[12]	indraḥ parameśvaraḥ /
17.1.[13]	indrāṇī śacī /
17.1.[14]	kamanīyaḥ kāmaḥ /
17.1.[15]	bhajanīyo bhagaḥ /
17.1.[16]	hrīrlajjā /
17.1.[17]	śrīḥ śrayaṇīyā /
17.1.[18]	lakṣaṇīyā lakṣmīḥ /
17.1.[19]	poṣaḥ puṣṭiḥ /
17.1.[20]	svāhā suhutamastu // 1 //
17.2.[1]	nāḍyādīni sarvāṇi vāditrāṇi gandhodakena sugandhinopalipya pūrvaṃ kanyaiva pravādayate /
17.2.[2]	vādyamāneṣu ca gurumaṃtraṃ paṭhati /
17.2.[3]	tatra nāḍī vaṃśaḥ, tūṇavo gomukho vādyaviśeṣaḥ /
17.2.[4]	maṃtrārthastu he dundubhe paṭaha svanaṃ vāyuṃ vada vādaya śabdaṃ kāraya /
17.2.[5]	kimartham /
17.2.[6]	suprajastvāya satprajārtham /
17.2.[7]	evaṃ he gomukha svanaṃ vadeti pūrvavat /
17.2.[8]	prakrīḍantu anyonyaṃ kanyāḥ sakhibhūtāḥ prakrāntavivāhayā kanyayā sahitāḥ /
17.2.[9]	tā api hi kanyā eva bhavitumarhanti samānaśīlānāṃ sakhitvasyānyonyāntaratvāt /
17.2.[10]	kīdṛśaḥ kanyāḥ /
17.2.[11]	sumanasyamānāḥ sumanaskā hṛṣṭā ityarthaḥ /
17.2.[12]	indrāṇyā saha indrāṇyapyatrotsave krīḍitumavataratvityāśāsyate /
17.2.[13]	sumaṃgalā maṃgalapradhānagītaghoṣiṇyaḥ //
17.2.[14]	atha gaudānikamaṃtrā vyākhyāyante yā āpo divyāḥ payasā saṃbabhūvuryā antarikṣyā uta pārthivāsaḥ /
17.2.[15]	tāsāṃ tvā sarvāsāṃ rucābhiṣiṃcāmi varcasā //
17.2.[16]	abhi tvā varcasāsicaṃ yajñena payasā saha /
17.2.[17]	yathāso mitravardhanastathā tvā savitākarat //
17.2.[18]	indrāya svāhā //
17.2.[19]	pūrvā virāṭ /
17.2.[20]	uttarānuṣṭup /
17.2.[21]	yā divyā divi bhavā āpo, yāśca antarikṣyā antarikṣe bhavāḥ, yāśca pārthivāsaḥ pārthivyaḥ, payasā sambabhūvuḥ kṣīreṇa yajñopayoginā sambhūtāḥ, tāsāṃ sarvāsāṃ rucā dīptyā varcasā ca sāreṇa balena he kanye tvāmabhiṣiñcāmi tvāmahamabhyasicamabhiṣiñcāmi yajñena payasā varcasā saha yajñādiyogyāṃ ca karomītyarthaḥ /
17.2.[22]	mitrasya mehanasya svargapaśuputrāderasau yajñādeśca vardhano yathā bhavati, tathā savitā āditya akarat tava karotu he kanye /
17.2.[23]	indrāya suhutamastu // 2 //
18.1-2.[1]	yajñamarhati yajñiyaḥ ‘yajñartvigbhyāṃ ghakhañau’ iti ghaḥ, yajñārhāṇāṃ vṛkṣāṇāṃ vaṭādīnāmanyatamasya sambandhinīṃ śākhāṃ sakṛdācchinnāṃ sūtratantunā prācyāṃ diśyāyatāṃ prasṛtāṃ sakṛdekenaiva prahāreṇa chinnāmekasāreṇa sūtratantunā pracchādya kanyāyai prayacchati ‘devasya tvā’ ityādinā ‘tāṃ prayacchāmi’ iti śabdāntena //
18.1-2.[2]	gururgṛhītaśākhāṃ kanyāmanumantrayate ‘yā te’ ityādinā /
18.1-2.[3]	he kanye yā te tava kācidalakṣmīralakṣaṇaṃ mātṛmayī pitṛmayī vā mātuḥ piturvā sakāśātsaṃkrāntā bījādidoṣāt anyato vā kutaścit saṃkrāntā, tāmahamanena mantreṇa nirbhajāmi tvāṃ prati nirbhāgāṃ karomi /
18.1-2.[4]	kimekakaḥ /
18.1-2.[5]	netyāha tiṣyeṇa devatayā sahakṛtaḥ, tathā nirṇudāmi niḥśeṣeṇa nudāmi apasārayāmi /
18.1-2.[6]	sā cāpasāritā satī dviṣantaṃ tava śatruṃ gacchatu /
18.1-2.[7]	alakṣaṇāpasāre codyatasya mama vighnāpasāraṇāya tiṣyabṛhaspatibhyāṃ namaskāro'stu /
18.1-2.[8]	anye tu ‘tiṣyabṛhaspatibhyāṃ namo namaḥ’ ityetaṃ yajurekadeśamācchidya śākhotsarge'pi prayuñjate //
18.3.[1]	sthāvarodakaṃ taḍāgādi /
18.3.[2]	tatra tasyāḥ śākhāyā utsargaḥ pratipattikarma śucau devagṛhe /
18.3.[3]	devagṛhaṃ madyopahāraśoṇitādinā apavitramapi sambhāvyeta, tadarthaṃ śucigrahaṇam //
19.1.[1]	haviṣyakalpa iti pāribhāṣikī karmaviśeṣasya saṃjñā // 1 //
19.2.[1]	varṣadaśakādūrdhvaṃ kumārī na sthāpayitavyā pitrā, agatyā vā dvādaśa varṣāṇi nātikramaṇīyāni // 2 //
19.3.[1]	brahmacaryāvasāne vivāhātpūrvaṃ gandharve nirmimittajalasrāviṇi deśe, devatāyatane vā laukiko dvāvagnī prajvālya, dvau paśū cchāgau kanyāsaṃskārārthamupākuryātpaśukalpavat, ekamaryamṇe dakṣiṇabhāgavartinyagnau, dvitīyaṃ prajāpataye uttaradigbhāgavartinyau /
19.3.[2]	itikartavyatāṃ samantravyākhyānāṃ paśukalpe eva vyākhyāsyāmaḥ //
19.4.[1]	pracurārthādyabhāve eka eva dvidaivataḥ paśurupākartavyaḥ /
19.4.[2]	avadānāni ca hṛdayādibhyo medo'ntebhyo dvādaśabhyo dvirdvirgrahītavyāni /
19.4.[3]	‘aryamaprajāpatibhyāṃ svāhā’ iti cohaḥ /
19.4.[4]	eka eva ca yogaḥ saṃhatayorekadeśatvadharmasamavāyāt /
19.4.[5]	ata evaca kecit hṛdayādibhyo dviguṇāni avadānāni necchanti // 4 //
19.5.[1]	dhanadaurgatye sati ahiṃsāniyame vā taṇḍulairvā kuryāt /
19.5.[2]	taṇḍulagrahaṇaṃ piṣṭakārtham // 5 //
19.6.[1]	yatraiva sthāne ājyabhāgābhyāṃ pūrvo mukhyapaśuḥ tatraiva piṣṭakapaśuḥ avadānānyapi hṛdayādibhyastadvat /
19.6.[2]	teṣāṃ ca śrapaṇahomau sarvadānyāpītikartavyatā raśanābandhayūpaniyojanopāyena viśasanādiḥ /
19.6.[3]	luptārthavarjaṃ haviḥ paśupuroḍāśasthāne sthālīpākastadapi yathāsthānaṃ paśupuroḍāśakrame, vapāhomasthāne tvājyahomaḥ //
19.7.[1]	sugandhacandanaghanasārādidravyayutenājyenāhutayo gandhāhutayaḥ, tābhiragnyādikāḥ saptadaśa devatā yajeta /
19.7.[2]	vātsīputra iti devatānāma yataḥ śabdaikasamadhigamyā devatā /
19.7.[3]	vibhaktivipariṇāmena caturthyantaiḥ svāhākārayuktaiḥ śabdairuddiśyāgnyādidevatā yaṣṭavyāḥ ‘agnaye khāhā’ ityādikaiḥ //
20.1.[1]	iyamapi pāribhāṣikī saṃjñā /
20.1.[2]	haviṣyeṇa vrīhyādinā puṇye'hani kriyamāṇatā śabdapravṛttinimittam // 1 //
20.2.[1]	udakasya samīpaṃ gatvā atidūrataḍāgādike tu grāme, yathopapatti yatropapadyate sthāne, tatra kṣīre sthālīpākaṃ kṛtvā māṃgalikabilvākṣoṭādiphalopetābhiḥ sarvauṣadhyādigandhayoginībhiścādbhirāmalakaiḥ kanyāṃ snāpayet /
20.2.[2]	saśiraskāmityanenānyadā strīṇāmaśiraskamapi snānaṃ bhavatīti sūcayati /
20.2.[3]	snāpanāhatavastrācchādanavyavadhānena ca sthālīpākena homaḥ, snānācca pūrvaṃ sthālīpāka iti vivakṣitaḥ kramaḥ /
20.2.[4]	caturthyā devatāpadapariṇāmaḥ svāhākāraśca pūrvavat /
20.2.[5]	jīvaputro'gnirityekaiva devatā jīvaḥ prāṇo vāyuḥ putro rakṣako'syeti bahuvrīhiranyapadārthapradhāno yogyaśca sannihito'gnirevānyapadārthaḥ /
20.2.[6]	mahārāja ityatra ‘na pūjanāt’ iti pratiṣedho nāsti niyamāśrayaṇāt ‘pūjāyāṃ svatigrahaṇaṃ kartavyam’ iti vacanāt anyathā hi paramarāja ityādāvapi ṭacaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ syāt /
20.2.[7]	ye ye tu mahārājā ityākārāntaṃ paṭhanti, te svatiniyamaṃ nādriyante //
21.1.[1]	ekā vivāhāhorātrarātristasyāḥ pūrvā yā dvitīyā rātriryasyāṃ pitā kanyāṃ vivāhayiṣyanbhavet vivāhayiṣyāmītyanenādhyavasāyena yuktaḥ, athavā yāṃ bhaviṣyantīṃ rātrimadhikṛtya pitā kanyāṃ vivāhayiṣyansyāttasyā yā pūrvā dvitīyā rātristāmāśrityetikartavyatāpravṛttaḥ san tasyāmeva rātryāmatīte madhyamapraharadvaye mahāniśākhye pūrvavatsthālīpākena yāgaṃ kuryāt gururagnyādibhyo devatābhyaḥ // 1 //
21.2.[1]	puṃso'pi tasyāṃ rātryāṃ saṃskārārthametayaivetikartavyatayā etā eva devatā yajeta kumbhādyāśca tisraḥ iti /
21.2.[2]	etāvāneva ca viśeṣaḥ striyo dvādaśāhutayaḥ, puṃsaḥ paṃcadaśa // 2 //
22.1.[1]	avidhavā jīvadbhartṛkāḥ /
22.1.[2]	śākamiśrāḥ piṃḍyaḥ śākapiṃḍya: ‘bhakṣyeṇa miśrīkaraṇam’ iti tatpuruṣaḥ /
22.1.[3]	catasro'ṣṭāviti ca prathamāntastrīpadasamānādhikaraṇam /
22.1.[4]	catasro'ṣṭau veti yathāsaṃbhavaṃ vikalpaḥ /
22.1.[5]	samasaṃkhyāniyamārthametat /
22.1.[6]	catuṣṭāṣṭatvaniyamārthamiti tu kecit /
22.1.[7]	tenāyamanvayaḥ anyūnāścatasṛbhyo'vidhavāḥ striyaḥ samasaṃkhyāḥ ṣaṭkavarjāḥ śākapiṃḍībhiranyaiśca yathāsambhavadbhirbhojanaviśeṣairbrāhmaṇānbhojayitvā vīṇayā vādyamānayā saha ye gāyanti tacchīlāstaiḥ saha saṃbhūtā bhūtvā maṃgalagānaṃ gāyeyuḥ /
22.1.[8]	brāhmaṇabhojanānantaraṃ maṃgalagānāvasaro'tra vivakṣito, natu samānakartṛtve'tīvādaraḥ tena te brāhmaṇānbhojayeyuranye vā, sarvathā brāhmaṇabhojanānantaraṃ maṃgalagānaṃ kartavyam /
22.1.[9]	apivā caturo nartanaṃ kuryāt caturo nartanapravīṇo nartanaṃ kuryāt yadi sauśīlyādiguṇayukto bhavet, viparyaye tu na tābhiḥ saha nartanaṃ kuryādityanenābhiprāyeṇāpivāśabdaḥ /
22.1.[10]	anuṣṭhānaṃ tvāryāvarte yathā dṛśyate, tathā brūmaḥ kanyāyā mātṛprabhṛtayo'ṣṭau catasro vāvidhavā yathāvibhavaṃ bhojayitvā brāhmaṇāṃścāvidhavābhiḥ saha vīṇāgāyibhiśca gāyanti nṛtyanti sotsāham /
22.1.[11]	tadanusāreṇāyamarthaḥ catasro'ṣṭau vā striyaḥ karmabhūtā brāhmaṇāṃśca śākapiṃḍībhiranyena ca bhojyaprakāreṇa bhojayitvā vīṇāgāyibhiḥ sahāvidhavābhiśca saṃgāyeyuḥ /
22.1.[12]	ke /
22.1.[13]	arthāt kanyāmātrādayaḥ /
22.1.[14]	apiveti samuccaye /
22.1.[15]	sakalo'sau strīgaṇaścaturaḥ sotsāho bhūtvā nartanaṃ kuryāt //
22.1.[16]	‘krīḍaṃ vaḥ’ ityanayā gāyatryānumantrayate /
22.1.[17]	vyākhyātā ceyaṃ kṛcchreṣu // 1 //
22.2.[1]	akṣatānāmanavahatānāṃ yavānāṃ saktubhiragniṃ puṣṭipatiṃ yajeta ‘agninā rayim’ ityetayarcā /
22.2.[2]	tathā prajāpatiṃ ‘prajāpate’ ityādimastreṇa /
22.2.[3]	etāvājyabhāgānte yāgau // 2 //
22.3.[1]	yatra nāmnā mantravarṇairvā devatānirdiṣṭā vivāhaprakaraṇokte karmaṇi, tatrāgniṃ puṣṭipatiṃ prajāpatiṃ ca yajeta prakṛtatvādakṣatasaktubhiḥ /
22.3.[2]	ājyabhāgānte bhaviṣyatsu prāsthānikādiṣvetadboddhavyam /
22.3.[3]	pūrvokteṣu tu kvacinnāmnā kvacinmantravarṇebhyo devatā sarveṣu pratītā //
22.3.[4]	agninā ijyamānenāhaṃ rayiṃ dhanamaśnavat ‘aśū vyāptau’ vyāpnuyām /
22.3.[5]	vyāptasya ca prāptasya poṣaṃ puṣṭiṃ dine dine aśnuyām /
22.3.[6]	kīdṛśaṃ rayim /
22.3.[7]	yaśasaṃ yaśaskaraṃ, vīravattamaṃ vīrapuruṣayuktaṃ, vīrairvā putrairatiśayena yuktam /
22.3.[8]	‘prajāpate nahi’ iti jātakarmaṇi vyākhyāsyate // 3 //
23.1.[1]	prasthānanimittaṃ prāsthānikaṃ karmānantaraṃ vakṣyata ityarthaḥ /
23.1.[2]	prasthānaṃ ca varasya śvaśuragṛhaprāptaye vivāhaṃ kartum // 1 //
23.2.[1]	tasminprāsthānike karmaṇi yathoktamupasamādhāya, agneḥ pūrvaṃ kartavyaṃ uddhatasya cāvokṣitasya ca parisaṃvāhanaparyukṣaṇaparistaraṇapūrvakamājyāhutipaṃcakena santanīhomaiścaikādaśabhiḥ saṃskaraṇamupasamādhānamucyate tatra jayaprabhṛtibhirmantrairhomaṃ kuryāt jayābhidhānānvā homān kuryāt ‘ākūtaṃ cākūtiśca’, ‘bṛhaspatipurohitāḥ’ ‘ṛtāṣāṭ’ ityādibhirmantrairjuhuyādityarthaḥ /
23.2.[2]	ete hi mantrāstatsādhyā vā homā jayābhyātarāṣṭrabhṛdājyabhāgādiśabdasādhyatayā prasiddhāḥ /
23.2.[3]	ājyabhāgānte cāgniṃ puṣṭipatiṃ prajāpatiṃ ca yajeta ‘sarvatrodvāhakarmasvanādiṣṭadevateṣu’ ityādisūtravacanaprāmāṇyāditi kecit /
23.2.[4]	anye tvāhuḥ sūtrakāraprāmāṇyādeva jayaśabdo'trāgniprajāpatidevatayorhomayoḥ paribhāṣyate ājyabhāgāntaṃ copasamādhānamiti /
23.2.[5]	kaścittvāha vivāhaprakaraṇe'ntarāntarā coditatvāt ājyabhāgāntāni karmāṇi kṛtvā puṣṭyarthamagnaye puṣṭipataye cākṣatasaktubhirhomaḥ kartavyaḥ sūtrakāravacanasaṃpratyayārthamiti /
23.2.[6]	anyathā hi nāmnā mantravarṇairvā sarvatra devatāvagamānnānādiṣṭadaivataṃ kiṃcidudvāhakarmasu karma vidyate iti sūtrārthasaṃpratyayābhāvaḥ syāt /
23.2.[7]	evaṃ jayahomeṣu kṛteṣu ājyabhāgānte varasya paścātsthitā satī bhaginī mukhyā upacaritā vā yathāsaṃbhavaṃ khaḍgakṣurikādīnāmanyatamaṃ śastraviśeṣaṃ haste tūṣṇīṃ gṛhītvā, tūṣṇīṃ sicamupariparidhānīyasya vāsaso bhrātuḥ sambandhino'ñcalaṃ gṛhṇāti paridhānadaśāṃ hastena spṛśatītyarthaḥ /
23.2.[8]	aṃcalagrahaṇamadṛṣṭasaṃskārārthaṃ śastragrahaṇamapi /
23.2.[9]	tathāca prāyastadeva śastramuttarakāle'pi rakṣārthaṃ śayanādisannidhau sthāpyamānamāryāvarte lakṣyate // 2 //
23.3.[1]	pūṣā mā prapathe pātvityādinā maṃtreṇodakasaṃmukhā vrajantītyarthaḥ // 3 //
23.4.[1]	udakāntaṃ prāpya udakopasparśanaṃ śirasi prakṣepaṇamācamanaṃ kṛtvā ‘prācī digagnirdevatā’ ityādinā mantreṇa yathādiśaṃ yā digyeṣāṃ gantavyā, tadabhidhāyinā mantreṇa yathāliṃgamabhidhāya varaprabhṛtayo gacchanti /
23.4.[2]	atra vivāhasya kārayitā yo guruḥ, sa eva pitā vā varasya maṃtrapāṭhe kartā //
23.4.[3]	pūṣā mā prapathe pātu pūṣā mā paśupāḥ pātu pūṣā mādhipatiḥ pātu //
23.4.[4]	puṣṇāti vardhayatīti pūṣā pṛthivī antarikṣaṃ dyauśca /
23.4.[5]	tathāca brāhmaṇam ‘iyaṃ vai pūṣā prapathe'ntarikṣaṃ paśupā dyauradhipatiḥ /’ iti /
23.4.[6]	etaddhi iyamityaparokṣanirdeśena prayuktasya pūṣaśabdasya mantre pṛthivyarthatāṃ darśayati /
23.4.[7]	antarikṣaṃ pūṣetyanenāpi madhyavartinā mantreṇa pūṣaśabdasyāntarikṣavṛttitvaṃ darśayati /
23.4.[8]	yathaiva hi bhūtāni puṣṇātīti pṛthvī pūṣā, tathaiva paśūnavakāśadānena pāti puṣṇātīti kṛtvā antarikṣaṃ pūṣā /
23.4.[9]	evaṃ dyaurapi pūṣā, sā hi sarvalokādhipatiḥ yato'sau sarvalokān vṛṣṭyādidvāreṇa puṣṇāti /
23.4.[10]	tenāyaṃ mantrārthaḥ pūṣā pṛthivī prapathe gantuṃ prastute pathi mārge māṃ pātu, tathā paśupā yaḥ pūṣā antarikṣalakṣaṇaḥ, so'pi māṃ pātu rakṣatu /
23.4.[11]	tathā adhipatiryaḥ pūṣā dyulakṣaṇaḥ so'pi māṃ pālayatu pathi gacchantam /
23.4.[12]	śanno devīrityādayo vyākhyātāḥ // 4 //
23.4.[13]	prācī digagnirdevatāgniṃ sa ṛcchatu yo maitasyā diśo‘bhidāsati, dakṣiṇā digindro devatendraṃ sa ṛcchatu yo maitasyā° pratīcī dik somo devatā somaṃ sa ṛcchatu yo maitasyā° udīcī dik mitrāvaruṇau devatā mitrāvaruṇau sa ṛcchatu yo maitasyā° ūrdhvā digbṛhaspatirdevatā bṛhaspatiṃ sa ṛcchatu yo maitasyā° iyaṃ digaditirdevatāditiṃ sa ṛcchatu yo maitasyā° //
23.4.[14]	yā prācī dik, tasyā agnirdevatā /
23.4.[15]	ata eva tasyā diśaḥ sambaṃdhī kaścit yo māmabhidāsati ‘dasu upakṣaye’ upakṣetumicchatyābhimukhyena so'gnimṛcchatu agnimabhyṛcchatu agniṃ lakṣaṇīkṛtyendriyapralayamanubhavatu agnistasyākṣyādinigrahaṃ karotvityarthaḥ /
23.4.[16]	eṣaiva sarvatra yojanā tulyā /
23.4.[17]	parvatārohaṇāvarohaṇamūrdhvamadhaśca gamanamastīti tatparatvamapi mantrasya yuktam /
23.4.[18]	kecidāhuḥ yadabhimukhaṃ gamanaṃ, talliṃgaka eva mantraikadeśaḥ prayoktavya iti /
23.4.[19]	tadyuktaṃ yata upadravanivāraṇāyaiṣa maṃtraḥ, anyatamadigabhimukhagamanapravṛttasya sarvadikkebhyo'pi saṃbhāvyate viplavaḥ sarpāśaniprabhṛtibhyo'dhastanoparitanebhyaḥ /
23.4.[20]	evaṃ pārśvādiprabhavebhyo'pīti /
23.4.[21]	sarvaprasthāneṣu caiṣetikartavyatā boddhavyā //
24.1.[1]	vivāhātpūrvameva pādyārghyamadhuparkairvivāhyaḥ śvaśureṇa pūjanīyaḥ /
24.1.[2]	tulyaṃ ca pūjāvidhānaṃ ṣaṇṇāmapīti ṣaṇṇāmuddeśaḥ /
24.1.[3]	ayaṃ pūjāmarhantīti arghyāḥ ṣaṭ bhavanti /
24.1.[4]	ācāryaḥ upanetā dhyāpayitā ca śiṣyasya /
24.1.[5]	ṛtvigyājyasya, tasyāpi prākkarmaṇaḥ saṃmānaḥ /
24.1.[6]	rājā kṣatriyo'pi, natvabhiṣekabhāvena sa janapadasya pūjyaḥ /
24.1.[7]	vivahanamarhatīti vivāhyaḥ ‘arhe kṛtyatṛcaśca’ iti kṛtyo ṇyatpratyayaḥ, sa kanyāyāḥ piturarghyārhaḥ /
24.1.[8]	tathā yo yasya priyo guṇotkarṣeṇa, sa tasya dānādyavasare arghyārhaḥ /
24.1.[9]	snātakastu sadyaḥsrāta ācāryasya // 1 //
24.2.[1]	athaśabdo vakṣyamāṇaprakārasvīkārārtho niḥpātānāmanekārthatvāt /
24.2.[2]	enamācāryādīnāmanyatamaṃ vakṣyamāṇaprakāreṇārhayanti pūjayanti saṃmānayanti // 2 //
24.3.[1]	vivāhottarakālamarhaṇaṃ vihitamiti yathācoditamānupūrvyamiti nayena vivāhādūrdhvameva madhuparkādidānaṃ kartavyamiti kecitprāhurata eva ca vivāhottarakāla evedamapakṛṣya vyācakṣate /
24.3.[2]	tannirāsāyedam /
24.3.[3]	karmaṇa ādāveva pūjanaṃ kartavyaṃ pāṭhakramādarthakramasya balīyastvāt /
24.3.[4]	saṃskāro hyayamutsāhādijananamukhena ṛtvikprabhṛtīnāṃ karmaṇi yogyatāviśeṣādhānārthaḥ, saṃvṛtte yajñavivāhādike karmaṇi ṛtvikprabhṛtīnāṃ kriyamāṇo niṣphala eva syāt /
24.3.[5]	smārto'picāyaṃ saṃskāraḥ, smṛtiṣu ca prāgeva karmaṇo'bhihitaḥ /
24.3.[6]	kiṃca vivāhya ityarhe āvaśyake vā kṛtyaḥ vivahanamarhatīti, vivahati vā avaśyaṃ kanyāmiti vivāhyaḥ ‘arhe kṛtyatṛcaśca’ ‘āvaśyakādhamarṇyayorṇiniḥ’ ‘kṛtyāśca’ iti smṛteḥ /
24.3.[7]	naca vivāhādūrdhvaṃ vivāhārho bhavati // 3 //
24.3.[8]	arghyalakṣaṇamāha
24.4.[1]	udakaṃ, vrīhiyavayoścānyatarat, darbhā etattrayamarghyam // 4 //
24.4.[2]	madhuparkalakṣaṇapūrvikāṃ pūjayituranupadeśāṃ pūjāpratipattimāha
24.5.[1]	atra pūjayitāraḥ ityarthāllabhyate /
24.5.[2]	kāṃsyapātre camase vā dārupātraviśeṣe dadhyāsicyate madhu ca /
24.5.[3]	madhu madhuparka ucyate /
24.5.[4]	tacca madhuparkapātraṃ bṛhatā pātreṇa pidhāya sthagayitvā viṣṭarābhyāṃ gṛhītvā pādyaṃ prathamaṃ yeṣāṃ pādyārghyamadhuparkāṇāṃ tairyathāyogyatamūrdhvamadho madhye ca pūjāṃ svayameva pratipadyante pūjayitāro, natu tatrāpyupadeśamapekṣante // 5 //
24.6.[1]	kanyāyā dātari vivāhyasya nikaṭībhūte sati ṛtvik pādyādikaṃ kanyādātṛsamīpamānāyayati /
24.6.[2]	tadānīyamānamanena maṃtreṇa vivāhyo'numaṃtrayate /
24.6.[3]	amaṃtrajñaścedvivāhyastadā ṛtvigevainaṃ pāṭhayati /
24.6.[4]	evaṃ sarvatra jñeyam /
24.6.[5]	ayaṃ mantrārthaḥ ‘duha prapūraṇe’ dohaḥ prapūrakaḥ āpyāyakaḥ, virāṭ svargādau prajāpatiḥ, pādyādikamucyate he pādyādika yastvaṃ mayi mannimitto madartho dohaḥ prapūrakaḥ sa virājaḥ prajāpateḥ dohaḥ pūrakaḥ jalādeḥ prajāpatinā divo niyuktatvādato mama pādyāyai pratipattaye tvaṃ bhava, virājaśca prajāpateḥ saṃbandhinaṃ dohaṃ pādyādikamahamaśīya vyāpnuyāṃ paśyeyamityarthaḥ /
24.6.[6]	pādyasya saṃskārārthaṃ darśanam // 6 //
24.7.[1]	viṣṭaro'sītyādinā maṃtreṇāsanāntarasyopari darbhaviṣṭaramāstīrya vivāhya upaviśati tūṣṇīm /
24.7.[2]	he viṣṭara asi tvaṃ viṣṭaraḥ viṣṭaro bhavasi ata ācchādayāsanāntaramācchādanārthameva mātari āsanāntare sīda tiṣṭha // 7 //
24.8.[1]	viṣṭare darbhācchāditāsanaviśeṣe āsīnāyopaviṣṭāya vivāhyāya pādyādīnāmekaikaṃ triḥ prāha kanyāyā dātā pādyaṃ 3 arghyaṃ 3 madhuparkaḥ 3 ācamanīyaṃ 3 iti /
24.8.[2]	āsīnāyeti saptamyarthe caturthī, viṣṭara āsīne vivāhya ityarthaḥ //
24.9.[1]	abhyarhaṇīyasyābhimukhyāpādanāya yat bho iti pūjāsaṃbodhanaṃ prāptaṃ, nāmasaṃbodhanaṃ ca mārṣa brahmadatta ityādi, tanniṣedhayati // 9 //
24.10.[1]	śanno devīrityādimaṃtraiḥ pūrvavyākhyātairapo'bhimaṃtrya viśeṣeṇa pādyābhiḥ pādayordhāvanasamarthābhiḥ pādau prakṣālayate abhyarhaṇīyasya kanyāyā dātā /
24.10.[2]	pādayoḥ prakṣālane yathāliṃgaṃ maṃtrau dakṣiṇamityādi, uttaramityādi /
24.10.[3]	idamityanena sadyaḥphalaṃ darśayati kanyāpradānaṃ vivāhāntarasādhitaṃ ca tatkṣaṇādeva karmānuṣṭhānādisambandhirūpam /
24.10.[4]	asya vivāhyasya brahmavarcasasampannaṃ uttaraṃ vāmapādamavanenije śodhayāmi /
24.10.[5]	idamahaṃ tejo vīryamannādyaṃ prajāṃ paśūn brahmavarcasaṃ dadāmi vivāhyādike arghyārhe /
24.10.[6]	māṃ mayi yattu māṃ prāptaṃ tejaḥprabhṛti, tanmayyeva ciramastvityarthaḥ // 10 //
24.11.[1]	āpo hi ṣṭhetyādibhirvyākhyātārthābhirarghyaṃ pratigṛhṇāti /
24.11.[2]	devasya tvetyādinā ‘madhuparkaṃ pratigṛhṇāmi ityadhyāhārapūritena savitṛdevatākena maṃtreṇa madhuparkaṃ pratigṛhṇāti /
24.11.[3]	viṣṭaro'sītimaṃtreṇoparitanaṃ viṣṭaramapakarṣati /
24.11.[4]	apakṛṣya cākṣipya uru tveti maṃtreṇāpasārayati /
24.11.[5]	taccakṣurityādinā madhuparkaṃ vīkṣya, pṛthivyāstvetyādinā maṃtreṇādhastane viṣṭare madhuparkapātraṃ nidadhāti /
24.11.[6]	madhu vātā ṛtāyate iti tisṛbhiraṃguṣṭhasamīpavartinyā pradeśinīsaṃjñayāṅgulyā pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā dadhimadhunī miśrayati /
24.11.[7]	pradiśati tarjayati tacchīlā pradeśinī tarjanī //
24.11.[8]	devasya tvā savituḥ prasave'śvinorbāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ madhuparkaṃ pratigṛhṇāmi //
24.11.[9]	devasya dānadyotanādiguṇakasya saviturādityasya prasave'nujñāyāṃ vartamānā aśvinordevabhiṣajorbāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇaśca hastābhyāṃ natu svābhyāṃ carmamayābhyāṃ madhuparkaṃ pratigṛhṇāmi //
24.11.[10]	viṣṭaro'syantarikṣamadhiviśrayasva //
24.11.[11]	asi tvaṃ viṣṭaraḥ mithyaivāvārakaḥ, ato'smādadhastanaviṣṭarādapasarāntarikṣamākāśamāśraya //
24.11.[12]	uru tvā vātāya //
24.11.[13]	he viṣṭara tvāmahaṃ pṛthivyāṃ prakṣipāmi, ataḥ uru dūraṃ gaccha /
24.11.[14]	kimartham /
24.11.[15]	vātāya vāyvartham //
24.11.[16]	taccakṣurdevahitaṃ purastācchukramuccarat /
24.11.[17]	paśyema śaradaḥ śataṃ jīvema śaradaḥ śatam //
24.11.[18]	tadetaccakṣuḥ śastaṃ yaddevahitaṃ satpurastāduccarati, tadeva kṛtakaraṇīyaṃ cakṣuḥ devārthaṃ havirādivīkṣaṇayāgadānahomādiṣu sādhanabhāvaṃ bhajata ityarthaḥ /
24.11.[19]	kīdṛśam /
24.11.[20]	śukraṃ śuklam /
24.11.[21]	ata āśāsmahe vayaṃ yāgādisādhanāni varṣaśataṃ paśyema, tadarthameva saṃvatsaraśataṃ jīvema //
24.11.[22]	pṛthivyāstvā nābhau sādhayāmi //
24.11.[23]	he madhuparka tvāmahaṃ pātrasthamapi santaṃ nābhāvadhastane darbhaviṣṭare sādhayāmi /
24.11.[24]	dhānyāni havīṃṣi vediprastare sādhyante /
24.11.[25]	pṛthivyā hi sāramoṣadhayastāsāmapi darbhā iti nābhitvaṃ darbhaviṣṭarasya //
24.11.[26]	madhu vātā ṛtāyate madhu kṣaranti siṃdhavaḥ /
24.11.[27]	mādhvīrnaḥ santvoṣadhīḥ // 1 //
24.11.[28]	madhu naktamutoṣasā madhumatpārthivaṃ rajaḥ /
24.11.[29]	madhu dyaurastu naḥ pitā // 2 //
24.11.[30]	madhumānno vanaspatirmadhumāṃ astu sūryaḥ /
24.11.[31]	mādhvīrgāvo bhavantu naḥ // 3 //
24.11.[32]	vātā vāyavaḥ madhu santu madhurasaparyavasāyino bhavantu /
24.11.[33]	kasmai /
24.11.[34]	ṛtāyate ṛtaṃ satyaṃ yajñaṃ vā ya icchati, tasmai /
24.11.[35]	siṃdhavo nadyaḥ madhu kṣaranti kṣarantu sravantu /
24.11.[36]	tathā oṣadhayaḥ phalapākāntāḥ vrīhyādayo madhumatyo'smākaṃ santu //
24.11.[37]	naktaṃ rātriprathamabhāgaḥ madhumānno bhavatu, uta apica uṣasā rātripaścimabhāgena saha /
24.11.[38]	madhumatpārthivaṃ rajaḥ rajo bhūmiloka ucyate, dhūlirvā /
24.11.[39]	dyaurdyulokaḥ madhvastu madhurasasyandinī vṛṣṭyādidvāreṇa bhavatu /
24.11.[40]	kīdṛśī dyauḥ /
24.11.[41]	pitā pālayitrī //
24.11.[42]	vanaspatiḥ phalī madhumānasmākaṃ bhavatu /
24.11.[43]	evamasmākaṃ sūryo madhumān bhavatu anena karmaṇā gāvaśca madhumatyo naḥ santu kṣīrādidānadvāreṇa madhurasāḥ // 11 //
24.12.[1]	prācyā ārabhya pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā bhakṣayantvantairmantrairmadhuparkapātraprānteṣu aṃgulilepān nirmāṣṭi /
24.12.[2]	pratidiśaṃ pratimantramitivacanātpaṃcamena mantreṇārthātpūrvoktadikkoṇe nirmārjanamāpatati /
24.12.[3]	mantrārthastu he lepa prācyāṃ diśi vartamānā vasavo devatāviśeṣāstvāṃ bhakṣayantu vasavastvayā tṛptā bhavantvityarthaḥ /
24.12.[4]	kīdṛśā vasavaḥ /
24.12.[5]	agnirājāno'gniryeṣāṃ rājā /
24.12.[6]	tatpuruṣe hi samāsāntaḥ syāt /
24.12.[7]	eṣā yojanā sarvamantreṣu tulyā // 12 //
24.13.[1]	yanmadhuna ityādimantreṇa madhuparkasya saṃbandhino bhāgānaṅguṣṭhasahitayā ekaikayā aṃgulyā gṛhītvā caturo vārānaśnāti aṃguṣṭhasahitayā kaniṣṭhayā prathamaṃ tato'nāmikayā, madhyamayā, pradeśinyā pratyekamaṃguṣṭhasahitayāvadānacatuṣṭaye gṛhīte yacchiṣyate, tatsuhṛde kanīyase bhrātṛprabhṛtaye prayacchati /
24.13.[2]	mantrārthastu pṛthivyādīni bhūtāni madhvivāmṛtamiva, madhavyaṃ madhusāraḥ amṛtasāraḥ sārasāra ityarthaḥ, yanmadhuno'mṛtasya saṃbandhi madhavyaṃ sārasāraḥ pṛthivīti ‘iyaṃ pṛthivī sarveṣāṃ bhūtānāṃ madhu’ ityādinā bṛhadāraṇyake pṛthivyā bhūtasāratvena pratipādanāt tasya madhavyasya pṛthivīlakṣaṇasya sārasārasya yatparamamutkṛṣṭatamaṃ rūpamannādilakṣaṇaṃ, tena bhuktenāhaṃ madhavyasya sarvāmṛtasārasya madhuno'mṛtasya nityānandarūpasya paramasya paramātmatādātmyavṛtterannādyasyādanīyasya susaṃvedanabhogyasya paramo'nnādaḥ paramātmasvarūpaḥ tatra layāt bhūyāsaṃ brahmabhūyamahaṃ gaccheyamiti yāvat /
24.13.[3]	kiṃca he madhuparka asi tvaṃ trayyai vidyāyai vedatrayasya yaśaḥ prakāśaḥ, tathā śriyai saṃpado yaśaḥ prakāśo'si, ato yaśase tvāmaśnāmi /
24.13.[4]	kiṃca brahmaṇaḥ paramātmano dīptiḥ prakāśastvaṃ, satyasya vedārthasya śrīḥ saṃpadasi yaśasaśca śrīḥ, ato mayi śrīḥ śrīḥ śrayatāṃ bhūyobhūyo mayi śrīstiṣṭhatvityarthaḥ // 13 //
24.14.[1]	anena mantreṇācāmati /
24.14.[2]	he ācamanodaka amṛtasya madhuparkasya upastaraṇamācchādakamasi // 14 //
24.15.[1]	arhayitā dattamadhuparkaḥ san khaḍgapāṇirbhūtvā tasmai arhaṇīyāya bhakṣitamadhuparkāya gāmāha ‘gāṃ kariṣye’ ityanujñāṃ prārthayate anyārthenetyarthaḥ /
24.15.[2]	gośca karaṇaṃ nipātanam // 15 //
24.16.[1]	tāṃ gāṃ śāsti ‘oṃ kuruṣva’ ityanujñāṃ arhaṇīyo dadātītyarthaḥ // 16 //
24.16.[2]	arhayitānuṃ mantramāha /
24.16.[3]	he gauḥ mama cāgniśarmaṇo'muṣya ca viṣṇuśarmaṇaḥ pūjyasya yaduddeśena vaidikavidhiparavaśīkṛto'hamidamakartavyaṃ karomi tasya pāpmānaṃ jahi nāśayeti yāvat, athavā hato me pāpmā nāstyataḥ karmaṇo mama pāpaṃ vidhicoditatvādityarthaḥ /
24.16.[4]	he viśasitāraḥ mama pāpmānaṃ hata nāśayata // 17 //
24.16.[5]	he viśasitāraḥ gauḥ kriyatāmityanujānātītyarthaḥ // 18 //
24.17-18.[1]	nānāgotrānnānāpravarāṃścādau caturo brāhmaṇān bhojayetpaścātsabāndhavamarhaṇīyam /
24.17-18.[2]	eṣa ādyo brāhmaṇāyopāyo gokaraṇādika upadiṣṭastena nātra vicikitsā kartavyetyarthaḥ // 19 //
24.19.[1]	niścite'pi yadiśabdo dṛṣṭaḥ ‘yadi vedāḥ pramāṇam’ iti yathā /
24.19.[2]	uktāmitikartavyatāṃ vidhāya gāmutsṛjet na hanyādityarthaḥ, mātā rudrāṇāmityādica paṭhet /
24.19.[3]	iyaṃ gau rudrāṇāmantarikṣacāriṇāṃ devatāviśeṣāṇāṃ mātā paripoṣikā payaḥprabhavāhutidvārakavṛṣṭyādidvāreṇa vasūnāṃ vāsayitṛṇāmoṣadhīnāṃ bhūmijānāṃ duhitā poṣaṇīyā, ādityānāṃ svasā bhaginī adititanayā, ato'haṃ pranuvocaṃ cikituṣe janāya nuśabdo niścaye, niścayaṃ kṛtvā pravadāmi cikituṣe caitanyātiśayavate janāya kiṃ vadāmi /
24.19.[4]	he viśasitāraḥ gāṃ mā vadhiṣṭa /
24.19.[5]	kīdṛśīm /
24.19.[6]	anāgāmapāpāṃ, aditimakhaṇḍitāṃ dainyaśūnyāṃ vā /
24.19.[7]	kutaḥ /
24.19.[8]	yasmādiyaṃ śobhanaṃ yavasaṃ ghāsamattīti sūyavasāt /
24.19.[9]	kiṃca he gauḥ bhago dhanaṃ payo yaśaśca vidyate yasyāḥ sā bhagavatī payasvinī tvaṃ bhūyāḥ, tathā vayamapi tvatprasādāt bhagavanto dhanayuktāḥ yaśasvinaśca syāma /
24.19.[10]	he anupahiṃsite tṛṇamaddhi bhuṅkṣva /
24.19.[11]	yatastvaṃ viśvadānī sarvasya dātrī payodvāreṇa /
24.19.[12]	piba śuddhamudakamā samantāt carantī viharantī // 20 //
24.20-21.[1]	arhayitāha omityavicāritasiddhaṃ kṛtvā he viśasitāraḥ yūyaṃ gāmutsṛjata /
24.20-21.[2]	utsṛṣṭā satī svācchandyena tṛṇānyattu bhakṣayatu ityuktvā tāmutsṛṣṭāṃ dṛṣṭvā paśuṃ chāgaṃ, paśvaṅgaṃ vā māṃsakhaṇḍaṃ pratinidhīta /
24.20-21.[3]	nāmāṃso māṃsavihīno madhuparkaḥ syāditi ha śrutito vijñāyate, haśabda itihāse /
24.20-21.[4]	apivā ghṛtamiśrita odana eva kartavyo māṃsadveṣiṇe tādṛśā vā //
25.1.[1]	anṛkṣarā ityādimantreṇa gṛhītajalabhāṇḍamudakasya āhartāraṃ preṣayati kanyāsnānādyupayogi jalamānetuṃ puruṣaṃ prahiṇotītyarthaḥ ṛgarthastu brahmaṇa ārṣa sūryasya vā /
25.1.[2]	triṣṭup /
25.1.[3]	paṃthā iti vyatyayenaikavacanam /
25.1.[4]	ṛkṣarāḥ kaṇṭakādayaḥ paruṣāstṛṇaviśeṣāḥ, na vidyante ṛkṣarāḥ yeṣu te anṛkṣarāḥ paṃthānaḥ santu, ṛjavaśvākuṭilāḥ /
25.1.[5]	yebhiryaiḥ no'smākaṃ saṃbandhinaḥ sahāyā vareyaṃ varaṇīyaṃ gaṃgādikaṃ jalāharaṇasthānaṃ yanti gacchanti /
25.1.[6]	sakhāya iti vyatyayena bahuvacanam /
25.1.[7]	kiṃcāryamā ādityaḥ bhagaśca no'smākaṃ saṃbandhinaṃ sakhāyaṃ sanninīyāt sa myagudkasthānaṃ prāpayet /
25.1.[8]	he devāḥ ṛtvigprabhṛtayaḥ ādityaprabhṛtayaśca yuṣmatprasādāt jāspatyaṃ jāyāyāḥ patyuśca samāgamaḥ samyak suyamamastu susaṃyataṃ sthirataraṃ saṃpūrṇamastu /
25.1.[9]	‘jāyāyāspatyau vā cchandasi’ iti jāspatyaśabdaśchandasi nipātitaḥ // 1 //
25.2.[1]	sa prahita udāhāraḥ udakakumbhaṃ śamīśākhayā sapatrayā pidhāya sthagayitvā udakamānayet // 2 //
25.3.[1]	etāsāmeva āhāritānāmapāṃ saṃbandhino bhāgānavadāyāvadāyodakasaṃpādyānarthān kanyājñānasuvarṇakṣāraṇāgniparyukṣaṇādīn kuryānnānyena jalena // 3 //
25.4.[1]	śanna āpa ityādimantreṇākevalābhiḥ sarvoṣadhyādigandhadravyayuktābhiḥ phalaviśeṣasahitābhiścādbhiḥ kanyāṃ snāpayet /
25.4.[2]	tato ‘yā akṛntan’ ityādinā ahatamapūrvaparihitamatyantābhinavaṃ vastraṃ paridhāpayet /
25.4.[3]	tataśca ‘āśāsānā’ ityādinā mantreṇāntare guptāṃ kṛtvā yathā na dṛśyate tathā vā sannahanaṃ kanyāyāḥ kuryāt mauñjena darbhanirmitena vā yoktreṇa //
25.4.[4]	śanna āpa ityanuṣṭup vyākhyātā /
25.4.[5]	yā imā udāhāreṇāhṛtāḥ, tāḥ śaṃ sukhaṃ naḥ saṃtviti viśeṣaḥ //
25.4.[6]	yā akṛntanniti jagatī /
25.4.[7]	he āyuṣmati kanye idaṃ vāsaḥ paridhatsva paridhehi /
25.4.[8]	tvāṃ ca sarvāstā devyo jarasā parivyayantu jarasā veṣṭayantu jarājarjaritāṃ sabhartṛkāṃ satīṃ tvāṃ devatāḥ sampādayantu dīrghamāyustava kurvantvityarthaḥ /
25.4.[9]	kāstā devyaḥ /
25.4.[10]	yā idaṃ vāso'kṛntan yābhiḥ kartanena saṃpāditamadhiṣṭhātrībhirdevatābhiḥ, yā avayan yābhirutaṃ saṃpāditaṃ vāsaḥ, yā atanvata yābhiḥ sūtramātataṃ dairghyeṇa prasāritaṃ, yāśca devīrantāṃ abhito'tatantha, ubhayato mūlapallavasya cāntāḥ prāntāḥ yābhirātānitā ityarthaḥ /
25.4.[11]	tāśca devatā mantrāntare svanāmnaivopāttāḥ ‘revatīstvā vyakṣṇan’ iti //
25.4.[12]	āśāsānā saumanasaṃ prajāṃ saubhāgyaṃ rayim /
25.4.[13]	agneranuvratā bhūtvā sanno sukṛtāya kam //
25.4.[14]	anuṣṭup /
25.4.[15]	pṛthivyā ārṣam /
25.4.[16]	ahaṃ sannahye vastraṃ badhnāmi /
25.4.[17]	kimartham /
25.4.[18]	sukṛtāya karmaṇe vivāhapūrvayāgadānahomādikarmārtham /
25.4.[19]	kamiti kāmāyetyarthaḥ /
25.4.[20]	yathā ‘cakṣuṣe kaṃ pūrvamātyajyate’ ityatra cakṣuṣkāmapratītiḥ, evaṃ sukṛtāya kamiti sukṛtakāmapratītiḥ /
25.4.[21]	kīdṛśī satī sannahye /
25.4.[22]	saumanasaṃ prasannamānasatvaṃ tathā saubhāgyaṃ bhartrānukūlyaṃ rayiṃ ca dhanamāśāsānā icchantī, tathā agneranuvratā satī āhavanīyādiparicaraṇaśīlā satī sannahye // 4 //
25.5-6.[1]	preto muñcātvityādibhistisṛbhiḥ udānīyasthānādutkṣipyotsaṃge kṛtvā sthānāntare pitā jyeṣṭho bhrātā vā yathoktaṃ vāsasa uparibhāgācchādanasyāpyadhastanācchādanavat ‘yā akṛntan'ityādinā mantreṇa karma kuryādityarthaḥ /
25.5-6.[2]	sūryasyārṣam /
25.5-6.[3]	prathamatṛtīye'nuṣṭubhau, dvitīyā triṣṭup /
25.5-6.[4]	he kanye itaḥ sthānātpramuñcātu pramuñcāmi tvāṃ nayāmi bhavatīm /
25.5-6.[5]	muñcātviti tiṅvyatyayaḥ puruṣavyatyayaśca tathāca śākhāntare preto muñcāmīti mantraḥ paṭhyate /
25.5-6.[6]	pitṛkule bhartṛkule ca subaddhāṃ suśliṣṭāṃ satīmetāṃ kanyāmamutaḥ pitṛkulādamutaśca bhartṛkulāt mākarat kaścinmā kārṣīt kuladvaye vigamaṃ tasyā mā kārṣīt kaścidapītyarthaḥ /
25.5-6.[7]	he indra parameśvara mīḍhvaḥ sektaḥ iyaṃ kanyā suputrā subhagā ca yathā bhavati, tathā kuru /
25.5-6.[8]	he kanye itaḥ sthānāt pūṣā indrastvāṃ nayatu /
25.5-6.[9]	hastagṛhya hastena gṛhītvā /
25.5-6.[10]	aśvinau ca tvāṃ rathena pravahatāmabhimataṃ sthānaṃ prāpayatām /
25.5-6.[11]	tathā krameṇa tvaṃ gṛhānbhartṛveśmāni gaccha /
25.5-6.[12]	tatra ca gṛhapatnī gṛhasya pālayitrī prabhuryathā asaḥ bhavasi, tathāstu /
25.5-6.[13]	vaśinī jitakarmakarajanādikā bhava /
25.5-6.[14]	vidathe ca yajñe mā vadāsi yajñapratikūlaṃ bharturmā vādīḥ vaidikakarmakalāpānukūlā bhavetyarthaḥ //
25.5-6.[15]	ye paripaṃthino mārge pratikūlācauraprabhṛtayo dampatī jāyāvarau āsīdanti duṣṭabuddhyā samāsīdanti, te tvāṃ mā vidan mā drākṣuḥ sugebhiḥ śobhanagamanairdurgaṃ mārgamatītāmatikrāntāṃ sarvam /
25.5-6.[16]	kiṃca apadrāntvarātayaḥ śatravo dānahīnāśca dhanābhāvāśca dāridryābhidhānā apadrāntu bhītāḥ parāṅmukhāḥ santaḥ palāyamānāḥ kutsitāṃ skhalanarūpāṃ gatiṃ labhantāmityarthaḥ //
25.7.[1]	asminnavasare ācārikāṇi ācārādāgatāni deśajātikuladharmatayā prasiddhāni karmāṇi kārayedityarthaḥ /
25.7.[2]	tadyathā āgamanaprayojanakathanaṃ kanyāyā nāmagrahaṇaṃ kuladevatāpūjanaṃ sumanolatābhistāḍanamityādīni // 6 //
25.8.[1]	‘eṣa aupasado'gnirvaivāhano vā’ ‘tasmin pākayajñāḥ’ iti vakṣyati /
25.8.[2]	vaivāhanasya vikalpyamānāścatasraḥ prakṛtayo'trocyante /
25.8.[3]	sadyaḥ araṇibhyāṃ nirmathito yastatra nirmanthyaśabdo rūḍhaḥ /
25.8.[4]	tatra nirmanthanasāmānyānnirmanthanāntaravanmantre prāpte tūṣṇīmityuktam /
25.8.[5]	eṣa ekaḥ /
25.8.[6]	brāṣṭrādvitīyaḥ /
25.8.[7]	sāntapanastṛtīyaḥ /
25.8.[8]	yo balenāgninā santaptādapasāritāgnikādbhūbhāgāt kārpāsagomayacūrṇādisaṃsargaṃ kṛtvotpādyate pāṣāṇaṃ kaṃsamaṇiṃ vā tāpayitvā sūryasaṃmukhaṃ sūryakāntamaṇiṃ vā sthāpayitvā, so'bhimataḥ /
25.8.[9]	yatra dīpyamānaścaturthaḥ /
25.8.[10]	atrāviśeṣaśrutāvapi tretāvasathaśmaśānaparigṛhītasūtakapatitādyagnivarjamiti jñeyam /
25.8.[11]	upasamādhāyeti pratyekaṃ sambandhanīyam, gārhapatyavaduddhatāvokṣite jānudaghne kuṇḍe sthāpayitvetyarthaḥ /
25.8.[12]	gṛhādbahireveti niyamaḥ /
25.8.[13]	parisamūhanaṃ sajalena kareṇa caturdiksaṃsparśanam /
25.8.[14]	paryukṣaṇamāsecanam /
25.8.[15]	evaṃ caturdikkameva darbhaiḥ paristaraṇaṃ prathitam /
25.8.[16]	prāgdakṣiṇodakṣvavastaraṇamityanye manyante tribhistaraiḥ stṛṇātīti vaiśravaṇīyadarśanāt /
25.8.[17]	ājyasya vilayanaṃ vigalanam, utpavanaṃ pavitreṇa pāvanam /
25.8.[18]	āghārādājyabhāgāntān homān hutvā agneḥ paścimabhāge sthitayoḥ satoḥ kanyāvarayoryathāsaṃkhyaṃ vāmadakṣiṇabhāgenāgneraparabhāge anaḥ śakaṭaṃ, rathaṃ syandanaṃ vā sayugamavasthāpya yoge yoga ityādikayarcā kanyāvarau yūpe yunakti dakṣiṇabhāge varamuttarabhāge kanyāṃ yoktreṇa saṃyojayatītyarthaḥ //
25.8.[19]	yoge yoge tavastaraṃ vāje vāje havāmahe /
25.8.[20]	sakhāya indramūtaye //
25.8.[21]	gāyatrī /
25.8.[22]	maitrī /
25.8.[23]	kaśyapasyārṣam /
25.8.[24]	vayamindraṃ havāmahe āhvayāmaḥ /
25.8.[25]	kutra /
25.8.[26]	yoge yoge, dampatyoḥ sahabhāvenāvasthitayoḥ parikarmasambandhe tathā vāje vāje, vājaśabdo'nnabalasaṃgamavacanaḥ, iha tvannavacano gṛhyate gārhasthyasyānnamūlatvāt vājaśabdena cānnasādhanaṃ vakṣyate, haviṣi haviṣi cājyeṣṭabhāgadānāyeti protsāhanā /
25.8.[27]	kimarthamāhvayāmaḥ /
25.8.[28]	ūtaye avanāya /
25.8.[29]	kīdṛśā vayam /
25.8.[30]	sakhāyaḥ samānakhyānāḥ /
25.8.[31]	kīdṛśamindram /
25.8.[32]	tavastaraṃ tavaḥśabdo balavacanaḥ mahattvavacano vā, balavattaraṃ mahattaraṃ vā // 7 //
25.9.[1]	prakṛtayoktrayuktāvivātrāpi prāptaṃ maṃtraṃ niṣedhayati tūṣṇīmiti /
25.9.[2]	vimucya kaśāyojitaṃ yoktraṃ mocayitvā /
25.9.[3]	khe rathasyetyādikayarcā hiraṇyaṃ darbhapavitreṇa baddhvā yugasya dakṣiṇabhāgagate randhre nidadhāti /
25.9.[4]	kathaṃ baddhā /
25.9.[5]	niṣṭarkyaṃ kṛtvā yathā sukhamocanaṃ bhavati tathetyarthaḥ, niṣṭarkyaṃ sukhavimocanam /
25.9.[6]	tatsuvarṇaṃ baddhvānantaraṃ dakṣiṇabhāge varasthāne kanyāmānīya sasuvarṇe dakṣiṇasminyugasya tarmaṇi cchidre pūrvoktābhiradbhiradhyadhi kṣārayati, ‘uparyadhyadhasaḥ sāmīpye’ iti vīpsāyāṃ sāmīpye adhyadhīti dvirvacanam, yugacchidrasyādhaḥ samīpe kanyāṃ sthāpayitvā mūrdhani suvarṇodakaṃ kṣārayatītyarthaḥ /
25.9.[7]	asminnavasare kanyāvarayoḥ sthānaparivṛttiḥ saṃpannā, punaḥ sthāna eva sthitirbhaviṣyati /
25.9.[8]	yadvakṣyati ‘dakṣiṇataḥ pumānbhavati’ iti //
25.9.[9]	khe rathasyetyaindrī anuṣṭup /
25.9.[10]	brahmaṇa ārṣam /
25.9.[11]	anyatrāpyucyamāne brahmaṇa evārṣam ‘anantaraṃ ca vakrebhyo vedāstasya vinirgatāḥ /’ iti sarvavedānāṃ sāmānyena taddṛṣṭatvasmṛteḥ /
25.9.[12]	he śatakrato anantakriya indrastejasvināṃ madhye parameśvara āditya etāṃ kanyāṃ sūryavarcasamādityakalpakānti karotu /
25.9.[13]	kiṃ kṛtvā /
25.9.[14]	triṣpūtvā trīn vārān pavitrayitvā /
25.9.[15]	kīdṛśīm /
25.9.[16]	apālāṃ vivāhātpūrvaṃ svacchandacāriṇīmata eva pāvanayogyām /
25.9.[17]	kva /
25.9.[18]	rathasya khe, tathā anasaḥ śakaṭasya yugasya ca khe cchidre /
25.9.[19]	athavā apālāmivendra imāṃ kanyāṃ pūtāṃ kṛtvā sūryavarcasaṃ karotviti ivārthagarbhaṃ vyākhyānam /
25.9.[20]	yathā kilāpāleti nāmnā atrerduhitā kuṣṭhavyādhigrastā śūnyāśrame snānādyarthāpastṛtamunike dṛṣṭā yūpādicchidreṣu suvarṇodakenābhiṣicyendreṇa vyapagatarogā sūryakāntiḥ saṃpāditā, tadvadetāmadhyapagatapāpāṃ kṛtvā sūryavarcasaṃ karotu indraḥ /
25.9.[21]	tathā cetihāsaḥ ‘apālātrisutā tvāsītkanyā tvagdoṣiṇī purā /
25.9.[22]	tāmindraścakame dṛṣṭvā vijane piturāśrame //
25.9.[23]	rathacchidre tu tāmindro yugasya śakaṭasya ca /
25.9.[24]	prakṣipya nicakarṣa tristataḥ sā sukhacābhavat //’ iti /
25.9.[25]	śaṃ te hiraṇyamiti jagatī /
25.9.[26]	he kanye te tava hiraṇyaṃ śaṃ sukhamastu /
25.9.[27]	śamu santvāpaḥ, u iti nipātaḥ samuccaye, āpaśca te sukhaṃ santu /
25.9.[28]	methī rathāvastambhanaṃ varūthaṃ śaṃ sukhaṃ tavāstu /
25.9.[29]	yugasya tarma cchidraṃ tava sukhakaramastu /
25.9.[30]	āpaste śatapavitrā bahupāvanyaḥ sukhakāriṇyo bhavantu /
25.9.[31]	enā patyā tanvā saṃsṛjasva, enā anena bhartrā saha tanvā śarīreṇa saṃsṛjasva saṃbadhyasva /
25.9.[32]	kvacittu śākhāyāṃ paṭhyate tanvaṃ saṃsṛjasveti, bhartrā saha saṃyojayeti tatrārthaḥ // 8 //
25.10.[1]	kanyāyā abhiṣekasaṃskāre kṛte sati punaragneraparabhāge prāṅmukhaḥ puruṣo bhavati dakṣiṇena, arthāt kanyā uttareṇa bhavatīti labhyate /
25.10.[2]	atra dakṣiṇabhāgamānīya saṃskriyamāṇatvāt kanyā pradhānamityeke, svatantratvāt sadā dakṣiṇabhāge cāvasthānāt puruṣaḥ pradhānaṃ vivāha ityanye // 9 //
25.11.[1]	athaśabdo maṃgalārtha iti māṭharaḥ, antarāle'kṣatasaktuhomadyotanāyāthaśabda ityādityadarśanaḥ /
25.11.[2]	avaśyaṃ hi uktayuktyā te homāntarālādāvapi hotavyā ityatraivāvasare na kṣatiriti /
25.11.[3]	homān krameṇāha agnaye ityādi /
25.11.[4]	‘pūrvaṃ devaiḥ striyo bhuktāḥ somagandharvavahnibhiḥ /’ iti śrūyate /
25.11.[5]	tena niṣkrayāya teṣāṃ homaḥ /
25.11.[6]	yadyapi ca somaḥ prathamastathāpyagrato homo'trāgnaye ‘yena karmaṇecchedagnimukhaṃ kuryāt’ ityabhiprāyeṇa /
25.11.[7]	agnaye svāhā suhutamastu /
25.11.[8]	kīdṛśāya /
25.11.[9]	janivide janī vadhūḥ janīṃ vetti vindate vā janivit tasmai /
25.11.[10]	evamanyat // 10 //
25.12.[1]	ekādaśa saṃtanya evamādyāḥ // 11 //
25.13.[1]	juhoti ityanuṣaṅgaḥ /
25.13.[2]	jayāścābhyātānāśca, tān rāṣṭrabhṛtaśca juhotītyarthaḥ // 12 //
25.14.[1]	tāni trīṇi jayādīni karmāṇyuktānatikrameṇa kartavyāni /
25.14.[2]	dvādaśagṛhītena jayāñjuhuyāditi laugākṣiḥ /
25.14.[3]	yathādhītaṃ mantramanudrutya ṛgantena svāhākāreṇa dvādaśaprakṣepā apīti kecit /
25.14.[4]	anye tu dvādaśāvadānagṛhītājyasya sarvamaṃtrānudravaṇe sarvānte svāhākāreṇaika eva prakṣepa ityanutiṣṭhanti, pratimaṃtraṃ tu dvādaśāvadānānyuddharanti /
25.14.[5]	abhyātānāṃ home tu caturgṛhītaṃ juhoti /
25.14.[6]	tatra ‘bṛhaspatipurohitāḥ’ ‘devahūtyām iti āghātagrahaṇam /
25.14.[7]	rāṣṭrabhṛtastu dvādaśagṛhītena trayodaśa homāḥ /
25.14.[8]	ṛtāṣāḍiti dvādaśabhirvaḍantairhutvā ‘sa no bhuvanasya pate’ iti rathamukhe'dhyadhyagniṃ priyamāṇasyeti yathoktatā /
25.14.[9]	pākayajñeṣu hyetattrayaṃ yathāvadvyavasthitaṃ, tatraiva samantrakaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ // 13 //
25.15.[1]	adhipatiśabdopalakṣitaliṃgādādhipatyānyucyante /
25.15.[2]	tāni sānuṣaṅgānyekaviṃśatiryajūṃṣi /
25.15.[3]	agnirbhūtānāmadhipatiḥ sa māvatu tasmai svāhā /
25.15.[4]	yamaḥ pṛthivyā adhi° vāyurantarikṣayādhi° sūryo divo'dhi° caṃdramā nakṣatrāṇāmadhi° viṣṇurdiśāmadhi° pūṣā pathīnāmadhi° tvaṣṭā rūpāṇāmadhi° savitā prasavānāmadhi° indro jyeṣṭhānāmadhi° mitraḥ satyānāmadhi° varuṇo dharmaṇāmadhi° rudraḥ paśūnāmadhi° bṛhaspatirbrahmaṇāmadhi° brāhmaṇo vācāmadhi° soma oṣadhīnāmadhi° samudraḥ sravatyānāmadhi° annaṃ sāmrājyānāmadhipatistanmāvatu tasmai svāhā /
25.15.[5]	gāyatrī cchandasāmadhipatnī sā māvatu tasyai svāhā /
25.15.[6]	maruto gaṇānāmadhipatayaste māvantu tebhyaḥ svāhā /
25.15.[7]	pitaraḥ pitāmahāḥ pare'varebhyaste naḥ pāntu te no'vantvasminbrahmaṇyasminkarmaṇyasminkṣetre'syāmāśiṣyasyāṃ purodhāyāmasyāṃ devahūtyāṃ svāhā //
25.15.[8]	bhūtānāṃ sthāvarajaṃgamānāmagniradhipatirniyantā sa mā avatu āgacchatu havirgrahītuṃ māṃ rakṣatu ca, tasmai svāhā suhutamastu ca /
25.15.[9]	yamaḥ pṛthivyā niyantā sa māvatu vāhetyanuṣaṃgaḥ /
25.15.[10]	evamanyatra /
25.15.[11]	viṣṇurdiśāmadhipatirvyāpakatvāt /
25.15.[12]	pūṣā pathīnāṃ pathikānām /
25.15.[13]	tvaṣṭā rūpāṇāṃ, tvaṣṭā prajāpatirviśvakarmā, sarūpāṇāṃ sarvākṛtīnāmadhipatiḥ /
25.15.[14]	savitā prasavānāṃ, prasūyanta iti prasavāḥ aṃkurādayaḥ /
25.15.[15]	indro jyeṣṭhānāṃ prāśastyānām /
25.15.[16]	mitraḥ satyānāmiti tathāca śrūyate ‘mitrāya satyapataye’ iti /
25.15.[17]	varuṇo dharmaṇāṃ dharmāṇo dhartārasteṣāṃ varuṇo'dhipatiḥ ‘varuṇo'si dhṛtavrato varuṇastvottabhnātu’ iti darśanāt, dhartṝṇāṃ pṛthivyādīnāṃ sarveṣāṃ varuṇo dharteti vaiśeṣikādibhirapyuktam /
25.15.[18]	rudraḥ paśūnāṃ sa hyabhyarthayate ‘ahameva paśūnāmīśe’ iti /
25.15.[19]	bṛhaspatirbrahmaṇāṃ vedānāmadhipatiḥ /
25.15.[20]	brāhmaṇo vācāṃ, sa eva hi daivīnāṃ mānuṣīṇāṃ ca vācāmupadeṣṭā ‘tasmādbrāhmaṇa ubhe vācau vadati daivīṃ ca mānuṣīṃ ca’ iti śruteḥ /
25.15.[21]	somaścandro grāmyāraṇyānāmoṣadhīnāṃ phalapākāntānāmadhipatiḥ /
25.15.[22]	sravatyānāṃ nadīnāṃ samudro'ntarikṣākhyo'dhipatiḥ, apāmāśrayaṇīyaṃ hyantarikṣaṃ sūkṣmāṇāmanyathāvaśyāyaḥ katham /
25.15.[23]	sāmrājyamaiśvaryaṃ teṣāmannaṃ, pṛthivyāḥ sauro raso'dhipatiḥ /
25.15.[24]	maruto gaṇānāṃ, sarveṣāmevāgnyādigaṇānāṃ maruto'dhipatayo vyākhyātāḥ /
25.15.[25]	avarebhyaḥ nikaṭebhyaḥ pitṛpitāmahādibhyo ye pare sargasamudbhavā hiraṇyagarbhamanuprabhṛtayaḥ pitaraḥ, te naḥ pāntu pālayantu ceti prakṛtamapekṣaṇīyamavateḥ prakṛtasya gatyarthatvāt /
25.15.[26]	kvāvantu /
25.15.[27]	asmin brahmaṇi, eteṣu brāhmaṇeṣu ṛtvikṣu dakṣiṇayā svīkṛteṣu, asmin vivāhākhye karmaṇi, asmin kṣetre pālane, asyāṃ cāśiṣi ṛtvigbhirādhīyamānāyāṃ dampatyoḥ phalabhūtāyāṃ, yadyapi ṛtvigviśeṣā māmavantvityuccārayanti, tathāpi karmaṇo dakṣiṇayā tadīyasya parikrītatvādyajamānasyaiva phalam, purodhāyāṃ paurohityakarmaṇi, devahūtyāṃ devānāṃ hūtirāhvānaṃ havirdānāya yatra, sā devahūtirvivāhabhūmiriha // 14 //
25.16-20.[1]	‘ākūtyai tvā’ ityādibhirmantrairājyaṃ hutvā hutvā kanyāyā mūrdhni saṃpātān hutājyaśeṣabiṃdūn mūrdhnyavanayet srāvayet /
25.16-20.[2]	tvetyantairiti svāhākārāntatāṃ nivartayatīti kecit /
25.16-20.[3]	anye tvāhuḥ tvāntānāmeva pāṭhāt tvāntatvāvyabhicārāt anyāntatvamapyastīti svāhākārāntatādyotanāya tvāntagrahaṇamiti /
25.16-20.[4]	hiraṇyagarbha ityādinā sakalenānuvākenaika eva homo mā vijñāyīti pratyṛcagrahaṇam /
25.16-20.[5]	āgnipāvamānībhirityagniliṅgābhiḥ pavamānaliṅgābhiśca //
25.16-20.[6]	ākūtyai tvā kāmāya tvā samṛddhyai tvā //
25.16-20.[7]	ākavanamākūtirabhiprāyaḥ, abhipretasiddhaye he ājya tvāṃ juhomītyarthaḥ /
25.16-20.[8]	vyākhyānāṃgaṃ juhotiradhyāhriyate, natu maṃtraikadeśaḥ /
25.16-20.[9]	adhyāhriyamāṇasya mantraikadeśatve ṛcāmapi sākāṃkṣatvādadhyāhārasahitānāṃ yatirvinaśyet, tataśca gāyatryanuvākyā triṣṭubiti nāvakalpate /
25.16-20.[10]	tasmādarthavyākhyānāṅgameva adhyāhāro, na maṃtrakadeśaḥ, ityāhuḥ /
25.16-20.[11]	kāmāya kāmyamānasiddhaye tvāṃ juhomi /
25.16-20.[12]	samṛddhiḥ saṃpat tadarthaṃ tvāṃ juhomi //
25.16-20.[13]	hiraṇyagarbhaḥ samavartatāgre bhūtasya jātaḥ patireka āsīt /
25.16-20.[14]	sa dādhāra pṛthivīṃ dyāmutemāṃ kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema //1// aṣṭānāmapi puruṣasya nārāyaṇasyārṣam /
25.16-20.[15]	hiraṇyagarbhaḥ prajāpatiḥ puruṣo nārāyaṇaḥ prāṇo jagatsūtraṃ kaḥ samrāḍiti paryāyāḥ /
25.16-20.[16]	hiraṇyagarbhaḥ agre sargādau samavartata prādurbabhūva /
25.16-20.[17]	sa ca jātaḥ prādurbhūtaḥ san eka eva bhūtasya samastasya pṛthivyādibhūtajātasya abhivyaṃgyasya vā mahadādeḥ patiḥ pālakaḥ prabhurāsīt vyatyayenātītavibhaktiḥ, prādurbhavati jagadādau hiraṇyagarbhaḥ patiśca bhavati sarvasyetyarthaḥ /
25.16-20.[18]	sa hīmāṃ pratyakṣāṃ pṛthivīṃ kṣitiṃ dādhāra dhārayate, uta tathā dyāṃ svargaṃ pṛthivīṃ ca /
25.16-20.[19]	pṛthivīśabdaḥ sāmīpyādantarikṣe vartate /
25.16-20.[20]	hiraṇyagarbha eva hi sarva protaṃ sūtre maṇigaṇā iva /
25.16-20.[21]	tasmai kasmai prajāpataye, devāya dānādiguṇayuktāya, haviṣā ājyena vidhema paricarāma, tasmai havirdadma iti yāvat //
25.16-20.[22]	yaḥ prāṇato nimiṣataca rājā patirviśvasya jagato babhūva /
25.16-20.[23]	īśe yo asya dvipadaścatuṣpadaḥ kasmai° // 2 //
25.16-20.[24]	yaḥ prāṇāpānādimato nimeṣādimataśca devamānuṣādeḥ rājā prabhuḥ patiḥ pālayitā /
25.16-20.[25]	prāṇena apānādyupalakṣyate, nimeṣeṇa sparśanādikaṃ buddhīndriyakarmendriyakriyāyogitvam /
25.16-20.[26]	prāṇanādikaṃ kurvataḥ nimiṣato jighrato viharata ityādi jñeyam /
25.16-20.[27]	viśvasya sarvasya jagato jaṃgamasya babhūva bhavati /
25.16-20.[28]	sahi īśe īṣṭe prabhavati dvipado devamanuṣyādeḥ, catuṣpado gavādeḥ /
25.16-20.[29]	tasmai kasmai devāyeti pūrvavat //
25.16-20.[30]	ya ojodā baladā yasya viśva upāsate praśiṣaṃ yasya devāḥ /
25.16-20.[31]	yasya cchāyāmṛtaṃ yasya mṛtyuḥ kasmai° // 3 //
25.16-20.[32]	oja utsāhaḥ, balaṃ sāmarthya, taddadātītyojodā baladāḥ /
25.16-20.[33]	yasya saṃbandhinaṃ praśiṣamanuśāsanamanujñāṃ viśve sarve janā devāścopāsate sevante'nuvartante /
25.16-20.[34]	yasya saṃbandhinī chāyā āśraya ārādhanam, amṛtaṃ mokṣaphalam /
25.16-20.[35]	yasya ca viparyaya arthādanārādhanaṃ, mṛtyuḥ saṃsārakārī /
25.16-20.[36]	tasmai kasmā iti samānam //
25.16-20.[37]	yena dyaurugrā pṛthivī dṛḍhā ca yena svaḥ stabhitaṃ yena nākam yo antarikṣaṃ vimame varīyaḥ kasmai° // 4 //
25.16-20.[38]	yena prajāpatinā dyaurantarikṣamugrā unnatā, dṛḍhā avaṣṭabdhā, tathā pṛthivī vyāptā, tathā svaḥ stabhitaṃ vyāptamavaṣṭabdhaṃ protaṃ, svargo'pyavaṣṭabdha ityarthaḥ /
25.16-20.[39]	yena nākamādityamaṇḍalamavaṣṭabdham /
25.16-20.[40]	svarityasya viśeṣaṇaṃ vā nākamiti, kaṃ sukhaṃ, na kamakaṃ duḥkhaṃ na vidyate yatra tannākam /
25.16-20.[41]	yaścāntarikṣaṃ vimame nirmame /
25.16-20.[42]	kīdṛśam /
25.16-20.[43]	varīya urutaram /
25.16-20.[44]	tulyamanyat //
25.16-20.[45]	ya ime dyāvāpṛthivī tastabhāne adhārayadrodhasī rejamāne /
25.16-20.[46]	yasminnadhi vitataḥ sūra eti kasmai° // 5 //
25.16-20.[47]	ime pratyakṣadṛśye dyāvāpṛthivyau rejamāne vepamāne satyau yo'dhārayat dhārayate /
25.16-20.[48]	kīdṛśyau /
25.16-20.[49]	rodhasī rundhāne /
25.16-20.[50]	kathaṃ kṛtvā /
25.16-20.[51]	tastabhāne niḥśalye kṛtvā /
25.16-20.[52]	yasminnadhi yasyopari sūra āditya eti gacchati /
25.16-20.[53]	kīdṛśaḥ /
25.16-20.[54]	vitato vistīrṇaḥ //
25.16-20.[55]	yasyeme viśve girayo mahitvā samudraṃ yasya rasayā sahāhuḥ /
25.16-20.[56]	diśo yasya pradiśaḥ paṃca devīḥ kasmai° // 6 //
25.16-20.[57]	yasya hiraṇyagarbhasya ime prasiddhā mervādayo girayaḥ mahitvā mahimānaṃ māhātmyamāhuḥ, tathā paṃca diśaḥ prāgādyā ūrdhvayā saha, vidiśaśca nāgyā saha paṃca yasya māhātmyamāhuḥ /
25.16-20.[58]	devīrdānādidharmikāḥ iti diśāṃ viśeṣaṇam //
25.16-20.[59]	āpo ha yanmahatīrviśvamāyangarbhaṃ dadhānā janayantīragnim /
25.16-20.[60]	tato devānāṃ niravartatāsurekaḥ kasmai° // 7 //
25.16-20.[61]	yasmin kāle sargādau mahatya āpaḥ prathamaṃ sṛṣṭāḥ satyo viśvaṃ sarvamāyan vyāptavatyaḥ /
25.16-20.[62]	kiṃ kurvāṇāḥ /
25.16-20.[63]	garbhaṃ dadhānāstameva hiraṇyagarbhaṃ garbharūpeṇa dadhānāḥ dhārayantyaḥ /
25.16-20.[64]	yathoktaṃ ‘apa eva sasarjādau tāsu vīryamavāsṛjat /’ iti /
25.16-20.[65]	kīdṛśyaḥ /
25.16-20.[66]	janayantīragnim /
25.16-20.[67]	agniṃ tejaḥpuṃjarūpaṃ, anyacca aṇḍādikaṃ janayantyaḥ /
25.16-20.[68]	athavā agnimiti garbhaviśeṣaṇaṃ, tejaḥpuñjarūpamityarthaḥ /
25.16-20.[69]	tato garbhādhānānantaraṃ devānāṃ dyotamānānāmindriyāṇāṃ prāṇināṃ vā gatyādiyogināṃ suramānuṣaprabhṛtīnāṃ ya eka evāsuḥ prāṇaḥ sarvasūtrarūpo niravartata nirvṛttaḥ, tasmai haviṣā vidhema //
25.16-20.[70]	ā naḥ prajāṃ janayatu prajāpatirdhātā dadhātu sumanasyamānaḥ /
25.16-20.[71]	saṃvatsara ṛtubhivāpāno mayi puṣṭiṃ puṣṭipatirdadhātu // 8 //
25.16-20.[72]	sa vyānarūpo hiraṇyagarbhaḥ prajāpatirno'smākaṃ prajāmājanayatu, dhātā vidhātā ca bhūtvā garbhaṃ dadhātu naḥ sumanasyamānaḥ prasannacittaḥ /
25.16-20.[73]	saṃvatsararūpaḥ san ṛtubhiścākllpāno vivartamānaḥ ārtavaiḥ padārthairvipariṇamamānaḥ /
25.16-20.[74]	cākllpāna iti liṭaḥ kānac /
25.16-20.[75]	upalakṣaṇametatprathamavivartasya /
25.16-20.[76]	jalasya hiraṇyagarbho vivartaḥ, tasyoṅkārastasya vedā ityādirūpeṇa sa eva vivartate /
25.16-20.[77]	sa hiraṇyagarbho yataḥ puṣṭipatistato'smākaṃ puṣṭimādadhātu //
25.16-20.[78]	mahāvyāhṛtayo vyākhyātāḥ //
25.16-20.[79]	agna āyūṃṣi pavasa āsuvorjamiṣañca naḥ /
25.16-20.[80]	āre bādhasva ducchunām // 1 //
25.16-20.[81]	tisro gāyatryaḥ /
25.16-20.[82]	kūṣmāṇḍānāmārṣam /
25.16-20.[83]	he agne tvamāyūṃṣi pavase punāsi rogajarādimalairvihīnāni saṃpādayasi /
25.16-20.[84]	no'smabhyamūrjaṃ balaṃ iṣaṃ cānnamāsuva janaya dehi /
25.16-20.[85]	duraḥ śuni paratastāntādeśe prātiśākhye ducchunāmityanvākhyānāt śunāmiva duṣṭānāṃ ducchunāṃ hiṃsrāṇāṃ bādhasva āre dūrata eva /
25.16-20.[86]	ducchunāmiti hiṃsārthānāmiti karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī // 1 //
25.16-20.[87]	agnirṛṣiḥ pavamānaḥ pāñcajanyaḥ purohitaḥ /
25.16-20.[88]	tamīmahe mahāgayam // 2 //
25.16-20.[89]	agnirṛṣiḥ duṣṭān pavamānaḥ punānaḥ, paṃcajanā manuṣyāścatvāro varṇāḥ anulomajavargaḥ paṃcamastebhyo hitaḥ, purohitaḥ ‘agnirvai devānāṃ purohitaḥ’ puro'gre paraloke vā hitaḥ karmasaṃpādanadvāreṇa taṃ vayaṃ īmahe yācāmahe mahāgayaṃ mahāgṛham // 2 //
25.16-20.[90]	agne pavasva svapā ase varcaḥ suvīryam /
25.16-20.[91]	dadhadrayiṃ mayi poṣam // 3 //
25.16-20.[92]	he agne asme asmān pavaskha punīhi /
25.16-20.[93]	apa iti karmanāma, śobhanānyapāṃsi yasya sa svapāḥ sukarmā agniḥ /
25.16-20.[94]	kiṃ kurvan punīhi /
25.16-20.[95]	varcastejaḥ śobhanaṃ ca vīryaṃ, tathā rayiṃ dhanaṃ poṣaṃ ca puṣṭiṃ dadhadvidadhānaḥ dadadvāsmabhyam // 3 // 15 //
25.16-20.[96]	yā ta ityādibhiśca tribhirmaṃtrairhutvā hutvā kanyāyā mūrdhni saṃpātānavanayedityanuṣaṃgeṇa samāptiḥ /
25.16-20.[97]	maṃtratrayārthastu he kanye yā te tava patighnī tanūstāmapatighnīṃ karomi anena saṃpātāvanayena, tathā tava yā aputriyā putrebhyo'hitā tanūstāṃ putrebhyo hitāṃ putriyāṃ karomi, yāca apaśavyā paśubhyo'hitā tanūstāṃ paśavyāṃ paśubhyo hitāṃ karomi /
25.16-20.[98]	atrāvasare pūrvanidarśitavidhānenākṣatasaktūn juhuyāt // 16 //
25.16-20.[99]	pāṇigrahaṇamāha
25.21.[1]	agnerudīcyāṃ diśi darbhāstīrṇe deśe prāṅmukhīṃ kanyāmavasthāpya gururdevasya ta ityādinā maṃtreṇa kanyāyāḥ saṃbandhinaṃ hastaṃ grāhayatītyadhyāhartavyaṃ samānakartṛkatvārtham /
25.21.[2]	kena prayujya grāhayatītyapekṣāyāmarthādvareṇopayantreti yojyam /
25.21.[3]	sacopayantā guruṇānujñātastaṃ gṛhṇāti /
25.21.[4]	kīdṛśo voḍhā gṛhṇāti /
25.21.[5]	śuciḥ karagrahaṇe'dhikṛtaḥ dharmopayoginī mameyamiti śuddhasaṃkalpaḥ, pratyaṅmukhaḥ kanyāyāḥ purastādagre sthitaḥ san /
25.21.[6]	‘prāṅmukhaḥ sarvakarmāṇi kurvīta’ ityasyāpavādārthaṃ pratyaṅmukha iti /
25.21.[7]	dakṣiṇaṃ lokaprasiddhaṃ, sāṅguṣṭhamaṅguṣṭhasahitamuttānaṃ nīcā dakṣiṇena nitāntamañcati ceṣṭāsu pragalbhate nyak dakṣiṇastena /
25.21.[8]	yathoktaṃ dhanurvede ‘pūrvaṃ vāmena śikṣeta pūrvasiddho hi dakṣiṇaḥ /’ iti /
25.21.[9]	nyañcatīti nyak tena nīcā nyagbhūtenetyāvṛttyā yojyam /
25.21.[10]	ariktaṃ sābharaṇaṃ, asambhave suvarṇakarṇikādiyuktam, atidaurgatye puṣpaphalādisahitam /
25.21.[11]	arikteneti tadvat /
25.21.[12]	evaṃ savyena savyamiti samastasya maṃtrāderatideśaḥ /
25.21.[13]	he kanye te tavāhaṃ hastaṃ gṛhṇāmi devasyāntarātmanaḥ savituḥ vaidikakarmāṇi cikīrṣoḥ prasave'nujñāyāṃ vartamānaḥ ādityasya vā savituḥ prasave'nujñāyāṃ vartamāno'śvinorbāhubhyāṃ natvātmīyābhyāṃ carmamayābhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ gṛhṇāmi // 17 //
25.22.[1]	gṛhṇāmi te suprajāstvāya hastau mayā patyā jaradaṣṭiryathāsaḥ bhago aryamā savitā puraṃdhirmahyaṃ tvādurgārhapatyāya devāḥ // 1// sūryāyā ārṣam /
25.22.[2]	māṃtravarṇikī devatā /
25.22.[3]	he patni ahaṃ te tava hastau gṛhṇāmi /
25.22.[4]	kimartham /
25.22.[5]	suprajāstvāya lokyaputrasiddhaye /
25.22.[6]	tvaṃ ca mayā patyā bhartrā satā jaradaṣṭiryathāsaḥ bhavasi, tathā bhūyāḥ jarājarjaritadehā bhūyāḥ asamaye bhavatyāḥ pramayo mā bhūdityarthaḥ /
25.22.[7]	amutra pakṣe jarayā daṣṭirupakṣayo yasyāḥ sā jaradaṣṭiḥ /
25.22.[8]	tvā tvāṃ bhagādayaścatvāro devā adurdattavantaḥ gārhapatyāya gārhapatyārtham //
25.22.[9]	tāṃ pūṣañśivatamāmerayasva yasyāṃ bījaṃ manuṣyā vapanti /
25.22.[10]	yā na ūrū uśatī viśrayāte yasyāmuśantaḥ praharāma śepam 2 he pūṣan āditya asyāḥ priyāyāstāṃ śivatamāṃ matiṃ ā īrayasva prerayasva tanuṃ vā /
25.22.[11]	yasyāṃ satyāmadhikaraṇabhūtāyāṃ bījaṃ reto manuṣyā vapanti kṣipanti /
25.22.[12]	yā no'smānuśatī kāmayamānā satī ūrū viśrayāte vividhaṃ kṛtvā śrayāte samarpayati vitatayati vātmīyāvūrū /
25.22.[13]	vayamapi yasyāmuśantaḥ kāmayamānāḥ santaḥ praharāma prakṣipāma śepaṃ prajananam, anyonyamāvayoḥ prītirastvityarthaḥ /
25.22.[14]	tathāhyayamupakāro bhavati ‘saṃprītiryatra dampatyostrivargastatra vardhate /’ somo'dadadgandharvāya gandharvo'dadadagnaye /
25.22.[15]	rayiṃ ca putrāṃścādādagnirmāmatho imām // 3 //
25.22.[16]	iyaṃ kanyā pūrvaṃ somasya saṃbandhinyāsīt /
25.22.[17]	sa somo bhuktvemāṃ gandharvāyādadat dadau, gandharvo'gnaye /
25.22.[18]	agnirmahyaṃ saṃprati dadātu /
25.22.[19]	na kevalamimāṃ yāvatā rayiṃ dhanaṃ putrāṃścāgnirmāṃ dadātu agnirimāṃ kanyāṃ mahyaṃ dattvā putradhanasamṛddhāṃ karotvityarthaḥ //
25.22.[20]	etamevārthaṃ caturthyarcā prapaṃcayati somaḥ prathamo vivide gandharvo vivida uttaraḥ /
25.22.[21]	tṛtīyo'gniṣṭe patisturīyo'haṃ manuṣyajaḥ // 4 //
25.22.[22]	he kanye tvāṃ somaḥ prathamo vivida patistava babhūva prathamaḥ /
25.22.[23]	tata uttaro dvitīyaḥ gaṃdharvo vivide /
25.22.[24]	tṛtīyo'gniste patistava patirbabhūva /
25.22.[25]	turīyaścaturtho'haṃ manuṣyajo mānuṣyaḥ saṃprati bhavāmi // 18 //
25.23-24.[1]	gīyanta iti gāthāḥ viśiṣṭā eva ṛcaḥ /
25.23-24.[2]	ata eva kāstā ityapekṣāyāṃ sarasvati predamavetyanuvāṃkamāha atrānuvāke yāḥ sthitāstā evetyarthaḥ /
25.23-24.[3]	dvyantarasvarayuktāsu ca kāsucidṛkṣu gāthāśabdo rūḍhaḥ /
25.23-24.[4]	yathoktaṃ ‘chandogā bahvṛcāścaiva tathā vājasaneyinaḥ /
25.23-24.[5]	uccanīcasvaraṃ prāhuḥ sa vai gāthika ucyate //’ iti /
25.23-24.[6]	ayaṃ samudāyārthaḥ tato'nantaraṃ sarasvatītyanuvākaparicchinnā gāthā gururvaraṃ vācayati bhāṇayati /
25.23-24.[7]	eke punarmanyante ubhāvapi kanyāvarau gāthā gururvācayati /
25.23-24.[8]	kiṃ sarvadā /
25.23-24.[9]	netyāha, yadi pṛthaktantramiti /
25.23-24.[10]	atrāyamabhiprāyaḥ vivāhodvāhau hi bhinne karmaṇī /
25.23-24.[11]	kanyāsaṃskāro vivāhaḥ /
25.23-24.[12]	varasaṃskāra udvāhaḥ /
25.23-24.[13]	tatra yadi deśakālakartraikyāttantreṇetikartavyatā, tadā sakṛdekaṃ varameva bhāṇayati gāthāḥ svādhyāyiko guruḥ, yadi tu deśakālaikye'pi kanyāvarayorevādhikṛtatvādṛtvijo dakṣiṇayā krītatvāt kartṛbhedāttaṃtrabhedastadobhāvapi vācayitavyau iti //
25.23-24.[14]	sarasvati predamava subhage vājinīvati /
25.23-24.[15]	yāṃ tvā viśvasya bhūtasya prāṇāyāmyasyāgrataḥ // 1 //
25.23-24.[16]	atrānuvāke brahmaṇa ārṣam /
25.23-24.[17]	anuṣṭup chandaḥ /
25.23-24.[18]	gandharvāpsarorājarṣiprabhṛtīnāṃ caritaṃ dvyantareṇa svareṇa yābhirgīyate, tā gāthā ityuktam /
25.23-24.[19]	iha ca sarvavāk sarasvatī, tadrūpeṇa ca vadhūrupacaryate /
25.23-24.[20]	manomeghaprabhṛtiśca gandharvaḥ /
25.23-24.[21]	tadrūpo varaḥ stutyarthamucyate sarasvatīti /
25.23-24.[22]	pretyupasargo'vetyākhyātena saṃbadhyate /
25.23-24.[23]	he sarasvati sā tvamidaṃ karma prāva ‘ava rakṣaṇe’ gopāya /
25.23-24.[24]	subhage sarvahitakāriṇi /
25.23-24.[25]	vājinīvati vājinyaḥ phalapākāntā oṣadhayastadvati /
25.23-24.[26]	stanayitnuvāgrūpā sarasvatī vṛṣṭyādidvāreṇa /
25.23-24.[27]	sā kā /
25.23-24.[28]	yāṃ tvāmahaṃ prāgāyāmi śabdayāmi staumi /
25.23-24.[29]	kīdṛśīm /
25.23-24.[30]	asya viśvasya sarvasya bhūtasyotpannasya sargādāvagre sthitāṃ śabdabrahmavivartatvāt sarvasya sarasvatyāśca śabdarūpatvāt //
25.23-24.[31]	yāgre sarvaṃ samabhavadyasyāṃ viśvamidaṃ jagat /
25.23-24.[32]	tāmadya vācaṃ gāsyāmi yā strīṇāmuttamaṃ manaḥ // 2 //
25.23-24.[33]	tāṃ cādya asminnahani sarasvatīṃ vācaṃ gāsyāmi śabdayiṣyāmi /
25.23-24.[34]	yā strīṇāmuttamaṃ manaḥ mānasaṃ prakāśanam, prakāśātmikā hi vāk, prakāśarūpaṃ ca hṛdayaṃ cetaḥ /
25.23-24.[35]	yāca agre prathamaṃ sargādau samabhavat sarvaṃ, vivartarūpā babhūva /
25.23-24.[36]	yasyāṃ cedaṃ vartamānaṃ viśvaṃ sarvaṃ jagadāśritam //
25.23-24.[37]	ya iha pūrve janā āsan pūrve pūrvatarebhyaḥ /
25.23-24.[38]	mūrdhanvāṃstebhyo gandharvaḥ purā devebhya ātapat // 3 //
25.23-24.[39]	ya iha pūrve janāḥ, ya iha jagati pūrve janā abhūvan, tatpūrvatarebhyo'pica pūrve, tebhyo'pi purā gandharvo mūrdhanvānnāmnāsīt /
25.23-24.[40]	kiṃ bahunā, devebhyo'pi yaḥ purā ātapat prakāśitavān brahmarūpa ityarthaḥ /
25.23-24.[41]	gāṃ sarasvatīṃ dhārayati vṛṇoti ca gaṃdharvaḥ /
25.23-24.[42]	sarasvatī vāgātmikeyamadhigīyamānā kanyā, prajāpatirūpo gandharvo vara iti prarocanārthaḥ // 3 //
25.23-24.[43]	ya eti sarvataḥ prāgbhyo diśo'dhipavamānaḥ /
25.23-24.[44]	mūrdhanvāṃstebhyo° // 4 //
25.23-24.[45]	yo vāyurūpaḥ san sarvata eti āgacchati adhipavamāna ādhikyena pavitrīkurvan /
25.23-24.[46]	ataśca prāgādibhyo digbhya āgacchantaḥ prācyādideśabhedena vyapadeśabhedabhinnā vāyavo bhavanti, tebhyo'pi devebhyo vāyubhyaḥ purā pūrvaṃ mūrdhanvāneva gandharvaḥ ātapat // 4 //
25.23-24.[47]	sa bhagavo na mariṣyasyahaṃ cedasmi bheṣajam /
25.23-24.[48]	mūrdhanvāṃstebhyo° // 5 //
25.23-24.[49]	yaḥ pūrvotpannaḥ san jīvātmanā saha prāṇākhyo vāyuḥ, he bhagavaḥ bhagavan jīva, sa tvaṃ maraṇadharmāpi na mariṣyasi yāvadahamasmi bhavāmi bheṣajaṃ tiṣṭhāmi indriyaiḥ saha /
25.23-24.[50]	tebhyo'pi devebhyo dyotanādidharmakebhyaḥ prāṇendriyebhyaḥ purā mūrdhanvān gandharva ātapat // 5 //
25.23-24.[51]	hiraṇyavarṇo vairampaḥ sa tvā manmanasaṃ karotu /
25.23-24.[52]	yadrājā yāti samitiṃ samudramiva saubhravaḥ // 6 //
25.23-24.[53]	sa prakṛto gandharvaḥ prajāpatiḥ he vadhu tvāṃ manmanasaṃ karotu iti vara āśāste madekacittāṃ pativratāṃ karotvityarthaḥ /
25.23-24.[54]	kīdṛśaḥ sa hiraṇyavarṇaḥ bhāsvaraprakāśaikarūpaḥ /
25.23-24.[55]	vairampo vīrasya yogino mohavaicitryamohanasamarthasya karma vairaṃ, tat pāti rakṣatīti vairampaḥ /
25.23-24.[56]	yat yaḥ saubhravaḥ śobhanabhrūmadhyasaṃyamātpratīto yogināṃ, rājā rājamānaḥ, samitiṃ saṃgrāmamiva samudramimaṃ saṃsāraduḥkhabhāraṃ yāti tārayatītyarthaḥ /
25.23-24.[57]	yaḥ eti sarvataḥ prāgbhyo diśa iti paṃcamyāḥ sthāne vyatyayena prathamā /
25.23-24.[58]	kecitprāgbhyo viśa iti paṭhanti, tatra cchāndaso varṇavyatyayaḥ /
25.23-24.[59]	purāṇataracchāndasāstu paṭhanti prāgvādibhyo'dhipavamāna iti, arthaṃ ca vyācakṣate prāk prathamaṃ vāti vāyate vā gacchati prāgvā, sarvābhyaḥ sarvato digbhyaḥ pavamāna etīti //
25.23-24.[60]	vicchinnasaṃpradāyeṣu śatādhyayanavartiṣu /
25.23-24.[61]	mantreṣvapauruṣeyeṣu yathecchaṃ parikalpanāt //
25.23-24.[62]	pāṭhānāṃ gatyabhāvena yathādṛṣṭi pradarśanam /
25.23-24.[63]	kriyamāṇaṃ satāmagryairnopālabhyaṃ kathaṃcana //
25.23-24.[64]	na vātasyābhi vāyate nodvātasyābhi dhīyate /
25.23-24.[65]	na vātasyā dhuraṃ vahato nodvātasyāpamīyate // 7 //
25.23-24.[66]	vātasyābhi agre na anyena kenāpi devena vāyate gamyate /
25.23-24.[67]	nodvātasyābhi dhīyate naca vātayābhimukhena kenāpi dhīyate āgantuṃ manyate /
25.23-24.[68]	vātasya dhuraṃ vahataḥ pṛthivyādikaṃ dhārayato vimānādikaṃ ca prerayato nānyena kenāpyapamīyate saha gamyate māhātmyamācaryate /
25.23-24.[69]	uditi nipātaḥ sahārthe /
25.23-24.[70]	punaḥpunarvātaśabdodīraṇamatiśayārthamaho ramaṇīyā aho ramaṇīyetyādivat /
25.23-24.[71]	kecittu paṭhanti nedvātasyāddha dhīyate na it vātasya āt ha dhīyate, ukāro varṇāgamaḥ, haśabda itihāse, anyenādhīyate sahāyenāgamyate // 7 //
25.23-24.[72]	ā satyaharito rathaḥ saubhravaḥ suhiraṇyayaḥ /
25.23-24.[73]	taṃ vāta iddhrajīyatyudvāto dṛḍhayā dhurā // 8 //
25.23-24.[74]	ā ityupasargo dhrajīyatītyanenākhyātena saṃbadhyate /
25.23-24.[75]	satyaḥ satyapradhāno harito haritavarṇaḥ ādityarathaḥ, athavā satyapradhānāśca te harayo'śvāste vidyante yasya sa satyaharita iti matvarthīyastakāraḥ /
25.23-24.[76]	saubhravaḥ bhrūsaṃyamena tīkṣṇadṛṣṭibhirapi draṣṭumaśakyaḥ /
25.23-24.[77]	hiraṇyayaḥ hiraṇmayastaijasaḥ /
25.23-24.[78]	tamudvāta ūrdhvagatirvāta ādhrajīyati ādhrajayati gamayatīti vivartasya prajāpatirūpasya vāyormāhātmyavarṇanam /
25.23-24.[79]	kayā ādhrajīyati udvātaḥ /
25.23-24.[80]	dṛḍhayā dhurā ūrdhva utkṛṣṭo vāta evaṃ dṛḍhā dhūstayā // 8 //
25.23-24.[81]	tavaiva rājandundubhayastava dundubhirānakaḥ /
25.23-24.[82]	tava vātodvātā aśvau tava caitrarathaṃ vanam // 9 //
25.23-24.[83]	mūrdhanvān gandharva ucyate /
25.23-24.[84]	he mūrdhanvan rājan tavaiva dundubhayo jayodghoṣaṇā vādyaviśeṣāḥ utkṛṣṭā vā śabdādayaḥ prakāśanaparāḥ, tathā ānakaḥ paṭahākhyo'pi dundubhiviśeṣaḥ, tavaiva vātastiryaggatiḥ pavanaḥ, udvātaḥ ūrdhvagatirvāto'dhaḥpatanādvā, tathā aśvau /
25.23-24.[85]	athavā dehagataḥ prāṇo vāyurudvātaḥ, apāno vātastau vātodvātau prāṇāpānau śarīrasya rathasya aśvāviva sarvaprāṇinām /
25.23-24.[86]	caitrarathākhyaṃ vanaṃ devodyānaṃ tavaiva, sarvavibhavāstvatsvāmikā ityarthaḥ // 9 //
25.23-24.[87]	te śukraṃ śakrasyāvindanparāñcaṃ nihitaṅguhā /
25.23-24.[88]	mūrdhanvāṃstebhyo gandharvaḥ purā jatrubhya ātṛdaḥ // 10 //
25.23-24.[89]	te devā vāyvādayaḥ śakrasya śaktasya sarvakāraṇasya prajāpateḥ śukraṃ sāramavindan jñātavantaḥ /
25.23-24.[90]	parāñcaṃ parokṣaṃ guhāyāṃ hṛdaye viduṣāṃ nihitaṃ, avidyābhedaprapañco vā guhā /
25.23-24.[91]	yadvā śakrasyendrasya śukraṃ prajananamudakalakṣaṇaṃ guhāyāṃ raśmisaṃghāte nihitaṃ parokṣaṃ jñātavantaḥ te devāḥ /
25.23-24.[92]	tebhyo devebhyaḥ purā pūrvaṃ mūrdhanvān gandharvo'vindat /
25.23-24.[93]	kimavadhi jñātavān /
25.23-24.[94]	jatrubhya ātṛdaḥ ājatrubhya ātṛdaḥ jatrūṇi saṃśleṣaṇāni sarvādhikaraṇāni ‘sṛpitṛdoḥ kasun’ tṛdaḥ tardanaṃ vināśaḥ āsṛṣṭerāpralayāt yadutpādanapālanapralayasaṃpādanasāmarthyaṃ, tanmūrdhanvānavindat sakalamicchātaḥ // 10 //
25.23-24.[95]	hiraṇyavarṇaṃ subhṛtaṃ śobhamānaṃ kanyāyā hastaṃ parigṛhya puṇyam /
25.23-24.[96]	sā putrakāmā subhagāya bhartre bhava vaśīyāngirivatsthirāya // 11 //
25.23-24.[97]	eṣa kaśmīreṣveva saṃprati paṭhyate /
25.23-24.[98]	vara āśāste kanyāyā hastaṃ gṛhītvā ahaṃ vaśīyānbhava bhūyāsam /
25.23-24.[99]	bhaveti vyatyayena madhyamapuruṣaḥ /
25.23-24.[100]	athavā antarātmābhidhīyate kanyāyā hastaṃ gṛhītvā he antarātman vaśīyānbhava girivatsthirāya parvatavat sthairyāya /
25.23-24.[101]	he vadhu tvamapi yā mayohyase sā bhartre bhartrarthaṃ putrakāmā bhava /
25.23-24.[102]	kāmanaṃ kāmaḥ putrārtha eva kāmo ratiryasyāḥ sā putrakāmā /
25.23-24.[103]	kimartham /
25.23-24.[104]	subhagāya saubhāgyāya, putravatī hi satī loke ślāghyā bhavati, natu ratyekaphalā /
25.23-24.[105]	bhartṛviśeṣaṇaṃ vā subhagāyeti /
25.23-24.[106]	hastaṃ viśinaṣṭi hiraṇyavarṇaṃ suvarṇakāntiṃ, subhṛtaṃ kaṅkaṇādyābharaṇaiḥ supūrṇamata eva śobhamānaṃ, maṃtravatparigrahātpuṇyaṃ pavitram // 11 //
25.23-24.[107]	vairampe muniparvate girau haritasaṃkāśe /
25.23-24.[108]	saṃkalparamaṇe'marāvubhau sumanasau carāvaḥ // 12 //
25.23-24.[109]	vara āha he vadhu vairampākhye munijanasevite haritasaṃkāśe suvarṇamaye merāviti yāvat, saṃkalpamātreṇa sarvābhilaṣitasatphalaprāptiryatra tatra saṃkalparamaṇe, amarāvamaraṇadharmakau devau bhūtvā ubhāvapi sumanasau prasannacittau carāvaḥ saṃcariṣyāvaḥ puruṣāyuṣe pūrṇe // 12 //
25.23-24.[110]	āṇī va rathaveṣṭasi vane vārivarṣaṇṇye /
25.23-24.[111]	apsarāḥ sūryavarcasinī vaśinī manmanā bhūyāḥ // 13 //
25.23-24.[112]	āṇī rathakāṣṭhikā, he vadhu tvamāṇī va rathaveṣṭasi rathavyāpinī yathā rathāvyabhicāriṇī, tathā mayi bhūyāḥ pavitrā /
25.23-24.[113]	vaśabda upamāyām /
25.23-24.[114]	tathā bane vārivarṣaṇṇye viyuddhatā yathā avyabhicāriṇī meghaṃ vanaṃ vinā na dṛśyate, tathā tvaṃ mayi bhūyāḥ /
25.23-24.[115]	vāri varṣat patat nayatyanumāpayatīti vārivarṣaṇṇyā taḍit /
25.23-24.[116]	apsarāśca setyāhuḥ /
25.23-24.[117]	tathā sūryavarcasinī tejasvinī bhūyāḥ vaśinī ca īśānā manmanāśca mayi dattacittā pativratā bhūyā ityarthaḥ // 13 //
25.23-24.[118]	yāsā upari tiṣṭhati vane vārivarṣaṇṇye /
25.23-24.[119]	vasugā sūryavarcasinī vaśinī manmanā bhūyāḥ // 14 //
25.23-24.[120]	athavā yāsau taḍidrūpadhāriṇī apsarā upari tiṣṭhati, saiveha tvaṃ rūpāntareṇāvatīrṇā ahaṃ ca megho vārivarṣaṇṇyaḥ /
25.23-24.[121]	ataśca tvaṃ mayi dattacittā bhūyā iti samānaṃ pūrveṇa /
25.23-24.[122]	vasugā dhanavatīti viśeṣaḥ // 14 //
25.23-24.[123]	aśvatthaka upari śyeno ramaṇīyataro nāma /
25.23-24.[124]	tasminha rambhā ramate śakra iva paritakmyāyām // 15 //
25.23-24.[125]	praśasto vaṭavṛkṣo'śvatthakastatropari śyenaḥ śaṃsanīyo ramaṇīyataro nāma gandharva āste /
25.23-24.[126]	tasminnapsarā rambhā nāma ramate krīḍate /
25.23-24.[127]	śakra ādityaḥ, sa yathā paritakmyāyāṃ rātrau viśrāmyati // 15 //
25.23-24.[128]	āsyandamānā subhage nirgiribhyaḥ sarasvati /
25.23-24.[129]	māteva duhitṛbhyaḥ kulyābhyo vibhajā vasu // 16 //
25.23-24.[130]	sarasvatīṃ nadīṃ vācaṃ vā madhyamāmabhyarthayate /
25.23-24.[131]	he sarasvati subhage nirgatā giribhyaḥ, syandamānā sravantī, kulyābhyo'nyanadībhyaḥ vasu jalamābhaja vibhaja māteva duhitṛbhyaḥ /
25.23-24.[132]	yathā mātā duhitṛbhyo dhanaṃ paitṛkaṃ vibhajate, tadvat /
25.23-24.[133]	madhyamavākpakṣe girayo dehāḥ, kulyā galabilāni //
25.23-24.[134]	idānīṃ ‘vāgvā anuṣṭup vāksarasvatī’ iti śrutyānuṣṭubhaḥ sarasvatīrūpatvapratipādanādanuṣṭupchandorūpeṇa stotumāha /
25.23-24.[135]	madhyaṃ tacchandasa āhuryatrādadhurnāma pareti devāḥ /
25.23-24.[136]	aruṇapiśaṅgo'śvo'sya dakṣiṇā yastadveda sa ihāgantumarhati // 17 //
25.23-24.[137]	chandasa iti vyatyayenaikavacanam /
25.23-24.[138]	chandasāṃ devānāmasurāṇāṃ ca tadanuṣṭup chando madhyaṃ madhyavarti devā ṛtvija āhurvadanti /
25.23-24.[139]	yatra cchandasi pareti parāgacchati devāsuracchandasāṃ madhyamanusarati anuṣṭubityanarthakaṃ nāma devā ādadhuḥ vihitavantaḥ /
25.23-24.[140]	atrāntarā madhye'nuṣṭup vyavasthitā /
25.23-24.[141]	tāni ṣoḍaśini grahe viniyuktāni /
25.23-24.[142]	tatra ca ṣoḍaśini grahe aruṇapiśaṅgo'śvo'sya dakṣiṇā matā /
25.23-24.[143]	sā cetaracchandomadhye vyavasthitasya rājaprakhyasyāsyaiva cchandaso'nuṣṭublakṣaṇasya bhavatīti sambhāvyate /
25.23-24.[144]	ata evaṃbhūtaṃ tadanuṣṭupchando yo veda vetti, sa iha pāṇigrahaṇasthāne āgantumarhati ṛtvigjanyaprabhṛtiḥ, nātadvit /
25.23-24.[145]	devāsuracchandasāṃ tu madhyavartitvamanuṣṭubha itthaṃ ‘gāyatryuṣṇiganuṣṭubho bṛhatīpaṃktitriṣṭubhaḥ /
25.23-24.[146]	jagatī ceti vijñeyāśchandasāṃ sapta jātayaḥ //’ tatraikaikākṣaravṛddhyā daivānyekākṣarādīni saptākṣarāntāni sapta cchandāṃsi bhavanti /
25.23-24.[147]	daivī ekākṣarā gāyatrī /
25.23-24.[148]	dvyakṣarā uṣṇik /
25.23-24.[149]	tryakṣarānuṣṭup /
25.23-24.[150]	evamādikrameṇa daivī jagatī saptākṣarā, āsurī tu paṃcadaśākṣarā /
25.23-24.[151]	ekaikākṣarahānyā ca prātilomyenānyānyāsurāṇi cchandāṃsi bhavanti /
25.23-24.[152]	tatra navākṣarā gāyatrī bhavati /
25.23-24.[153]	evaṃ caikākṣarādārabhya saptamākṣaraparyantānyānulomyena daivāni cchandāṃsi sthitāni /
25.23-24.[154]	paṃcadaśākṣarādārabhya prātilomyena navamamakṣaraṃ yāvadāsurāṇi /
25.23-24.[155]	aṣṭamaṃ tvakṣaraṃ vargadvayasya madhye bhavati /
25.23-24.[156]	teneyamaṣṭākṣarā anuṣṭup madhye bhavatītyalamativaitatyena // 17 //
25.23-24.[157]	iṣīkavarṇe lekhabhrūḥ subhage susmite /
25.23-24.[158]	mūrdhanvāṃstvā gandharvo māmabhiniyacchatu // 18 //
25.23-24.[159]	iṣīkaṃ śarakāṇḍaṃ suvarṇamityeke /
25.23-24.[160]	he suvarṇavarṇe śarakāṇḍagaurākāre vā, he lekhabhrūḥ aṃjanalekhāvadbhruvau yasyāḥ, sā sambodhyate, he subhage priyadarśane, susmite cāruhāsini, tvāṃ mūrdhanvāngandharvo māmabhi māṃ prati niyacchatu niyatāṃ madekādhīnāṃ karotu /
25.23-24.[161]	sa hi kanyāsvāmītyuktam // 18 //
25.23-24.[162]	ubhaye tvā devagandharvāḥ sadhryañco vihvayāmahe /
25.23-24.[163]	teṣāṃ yatarānkāmayase tānabhyehi sarasvati // 19 //
25.23-24.[164]	somakrayiṇī vāk sarasvatītyucyate /
25.23-24.[165]	he sarasvati devā gandharvāścobhaye sadhryañcaḥ sahāñcamānāḥ saha bhūtvā tvāṃ vihvayāmahe tava vividhamāhvānaṃ kurmaḥ /
25.23-24.[166]	teṣāmubhayeṣāṃ madhye yatarān kāmayase devān gandharvānvā, tānabhyehi ābhimukhyena gaccha // 19 //
25.23-24.[167]	abhyāvarte'haṃ devāngāyataḥ kāmayāmahe /
25.23-24.[168]	gāyantaṃ striyaḥ kāmayante na tathā brahmavādinam // 20 //
25.23-24.[169]	sarasvatyāha gāyato devānevāhamabhyāvarte ābhimukhyena varte, natu vedaṃ paṭhataḥ surān /
25.23-24.[170]	yato'haṃ gāyata eva kāmayāmahe kāmaye iti vacanavyatyayaḥ /
25.23-24.[171]	tathāhi gāyantameva hi striyaḥ kāmayante, natu brahmavādinaṃ vedānāṃ pāṭhakam //20// yā sā upari parvata ātmanā ramamāṇeva /
25.23-24.[172]	kṣaumamṛdvī ha vā asi tvota ojasi śṛṇomi // 21 //
25.23-24.[173]	yā upari parvate girau meghe vā vidyudrūpeṇa madhyamavāgrūpeṇa vā ātmanā svena rūpeṇa ramamāṇeva krīḍantīva tiṣṭhati sarasvatī, sā he vadhu asi bhavasi tvaṃ, nāsti naḥ saṃśayaḥ /
25.23-24.[174]	kīdṛśī /
25.23-24.[175]	kṣaumamṛdvī dukūlavatkomalā jalavṛṣṭidānenārthābhidhānena vā /
25.23-24.[176]	ha vai iti nipātau pādapūraṇau /
25.23-24.[177]	evaṃ ca sati vadhūṃ vadati varaḥ yatastvaṃ sarasvatī, tena tvayā ūto rakṣitaḥ sannahamojasi sati śṛṇomi ākarṇayāmi sakalaṃ kartavyaṃ śrutismṛtivihitaṃ kartavyatayā vyavasyāmi sahadharmacāriṇyāstava lābhabalenetyarthaḥ /
25.23-24.[178]	kecittu śṛṇotviti paṭhanti /
25.23-24.[179]	tatrāpyayaṃ madātmā śṛṇotvityarthaḥ // 21 //
25.23-24.[180]	iti sārasvatānuvākavivṛtiḥ //
25.23-24.[181]	tato gāthā vācayati sarasvati predamavetyanuvākamubhāvityeke yadi pṛthaktantramiti vivṛtamiyatā /
25.23-24.[182]	yadi pṛthaktantramityuttarasūtreṇāpi saṃbadhyate // 19 //
25.23-24.[183]	pṛthaktaṃtrapakṣe'gnipradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā vadhūvarāvānīya punastatraivopaveśya yatra pāṇigrahaṇaṃ vṛttaṃ, saṃsthāpayet samāpayedṛtutithyādikaṃ bhaviṣyattantramudvāhasaṃbandhitayā, tato vivāhasaṃbandhitayā bhūya udvāhanatatraṃ sakalaṃ pūrvaṃ pradarśitaṃ vivāhasaṃbandhitayopakramya vakṣyamāṇaṃ kuryādityarthaḥ // 20 //
25.25.[1]	karmaśabdaḥ prayogavacanaḥ /
25.25.[2]	tantramitikartavyatā vidhyantā /
25.25.[3]	sakṛdanuṣṭhīyamānetikartavyatopakārapakṣe uttareṇāgniṃ pratyetya pradakṣiṇamakṛtvaiva uttarabhāgenaiva katipayakramān gatvā pratyāgatya tato vivāhaḥ vivāhāṅgatayā vakṣyamāṇānāmṛtutithyādīnāṃ prayogaḥ /
25.25.[4]	tatreṇa codvāhopakāroktānāṃ vakṣyamāṇānāṃ ca āvṛttyānuṣṭhānamityarthaḥ /
25.25.[5]	ekakarmaṇi tantre vivāhodvāhalakṣaṇa ityapi kecitpadayojanāṃ kurvanti // 21 //
25.25.[6]	eta eva tatrāvṛttī spaṣṭārthamekenaiva sūtreṇa vivarītumāha
25.26.[1]	udvāhe homā ye jayaprabhṛtayaḥ, ya ime dyāvāpṛthivītyādayaśca tathā sviṣṭakṛt, tathā ājyabhāgau /
25.26.[2]	ete sarve na ekakarmaṇi tantre āvṛttyā kartavyā ityarthājjñāyate /
25.26.[3]	tena śrutyarthānāṃ vidhiniṣedhalakṣaṇamarthadvayaṃ yathāsaṃbhavamanena nidarśitam /
25.26.[4]	sviṣṭakṛcchabda uparitanasya tantrakhaṇḍasyopalakṣaṇārthaḥ, ājyabhāgaśabdo'pyadhastanasya // 22 //
25.27.[1]	ekakarmaṇi tatre uttareṇāgniṃ pratyetya pratyānīyāgneḥ paścāddarbheṣu vinihitacaraṇau vadhūvarau kṛtvā ‘sā tvamasi’ iti varaṃ gururvācayati //
25.27.[2]	sā nāma ṛgāsīt amo nāma sāma, sā ca amaśca sāmaṃ ṛk ca gītiścetyarthaḥ /
25.27.[3]	evaṃ sāmaśabdasya vyutpattiḥ /
25.27.[4]	ṛksāmarūpāvāvāmiti vibhajya varaḥ pradarśayati he vadhu tvaṃ sā ṛgasi bhavasi, amo'hamasmi ahamamaḥ sāma bhavāmi /
25.27.[5]	sā tvaṃ sā tvaṃ bhavasi, amo'hamamo'haṃ bhavāmīti dviruktyā ṛksāmarūpatvaṃ draḍhayati /
25.27.[6]	tā ehi vivahāvahai tau dvāvāvāṃ he vadhu ehyāgaccha vivahāvahai vivāhaṃ kurvaḥ /
25.27.[7]	kimartham /
25.27.[8]	puṃse putrāya kartave, kartave iti tumarthe bhāve tavenpratyayaḥ, puṃse putrāyeti subvyatyayaḥ, pumāṃsaṃ putraṃ kartum /
25.27.[9]	tathā rāyo dhanasya poṣāya puṣṭaye, suprajāstvāya śobhanaprajālābhāya, suvīryāya suvīryaṃ karmasvojasvitā tadartham // 23 //
25.28.[1]	agnimabhidakṣiṇaṃ vadhūvarāvānīya, agneruttarabhāge'śmānaṃ sthāpayitvā dakṣiṇena caraṇena āsthāpayati guruḥ prayojakaḥ, vadhūvarāvātiṣṭhata ākrāmataḥ /
25.28.[2]	yathāmantraliṅgamādyena varo'śmānamākrāmati, uttareṇa vadhūḥ /
25.28.[3]	gurustvāśāste tayormantreṇeṣṭam he vara aśmānamātiṣṭha aśmavat sthiro bhava, kiṃca te tava viśvedevāḥ śaradaḥ śatamāyuḥ kṛṇvantu kurvantu, he vadhu imamaśmānamātiṣṭha tvaṃ cāśmavat sthirā bhava, tathā duvasyavaḥ duvasyūn upatāpamicchataḥ śatrūn pramṛṇīhi jahi, tathā pṛtanyataḥ pṛtanāṃ senāmicchato yuyutsamānān sahasva prasahasva abhibhava /
25.28.[4]	dakṣiṇena padetyuttaramantre'pyanuṣajyate // 24 //
25.29.[1]	ājyenāñjalāvupastṛṇāti caturavadānena /
25.29.[2]	tata idaṃ havirityādinā matreṇa śūrpasthān śamīparṇamiśrāṃllājānabhimṛśati varaḥ /
25.29.[3]	anantaramañjalāvasyā vadhvā bhrātā, brahmacārī vā bhrāturasannidhāne śamīparṇamiśrāṃllājānāvapati //
25.29.[4]	idaṃ haviḥ prajananaṃ me astu daśavīraṃ sarvagaṇaṃ svastaye /
25.29.[5]	ātmasani prajāsani paśusanyabhayasani lokasani /
25.29.[6]	agniḥ prajāṃ bahulāṃ me karotu annaṃ payo reto asmāsu dhatta //
25.29.[7]	kokilasya rājaputrasyārṣam /
25.29.[8]	anuṣṭup chaṃdaḥ /
25.29.[9]	idaṃ lājākhyaṃ haviḥ me mama prajananaṃ daśaputrasaṃpādanaṃ bhavatu, tathā sarvagaṇaṃ sarveṣāṃ gaṇaiḥ putraprabhṛtīnāṃ paśūnāṃ gaṇairyuktaṃ svastaye'vināśāya cāstu /
25.29.[10]	ātmasani ātmānaṃ śarīramātmīyatvātsanati ‘ṣaṇu dāne’ ityasmāddhātoḥ dadāti prajñāpayatītyātmasani /
25.29.[11]	evaṃ prajāsani paśusanyabhayasani lokasani /
25.29.[12]	sarvatreha haviranyapadārthaḥ /
25.29.[13]	agnirmama putrapautrādikāṃ bhūyasīṃ prajāṃ karotu /
25.29.[14]	annādikaṃ cāsmākaṃ dhatta sthiraṃ kuruta /
25.29.[15]	bahuvacanādaryamagandharvatryambakā ijyamānā evaṃ prārthyante'parārdhe // 25 //
25.30.[1]	tān lājān avicchindatī vicchedamakurvatī ekenaiva prakṣepeṇa juhotyaryamaṇaṃ nu devamityādimantreṇa //
25.30.[2]	aryamaṇaṃ nu devaṃ kanyā agnimayakṣata /
25.30.[3]	so'smāndevo aryamā preto muñcātu māmuṣya gṛhebhyaḥ svāhā //
25.30.[4]	brahmaṇa ārṣam /
25.30.[5]	aryamagandharvatryambakā devatāḥ /
25.30.[6]	upariṣṭādbṛhatyo homamaṃtrāḥ /
25.30.[7]	iyaṃ nārītyanuṣṭup kanyā agniṃ devamayakṣata iṣṭavatyaḥ /
25.30.[8]	aryamaṇamityagnerviśeṣaṇam /
25.30.[9]	arīn yacchatītyaryamāgniḥ, tam /
25.30.[10]	ayakṣateti tiṅvyatyayaḥ yajante /
25.30.[11]	anye tvagnimityapi dvitīyāṃ saptamyāḥ sthāne varṇayanti anāvaryamaṇaṃ kanyā yajante /
25.30.[12]	atra pakṣe'ryamaiva devatā /
25.30.[13]	evamanūcya vadhūryajñaphalamāśaṃsati /
25.30.[14]	amuṣyeti sāmānyena bhartṛnāma lakṣyate /
25.30.[15]	so'ryamā iṣṭaḥ san amuṣya devadattasya ito gṛhebhyo'smānmā pramuñcātu, mā iti niṣedhārtho nipātaḥ, ito bhartṛgṛhebhyo'smākaṃ cyāvaṃ mā kārṣīdityarthaḥ /
25.30.[16]	svāhā sudrutamastu //
25.31.[1]	varaṃ bhāṇayati gururagnirityādimantramityarthaḥ //
25.31.[2]	agnirmā janimānanayā janimantaṃ karotu /
25.31.[3]	jīvapatnirbhūyāsam //
25.31.[4]	janī jāyā /
25.31.[5]	agniryato jāyāvānato māmapi jāyayā avicchinnasaṃbandhaṃ karotu /
25.31.[6]	tatprasādādahamapi jīvapatniyāsaṃ jīvā patnī yasya sa jīvapatnirahaṃ syām // 27 //
25.32.[1]	iyaṃ nārītyasya anuṣṭubhaḥ triṣvapyanuṣaṅgaḥ kartavyaḥ //
25.32.[2]	iyaṃ nāryupabrūte tokmānyāvapantikā /
25.32.[3]	dīrghāyurastu me patiredhantāṃ jñātayo mama //
25.32.[4]	eṣā nārī bravīti /
25.32.[5]	kim /
25.32.[6]	dīryāyurastu me patirjñātayaśca mitrādayo mama vardhantāmiti /
25.32.[7]	kiṃ kurvatī bravīti /
25.32.[8]	tokmānyāvapantī lājān juhvatītyarthaḥ // 28 //
25.33.[1]	dvau vārau dviḥ /
25.33.[2]	evamuttaraṃ karma dvau vārau kartavyam // 29 //
25.33.[3]	tadeva sphuṭaṃ darśayitumāha
25.34-35.[1]	paryayaṇamagniparigamanaṃ yajamānānuṣañjanam /
25.34-35.[2]	tatra ca varaḥ kartā arthāt /
25.34-35.[3]	tato'śmanaḥ sthāpanam /
25.34-35.[4]	tatra paristīrya lājānāmāvapanaṃ gandharvaṃ pativedanamiti //
25.34-35.[5]	gandharvaṃ pativedanaṃ kanyā agnimayakṣata /
25.34-35.[6]	so'smāndevo gandharvaḥ preto muñcātu māmuṣya gṛhebhyaḥ svāhā //
25.34-35.[7]	gāṃ pṛthvīṃ dhārayatīti gandharvastamagniṃ pativedanaṃ patyurlambhayitāraṃ kanyā anyā yato'yakṣata iṣṭavatyaḥ, ato'hamapi yaje iti nārī brūte ityarthaḥ /
25.34-35.[8]	saca devo'gniriṣṭaḥ san gandharvo'muṣya bharturgṛhebhyo'smān mā pramuñcātu iti pūrvavatpratiṣedhaḥ // 30 //
25.36.[1]	soma ityādimatraṃ gururvācayatītyarthaḥ //
25.36.[2]	somo mā jñātimānanayā jñāntimantaṃ karotu /
25.36.[3]	jīvapatnirbhūyāsam //
25.36.[4]	yataḥ somo jñātimānato māmapyanayā nāryā jñāntimantaṃ karotu /
25.36.[5]	jīvapatnirbhūyāsamiti vyākhyātam // 31 //
25.37.[1]	tryambakamityādinā tṛtīyo homaḥ //
25.37.[2]	tryambakaṃ yajāmahe sugandhiṃ patipoṣaṇam /
25.37.[3]	urvārukamiva bandhanānmṛtyormukṣīya māmuṣya gṛhebhyaḥ svāhā //
25.37.[4]	tryambakaṃ śaṃkaraṃ yajāmahe havirdānena pūjayāmaḥ /
25.37.[5]	sugandhiṃ suyaśasaṃ, gandhaśabdo yaśo'bhidhāyī prasiddhaḥ /
25.37.[6]	patipoṣaṇaṃ bhartuḥ poṣayitāram /
25.37.[7]	ahaṃ ca tryambakasya pūjitasya prasādāt mṛtyoḥ sakāśāt mukṣīya /
25.37.[8]	kutaḥ kiṃvat /
25.37.[9]	urvārukamiva bandhanāt urvārukaṃ karkarīphalaṃ, tadyathā bandhanādvṛntātpakvaṃ sarasvata eva vimucyate vā arthibhistroṭyate, tadvadahaṃ mṛtyoḥ sakāśānnityaviśliṣṭā syāmityarthaḥ /
25.37.[10]	amuṣya bharturgṛhebhyaḥ punarmā kadācana mukṣīyeti niṣedhaḥ //
25.40.[1]	... ityarthaḥ /
25.40.[2]	ihāpi parikrītenartvijā arthyamānasya yajamānārthatayā yajamānasyāśīrbhavati /
25.40.[3]	raśanāraśmiśabdau ca yoktraparyāyau, paryāyaprayogo'tiśayārthaḥ /
25.40.[4]	athavā yoktrāṇi vimuñcāmi na kevalaṃ yoktrāṇyeva raśanāṃ ca avidyāmityarthaḥ, vi raśmīn raśmīṃścā vidyāmūlānrāgādīnityarthaḥ /
25.40.[5]	dampatyośca yoktravimokena vivāhabhūmau sthito'gnirmukto bhavati svātatryasaṃcaraṇena tasya saṃkaṭaparihārāt /
25.40.[6]	ato vimuktaḥ pūrvavadabhyarthyate //
25.41.[1]	agneruttareṇāstīrṇeṣu darbheṣu prāṅmukhīṃ vadhūṃ prakrāmayati kartā saptapadāni saptabhirmaṃtraiḥ /
25.41.[2]	viṣṇustvānvetviti sarvatrānuṣaṅgaḥ /
25.41.[3]	ekamiṣe viṣṇustvānvetu ekaṃ padamiṣe'nnāya nidhehi, tvāṃ ca gacchantīṃ viṣṇuranvetu /
25.41.[4]	dve ūrje viṣṇustvānvetu dve pade ūrje balāya nidhehīti pūrvavat /
25.41.[5]	trīṇi rāyaspoṣāya viṣṇustvānvetu trīṇi padāni rāyo dhanasya puṣṭaye nidhehi /
25.41.[6]	catvāri mayobhavāya viṣṇusvānvetu mayaḥ sukhaṃ tadbhavatyasmāditi mayobhūstasyedaṃ mayobhavaṃ, tadarthaṃ catvāri padāni nidhehi sukhabhavanaprārthanāyetyarthaḥ /
25.41.[7]	paṃca prajābhyo viṣṇustvānvetu putrapautraprajārthaṃ paṃca padāni nidhehi /
25.41.[8]	ṣaḍṛtubhyo viṣṇustvānvetu ṣaṭ padāni ṛtusāṃmukhyāya nidhehi, te ca ṛtavaḥ saṃmukhībhūtāḥ phalaiḥ saṃbadhnantu tvāmityarthaḥ /
25.41.[9]	dīrghāyutvāya saptamaṃ sakhā saptapadā bhava /
25.41.[10]	sumṛḍīkā sarasvati mā te vyoma sandṛśi //
25.41.[11]	viṣṇustvānvetu dīrghāyutvāyāyuṣe saptamaṃ padaṃ nidhehi /
25.41.[12]	ebhiśca saptabhiḥ padbhirbhartuḥ sukhāya bhava /
25.41.[13]	sumṛḍīkā ‘mṛḍa sukhane’ susukhā /
25.41.[14]	he sarasvati mā te tava vyoma ākāśasthaḥ kaścitsaptamaṃ padaṃ drākṣīt pavanāndolitavāsaso nagnaṃ vā kaṃcitpradeśam // 37 //
25.42.[1]	taccakṣurityādinā kartā kanyāmādityamupasthāpayati //
25.42.[2]	taccakṣurdevahitaṃ purastācchukramuccarat /
25.42.[3]	paśyema śaradaḥ śataṃ jīvema śaradaḥ śatam //
25.42.[4]	devahitaṃ devavihitaṃ, devebhyo vā hitaṃ hitakāri /
25.42.[5]	śukraṃ śuklam/ uccarat ūrdhvaṃ carat gacchat udyat // 38 //
25.43.[1]	vivāhe kriyamāṇe yadi rātrirbhavati rātrau vā vivāhaḥ, tadā taccakṣurityanayāgnimupasthāpayet // 39 //
25.44.[1]	jīvantīṃ kanyāmicchan dhruvādikaṃ darśayet /
25.44.[2]	atra kecidrātrāvityanuvartayanti divā dhruvādidarśanābhāvāt, apare nānuvartayanti yato'gre paśyasīti praśne apaśyantī api paśyāmīti prativacanamāhetyartho lakṣyate /
25.44.[3]	darśanamātraviva kṣayā hi paśyeḥ praiṣaḥ paśyāmi navetyatra cottaraṃ paśyema // 40 //
25.44.[4]	paśyasītyekaikasya nāma gṛhītvā pṛcchedguruḥ //
25.44.[5]	sāpi pṛṣṭā satī paśyāmīti pratibrūyāt //
25.45.[1]	vīkṣitān dhruvādīn gururanumantrayate /
25.45.[2]	sumaṃgalīrityādyānuṣṭup /
25.45.[3]	iyaṃ vadhūḥ śobhanamaṃgalayuktā bhavatu bhavatprasādāt /
25.45.[4]	imāṃ sametya saṃbhūya paśyata /
25.45.[5]	asyai ca saubhāgyaṃ dattvā paścādastaṃ gacchata /
25.45.[6]	dattvāyeti ktvo yak /
25.45.[7]	tena divāpi jñeyametat /
25.45.[8]	dhruvādidarśanaṃ hi jīvanadyotanamāhuḥ /
25.45.[9]	tadihāvasare'paśyantyā api paśyāmīti prativacanamapamṛtyuvyāghātāya smaryate /
25.45.[10]	ata eva dhruvādikaṃ yaddarśayet, tatsvastyavināśameva darśayedityarthaḥ // 43 //
25.46.[1]	uduttamamityādinā anuṣṭupcatuṣṭayenāvasathaṃ gṛhaṃ yatīṃ gacchantīṃ prāgudīcīmuttarapūrvadigabhimukhīmanumanyate /
25.46.[2]	yatra vā āvasathaḥ syāt, tadabhimukhaṃ gacchet //
25.46.[3]	uduttamamārohantī vyasyantīva pṛtanyataḥ /
25.46.[4]	mūrdhānaṃ patyurāroha prajayā ca virāḍbhava // 1 //
25.46.[5]	he vadhu uttamamutkṛṣṭaṃ gṛhaṃ sucaritaṃ vā ārohantī, pṛtanyataḥ pṛtanāṃ senāmicchataḥ śatrūn vyasyantīva kṣipantīva, patyurbharturmūrdhānamadhiroha tasya svaguṇagaṇena mānyā bhavetyarthaḥ, tathā prajayā putrapautrādikayā viśeṣeṇa rājamānā bhava //
25.46.[6]	imāṃ tvamindra mīḍhvaḥ suputrāṃ subhagāṃ kṛṇu /
25.46.[7]	daśāsyāṃ putrānādhehi patimekādaśaṃ kṛdhi // 2 //
