25.46.[8]	he indra mīḍhvaḥ ‘miha secane’ sektaḥ, garbhagrahaṇākhyāyā retaḥsthiterindraprasādāyattatvādevaṃ saṃbodhanam, imāṃ vadhūṃ suputrāṃ saubhāgyayuktāṃ ca kuru /
25.46.[9]	daśāsyāṃ putrānādhehi vidhehi ekādaśaṃ patiṃ sampādaya // 2 //
25.46.[10]	samrājñī śvaśure bhava samrājñī śvaśrvāṃ bhava /
25.46.[11]	nanāndari samrājñī bhava samrājñī adhidevṛṣu // 3 //
25.46.[12]	he vadhu samrājñī śvaśure tvaṃ samrājñī mānanīyatamā samyagrājamānā bhava, tathā śvaśrvāṃ na nāndari ca bharturbhaginyāmevamadhidevṛṣu devareṣu //
25.46.[13]	snuṣāṇāṃ śvaśurāṇāṃ ca prajāyāśca dhanasya ca /
25.46.[14]	patīnāṃ ca devṛṇāṃ ca sajātānāṃ virāḍbhava // 4 //
25.46.[15]	sajātāḥ bāndhavaparijanaprabhṛtayaḥ /
25.46.[16]	devṛṇāṃ ‘chandasyubhayathā’ iti havaḥ, madhyadeśe tu dīrghaḥ paṭhyate, devarāṇām /
25.46.[17]	sarvaṃ gṛhagataṃ tavāyattamastvityarthaḥ /
25.46.[18]	ata ūrdhvaṃ tvaṃ no agna ityāditaṃtraparisamāptiḥ /
25.46.[19]	atra bhartṛgṛhagamanāvasare madhuparkakāṇḍikā paṭhyate /
25.46.[20]	sā ca snātakaprakaraṇe vyākhyāsyate // 44 //
26.1.[1]	yadā vadhūḥ puṇye divase bhartṛgṛhaṃ gacchati tadā rathaṃ śivikāṃ vā yathāsambhavaṃ yuṃkte /
26.1.[2]	tatra ca yoge yoga iti vyākhyātamaṃtrāvṛttyā aśvādikaṃ yunakti // 1 //
26.2.[1]	aṅkunyaṅkāvityādikayā jagatyā āgnimārute rathacakre'numaṃtrayate ṛtvik pārśve vā /
26.2.[2]	sakṛcca maṃtraḥ prayoktavyo dvivacanaliṃgāt /
26.2.[3]	aṃcatītyaṃkuḥ, nyañcatīti nyaṅkaḥ, aṃkuśca nyaṃkaścāṅkunyaṃkau añcakanyañcakau gantṛviśeṣau yābhyāṃ cakre gacchataḥ /
26.2.[4]	aṅkunyaṅkau rathasyābhitaḥ sthitau no'smākaṃ te'gnayaḥ pārayantu pathastārayantu pālayantu vā pathi /
26.2.[5]	ke te'gnayaḥ /
26.2.[6]	ye dhvāntāstamorūpāḥ kāṣṭhādīndhanajāḥ /
26.2.[7]	ye ca vātāgramabhisaṃpatanti vaidyutādirūpā ityarthaḥ /
26.2.[8]	yaśca dūrehetirdūragatārcirādityādirūpaḥ /
26.2.[9]	yaśca patatriṇīvājinīvān patatriṇīvān vājinīvāṃścetyarthaḥ, patatriṇīvān vāyugaruḍādimūrtiṣu vyavasthitaḥ, vājinīvān vrīhyādimūrtyāśritaḥ /
26.2.[10]	kīdṛśā agnayaḥ /
26.2.[11]	paśyaḥ ‘pṛ pālanapūraṇayoḥ’ prīṇantīti paprayaḥ pālayitāraḥ pūrayitāro vā kāmānāṃ, ‘prā pūraṇe’ ityasya vā patriśabdaḥ // 2 //
26.3.[1]	khe rathasyetyādinā yugasya tarmasu cchidreṣu śamīśākhāmavadadhāti /
26.3.[2]	rathasya khe ākāśe chidre avadadhāmi śākhāṃ, tathā khe'nasaḥ gantryāḥ, evaṃ yugasya tarmasu cchidreṣu, tathā khe akṣasya rathādhārakāṣṭhaviśeṣasyānyatrāpi ca khe chidre śāntyarthaṃ śamīśākhāmavadadhāmi // 3 //
26.4.[1]	sukiṃśukamityādinā vadhūṃ rathamāropayati /
26.4.[2]	he vadhu rathamāroha /
26.4.[3]	kīdṛśam /
26.4.[4]	sukiṃśukaṃ śobhanapalāśakusumaistadupalakṣitairanyapuṣpaiśca parijanāhitaiḥ śobhanaṃ, śalmaliṃ ‘śala hula pallṛ gatau’ gamanaśīlaṃ, athavā kiṃśukaśalmalidārunirmitatvādevamucyate, viśvarūpaṃ nānākāraṃ, hiraṇyavarṇaṃ ujjvalarūpaṃ, suvṛtaṃ phalakusumādibhiḥ parivṛtaṃ suvartulaṃ vā suvartanaṃ sukhaceṣṭaṃ vā, tathā śobhanacakraṃ, amṛtasya yoniṃ amaraṇadharmasya kāraṇamapramāpaṇakāriṇam /
26.4.[5]	patye bhartre vyatyayena bhartuḥ syonaṃ sukhaṃ kṛṇuṣva kuruṣvainaṃ vahatuṃ vahatīti vahatustam // 4 //
26.5.[1]	‘mā vidanparipanthinaḥ’ iti ‘sumaṃgalīḥ’ iti caitābhyāṃ vyākhyātārthābhyāṃ pravāhayate ratham //
26.6.[1]	etāṃ jagatīṃ sāvitrīṃ vadhūsaṃgame japati saṃkāśayetyādikām /
26.6.[2]	aśvāvucyete /
26.6.[3]	samyaganayā prakāśamānayā dṛṣṭyā idamano vivahataṃ prāpayatam /
26.6.[4]	brahmaṇā annena saha, gṛhaiśca patyā gṛhaśabdena gṛhasthapatnyucyate, aghoreṇa śivena, cakṣuṣā maitreṇa mitrasambandhinā, natu śātraveṇa /
26.6.[5]	kīdṛśaṃ vahatam /
26.6.[6]	paryāṇaddhaṃ samantācchannam /
26.6.[7]	tathā nānārūpaṃ yadanaḥ asyā vadhvāḥ patibhyaḥ syonaṃ sukhaṃ patibhya iti vacanavyatyayaḥ patye tacca savitā ca sukhādikaṃ sarvaṃ karotu /
26.6.[8]	rathayoranyonyasaṃghāte vighātaśaṃkāyāmeṣa japaḥ //
26.7.[1]	vyākhyātau maṃtrau /
26.7.[2]	ye pathīnāmityanuṣṭup /
26.7.[3]	ime catvāra iti triṣṭup /
26.7.[4]	sūtraṃ spaṣṭārtham // 7 //
26.7.[5]	japatītyanuṣaṅgaḥ //
26.7.[6]	ye śmaśāneṣu puṇyajanāḥ śāvāsteṣu śerate /
26.7.[7]	tatraiva te ramantāṃ mā vadhūranvavekṣata //
26.7.[8]	śmaśāneṣu śavaśayaneṣu ye puṇyajanā yakṣā ye ca śāvāḥ pretāsteṣu śmaśāneṣu śerate tiṣṭhanti, tatraiva te ramantāṃ ratiṃ kurvantu, mā vadhūranvavekṣata mā drākṣurvadhūm /
26.7.[9]	vadhūriti subvyatyayaḥ // 8 //
26.8.[1]	spaṣṭam /
26.8.[2]	maṃtro'pi vivṛtaḥ // 9 //
26.9.[1]	iha raḍirityādikaṃ krūraṃ siṃhādikaṃ dṛṣṭvā japatītyanuṣaṃgaḥ //
26.9.[2]	iha raḍiriha ratiriha dhṛtiriha vidhṛtiriha svadhṛtiriha rantiriha ramatāmagre veṭ svāhā vaṭ //
26.9.[3]	‘laḍa vilāse’ laḍanaṃ raḍiḥ krīḍā iha asmāsu ramatām /
26.9.[4]	tathā ratiḥ prītiḥ /
26.9.[5]	sarvatra ramatāmityanuṣajati /
26.9.[6]	iha dhṛtiḥ saṃtoṣaḥ /
26.9.[7]	iha vidhṛtirvidharaṇaṃ sthairyam /
26.9.[8]	svadhṛtiḥ svasya dhanasya dhāraṇam /
26.9.[9]	iha raṃtiḥ ramaṇaṃ rantiḥ, raḍyādikaṃ hiṃsradarśanādasmatsakāśānmā dūrībhūdityarthaḥ /
26.9.[10]	agre veṭ svāhā vaṭ saṃpradānārthīyā nipātāḥ // 10 //
26.10.[1]	dṛṣṭvā japatītyanuṣaṃgaḥ //
26.10.[2]	namo astu sarpebhyo ye ke ca pṛthivyāmadhi /
26.10.[3]	ye antarikṣe ye divi tebhyaḥ sarpebhyo namaḥ //
26.10.[4]	yeṣu vā yātudhānā ye vā vanaspatīṃranu /
26.10.[5]	ye vāvaṭeṣu śerate tebhyaḥ sarpebhyo namaḥ //
26.10.[6]	ye vādo rocane divo ye vā sūryasya raśmiṣu /
26.10.[7]	ye'psu sadāṃsi cakrire tebhyaḥ sarpebhyo namaḥ //
26.10.[8]	gatārtham // 11 //
26.11.[1]	tīrthe japati pratīkamudritānmantrānityarthaḥ /
26.11.[2]	ye tīrthānīti vyākhyātā /
26.11.[3]	tīrthamatra nipānaṃ nadyavatārasthānam /
26.11.[4]	yathoktaṃ ‘tīrthābhidhānamicchanti tritayaṃ kṛtabuddhayaḥ /
26.11.[5]	śāstraṃ caiva nipānaṃ ca vāri cāpyṛṣisevitam //’ iti //
26.11.[6]	tā mandamānā manuṣo duroṇa adhattaṃ rayiṃ sahavīraṃ vacasyave /
26.11.[7]	kṛtaṃ tīrthaṃ suprapāṇaṃ śubhaspatī sthāṇuṃ patheṣṭhāmapa durmatiṃ hatam //
26.11.[8]	āśvinī /
26.11.[9]	jagatī /
26.11.[10]	he aśvinau mandamānau stūyamānau harṣayuktau mada stutimodamadetyādikādarthanirdeśāt manuṣo manuṣyasya duroṇe gṛhe rayiṃ dhanaṃ adhattaṃ chāndaso hrasvaḥ ādhattam /
26.11.[11]	kīdṛśaṃ dhanam /
26.11.[12]	sahavīram putrasahitaṃ, sahasravīryaṃ vā putrapautrādimālāyuktamityarthaḥ /
26.11.[13]	kiṃca tīrthaṃ suprapāṇaṃ kṛtaṃ yuvāṃ kurutaṃ svavagāhaṃ, tathā sthāṇuṃ tiṣṭhantyasmin saṃpada iti sthāṇuḥ /
26.11.[14]	kasmai /
26.11.[15]	vacasyave vaca icchatyātmanaḥ ‘supa ātmanaḥ ‘kyac’ ‘kyācchandasi’ ityutvaṃ tasmai vacasyave /
26.11.[16]	he śubhaspatī śubhasya pālayitārau durmatiṃ duṣṭāṃ matimasya manuṣyasya apahataṃ vināśayatam /
26.11.[17]	kīdṛśīṃ durmatim /
26.11.[18]	patheṣṭhāṃ pathi tiṣṭhati patheṣṭhā tāṃ surūḍhāmityarthaḥ //
26.11.[19]	ayaṃ no mahyāḥ pāraṃ svasti naiṣadvanaspatiḥ /
26.11.[20]	sīrā naḥ sutarā bhava dīrghāyutvāya varcase //
26.11.[21]	viśeṣataraṇe'yaṃ maṃtraḥ /
26.11.[22]	gāyatrī /
26.11.[23]	ayaṃ vanaspatirvānaspatyo rathaḥ no'smān mahyāḥ mahatyā nadyāḥ pāraṃ naiṣat nayatu /
26.11.[24]	svasti avināśaṃ kṛtvā /
26.11.[25]	sīrā ca nadī no'smākaṃ sutarā bhava bhavatu /
26.11.[26]	dīrghāyutvāya dīrghāyuṣe, varcase ca asmākaṃ sīrā bhavatu /
26.11.[27]	dīrghāyutvāyetyatra tvapatyoriti salopaśchāndasaḥ //
26.11.[28]	aśmanvatī rīyate saṃrabhadhvamuttiṣṭhata pratarāma sakhāyaḥ /
26.11.[29]	atrājahāma ye asannaśevāḥ śivānvayamuttaremābhivājān// anena prakṛtā nadī tīryate /
26.11.[30]	he sakhāyaḥ janyāḥ uttiṣṭhata, saṃrabhadhvaṃ saprayatnā bhavata, pratarāmo nadīm /
26.11.[31]	prayatnaviśeṣeṇa preṣaṇe hetumāha yato'śmanvatī pāṣāṇasaṃghavatī nadī rīyate tīryate /
26.11.[32]	śeva iti sukhanāma /
26.11.[33]	ye cāśevā asukhā asan saṃti, tānatraiva sthāne ājahāma tyajāmaḥ tyaktvā tāngacchāma ityarthaḥ /
26.11.[34]	vayaṃ ca śivāndeśaviśeṣān abhivājān vājābhiḥ mukhān annaviśeṣayuktān tarema tīrtvā prāpnuyāmetyāśaṃsā // 12 //
27.1.[1]	gatārthaṃ samantrakam // 1 //
27.2.[1]	aviśeṣābhidhānādyasminkasmiṃścidrathāṅge viśīrṇe ślathe rathe ya ṛta ityādikāmaindrīṃ bṛhatīṃ japatītyarthaḥ //
27.2.[2]	ya ṛte cidabhiśriṣaḥ purā jatrubhya ātṛdaḥ /
27.2.[3]	sandhātā sandhiṃ maghavā purūvasurniṣkartāvihrutaṃ punaḥ //
27.2.[4]	he ratha yastvaṃ jatrubhyo granthibhyo bandhanebhyaḥ ṛte vinā abhiśriṣaḥ viśīrṇo vināśaṃ prāptaḥ purā pūrvamevātṛdaḥ ātardanādahiṃsita eva naṣṭa ityarthaḥ, taṃ tvā maghavā punaḥ niṣkartā sandhiṃ sandhīyata iti sandhistaṃ niḥśeṣeṇa punaḥ kariṣyatītyarthaḥ /
27.2.[5]	sahi sandhātā sandhānaśīlaḥ /
27.2.[6]	kīdṛśaṃ sandhīyamānaṃ tvāṃ kariṣyati /
27.2.[7]	avihrutamakuṭilagatiyogyam /
27.2.[8]	kīdṛśo maghavā /
27.2.[9]	purūvasuḥ bahudhanaḥ /
27.2.[10]	ciditi pādapūraṇo nipātaḥ //
27.3.[1]	aparāhnasamaye'dhivṛkṣasūrye yadā vṛkṣāṇāmuparyeva raviraśmayo dṛśyante nādhastāt tadā gṛhānupayāya, gṛhagrahaṇena svagrāma upalakṣyate, svagrāmasamīpaṃ gatvā, tatra svagṛhān pratidṛśya ābhimukhyena dṛṣṭvā ūrjaṃ bibhratītyādi japati /
27.3.[2]	vadhvā eṣa japo maṃtraliṅgāt //
27.3.[3]	ūrjaṃ bibhratī vasuvaniḥ sumedhā gṛhānāgāṃ modamānā suvarcāḥ /
27.3.[4]	aghoreṇa cakṣuṣā maitreṇa gṛhāṇāṃ paśyantī vaya uttirāmi //
27.3.[5]	gṛhāṇāmāyuḥ pra vayaṃ tirāma gṛhā asmākaṃ pratirantvāyuḥ /
27.3.[6]	gṛhānahaṃ sumanasaḥ prapadye vīraghnī vīrapatiḥ suśevā //
27.3.[7]	irāṃ vahato ghṛtamukṣamāṇāsteṣvahaṃ sumanāḥ saṃviśāmi /
27.3.[8]	yeṣāṃ madhye'dhipravasanneti saumanasaṃ bahu //
27.3.[9]	gṛhānupahvayāmahe te no jānantu jānataḥ /
27.3.[10]	sūnṛtāvantaḥ svadhāvanta irāvanto ha sāmadāḥ //
27.3.[11]	akṣudhyā atṛpyāsta gṛhā māsmadbibhetana /
27.3.[12]	upahūtā iha gāva upahūtā ajāvayaḥ //
27.3.[13]	atho annasya kīlāla upahūto gṛheṣu me /
27.3.[14]	upahūtā bhūridhanāḥ sakhāyaḥ sādhusammadāḥ //
27.3.[15]	ariṣṭāḥ sarvapūruṣā gṛhā naḥ santu sarvadā /
27.3.[16]	ahaṃ gṛhānāgāṃ āgatā, ūrjaṃ bibhratī annaṃ dhārayantī puṣṇatī ca, vasuvaniḥ ‘vana ṣaṇa saṃbhaktau’ vasūni dhanāni vibhajamānā, sumedhāḥ śobhanayā prajñayā yuktā, modamānā hṛṣyantī, suvarcāḥ śobhanadīptiḥ, gṛhāṇāmiti vyatyayena dvitīyārthe ṣaṣṭhī, aghoreṇa saumyena, maitreṇa hitaiṣiṇā cakṣuṣā gṛhānpaśyantī /
27.3.[17]	vaya iti dhananāma, dhanamuttirāmi dadāmi parijanāya /
27.3.[18]	vayameteṣāmāyuḥ pratirāmaḥ upalepanādidvāreṇa sthairyaṃ sampādayāmaḥ /
27.3.[19]	gṛhā api gṛhādhiṣṭhātryo devatā asmākamāyuḥ pratirantu sampādayantu /
27.3.[20]	ahametān gṛhān prapadye gacchāmi praviśāmi /
27.3.[21]	kīdṛśān /
27.3.[22]	sumanasaḥ saumanasyakāriṇaḥ /
27.3.[23]	vīraghnī gatyartho'tra hantiḥ putrāṇāṃ prāpikā lambhikā /
27.3.[24]	vīrapatiḥ vikrāntiyuktabhartṛkā /
27.3.[25]	suśevā śevo'nnaṃ dhanaṃ ca, sudhanā /
27.3.[26]	kīdṛśān gṛhān /
27.3.[27]	irāmannaṃ vahataḥ dhārayataḥ /
27.3.[28]	tathā ghṛtamukṣamāṇā āsiñcanto bahugavādikatvāt ye gṛhāstānahaṃ sumanaskā satī praviśāmi /
27.3.[29]	kiṃca yeṣāṃ gṛhāṇāṃ madhye nivasan bahu saumanasameti prapadyate, tān gṛhānupahayāmahe āhvayāmaḥ /
27.3.[30]	te'smāñjānato jñānayuktān jānantu /
27.3.[31]	gṛhādhiṣṭhātṛdevatāprasādācca vayaṃ sūnṛtāvantaḥ satyavācaḥ syāma, tathā svadhāvantaḥ pitṛyajñakāriṇaḥ irāvanto'nnavantaḥ, hetyanarthakaḥ, sāmadāḥ syāma sāntvanalakṣaṇena prathamenopāyena svīkārakāḥ syāmetyarthaḥ /
27.3.[32]	yathoktaṃ ‘sāma dānaṃ ca bhedaśca daṇḍaśceti caturvidhaḥ /
27.3.[33]	māyendrajālopekṣāśca saptopāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ //’ iti /
27.3.[34]	asmabhyamiti tādarthye caturthī, tenāsmadarthaṃ satyavacanayuktā yūyaṃ bhavatetyapyarthaḥ sampadyate /
27.3.[35]	asmabhyaṃ sāmadā bhavateti pradāne caturthī api yojyā /
27.3.[36]	he gṛhā asmābhiradhiṣṭhitāḥ santaḥ asmat mā bibhetana asmatsakāśādbhyaṃ mā kārṣuḥ //
27.3.[37]	iha ca gṛheṣu upahūtā āhūtā gāvastathā ajā avayaśca atho tathā annasya saṃbandhī kīlālo mṛṣṭarasa āhūto mama gṛheṣu, tathā sakhāyaḥ sahāyāḥ, bhūridhanāḥ bahuvittāḥ, āhūtāste sādhu kṛtvā sammadāḥ samyak harṣayuktāḥ sarvadā santu, tathā ariṣṭā anupahiṃsitā no'smākaṃ gṛhāḥ sarvapūruṣāśca sarvadā bhavantu // 3 //
28.1.[1]	ulapo vīraṇaḥ, prasūnā dīrghadarbhā iti tu prasiddhihīnaṃ vaco madhyadeśādau vīraṇānāmeva tathā prasiddheḥ /
28.1.[2]	ṛtvik vīraṇapaṃktiṃ stṛṇāti racayati rathāvataraṇasthānādārabhya vadhūśayanagṛhaviśeṣaṃ yāvat // 1 //
28.2.[1]	tathā rājyā praviśati gṛhaṃ rathādavatīrya vadhūsahito varaḥ // 2 //
28.3.[1]	adhyāhitaḥ sthāpito vivāhāgniryatra taṃ, tathā sodakamudakumbhabhūṣitaṃ, sauṣadhaṃ vrīhyādyoṣadhisanāthaṃ, āvasathaṃ gṛhaviśeṣaṃ pratipadyate praviśati /
28.3.[2]	ata ūrdhvaṃ hi pākayajñeṣvadhikriyate /
28.3.[3]	vāstuhomānantaraṃ caiṣa praveśa iṣyate /
28.3.[4]	uktaṃ hi sūtraṃ ‘amīvahā vāstoṣpata iti catasṛbhirvāstoṣpatīyasya sthālīpākasyeṣṭvātha vāstvāviśet’ iti //
28.3.[5]	amīvahā vāstoṣpate° //
28.3.[6]	ādyā gāyatrī /
28.3.[7]	tisrastriṣṭubhaḥ /
28.3.[8]	brahmaṇa ārṣam /
28.3.[9]	he vāstoṣpate mādhyamikadevatāviśeṣa vāyurūpa no'smākaṃ anamīva edhi, ‘ama roge’ rogaśūnyo bhava asmānnīrogānkurvityarthaḥ /
28.3.[10]	amīvānaṃ vyādhiṃ hantīti amīvahā vyādhipradhvaṃsakārī, anamīvastu rogaprāgabhāvasyaiva sthairyaheturityapaunaruktyam, tathā suśevaḥ sukhasevyo bhava /
28.3.[11]	kiṃ kurvan /
28.3.[12]	viśvā rūpāṇyāviśan nānārūpāṇi dhārayan, aśvādīni nānārūpāṇi vā āviśan praveśayan samṛddhaṃ gṛhaṃ kurvannityarthaḥ // 1 //
28.3.[13]	he vāstoṣpate asmān pravivikṣūn pratijānīhi, ābhimukhyenānukūlyena paśya, tataśca svāveśaḥ supraveśo rogarahito'smākaṃ bhava /
28.3.[14]	yat tvā īmahe yācāmahe, tannaḥ pratijuṣasva tena yācitenāsmān prīṇīhītyarthaḥ /
28.3.[15]	tasmādasmākaṃ dvipade mānuṣarūpe, catuṣpade gavādike śaṃ bhava sukharūpo bhava // 2 //
28.3.[16]	he vāstoṣpate asmākaṃ prataraṇo bhava durgamasthānebhyo'smān pratārayetyarthaḥ /
28.3.[17]	he indo mādhyamikatvasāmānyāt candra asmākaṃ gobhiraśvaiśca gaye gṛhe sphānaḥ sphīto bhava /
28.3.[18]	tena tava sakhye vartamānā vayaṃ ajarāsaḥ ajīrṇāḥ syāma /
28.3.[19]	tvaṃ cāsmān pratijuṣasva prīṇīhi /
28.3.[20]	ka iva kān /
28.3.[21]	piteva putrān // 3 //
28.3.[22]	he vāstopate te tava sambandhinyā saṃsadā vegādisaṃpadā śagmayā sukharūpayā vayaṃ sakṣīma saṃgacchema /
28.3.[23]	hiraṇvayā suvarṇādikayā, gātumatyā yajñādikarmavatyā yajñādyupayoginyetyarthaḥ /
28.3.[24]	varamutkṛṣṭaṃ kṛtvā no'smān alabdhalābhātmake yoge, prāptaparirakṣaṇātmake ca kṣeme vartamānaḥ pāhi rakṣa /
28.3.[25]	yūyaṃ tvaṃ vyatyayena pāta pāhi svastibhiravināśaiḥ sarvakālam // 4 //
28.4-5.[1]	rohiṇyā mūlena vā nakṣatreṇa yukte candramasīti jñeyam /
28.4-5.[2]	yadvā puṇyoktaṃ jyotiḥśāstre puṇyarūpaṃ śreyaskaraṃ yaddinamuktaṃ, tatra vā /
28.4-5.[3]	apareṇāgniṃ prakṛtatvādāvasathyam, anaḍuha idamānaḍuhaṃ vārṣabhaṃ tatra, rohite carmaṇyupaveśya vadhūṃ varaḥ svayaṃ copaviśya, kevaleṣu vā darbheṣu vadhūmupaveśya svayaṃ copaviśya jayahomaprabhṛtikamājyabhāgāntamājyasādhanatvādarthādājyadharmayuktamupasamādhānādipūrvakaṃ hutvā, agniraitu prathama ityādibhiśca karmāntarāṇi kuryāt /
28.4-5.[4]	kāni tāni /
28.4-5.[5]	pākayajñā arthāt //
28.4-5.[6]	agniraitu prathamo devatānāṃ so'syāḥ prajāṃ nayatu sarvamāyuḥ /
28.4-5.[7]	tadayaṃ rājā varuṇo'numanyatāṃ yatheyaṃ strī pautramaghaṃ nirundhyātsvāhā // 1 //
28.4-5.[8]	agniraitu iti vaiśvadevyaścatastrastriṣṭubhaḥ /
28.4-5.[9]	viśveṣu deveṣvāgacchatsu sarvadevatānāṃ prathamo'gre'gnirā etu aitu āgacchatu /
28.4-5.[10]	so'gniḥ sarvadevapuraḥsaro'syā vadhvāḥ prajāṃ nayatu prāpayatu, tāṃ ca prajāṃ sarvamāyuḥ nayatu prāpayatu /
28.4-5.[11]	dvikarmakaḥ ajāṃ nayati grāmamitivat /
28.4-5.[12]	taccāyuragninā prāpyamāṇaṃ varuṇo rājānumanyatāṃ tatrānumatiṃ dadātvevamastviti /
28.4-5.[13]	rājagrahaṇaṃ tenānumatena tadanucaratvātsarve devā anumanyante ityāśayena /
28.4-5.[14]	yathāca iyaṃ strī vadhūḥ putrasyedaṃ pautramaghaṃ pāpaṃ nirundhyāt putraśokaṃ nānubhavettathā tena prakāreṇa varuṇo rājā anumanyatām // 1 //
28.4-5.[15]	agnirimāṃ trāyatāṃ gārhapatyaḥ so'syāḥ prajāṃ muñcatu mṛtyupāśāt /
28.4-5.[16]	ariktopasthā jīvatāmastu mātā pautramānandamabhivibudhyatāmiyaṃ svāhā // 2 //
28.4-5.[17]	imāṃ vadhūmagnirāvasathyastrāyatāṃ rakṣatu /
28.4-5.[18]	iyaṃ vadhūrariktopasthā astu upastha utsaṅgo bālakasutaiḥ krameṇa jāyamānairasyā utsaṅgo'rikto'śūnyo'stvityarthaḥ /
28.4-5.[19]	tatheyaṃ jīvatāṃ cirāyuṣāṃ putrāṇāṃ mātā bhavatu /
28.4-5.[20]	putrāṇāmayaṃ pautrastaṃ cānandaṃ sukhamiyamābhimukhyena viśeṣeṇa budhyatām // 2 //
28.4-5.[21]	mā te gṛhe niśi ghora utthādanyatra tvadrudatyaḥ saṃviśantu /
28.4-5.[22]	jīvaputrā patiloke virāja paśyantī prajāṃ sumanasyamānāṃ svāhā // 3 //
28.4-5.[23]	he vadhu te tava gṛhe niśi divā ghoro rodanādiśabdo mā utthāt rodanādiśabdo duṣṭastvadgṛhe mā bhūtkadācidityarthaḥ /
28.4-5.[24]	rudatyo rodanaṃ kurvatyastvattava sakāśādanyatra saṃviśantu anyatra tava dūravartini deśe tiṣṭhantvityarthaḥ /
28.4-5.[25]	tvaṃ patiloke patikule viśeṣeṇa rāja śobhasva jīvaputrā dīrghāyurbahuputrā satī, tathā sumanasyamānāṃ sukhinīṃ prajāṃ putrādikāṃ paśyantī satī // 3 //
28.4-5.[26]	mā te kumāraḥ stanadhaḥ pramāyi mā tvaṃ vikeśyura āvadhiṣṭhāḥ /
28.4-5.[27]	stanandhayaṃ te savitābhirakṣatvā vāsasaḥ paridhānādbṛhaspatirviśvedevā abhirakṣantu nityaṃ svāhā // 4 //
28.4-5.[28]	tava kumāro bālakaḥ stanandhayaḥ stanapaḥ mā pramāyi mā mṛta /
28.4-5.[29]	mā ca tvaṃ vikeśī muṇḍā satī uro vakṣa āvadhiṣṭhāḥ bhartṛvirahakṛtamurastāḍanaṃ tava mā bhūdityarthaḥ /
28.4-5.[30]	tava stanandhayaṃ savitā abhirakṣatu bṛhaspatiśca abhirakṣatu ā vāsasaḥ paridhānāt paridhānavastraparyantaṃ yāvat rakṣatu, viśve devāśca nityamabhirakṣantu // 4 //
28.4-5.[31]	etābhiścatasṛbhirṛgbhiścatasra āhutayo dātavyā vareṇa svayamevamuttarā api /
28.4-5.[32]	agne prāyaścitta ityādibhiryajurbhiranyā daśa ājyāhutayaḥ kramāpakramābhyām //
28.4-5.[33]	agne prāyaścitte tvaṃ devānāṃ prāyaścittirasi /
28.4-5.[34]	yāsyāṃ bhṛśā tanūstāmasyā nāśaya svāhā //
28.4-5.[35]	prāyaścittaṃ pāpanivāraṇaṃ dharmajananaṃ ca karmocyate /
28.4-5.[36]	tatkāraṇatvādagniḥ prāyaścittiḥ /
28.4-5.[37]	he agne prāyaścitte tvaṃ devānāṃ prāyaścittirdoṣāpasāre śubhajanane ca nimittamato'syāṃ vadhvāṃ yā bhṛśā apavitrā atiśayena bījavaśena bālabhāvakṛtakuceṣṭāvaśena ca tanūstāmasyā vadhvā nāśaya tadgatamaśubhaṃ nāśaya /
28.4-5.[38]	varasya hi gārbhabaijikadoṣā jātakarmādibhirnāśitāḥ, vadhvāstu tāni prāyeṇa na kṛtāni ‘gārbhairhomairjātakarmacauḍamauñjīnibandhanaiḥ /
28.4-5.[39]	baijikaṃ gārbhikaṃ caino dvijānāṃ pratihanyate //’ iti smṛteḥ /
28.4-5.[40]	enaḥ pāpamaśuddhiḥ //
28.4-5.[41]	vāyo prāyaścitte° /
28.4-5.[42]	sūrya prāyaścitte° /
28.4-5.[43]	candra prāyaścitte° /
28.4-5.[44]	viṣṇo prāyaścitte° /
28.4-5.[45]	viṣṇo prāyaścitte° /
28.4-5.[46]	candra prāyacitte° /
28.4-5.[47]	sūrya prāyaścitte° /
28.4-5.[48]	vāyo prāyaścitte° /
28.4-5.[49]	agne prāyaścitte° //
28.4-5.[50]	etāni sānuṣaṅgāṇi parāṇi pañca yajūṃṣi apakrameṇa /
28.4-5.[51]	tenargbhiścatasṛbhiścatasro, yajurbhiśca daśabhirdaśeti caturdaśāhutayaḥ saṃpannāḥ, tryāyuṣamityanena paṃcadaśī, ityādityadarśanaḥ /
28.4-5.[52]	sa ājyaikadeśe yo'nena yajuṣā vakṣyamāṇa āsekastāmevāhutiṃ manyate maṃtrāvṛttiṃ vā // 4 //
28.4-5.[53]	svayaṃkartṛkatvādāsāṃ sruveṇa pūrvoktā ghṛtāhutīrhutvā tryāyuṣamityādiyajuṣā pṛthakpātroddhṛte ghṛte ghṛtaikadeśe dadhyāsicya ‘dadhikrāvṇaḥ’ ityanayā trīnvārān vadhūṃ dadhi bhakṣayitvā varo māṇavakāya vadhvā utsaṅge nihitāya phalāni pradadāti ‘irāmagne’ iti mantreṇa /
28.4-5.[54]	maṇibhirmantrairoṣadhibhistribhirupāyaiḥ sādhyamānatvāt tryāyuṣaṃ bālayuvavṛddhāvasthātrayabhāvitvāt yāgadānahomasādhyatvāttadārambhakatvādvā tryāyuṣaṃ yat jamadagneḥ tryāyuṣaṃ, yacca kaśyapasya, yacca devānāṃ, tatsarvamastviti vara āśāste //
28.4-5.[55]	dadhikrāvṇo akāriṣaṃ jiṣṇoraśvasya vājinaḥ /
28.4-5.[56]	surabhi no mukhā karatpra ṇa āyūṃṣi tāriṣat //
28.4-5.[57]	āgneyī /
28.4-5.[58]	anuṣṭup /
28.4-5.[59]	indrasyārṣam /
28.4-5.[60]	dadhi krāmatīti dadhikrāvā ‘anyebhyo'pi dṛśyate’ iti kvanip /
28.4-5.[61]	agnirvaiśvānara ucyate /
28.4-5.[62]	sahi sarve bhakṣitaṃ jarayati jaṭhare sthito dadhyādikam /
28.4-5.[63]	tasya dadhikrāvṇo'gnerjāṭharasyāhamakāriṣaṃ karomi santarpaṇamarthāt /
28.4-5.[64]	kīdṛśasya /
28.4-5.[65]	jiṣṇorjayanaśīlasya, aśvasya aśanasya vyāpino vā, vājino'nnapateḥ /
28.4-5.[66]	no'smākaṃ surabhi sugandhi vidyādyudgārabhūṣitamarthānmukhaṃ dadhi bhakṣyamāṇamākarat karotu /
28.4-5.[67]	loḍarthe leṭ /
28.4-5.[68]	no'smākamāyūṃṣi pratāriṣat prataratu dadhātu /
28.4-5.[69]	pūrvavat paṃcamo lakāraḥ /
28.4-5.[70]	irāmagna itīyaṃ vyākhyātā // 5 //
29.1.[1]	tūṣṇīmeva yatropacāro nirvāpādistaṃ caruṃ svarasasiddhatvādudakena śrapayitvā tasyāṃśenāgniṃ prajāpatiṃ ceṣṭvā nāmneva tūṣṇīṃgrahaṇāt hutaśeṣaṃ prāśnītaḥ vadhūvarāvekatra pātre saha /
29.1.[2]	gṛhyāntareṣu hi samaśanamiti saṃjñā /
29.1.[3]	sahāśanaṃ ca samaśanamiti prasiddham /
29.1.[4]	saṃvananamiti ca mantraliṅgam /
29.1.[5]	anye tvatrāpi caikapātre na saha bhojanamicchanti /
29.1.[6]	yathāhi yajamānapañcamā irāṃ prāśnanti sapatnīkā bhuñjata ityataḥ pañcasaṃkhyāsahaśravaṇe'pi iḍāyā gṛhamedhīyayoḥ pṛthagevāśanaṃ, tadvadihāpi bhavitavyam /
29.1.[7]	pākayajñapratiṣedhārthaṃ punastūṣṇīmupacaritagrahaṇam /
29.1.[8]	uktaṃ hyetat ‘teṣvāvṛdupacārastūṣṇīm’ iti /
29.1.[9]	bhakṣaṇaṃ tu annameva vivananamityādibhiścatasṛbhiranuṣṭubbhiḥ mantroccāraṇaṃ carukarmakam //
29.1.[10]	‘vana ṣaṇa saṃbhaktau’ annameva vivananaṃ vibhajanaṃ, annameva saṃvananaṃ smṛtaṃ saha bhujyamānaṃ saṃśleṣaṇamityarthaḥ /
29.1.[11]	annaṃ paśūnāṃ prāṇaḥ tena hi jīvanti /
29.1.[12]	annameva jyeṣṭhaṃ praśastatamaṃ bhiṣagbheṣajaṃ smṛtam /
29.1.[13]	tena hi bubhukṣādikṛtā vyādhayo nivartyante //
29.1.[14]	varo brūte he vadhu tavāhaṃ hṛdayaṃ ca manaśca sinomi ‘ṣiñ bandhane’ badhnāmi /
29.1.[15]	mananaṃ mano jñānaṃ manyate'nena manaḥ bāhyendriyapañcakaṃ, hṛdayaṃ cittam /
29.1.[16]	kena /
29.1.[17]	satyagranthinā satyaṃ nirvyājacaritameva granthistena, pṛśninā śuklena śucinā dharmarūpeṇetyarthaḥ /
29.1.[18]	annaṃ maṇiriva, prāṇaḥ sūtramiva hārāyalaṃkārarūpametat //
29.1.[19]	he vadhu tava ca mama ca vācā saha mano'stu yādṛśaṃ vacanaṃ tādṛśaṃ nirvyājaṃ cittamastu, natu daurjanyenānyaccetasi anyadvāci /
29.1.[20]	evamāvayościttaṃ caitanyaṃ samānamastu, vrataṃ ca saphalaṃ vihitaṃ karma /
29.1.[21]	tava mano māmevānvetu cakramivānaḍuhaḥ padaṃ yathā śakaṭacakraṃ śakaṭakarṣakasya vṛṣabhasya padamanugacchati //
29.1.[22]	māmeva sūryameva ca paśya /
29.1.[23]	anyeṣu puruṣeṣu mano mā kṛthāḥ /
29.1.[24]	mama cāmuṣyāśca vadhvāścākravākamiva saṃvananaṃ bhūyāt /
29.1.[25]	yathā cakravākapakṣimithunaṃ yathāprāptamatisnehāt vṛṣṭyādikaṃ saṃvibhajya bhuṃkte tadvadāvāṃ, tadvadatiprītirāvayorastvityarthaḥ // 1 //
29.1.[26]	iti śrījālandharīyabhaṭṭopendrasūnuharipālaputradevapālaviracite samantracārāyaṇīyagṛhyabhāṣye vivāhaḥ paripūrṇaḥ //
30.1.[1]	brahmacaryamamaithunaṃ caritvā garbhādhānaṃ kāryamiti /
30.1.[2]	tatpūrṇimāyāmamāvasyāyāṃ na maithunaṃ kartavyamiti ca saṃkalpaḥ /
30.1.[3]	ekaikakartṛkamatra vratam /
30.1.[4]	saṃvatsaraṃ prathamaḥ kalpaḥ /
30.1.[5]	yauvanamadasyātiśayāttvanukalpenāpatkalpo vikalpaḥ dvādaśa rātrīḥ ṣaṭ tisra ekāṃ veti // 1 //
30.2.[1]	tau vadhūvarāvekasmin śayane bhavataḥ /
30.2.[2]	vivāhottarakālaprathamaśayane ādhāne ca samānametadvidhānamanantaramantracatuṣṭayajapasahitam // 2 //
30.3.[1]	etāstriṣṭubhaḥ prathamasaṃveśane garbhādhāne ca vadhūvarau japataḥ stryādivyatyāsaṃ kṛtvā prathamāṃ strī, dvitīyāṃ varaḥ, tṛtīyāṃ strī, caturthī varaḥ /
30.3.[2]	vyatyāso viparyayaḥ /
30.3.[3]	puruṣo hi pradhānam /
30.3.[4]	tasya pūrvaṃ kriyāyogo'nyatra iha tu viparyayaḥ /
30.3.[5]	strī ādiryatra vyatyāse, sa stryādivyatyāsaḥ //
30.3.[6]	vadhūrvadati he putrakāma tvāmahamapaśyaṃ paśyāmi, cekitānaṃ dedīpyamānaṃ brahmavarcasādinā atiśayena dīptimantam /
30.3.[7]	kena paśyāmi /
30.3.[8]	manasā, natu cakṣuṣā /
30.3.[9]	kīdṛśam /
30.3.[10]	tapaso jātaṃ tapa iti prajāpateḥ satkarmaṇaśca nāma, prajāpaterbrahmaṇaḥ sakāśājjātaṃ, tapasaścāvirbhūtaṃ vṛddhiṃ gatam /
30.3.[11]	iha prajāṃ mayi putrarūpāṃ rayiṃ ca dhanaṃ rarāṇa ādadat prajayā prajāyasva prajāmutpādayetyarthaḥ // 1 //
30.3.[12]	vara āha paśyāmi tvāṃ he putrakāme dīdhyānāṃ dīptimatīṃ manasā /
30.3.[13]	kīdṛśīm /
30.3.[14]	nādhamānāṃ ‘nādhṛ nāthṛ yājñopatāpaiśvaryāśīḥṣu’ prajāṃ yācamānām /
30.3.[15]	kutra /
30.3.[16]	svāyāṃ tanū svasyāṃ tanvām /
30.3.[17]	kimartham /
30.3.[18]	ṛddhyai samṛddhyai lokadvayābhyudayāya /
30.3.[19]	māmupa mama samīpe vartamānā tvamuccā mahatī pūjyatamā satputrādiyogāt yuvatistaruṇī satī babhūyāḥ atiśayena bhūyāḥ /
30.3.[20]	prajayā prajāyasva ātmā vai putranāmeti vacanāt prajārūpeṇa prajāyasva putravatī bhava // 2 //
30.3.[21]	vadhūrāha bhartari prajāpatitvamadhyāropya he prajāpate mama tanvaṃ tanūṃ śarīraṃ juṣasva /
30.3.[22]	he tvaṣṭaḥ he prajāpate tvaṃ indraḥ san sahasā balena devairviśvaiśca devairanupatitaḥ san no'smākaṃ saṃvidānaḥ samyak jānānaḥ /
30.3.[23]	yajñiyairyajñārhairiti devaviḥśeṣaṇam /
30.3.[24]	vayaṃ ca bahūnāṃ puṃsāṃ putrāṇāṃ mātaro nirmātrayaḥ syāma // 3 //
30.3.[25]	vara āha oṣadhīṣu phalapākāntāsu ahameva garbhaṃ phalajananasāmarthyamādadhāmādadhe /
30.3.[26]	jīvātmanāṃ paramātmano bhedābhāvādevamabhidhānam /
30.3.[27]	ata evāha viśveṣu sarveṣu bhūteṣu ahamevāntastiṣṭhāmi antaryāmitayā, pṛthivyāmahameva prajāmanavadyāmajanayaṃ janayiṣyāmi ca /
30.3.[28]	ahameva janibhyo jananīnāṃ strīṇāmavarīṣu jaṭharābhyantaravartinīṣu garbhagrahaṇīṣu putrān janayāmi bījamādadhāmi // 4 //
30.4.[1]	gatārtham // 4 //
30.5.[1]	karaditi yajuṣā bhasadaṃ strīcihnaṃ varo'bhimṛśati /
30.5.[2]	karat kurvāṇaṃ prajāṃ, bhavetyarthaḥ // 5 //
30.6.[1]	puṃcihnaṃ bhasaditi yajuṣā abhimṛśati strī /
30.6.[2]	he puṃjanana tvaṃ bhasaddīpyamānaṃ satkāryajananasamarthaṃ bhavetyarthaḥ // 6 //
30.7.[1]	bṛhadityanena jātaṃ vīryaṃ prakṣipati /
30.7.[2]	bṛhadvistīrṇaṃ putrajananasamarthaṃ bhavetyarthaḥ // 7 //
31.1-2.[1]	garbhagrahaṇādārabhya yastṛtīyo māsastatra śuklapakṣasya parvaṇi mukhye dine sīmantonnayanasaṃjñayā yaugikyā prasiddhaṃ yatsaṃskārakarma, tatkārayate, natu vidvānapi svayaṃ kuryāditi ṇicaḥ prayogāt darśitam /
31.1-2.[2]	etacca pātrasyaiva kecitsaṃskāramicchanti ādhārasaṃskārādeva garbhasyopakāro bhaviṣyati golakasaṃskāreṇeva cakṣuṣa iti vadantaḥ /
31.1-2.[3]	tathāca smṛtiḥ ‘sakṛtsaṃskṛtasaṃskārāḥ sīmantena dvijastriyaḥ /
31.1-2.[4]	yaṃ yaṃ garbhaṃ prasūyante sa sarvaḥ saṃskṛto bhavet //’ iti /
31.1-2.[5]	anye tu garbhasyaiva saṃskāraṃ manyante tatraiva tṛtīye garbhamāsa ityasyopapatteḥ /
31.1-2.[6]	pātramātrasaṃskāratve hi kiṃ garbhamāsavyapekṣayā, yadā kadācitsīmanto vidhīyate, kāryaḥ sīmanta iti /
31.1-2.[7]	smṛterapi ‘gārbhairhomairjātakarmacauḍamauñjīnibandhanaiḥ /
31.1-2.[8]	baijikaṃ gārbhikaṃ caino dvijānāṃ pratihanyate //’ iti /
31.1-2.[9]	apare tūbhayasaṃskāramāhuḥ /
31.1-2.[10]	tatra kṣetrasaṃskāra evānumatatamaprāyo vedārthavidāṃ sakṛdanuṣṭhānasya prasiddhatvādbāhulyena /
31.1-2.[11]	yathoktamupasamādhānaṃ kṛtvā jayaprabhṛtibhirājyabhāgāntaṃ hutvā, prakṛtasya āvasathyasya agneḥ paścādbhāge agnerdarbheṣu prāṅmukhyā upaviṣṭāyāḥ sarvān keśān samyak prakarṣeṇa muktān kṛtvā, kaṅkatena dārumayobhayadikkabhūritaradantayoginā vālaspaṣṭīkaraṇena prasādhayate spaṣṭīkaroti vakṣyamāṇābhistisṛbhirṛgbhiḥ // 1 //
31.1-2.[12]	itiśabdaḥ karaṇapradhānaḥ /
31.1-2.[13]	anena mantratrayeṇa keśān prasādhayate iti pūrveṇa saṃbandhaḥ //
31.1-2.[14]	yaṃ sīmantaṃ te tava kaṅkataścakāra kṛtavān, kṣuro vā yaṃ cakāra sīmantaṃ, kṣura iva tīkṣṇatvātkaṅkata iti vyācakṣate vivāhādūrdhvaṃ kṣurasaṃsargasya strīṣvamāṅgalikatvāt /
31.1-2.[15]	dṛṣṭaścopamāyāṃ vāśabdaḥ ‘samudro vā mahāsattvaḥ’ ityādau nipātānāmanekārthatvāt /
31.1-2.[16]	yat vapan keśānspaṣṭīkurvan kaṅkataste tava parīvavarja varjitavān vālānāṃ śirovidāraṇabhayāt, tadrūpaṃ sīmantākhyasaṃskārayuktatvātstrīṣu he aśvinau nidhattaṃ kurutaṃ, tathaiva tadrūpaṃ pauṃsnena vīryeṇa saṃsṛjatamaśvinau // 1 //
31.1-2.[17]	amuṃ kaṅkatamindrāṇī śacī cakre kṛtavatī /
31.1-2.[18]	ato'yamutkṛṣṭatvātkaṅkataḥ sīmantaṃ visarpatu cinotu saṃpādayatvityarthaḥ /
31.1-2.[19]	he agne iyaṃ patnī tvayā vivāhasamaye dattā, idānīṃ punaḥ prajayā saha patibhyaḥ etāṃ jāyāṃ dāḥ dehi putravatīṃ sampādayetyarthaḥ // 2 //
31.1-2.[20]	agnirimāṃ patnīṃ punaradāt dadau āyuṣā varcasā ca saha /
31.1-2.[21]	asyā yaḥ patirbhartā sa dīrghāyurastu /
31.1-2.[22]	jīvāti śaradaḥ śataṃ, jīvātīti loḍarthe laṭ, śaradāṃ śataṃ jīvatu varṣaśataṃ jīvatādityarthaḥ // 2 //
31.3.[1]	trīnvārān triḥ, śvetayā śuklayā, śalalyā śalaliḥ śvāvitsedhā, tasyāḥ śalākā śalalirupacārāt tayā, śamīśākhayā sapalāśayā sapatrayā sīmantaṃ vicinoti ‘yāste rāke’ iti triṣṭubhā /
31.3.[2]	śalalyā tāmraśalākayā śvetayālohitayeti yayācakṣate, tanna dṛṣṭānurūpam //
31.3.[3]	yāste rāke sumatayaḥ supeśaso yābhirdadāsi dāśuṣe vasūni /
31.3.[4]	tābhirno adya sumanā upāgahi sahasrapoṣaṃ subhage rarāṇā //
31.3.[5]	brahmaṇa ārṣam /
31.3.[6]	he rāke devaputri yāstava śobhanā matayaḥ, supeśasaḥ surūpā abhimataphaladānonmukhatvaṃ matīnāṃ surūpatvaṃ, yābhiḥ sumatibhirdāśuṣe dātre yajamānāya vasūni dhanāni dadāsi tābhirupalakṣitā satyadyāsminnahani no'smānupāgahi upāgaccha, sumanāḥ prasannacittā satī, he subhage sundari rāke sahasrapoṣaṃ sahasrasaṃkhyaṃ dhanaṃ rarāṇā dadatī // 3 //
31.4.[1]	anantaramasyā garbhiṇyāḥ kaṅkatasamīkṛtānāṃ śalalyā vibhajyamānābhiḥ rekhābhiḥ paricchedena kṛtasīmantabhāgānāṃ keśānāṃ kṛtau pṛthagdvau pakṣau pārśvadvayagatau sannahyati badhnāti nīlalohitena sūtreṇa nīlalohitamityādikayānuṣṭubhā //
31.4.[2]	nīlalohitamidaṃ sūtraṃ bhavati /
31.4.[3]	kṛtiḥ kriyā tathā śaktirvyajyate garbhasya puṃstvaṃ vyajyata ityarthaḥ, asyā garbhiṇyā jñātaya edhante vardhante loḍarthe laṭ vyajyatāṃ śaktirvardhantāṃ jñātaya ityarthaḥ, patiśca snehādibandheṣu satsu baddhyatām // 4 //
31.5.[1]	yo guruḥ sīmantonnayanasya kartā brāhmaṇastamarhayedyathāśakti madhuparkadānādinā pūjayet // 5 //
31.6.[1]	atraiva kāle vāgdattānāṃ kumārīṇāṃ saṭoddharaṇaṃ karma kartavyaṃ keśaracanāviśeṣātmakam /
31.6.[2]	anulepanaṃ sarvauṣadhikuṅkumaprabhṛtibhiranulepanaṃ śobhāviśeṣādhāyi sīmantasya /
31.6.[3]	atrāgneyyā ye ke ca jmetyādikayā caturgṛhītena pradhānayāgaḥ //
32.1.[1]	athetyānantarye sīmantonnayanānantaraṃ puṃsavanasaṃjñakaṃ garbhasaṃskārakarma kartavyamiti // 1 //
32.2-3.[1]	‘daśame māsi sūtave’ iti śruteḥ, darśanācca daśa garbhamāsāḥ /
32.2-3.[2]	tatra pañca ardhabhāgaḥ, ṣaṭ bhūyāṃsaḥ, sapta bhūyiṣṭhāḥ /
32.2-3.[3]	bhūyiṣṭhaḥ saptamo gato yeṣu, teṣu garbhamāseṣu satsu, aṣṭame māsi śiṣṭācārāt /
32.2-3.[4]	trīn sthālīpākān śrapayet āgneyamaindraṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ ca /
32.2-3.[5]	teṣāṃ madhyādanyatamamanyatamaṃ gṛhītvā yathādaivataṃ juhoti /
32.2-3.[6]	yatraikaḥ sthālīpākastatra devatābhede'pi ekaṃ karma dravyadevatāsaṃyogasyaikyāt /
32.2-3.[7]	iha tūbhayabhedāt saṃyogabhedena karmabahulatvam /
32.2-3.[8]	agnistuvītyādinā agniṃ juhoti, indra kṣattramityādinā indram, pra tadviṣṇurityādinā viṣṇum, pumānityādinaikaikasmādbhāgamuddhṛtya sviṣṭakṛtaṃ juhoti //
32.2-3.[9]	agnistuviśravastamaṃ tuvibrahmāṇamuttamam /
32.2-3.[10]	atūrtaṃ śrāvayatpatiṃ putraṃ dadāti dāśuṣe // 1 //
33.1.[1]	anantaraṃ soṣyantīsavanaṃ nāma dṛṣṭārthaṃ karmocyate /
33.1.[2]	yaugikīyaṃ saṃjñā /
33.1.[3]	sūyate'neneti savanaṃ sukhaprasavaṃ karma /
33.1.[4]	soṣyamāṇāyā āsannaprasavāyāḥ savanaṃ soṣyantīsavanam // 1 //
33.2-3.[1]	vijaniṣyamāṇāyā āsannaprasavāyāḥ adbhiḥ sravantaṃ pāṇiṃ śirasyādhāya hṛdayaṃ yāvadabhimṛśet /
33.2-3.[2]	bhartā atra kartā, tadasannidhāvāptaḥ kaściddevarādiḥ // 2 //
33.2-3.[3]	mantramāha /
33.2-3.[4]	anena mantreṇābhimṛśet /
33.2-3.[5]	tathā sati kṣiprameva sukhena prasūyate iti dṛṣṭārthatāmasya karmaṇa āha //
33.2-3.[6]	yathā pratyakṣo vāyurayaṃ vegavāhī pavate dhāvati, yathāvā samudra ejati kampate, evaṃ te tava garbha ejatu tūrṇaṃ prajāyatāṃ, jarāyuṇā garbhāśayena saha avapadyatāṃ nirgacchatu // 3 //
34.1.[1]	putre jāte jātakarma kṛtvā nābhivardhanādanantaraṃ nāma dhīyate saṃkalpyate idaṃ nāma kariṣyate iti kecidvyākurvate, nāmakaraṇaṃ hi ‘ekādaśyāṃ nāma kurvīta puṇye vāhani’ ityaśaucaśuddhau smṛtam /
34.1.[2]	anye vāhuḥ jāte sati ekādaśaṃ tadanantaraṃ vā sulagnaṃ nāmakarmaṇi nātikrāmedityevaṃparametaditi /
34.1.[3]	vayaṃ tu tattvamadūre vakṣyāmaḥ // 1 //
34.2.[1]	nāmna ādau ghoṣavadakṣaraṃ kartavyam madhye cāntasthasaṃjñakam, catvāryakṣarāṇi yatra tat /
34.2.[2]	akṣarāṇi aco'tra halāmanavadhāraṇāt // 2 //
34.3.[1]	yathāvā devatāprasādalabdhatvādyanusāreṇa tadupapadyate, tathā kartavyam // 3 //
34.4.[1]	yatra gṛhe prasavastatra laukikamagnimāhṛtya tatraivājyabhāgāntān homān kṛtvā hiraṇyayukte kāṃsyapātre saṃpātān hutaśeṣabindūnavanayet srāvayet hiraṇyagarbha ityaṣṭābhirāhutibhiḥ /
34.4.[2]	hiraṇyagarbha ityekāhutiḥ /
34.4.[3]	saṃvatsarasya pratimāmiti dvitīyā /
34.4.[4]	kāya svāhā, kasmai svāhā, katamasmai svāhā, prajāpataye svāheti catasraḥ /
34.4.[5]	prajāpate nahi tvaditi dvābhyāṃ dve /
34.4.[6]	evamaṣṭau bhavanti /
34.4.[7]	kecit pradhānakarmatvāccaturgrahītenaiva homa ityāhuḥ //
34.4.[8]	hiraṇyagarbhaḥ samavartatāgre bhūtasya jātaḥ patireka āsīt /
34.4.[9]	sa dādhāra pṛthivīṃ dyāmutemāṃ kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema //
34.4.[10]	eṣā vivāhakāṇḍe vivṛtā //
34.4.[11]	saṃvatsarasya pratimāṃ ye tvā rātryupāsate /
34.4.[12]	teṣāmāyuṣmatī prajāṃ rāyaspoṣeṇa saṃsṛja //
34.4.[13]	he rātri tvaṃ saṃvatsarasya pratimā nirmātrī, tvāṃ ye janāḥ upāsate, teṣāṃ prajāmāyuṣmatīṃ kuru rāyaspoṣeṇa dhanapuṣṭyā saṃsṛja saṃyojaya //
34.4.[14]	kāya svāhā //
34.4.[15]	kāya prajāpataye suhutamastu /
34.4.[16]	kasmai svāhā /
34.4.[17]	katamamai svāhā /
34.4.[18]	prajāpataye svāhā //
34.4.[19]	kaprabhṛtīni catvāri prajāpatināmāni //
34.4.[20]	prajāpate nahi tvadanya etā viśvā jātāni paritābabhūva /
34.4.[21]	yatkāmāste juhumastanno astu svāhā //
34.4.[22]	virāṭ /
34.4.[23]	he prajāpate tvadanyo nāsti ya etāni viśvāni sarvāṇi jātāni janmavanti bhūtāni paribabhūva paribhūtavān vaśīkaroti vyāpnotīti yāvat /
34.4.[24]	etā etāni, viśvā viśvāni ‘śeśchandasi bahulam’ iti śerluk /
34.4.[25]	paritetyatra ta iti varṇāgamaḥ /
34.4.[26]	yatphalaṃ kāmayamānā juhumastanno'stu //
34.4.[27]	asā amuṣya putro'muṣyāsau putraḥ /
34.4.[28]	vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīṇāṃ svāhā //
34.4.[29]	asā amuṣya ceti nāmaviśeṣanirdeśaḥ /
34.4.[30]	asau viṣṇumitro'muṣya yajñamitrasya putra iti pitāputrayordvirnāmoccāraṇaṃ ṣaṣṭhyantasya pitṛnāmno madhye, putranāmna ādyantayoḥ /
34.4.[31]	vayaṃ rayīṇāṃ dhanānāṃ patayaḥ svāminaḥ syāma sampadyemahe //
34.5.[1]	agnerāyurasītyādinā mantreṇa hiraṇyena mukhaṃ medhyaṃ pavitraṃ kṛtvā jalāvilena hastena mukhaṃ spṛṣṭvā bālakasya mātuḥstanānanumantrayate prakṣālya bālakasya pitā, tadasannidhau purohita ekaikayā ṛcā ekaikam, uttamayānyayā tūbhau /
34.5.[2]	tadapekṣameva bahuvacanaṃ stanāniti /
34.5.[3]	madhu vāta iti dakṣiṇam, madhu naktamiti vāmam, madhumānna iti dvau /
34.5.[4]	madhuśabdo jagatprajananasyāmṛtasya nityānandamayasya madhuvidyāprasiddhasya nāma mantratraye jñeyaḥ //
34.5.[5]	madhu vāta ṛtāyate madhu kṣaranti sindhavaḥ /
34.5.[6]	mādhvīrnaḥ santvoṣadhīḥ //
34.5.[7]	madhu naktamutoṣasā madhumatpārthivaṃ rajaḥ /
34.5.[8]	madhu dyaurastu naḥ pitā /
34.5.[9]	madhumānno vanaspatirmadhumāṃ astu sūryaḥ /
34.5.[10]	mādhvīrgāvo bhavantu naḥ //
34.5.[11]	ṛto yajñaḥ /
34.5.[12]	yajñamicchati yaḥ sa ṛtāyacchabdena kyajantena śatrantena cocyate, ṛtāyate yajñamicchate yajamānāya vāto madhu astu amṛtatvakārī bhavatu /
34.5.[13]	sindhavo nadyo madhu jalaṃ kṣaranti kṣarantu /
34.5.[14]	oṣadhīḥ oṣadhyaḥ phalapākāntāḥ mādhvīrmadhurarasasaṃyuktā bhavantu /
34.5.[15]	madhu naktam, utaśabdo'pyarthe, naktaṃ sandhyā, sāpi uṣasā rātryā saha madhvastu naḥ /
34.5.[16]	pārthivaṃ rajaḥ pārthivalokaḥ madhumānastu /
34.5.[17]	dyaurantarikṣaṃ madhvastu naḥ pitā /
34.5.[18]	vanaspatayo madhumantaḥ santu, sūryaścāsmākaṃ madhumānastu, gāvaścāsmākaṃ mādhvīrmādhvyo madhumatyaḥ santu // 5 //
34.6.[1]	suvarṇena saṃpātān sannighṛṣya bālasya mukhe kṛtvā pāyayati /
34.6.[2]	eke punarmanyante madhu ca, madhuyuktān saṃpātān sannighṛṣya pāyayedityarthaḥ /
34.6.[3]	utsargeṇa pitṛkarmakatvāt jātakarmaprabhṛtīnāṃ, pitā brūte he bālaka āyurdhaya piva, evaṃ jarāṃ piva, pīyamānaṃ sampātaghṛtaṃ samadhu vā stanakṣīraṃ ca tavāyurādeḥ kārakamastvityarthaḥ /
34.6.[4]	ūrjamannaṃ balaṃ ca /
34.6.[5]	rāyaspoṣo dhanapuṣṭiḥ /

34.7.[1]	bodhaścametyanuvākam /
34.7.[2]	svārthe ṇic vācayatīti /
34.7.[3]	śiṣṭaṃ spaṣṭam //
34.7.[4]	bodhaśca mā pratībodhava purastādgopāyatāmasvapnaśca mānavadrāṇaśca dakṣiṇato gopāyatāṃ gopāyamānaśca mā rakṣamāṇaśca paścādgopāyatāṃ jāgṛviśva mārundhatī cottarādgopāyatām //
34.7.[5]	anamitraṃ no adharāganamitramudakṛṣi /
34.7.[6]	indrānamitraṃ naḥ paścādanamitraṃ puraskṛdhi //
34.7.[7]	anamiratraihobhiḥ sacemahi viśve devā anamitrā na uṣasaḥ santu nimrucaḥ //
34.7.[8]	yāḥ ṣaḍurvīḥ pañca pradiśastā naḥ pāntu mitradhā no mitre dadhātā abhayaṃ no astu //
34.7.[9]	ye rātrīmanutiṣṭhatha ye ca bhūteṣu jāgṛtha /
34.7.[10]	paśūnye sarvānrakṣatha te na ātmasu jāgṛta /
34.7.[11]	bodha pratībodhāsvapnānavadrāṇa gopāyamāna rakṣamāṇa jāgṛve'rundhati ye devāstanūpāḥ stha te ma iha tanvaṃ pāta bodhapratībodhetyasau vā ādityo bodho'gniḥ pratībodho'svapnānavadrāṇeti candramā vā asvapno'yaṃ yaḥ pavate so'navadrāṇo gopāyamāna rakṣamāṇetyaha gopāyamāno rātrī rakṣamāṇo jāgṛve'rundhatīti yajño vai jāgṛvirdakṣiṇārundhatyete vai devā rāṣṭrabhṛtastāneveṭṭe ātmano gopīthāya //
34.7.[12]	etatsvastyayanaṃ, svastiravināśastasyāyanaṃ prāpaṇaṃ avināśalābhakāraṇam /
34.7.[13]	rāṣṭrabhṛtāmārṣam /
34.7.[14]	rāṣṭraṃ jagadbibhrati dhārayanti puṣṇanti ca ye te rāṣṭrabhṛta ādityādaya ṛtavo'pītyeke /
34.7.[15]	bodhādayo'traivānuvāke purastādvyākhyātāḥ /
34.7.[16]	ādityo bodhaḥ, agniḥ pratībodhaḥ prakāśakatvāt /
34.7.[17]	candramā manorūpeṇāsvapnaḥ satatajāgaraṇāt prāṇarūpo vāyuranavadrāṇaḥ akutsitagatitvāt /
34.7.[18]	divaso gopāyamāno jīvananimittakriyānuṣṭhāpanadvāreṇa, rakṣamāṇo rātriḥ /
34.7.[19]	jāgṛviḥ yajñaḥ prajāpatirūpaḥ ‘yajño vai prajāpatiḥ’ iti śruteḥ sarvāntaryāmirūpeṇa sarvaprāṇiṣu jāgaraṇājjāgṛviḥ, arundhatī dakṣiṇā /
34.7.[20]	sāhi arīnnivārayantī satī yajamānāya phalaṃ dadāti //
34.7.[21]	bodha ādityo māṃ purastāt pūrvasyāṃ diśi gopāyatāṃ rakṣatu, pratībodhaścāgniḥ /
34.7.[22]	asvapnaścandro māṃ dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi gopāyatāṃ, anavadrāṇaśca vāyuḥ /
34.7.[23]	prāṇaḥ gopāyamāno divaso māṃ paścimadigbhāge gopāyatāṃ, rakṣamāṇaśca rātrikālaḥ /
34.7.[24]	jāgṛviryajñaḥ prajāpatiruttaradigbhāge māṃ gopāyatāṃ, arundhatī ca dakṣiṇā /
34.7.[25]	anamitraṃ no'dharāgityaindrī, anuṣṭup /
34.7.[26]	na mitramamitraṃ nāmitramanamitraṃ mitramityarthaḥ nañdvayena prakṛtārthābhidyotanāt /
34.7.[27]	he indra no'smākaṃ adharāgadhastanadigbhāge udakcottaradigbhāge'namitraṃ kṛdhi kuru, yastatrāsmānhiṃsitumicchati, tamanukūlaṃ sampādayetyarthaḥ /
34.7.[28]	evamuttaratra /
34.7.[29]	paścātpaścimadiśi /
34.7.[30]	puraḥ pūrvasyāṃ diśi //
34.7.[31]	anamitrairahobhiriti dve śakkaryuṣṇihau /
34.7.[32]	abhidheyā sarvatra devatā /
34.7.[33]	he viśve devāḥ sarve devā vayaṃ mitrībhūtairahobhiḥ sacemahi, upasaḥ prabhātakālāḥ, nimrucaśca rātrayo'smākaṃ mitrāṇi santu /
34.7.[34]	‘mrucumlucu gatau’ nitāntaṃ gacchatyābhya āditya iti nimrucaḥ //
34.7.[35]	yāḥ ṣaḍdevatā urvī urvyaḥ mahatyaḥ /
34.7.[36]	kāstāḥ //
34.7.[37]	dyauḥ, pṛthivī, ahaḥ, rātriḥ, uṣaḥ, oṣadhayaḥ tathā pañca pradiśaścatasraḥ prāgādyā ūrdhvā pañcamī /
34.7.[38]	tā no'smān pāntu rakṣantu /
34.7.[39]	he anantaroktā yato yūyaṃ mitradhā hitasya kāryasya vidhātryastato no'smān mitre śubhakarmaṇi dadhāta dhārayata, abhayaṃ cāsmākamastu yuṣmatprasādāt //
34.7.[40]	he pradarśitadevā ye yūyaṃ rātrīmanutiṣṭhatha rātrīṃ lakṣaṇīkṛtya tiṣṭhatha, ye ca bhūteṣu jāgṛtha, sarvāṃśca paśūn rakṣatha, te no'smākaṃ sambandhiṣu ātmasu śarīreṣu jāgṛta //
34.7.[41]	bodha pratībodhetyādināṣṭānāṃ saṃbodhanam /
34.7.[42]	he bodhādayaḥ arundhatīparyantāḥ ye yūyaṃ devāstanūpāḥ stha tanūnāṃ śarīrāṇāṃ rakṣakā bhavatha, te me mama iha gahane bhave tanvaṃ tanūṃ pāta rakṣata /
34.7.[43]	bodhādīn pratīkairavacchidya vyācaṣṭe bodhapratībodhetyādinā, gatārthametat /
34.7.[44]	ete vai devāḥ, vaiśabdo'vadhāraṇe, eta eva bodhādayo rāṣṭrasya jagato bhartāra ṛtavaśca, ato'haṃ tāneveṭṭe staumi /
34.7.[45]	kimartham /
34.7.[46]	ātmano gopīthāya rakṣaṇāya /
34.7.[47]	anyānyapyatra svastyayanāni paṭhanīyāni /
34.7.[48]	vaciśvarādau paṭhyate, tataḥ svārthe ṇic svastyayanaṃ vācayatīti /
34.7.[49]	tena yuktaṃ svakartṛkaṃ vacanaṃ pituḥ /
34.7.[50]	svakartṛkāṇi hyetānyutsargeṇa prāk cūḍākaraṇāt // 7 //
35.1.[1]	bālakasūtikayoḥ rakṣārthā aśaucakāle'mī homāḥ, ataśca dṛṣṭārthā eva /
35.1.[2]	phalīkaraṇaṃ kambukāḥ, tairmiśritānsarṣapāndarvyā daśāhaṃ yāvat sāyaṃprātarjuhuyāt śaṇḍa ityādicaturbhirmantraiḥ //
35.1.[3]	śaṇḍo markopavītastauṇḍuleya ulūkhalaścapalo naśyatāmitaḥ svāhā // 1 //
35.1.[4]	iha sūtikāsthānācchaṇḍādayo naśyantu palāyantāmiti samudāyārthaḥ /
35.1.[5]	śaṇḍādayaḥ piśācānāṃ saṃjñāḥ /
35.1.[6]	ekaiko mantrasaṃbandhaḥ /
35.1.[7]	śaṇḍa itaḥ sthānānnaśyatu, evaṃ markaḥ, upavītaḥ, tauṇḍuleyaḥ, ulūkhalaścapalo naśyatāmitaḥ /
35.1.[8]	svāhā suhutamastu // 1 //
35.1.[9]	ālikhannavalikhankiṃvadanta ulūkhalaścapalo naśyatāmitaḥ svāhā // 2 //
35.1.[10]	samānaṃ pūrveṇaitat // 2 //

35.1.[12]	keśinī śvalominī kacā kaucāpakāśinyapeto naśyatāmitaḥ svāhā // 4 //
35.1.[13]	haryakṣaṇa ityādayaḥ saṃjñāḥ /
35.1.[14]	keśinī nāma rākṣasī /
35.1.[15]	tathā śvalominī, kacā, kaucā, apakāśinītyetānyapi rākṣasīviśeṣanāmāni // 4 //
35.2.[1]	anena prakāracatuṣṭayena daśāhaṃ juhuyāt aśaucakālaṃ yāvajjuhuyādityarthaḥ // 2 //
36.0.[1]	atha nāmakaraṇam
36.1.[1]	daśamyāṃ vyatītāyāmaśaucaśuddhāvekādaśe'hani dvādaśe'hani vā tatra nakṣatrādivaiguṇye dināntare nāmadheyaṃ daśamyāṃ dvādaśyāṃ vāpi kārayet ‘puṇye'hani muhūrte vā nakṣatre vā guṇānvite /’ iti smaraṇāt /
36.1.[2]	audayikyā ca vyavasthayā trayodaśī tithirgṛhyate, natvanyāyyādutthānādanyāyyācca saṃveśanādanadyatanakāla ityādikayā, ‘rātriśeṣe dvābhyāṃ prabhāte tisṛbhiḥ’ iti vibhātāyāmapi rajanyāmudayāt prāgaśaucānuvṛttidarśanāt /
36.1.[3]	tasminneva sūtikāgārasthe sūtakāgnau payasi sthālīpākaṃ śrapayitvā sarvoṣadhiprabhṛtibhiḥ sugandhidravyaviśeṣairuparivinihitamaṅgalārthajātīpūgaphalaviśeṣaiḥ saśiraskaṃ snāpayitvā, puṃliṅganirdeśāt striyaṃ varjayati, anupabhuktena vastreṇa saṃcchādya tasya sthālīpākasya saṃbandhibhiravadānairvyatyayena sthālīpākena juhoti kayā naścitreti pañcāhutīḥ // 1 //
36.2.[1]	agnerāyurasītyādikamāyuṣeṣṭyā tulyamityatideśaḥ /
36.2.[2]	avadhimāha ā lalāṭābhimarśanāt /
36.2.[3]	‘tasya lalāṭamabhimṛśyāśvinoḥ prāṇa iti japati’ iti vakṣyati /
36.2.[4]	tadanantaramāyuṣeṣṭyā samānamityarthaḥ // 2 //
36.3.[1]	atrānuvāke asāvityasya sthāne tadeva nāma dhīyate yattu jātakarmaṇi kṛtaṃ, nānyat // 3 //
36.4.[1]	eke punarāhuranyadvidhīyate /
36.4.[2]	dve hi nāmnī brāhmaṇasya kartavye /
36.4.[3]	tatra yadrahasyaṃ jātakarmaṇyuktaṃ ‘putre jāte nāma dhīyate’ iti, tasya prayojanaṃ parairabhicāre kriyamāṇe'nuccāraṇādi, prakaṭaṃ tvekādaśāhādau vyāvahārikam /
36.4.[4]	tathāca śrutiḥ ‘tasmādbrāhmaṇo dvināmā’ iti // 4 //
36.5.[1]	sviṣṭakṛtaḥ pūrvaṃ pūtamājyaṃ kāṃsyapātre āsicya prakṣipya, tatra ca hiraṇyaṃ prakṣipya agnerāyurasītyādinā mantreṇa /
36.5.[2]	kīdṛśaṃ suvarṇam /
36.5.[3]	ābandhanīyaṃ bālakasya kaṇṭhādau bandhanārham /
36.5.[4]	tasyājyasya juhoti indrasya prāṇa ityādibhiḥ pañcabhirmantraiḥ // 5 //
36.6.[1]	saṃsthitayajurhomātpūrvaṃ brahmā ghṛte hiraṇyamavapadyate avaṣṭabhnāti yattadbālagalādibandhanārthaṃ ghṛte nihitaṃ sarve ca ṛtvijastadvaṣṭabhnanti yadasarpa ityādimantraiḥ // 6 //
36.7.[1]	ājyātsuvarṇaṃ pāvamānenetyuddhṛtya yajamānāya prayacchati devā āyuṣmanta ityādimantraiḥ //
36.8-9.[1]	tat suvarṇaniḥsrāvamājyaṃ bālakaḥ pibati /
36.8-9.[2]	tacca niḥśeṣeṇāvadhayet pibet // 8 //
36.8-9.[3]	hiraṇyalagnaṃ ghṛtaṃ prakṣālya taddhiraṇyaṃ badhnāti bālakasya galādau imamagna ityādinā // 9 //
36.10.[1]	lalāṭataṭaṃ hastena spṛṣṭvā japati aśvinoḥ prāṇa ityādikam // 10 //
36.11.[1]	aṅgādaṅgādityādinā bālasya mūrdhani śiṅghanaṃ kṛtvā svastyayanaṃ vakti /

36.11.[4]	ṛtvigvā pituḥ prayojako vivakṣitaḥ // 11 //
36.12.[1]	ato nāmakaraṇādūrdhvaṃ yadā pravāsādāyāti pitā, tadānenaiva prakāreṇa mūrdhanyabhighrāṇaṃ kuryāt // 12 //
36.12.[2]	evameva pratimāsaṃ janmadine sthālīpākena jātakarmavidhivadājyeneṣṭā nighrāṇaṃ mūrdhani kuryāt // 13 //
36.12.[3]	pratimāsamimāṃ kartavyatāṃ saṃvatsaraṃ yāvakuryāt // 14 //
36.13.[1]	māṃsaṃ tu bālakasya mātā pitā ca saṃvatsaraṃ yāvannāśnīyāt // 15 //
36.14.[1]	prathame saṃvatsare samāpte ajenāgnimavinā dhanvantarimiṣṭvā vāśabdādājyena sthālīpākena vā sarpiṣā pracureṇa yuktamanyena ca pavitreṇa dadhiprabhṛtinā annaṃ brāhmaṇān bhojayet /
36.14.[2]	taiḥ suprītaiḥ svastyayanāśīḥprabhṛtibhirabhinandedenam // 16 //
36.14.[3]	kayā naścitra ābhuvadūtī sadāvṛdhaḥ sakhā /
36.14.[4]	kayā śaciṣṭhayā vṛtā // 1 //

36.14.[10]	avanamūtiḥ ‘supāṃ sulukpūrvasavarṇā .....’ iti tṛtīyaikavacanasya pūrvasavarṇaikādeśaḥ ūtīśabdālluk ca /
36.14.[11]	kīdṛśaḥ prajāpatiḥ /

36.14.[13]	kīdṛśānasmān /

36.14.[15]	kayā vṛtā vartanenābhāvayati /
36.14.[16]	kayā śaciṣṭhayā śaktyatiśayena caitanyātiśayena vā atiśayena śaktitā śaciṣṭhā ‘turiṣṭhemeyaḥsu’ iti tṛco lopaḥ, chāndaso varṇavyatyayaścakāraḥ, kena śaktyatiśayena vartayedityarthaḥ /
36.14.[17]	sraṣṭṛtvādiśaktyatiśayayuktaḥ prajāpatirvṛddhiviṣaye ṛtāvasmābhirijyate, sa iṣṭyā prītaḥ san bālaṃ vṛddhyādisaṃyuktaṃ saṃpādayatviti tātparyārthaḥ //
36.14.[18]	he prajāpate ko yajamānaḥ tvā matsat mādayati, andhaso'ndhasā haviṣā, dṛḍhā dṛḍhāni, vasu vasūni dhanāni, āruje ārujati vitarati dakṣiṇādidvāreṇa /
36.14.[19]	kīdṛśo yajamānaḥ /
36.14.[20]	satyaḥ uttamasattvaḥ, tathā madānāṃ maṃhiṣṭhaḥ hṛṣṭānāmānandayogināṃ madhye vṛddhatamaḥ paramānandayukto brahmasvabhāva ityarthaḥ /
36.14.[21]	‘bahi mahi vṛddha’ iti dhātoḥ prakṛtitvaṃ maṃhiṣṭhaśabde iṣṭhannante //
36.14.[22]	kayā tacchṛṇve śacyā śaciṣṭho yayā kṛṇoti muhu kācidṛṣvaḥ /
36.14.[23]	puru dāśuṣe vicayiṣṭho aṃho'thā dadhāti draviṇaṃ jaritre /
36.14.[24]	atrāpi prajāpatirdevatā /
36.14.[25]	ahaṃ śṛṇve śṛṇomi vedāt /
36.14.[26]	kiṃ tat /
36.14.[27]	kācidevāsya prajāpateḥ śaktirlokottarāsti prajñā vā /
36.14.[28]	kā /
36.14.[29]	yayā śacyā śaktyā prajñayā vā sa ṛṣvo mahattamaḥ puru aṃhaḥ pāpaṃ muhurmuhuḥ punaḥpunaḥ kṛṇoti kṛntati nāśayati /
36.14.[30]	kasmai /
36.14.[31]	dāśuṣe yajamānāya /

36.14.[33]	kīdṛśaḥ prajāpatiḥ /

36.14.[40]	anena hiraṇyaṃ ghṛte'vadadhāti /
36.14.[41]	he suvarṇa asi tvamagnerāyuḥ, āyātītyāyuḥ, agnerāgataṃ tvamutpannamityarthaḥ /
36.14.[42]	tathāca śrutiḥ ‘agneryadretaḥ sicyate taddhiraṇyamabhavat’ iti /
36.14.[43]	tasyaivaṃbhūtajananasya te tava manuṣyā āyuṣkṛta indhanādhmānanirmanthanajāgaraṇādinā manuṣyā agnerāyuḥ kurvanti, taddvāreṇa suvarṇasya /
36.14.[44]	tena manuṣyāṇāmupakārakatvādasmai yajamānāya, amuṣmai ca bālakāyāyurdehi kuru vā //
36.14.[45]	indrasya prāṇaḥ sa te prāṇaṃ dadātu yasya prāṇastasmai te svāhā //
36.14.[46]	indro'tra devatā /
36.14.[47]	indrasya prāṇaḥ, indraḥ prāṇasya svāmī, ataḥ sa indrastubhyaṃ prāṇaṃ dadātu /
36.14.[48]	yasya prāṇastasmai indrāya te tubhyaṃ svāhā //
36.14.[49]	pitṝṇāṃ prāṇaste te prāṇaṃ dadatu yeṣāṃ prāṇastebhyo vaḥ svāhā //
36.14.[50]	pitṛdevatāko yataḥ pitṛsvāmikaḥ prāṇo‘taste pitaraste tubhyaṃ prāṇaṃ dadatu /
36.14.[51]	yeṣāṃ prāṇastebhyaḥ pitṛbhyo vo yuṣmākaṃ suhutamastu /
36.14.[52]	marutāṃ prāṇaste° viśveṣāṃ devānāṃ prāṇaste° prajāpateḥ prāṇaḥ sa te prāṇaṃ dadātu parameṣṭhinaḥ prāṇaḥ sa te prāṇaṃ dadātu yayoḥ prāṇastābhyāṃ vāṃ svāhā //
36.14.[53]	prajāpatiḥ prāṇasya svāmī /
36.14.[54]	sa tubhyaṃ prāṇaṃ dadātu /
36.14.[55]	parameṣṭhī prāṇasya prabhuḥ /
36.14.[56]	sa tubhyaṃ prāṇaṃ dadātu /
36.14.[57]	ubhayoḥ prajāpatiparameṣṭhinoryayoḥ prāṇastābhyāṃ vāṃ yuvābhyāṃ svāhā //
36.14.[58]	yadasarpastatsarpirabhavo yannavamaistannavanītamabhavo yadapriyathāstaddhṛtamabhavaḥ //
36.14.[59]	ghṛtaṃ nirucyate he ghṛta yat yasmāttvamasarpaḥ sṛptaṃ, tataḥ sarpirbhūtamasi /
36.14.[60]	yasmācca navaṃ pratyagraṃ sat aiḥ āgatamasi, tato navanītamucyase /
36.14.[61]	yasmādadhriyathāstaddhṛtaṃ bhūtamasi ‘dhṛ dhāraṇe’ ityasya varṇavyatyaye ghṛtaśabdaḥ //
36.14.[62]	ghṛtasya dhārāmamṛtasya panthāmindreṇa dattaṃ prayataṃ marudbhiḥ /
36.14.[63]	tattvā viṣṇuranvapaśyattaveḍā gavyairayat //
36.14.[64]	viṣṇorārṣam /
36.14.[65]	dhārāṃ panthāmiti prathamāyāḥ sthāne dvitīyā /
36.14.[66]	yeyaṃ ghṛtasya dhārā, sā amṛtasya amaraṇadharmasya panthā upāyaḥ /
36.14.[67]	idaṃ hi ghṛtamindreṇa yajamānebhyo dattaṃ vṛṣṭyādidvāreṇa, prayataṃ ca marudbhiḥ prakarṣeṇa yataṃ niyamya sthāpitaṃ vacanādidvāreṇa /
36.14.[68]	tat dīyamānaṃ niyamyamānaṃ ca tvāṃ viṣṇurapaśyat /
36.14.[69]	tattvāmiḍā devatāviśeṣaḥ gavi airayannikṣiptavatī //
36.14.[70]	pāvamānena tvā stomena gāyatryā vartanyopāṃśorvīryeṇoddharāmyasau //
36.14.[71]	pāvamānena stomena barhiṣpavamānādinā, gāyatryā varcā, vartanyā sāmāvayavena, upāṃśorgrahasya vīryeṇa sāmarthyena uddharāmi tvām /
36.14.[72]	asāviti nāma pratīyāt //
36.14.[73]	bṛhatā tvā rathantareṇa triṣṭubhā vartanyā śukrasya vīryeṇotsṛjāmyasau //
36.14.[74]	gatārtham //
36.14.[75]	agnestvā mātrayā jagatyā vartanyā devastvā savitonnayatu jīvātave jīvanasya yā asau //
36.14.[76]	agnerunnayāmīti vipariṇatasyānuṣaṅgaḥ, natūddharāmītyasyānuṣaṅgaḥ ‘vyavayānnānuṣajyeta’ iti nyāyāt /

36.14.[80]	āyuṣmantaste'mṛtenāyuṣmantasteṣāmayamāyuṣāyuṣmānastvasau // 1 //
36.14.[81]	teṣāmāyuṣā devānāmāyuṣā tatparimāṇena jīvanena ayaṃ yajamāno bālaścāyuṣmānastu /

36.14.[83]	brahmāyuṣmattadbrāhmaṇairāyuṣmattasyāyamāyuṣāyuṣmānastvasau // 2 //
36.14.[84]	brahma vedaḥ /
36.14.[85]	taccāyuṣmadavināśi /
36.14.[86]	taddhi brāhmaṇairbrahmasambandhibhiradhyayanadhāraṇādibhiranucchittikarmakam /
36.14.[87]	tasyāyamityādi pūrvavat //
36.14.[88]	agnirāyuṣmānsa vanaspatibhirāyuṣmāṃstasyāyamāyuṣāyuṣmānastvasau // 3 //
36.14.[89]	vanaspataya indhanāni araṇyaṃ ca /
36.14.[90]	samānamanyat //
36.14.[91]	yajña āyuṣmānsa dakṣiṇābhirāyuṣmāṃstasyāyamāyuṣāyuṣmānastvasau // 4 //
36.14.[92]	dakṣiṇālobhena ṛtvijaḥ abhyasyanti yajñavidyāṃ samyaganutiṣṭhanti ca karmāṇi /
36.14.[93]	tena dakṣiṇayā āyuṣmattvaṃ yajñasya //
36.14.[94]	soma āyuṣmānsa oṣadhībhirāyuṣmāṃstasyāyamāyuṣāyumānastvasau // 5 //
36.14.[95]	oṣadhayo vrīhyādyāḥ, tābhiḥ /
36.14.[96]	carupuroḍāśādinā iṣṭamannādi candramasamāpyāyayatīti kṛtvā bhavatyoṣadhībhirāyuṣmān somaḥ //
36.14.[97]	oṣadhaya āyuṣmatīstā adbhirāyuṣmatīstāsāmayamāyuṣāyuṣmānastvasau // 6 //
36.14.[98]	vṛṣṭyā vardhante dhriyante cauṣadhayaḥ //
36.14.[99]	imamagna āyuṣe varcase kṛdhi tigmamojo varuṇa saṃśiśādhi /
36.14.[100]	mātevāsmā adite śarma yaccha viśve devā jaradaṣṭiryathāsat //
36.14.[101]	he agne imaṃ bālakaṃ yajamānaṃ ca āyuṣe varcase ca kṛdhi kuru, vidyāsaṃpattirvarcaḥ yathā etasyāyurvarcaśca bhavati tathā kurvityarthaḥ /
36.14.[102]	he varuṇa tvamapi tigmamutkaṭamojo balaṃ saṃśiśādhi samyak saṃpādaya /
36.14.[103]	he adite devamātastvamasmai śarma sukhaṃ yaccha dehi māteva jananī yathā /
36.14.[104]	he viśve devā yūyaṃ yathā jaradaṣṭirasat bhavati, tathā kuruta, jarāmaśnoti vyāpnoti jaradaṣṭiḥ, jarājarjaritaśarīramenaṃ kurutetyarthaḥ //
36.14.[105]	aśvinoḥ prāṇastau te prāṇaṃ dattāṃ tena jīva /
36.14.[106]	mitrāvaruṇayoḥ prāṇastau te prāṇaṃ dattāṃ tena jīva //
36.14.[107]	bṛhaspateḥ prāṇaḥ sa te prāṇaṃ dadātu tena jīva /
36.14.[108]	aśvināvatra devatā /
36.14.[109]	aśviprabhṛtibhirdattena prāṇena jīveti gatārtham //
36.14.[110]	aṅgādaṅgātsaṃbhavasi hṛdayādabhijāyase /
36.14.[111]	ātmā vai putranāmāsi jīva śaradaḥ śataṃ paśya śaradaḥ śatam //
36.14.[112]	sarvāṅgaparisrutarasasāravīryasaṃbhūtatvādaṅgādaṅgātsamyagbhavasi, hṛdayasaṃkalpitamanorathasaṃbhūtatvācca hṛdayādādhikyena jāyase /
36.14.[113]	vaiśabdo'vadhāraṇe /
36.14.[114]	kiṃ bahu brūmahe, ātmā vai putranāmāsi, tvaṃ maccharīreṇa saṃbhūtatvānmadīyameva mūrtyantaramasi putranāmāṅkitamupakāritaramityarthaḥ /
36.14.[115]	evaṃbhūtastvaṃ śaradāṃ śataṃ prāṇāndhāraya paśya ca paṭvindriyo bhava varṣaśatam /
36.14.[116]	evaṃ hi garbhādhānādi nāmakaraṇāntaṃ vyākhyātam /
36.14.[117]	anantaraṃ cūḍākarma sūtrakāreṇoktam /
36.14.[118]	smṛtiṣu hi niṣkramaṇānnaprāśane nāmakāraṇānantaramukte ‘tṛtīye māsi kartavyaṃ śiśorniṣkramaṇaṃ gṛhāt /’ ‘ṣaṣṭhe māsyannaprāśanaṃ kartavyam’ ityādinā, tena te'pi avaśyakartavye /
36.14.[119]	candradarśanaṃ cāto gṛhyāntarānusāreṇehāpi darśayati // 16 //
37.1-2.[1]	janmanaḥ prabhṛti māsadvaye vyatīte tṛtīyasya māsasya prathamārdhe'tīte ādityasya darśanaṃ bālaḥ kārayitavyaḥ /
37.1-2.[2]	tatreyamitikartavyatā /
37.1-2.[3]	puṇyadine jyotiḥśāstraśuddhe, parvaṇi vā sunakṣatrādiyogini darśanaṃ kārayitavya ityekasyaiva parvaṇa itaratithisamudāyena saha vikalpadarśanādutkarṣātiśayaḥ pratīyate /
37.1-2.[4]	udite evāditye rathacakraparimāṇaṃ sthaṇḍilamupalipya, gehāṅgane ādityaraśmyalaṅkṛte tatropalite pratiṣṭhāpya laukikamagniṃ yathoktamupasamādhāya upasamādhānamuddhatāvokṣaṇaparisamūhanaparyukṣaṇaparistaraṇapavitrakaraṇājyavilayanājyavīkṣaṇāgnyupasthānarūpaṃ kṛtvā, tato jayaprabhṛtibhirjayākārairāghārādājyabhāgāntairhutvā taraṇirviśvadarśata iti divo rukma iti udu tyamiti citraṃ devānāmiti catasṛbhirājyasya juhoti // 1 //
37.3.[1]	juhotītyanuṣajyate /
37.3.[2]	mitro janāniti pra sa mitreti ca dvābhyāṃ sthālīpākasya juhoti // 2 //
37.4.[1]	abhyāvartasvetyādinā mantreṇa kumāramabhimukhaṃ kṛtvā unnamayyānayati pitā gururvā // 3 //
37.5.[1]	draṣṭre nama upadraṣṭre nama ityādinā bālasya pitā ādityopasthānaṃ karoti bālaṃ sammukhaṃ kṛtvotsaṅge // 4 //
37.6.[1]	bahughṛtadadhyādiyuktaṃ haviṣmadannaṃ brāhmaṇānbhojayet //
37.6.[2]	taraṇirviśvadarśato jyotiṣkṛdasi sūrya /
37.6.[3]	viśvamābhāsi rocanam //
37.6.[4]	prajāpaterārṣamuttaratrāpi /
37.6.[5]	gāyatrī /
37.6.[6]	sūryo devatā /
37.6.[7]	he sūrya asi tvaṃ taraṇistārayati saṃsārasāgarāditi taraṇiḥ, tathā darśato draṣṭurviśvasya sarvasya jyotiṣkṛt prakāśakārī andhatamasasyāpasārakaḥ, viśvamābhāsi rocanaṃ yatkiṃcidrocanaṃ prakāśamānaṃ tadviśvaṃ samastaṃ tvamevābhāsi prajāpatirūpaḥ //
37.6.[8]	divo rukma urucakṣā udeti dūre arthastaraṇirbhrājamānaḥ /
37.6.[9]	nūnaṃ janāḥ sūryeṇa prasūtā ayannarthāni kṛṇavannapāṃsi //
37.6.[10]	ayamādityo dūre udeti dūraṃ gacchati ceṣṭate /
37.6.[11]	kutaḥ /
37.6.[12]	divaḥ antarikṣāt /
37.6.[13]	rukmaḥ ‘ruca dīptau’ dīptaḥ, suvarṇavarṇo vā /
37.6.[14]	urucakṣā bṛhaddarśanaḥ /
37.6.[15]	arthaḥ aryate prāpyate ardhyate vā mokṣārthibhirityartho brahmā /
37.6.[16]	taraṇirvyākhyātaḥ /
37.6.[17]	bhrājamāno dīpyamānaḥ /
37.6.[18]	jāyanta iti janāstrayo lokā nūnaṃ niścitaṃ kṛtvā sūryeṇa prasūtā janitā jagatāṃ prajāpativivartatvāt brahmapariṇāmatvādvā sūryasya ca brahmātmakatvāt /
37.6.[19]	ayaṃ hi sūryaḥ apāṃsyannāni āviṣkurvan vṛṣṭidvāreṇa arthāṃśca yāgadānādīn vegenāryamāṇānayanpravartayan divasakaraṇadvāreṇa dṛśyate /
37.6.[20]	‘udu tyaṃ’ ‘citraṃ devānāṃ’ ‘mitro janā’niti vyākhyātāḥ //
37.6.[21]	pra sa mitra marto astu prayasvānyasta āditya śikṣate vratena /
37.6.[22]	na hanyate na jīyate tvoto nainamaṃho aśnotyantito na dūrāt //
37.6.[23]	he mitra āditya yo marto martyastava vratena vrataṃ karma śikṣate, sa prayasvān annavān prāstu prakarṣeṇa bhavatu /
37.6.[24]	yaḥ tvotaḥ tvayā rakṣitaḥ, sa na kenaciddhanyate, na jīyate parābhūyate /
37.6.[25]	nāpyenamaṃhaḥ pāpamaśnoti vyāpnoti antitaḥ antikāt, nāpi dūrāt //
37.6.[26]	abhyāvartasva pṛthivi yajñena payasā saha /
37.6.[27]	vapāṃ te agniriṣito arohat //
37.6.[28]	he pṛthivi yajñena payasā ca saha abhyāvartasva mama sāmmukhyena āgaccha, prasannā bhūtvā māṃ payasvantaṃ yājñikaṃ ca sampādaya /
37.6.[29]	agniriṣitaḥ preṣitaḥ san te tava va sāraṃ vedimarohat ārohatu //
37.6.[30]	draṣṭre nama upadraṣṭre namo'nudraṣṭre namaḥ khyātre nama upakhyātre namo'nukhyātre namaḥ śṛṇvate nama upaśṛṇvate namaḥ sate namo'sate namo jātāya namo janiṣyamāṇāya namo bhūtāya namo bhaviṣyate namaścakṣuṣe namaḥ śrotrāya namo manase namo vāce namo brahmaṇe namaḥ śrāntāya namastapase namaḥ //
37.6.[31]	ghorāṇāmārṣam /
37.6.[32]	ādityaḥ stūyate parabrahmarūpatvātsarvamayatvena /
37.6.[33]	draṣṭā jīvātmā, upadraṣṭā antaryāmī /
37.6.[34]	tasmai ubhayātmane namaḥ /
37.6.[35]	vedādipramāṇena dṛṣṭaṃ dharmādikamanu paścādyogābhyāsena sphuṭaṃ paśyatītyanudraṣṭā yogyātmā, tasmai namaḥ /
37.6.[36]	khyātīti khyātā prakāśamānaḥ sarvo loko dharmirūpaḥ, upakhyātā dharmo rūpādiḥ, anukhyātā dharmādharmarūpādigataḥ /
37.6.[37]	śiṣṭaṃ spaṣṭam //
37.6.[38]	adṛśrannasya ketavo viraśmayo janāṁ anu /
37.6.[39]	bhrājanto agnayo yathā //
37.6.[40]	asya ādityasya ketavaḥ aśvā raśmayo vā adṛśran dṛśyante janānanu jāyamānāṁllakṣaṇīkṛtya /
37.6.[41]	viraśmayo vigatarajjavo bandhanaśūnyā ityarthaḥ /
37.6.[42]	bhrājanto dedīpyamānā agniprakhyāḥ //
38.1.[1]	evaṃśabdena rathacakraparimāṇasthaṇḍilopalepanāntasyātideśaḥ // 1 //
38.1.[2]	viśeṣamāha
38.2-5.[1]	navo nava ityanena mantreṇa candramasaḥ upasthānaṃ kartavyam /
38.2-5.[2]	prakāśa ādarśo dakṣiṇā dātavyā //
38.2-5.[3]	makṣūdhātā mātariśvā vacobhiścandro amṛtādvardhate jāyamānaḥ /
38.2-5.[4]	āyuḥ prajāmamṛtaṃ saubhagatvaṃ pra candramāstirate dīrghamāyuḥ //
38.2-5.[5]	candramā dīrghamāyuḥ pratirate pratiratu dadātu, tathā prajāṃ putrādikāmamṛtamamaraṇadharmakatvaṃ saubhagatvaṃ saubhāgyaṃ lokapriyatvam /
38.2-5.[6]	dvirāyurgrahaṇamatiśayārtham /
38.2-5.[7]	sa hi pratipadādāvamṛtāt parabrahmaṇo jāyamāno vardhate pratidinam /
38.2-5.[8]	auṇādiko'siḥpratyayaḥ /
38.2-5.[9]	pūjitasya caturthapuruṣārthasya dhātā vidhātā bhavati //
38.2-5.[10]	bhūyo jāto haviṣaścandramā asmātpūrṇaḥ purastātpayaso havirbhiḥ /
38.2-5.[11]	payo garbho devatā pinvamānaścandro'mṛtatvamabhayaṃ kṛṇotu //
38.2-5.[12]	payobhiśca bhūyaḥ punaḥ punarbahukṛtvo vā payaḥ kṣīraṃ, garbhaḥ garbhān devatā yajñoddeśyāḥ pinvamāna oṣadhyādyāpyāyanamukhena poṣayaṃścandro duḥkhabhayarahitamamṛtatvaṃ me karotu //
38.2-5.[13]	āpyāyasva sametu te viśvataḥ soma vṛṣṇyam /
38.2-5.[14]	bhavā vājasya saṅgathe //
38.2-5.[15]	he soma āpyāyasva vardhayāsmān /
38.2-5.[16]	vṛṣṇyaṃ sektṛtvamāpyāyakatvaṃ te tava viśvataḥ sarvataḥ sametu samāgacchatu /
38.2-5.[17]	kiṃca vājasyānnasya saṅgathe sambandhanimittaṃ bhava //
38.2-5.[18]	saṃ te payāṃsi samu yantu vājāḥ saṃ vṛṣṇyānyabhimātiṣāhaḥ /
38.2-5.[19]	āpyāyamāno amṛtāya soma divi śravāṃsyuttamāni diṣva //
38.2-5.[20]	he soma te tava payāṃsi saṃyantu tvayā saṃgacchantām /
38.2-5.[21]	vājā vājāni annāni ca saṃgacchantām /
38.2-5.[22]	vṛṣṇyāni ca āpyāyakatvāni tvayā saṃgacchantām /
38.2-5.[23]	kīdṛśasya tava /
38.2-5.[24]	abhimātiṣāhaḥ saṅgrāmāṇāṃ prasoḍhurabhibhavituḥ /
38.2-5.[25]	he soma asmābhirāpyāyamāno haviṣā amṛtatvāya bhava svargāyetyarthaḥ /
38.2-5.[26]	śravāṃsi cānnānyuttamāni dehi yajñopayogīni //
38.2-5.[27]	navo navo bhavati jāyamāno'hnāṃ keturuṣasāmetyagram /
38.2-5.[28]	bhāgaṃ devebhyo vidadhātyāyanpra candramāstirate dīrghamāyuḥ //
38.2-5.[29]	ayaṃ candramāḥ pratipadādau vardhamāno navo navo bhavati /
38.2-5.[30]	ahnāṃ dinānāmuṣasāṃ ca rajanyantānāmagrametyāgacchati ketuścihnabhūtaḥ pratipadādikālasya sūcakatvāt /
38.2-5.[31]	kiṃca bhāgaṃ devebhyo dadātyamṛtamayatvādamṛtasya ca dīrghamāyuḥ pratirate /
38.2-5.[32]	iti candradarśanam //
39.1.[1]	prasavādārabhya ṣaṣṭhe māse bālakasyānnaprāśanaṃ kartavyam // 1 //
39.2.[1]	sarvāṇi haviṣyānnāni miśrīkṛtya āyurdā deva iti ghṛtapratīka iti ca dvābhyāṃ hutvā annapate annasyeti mantreṇa kumāramannaṃ prāśayet //
39.2.[2]	āyurdā deva jarasaṃ vṛṇāno ghṛtaṃ vasāno ghṛtapṛṣṭho agne /
39.2.[3]	ghṛtaṃ pibannamṛtaṃ cāru gavyaṃ piteva putraṃ jarasaṃ nayemam //
39.2.[4]	he agne gavyaṃ goprabhavamamṛtamamṛtatvakāri, cāru utkṛṣṭaṃ ghṛtaṃ piban imaṃ bālaṃ jarasaṃ naya vṛddhatvaṃ prāpaya /
39.2.[5]	ka iva kam /
39.2.[6]	piteva putram /
39.2.[7]	he deva dyotamāna āyurdā āyuṣo dātā tvaṃ, ato jarasaṃ jarāṃ vṛṇāno vardhayan ghṛtaṃ ca vasāna ācchādayan vitaran ghṛtapṛṣṭhaḥ san hūyamānenoparivartinā ghṛtena yuktaḥ san jarasaṃ nayemam //
39.2.[8]	ghṛtapratīko ghṛtapṛṣṭho agnirghṛtāhavano ghṛtamasya dhāma /
39.2.[9]	ghṛtapruṣo haritastvā vahantu ghṛtaṃ pibanyajatāddeva devān //
39.2.[10]	triṣṭup /
39.2.[11]	āgneyī /
39.2.[12]	ghṛtaṃ pratikāyati āhvayati yaḥ, sa ghṛtapratīkaḥ /
39.2.[13]	ghṛtapṛṣṭho vyākhyātaḥ /
39.2.[14]	ghṛtasya ā samantāt havanaṃ homo yatra, sa ghṛtāhavanaḥ /
39.2.[15]	tathā ghṛtamasyāgnerdhāma gṛham /
39.2.[16]	yatastvamevaṃbhūto'gnirato he bhagavan deva agne ghṛtapruṣo ghṛtakaṇāḥ harito'śvā iva tvāṃ vahantu prāpnuvantu āpyāyantvityarthaḥ /
39.2.[17]	tvaṃ ca ghṛtaṃ piban he deva devān yaja pūjaya prīṇīhi /
39.2.[18]	agnidvāreṇa hi devānāṃ tṛptirbhavati //
39.2.[19]	annapate annasya no dehyanamīvasya śuṣmiṇaḥ /
39.2.[20]	pra pradātāraṃ tāriṣa ūrja no dehi dvipade catuṣpade //
39.2.[21]	he annapate somarāja ‘somo vā oṣadhīnāṃ rājā’ iti śruteḥ annasya no dehi annamasmabhyaṃ prayaccha, anamīvasya śuṣmiṇaḥ, amīvo rogastadrahitaṃ, śuṣmaṃ sukhaṃ sukhakāri /
39.2.[22]	pradātāraṃ pratāriṣaḥ, prakarṣeṇa tāraya saṃsārasāgarakleśamapasārayāsya /
39.2.[23]	ūrjamannaṃ balaṃ ca no'smākaṃ dehi dvipade catuṣpade ca gavāśvādike /
39.2.[24]	ityannaprāśanam //
40.1.[1]	janmanaḥ prabhṛti yastṛtīyo varṣastasya bhūyiṣṭhe bhāge gate sati cūḍākarma kartavyam /
40.1.[2]	ardhamavadhiṃ kṛtvā saptamo māso bhūyān, aṣṭamastu bhūyiṣṭhastasmin gate navame māsi kartavyam /
40.1.[3]	dakṣiṇena viduṣāpi na svayaṃ pitrā kartavyamiti ṇicoktam // 1 //
40.2.[1]	kapūjā cūḍā /
40.2.[2]	sā vasiṣṭhagotrasaṃbhūtānāṃ dakṣiṇe śiraso bhāge kartavyā /
40.2.[3]	dakṣiṇe dakṣiṇata ādyādibhyastasiḥ // 2 //
40.3.[1]	ubhayoḥ śiraso dakṣiṇottarabhāgayoratrigotre kaśyapagotre ca jātānāṃ śikhā kartavyā // 3 //
40.4.[1]	bhṛgugotrajā muṇḍā niḥśikhāḥ kartavyāḥ // 4 //
40.5.[1]	āṅgirasagotre ye jātāste pañcacūḍāḥ kartavyāḥ // 5 //
40.6.[1]	eke vājimicchanti āṅgirasānām /
40.6.[2]	vājiḥ keśapaṅktiḥ // 6 //
40.7.[1]	ye kathitebhyo'nye'gastyaviśvāmitrādigotrajāste śikhino bhavanti /
40.7.[2]	kimartham /
40.7.[3]	maṅgalārtham /
40.7.[4]	niḥśikhatvaṃ tvamaṅgaladharmaḥ ariṣṭahetuḥ /
40.7.[5]	tathāca paṭhanti ‘amedhyametacchiro yadaśikham /’ iti /
40.7.[6]	‘yatra bāṇāḥ sampatanti kumārā viśikhā iva /’ iti ca nindāvādo yanmūlaṃ śikhākarmasmaraṇam // 7 //
40.8.[1]	kuladharmānatikrameṇa vā ekaśikhatvādi kartavyaṃ kulācārāṇāmapi dharmatvena smaraṇāt ‘yenāsya pitaro yātā yena yātāḥ pitāmahāḥ /
40.8.[2]	tena yāyātsatāṃ mārgaṃ tena gacchanna riṣyati //’ 
40.9.[1]	puṇyāha ityādi hutvetyantaṃ vyākhyātam /
40.9.[2]	āyamagādityādinā uṣṇā apo'bhimantrayate mantreṇa /
40.9.[3]	jagatī cchandaḥ /
40.9.[4]	viśvedevā devatā /
40.9.[5]	brahmaṇa ārṣamupanayanasamāptiṃ yāvat /
40.9.[6]	ayaṃ savitā kṣureṇoṣṇena codakena sahāgāt āgataḥ /
40.9.[7]	ato he vāyo tvamapyābhyāṃ saha ehi āgaccha /
40.9.[8]	he ādityāḥ rudrāḥ vasavaḥ sacetasa ekacittāḥ santo yūyamapyasya somasyeva rājño māṇavakasya vapata muṇḍayatainamityarthaḥ ‘somo vā oṣadhīnāṃ rājā’ iti śruteḥ rājānamivainaṃ gauravabhājanaṃ manyamānā muṇḍayateti yāvat // 9 //
40.10.[1]	uṣṇāścetyādinā varcase ityantenābhyundet ‘undī kledane’ māṇavakasya śiraḥ abhimantritābhiradbhiḥ prakṣālayedityarthaḥ //
40.10.[2]	he āpaḥ ihaiva sthāne enaṃ māṇavakamavata rakṣata uṣṇāśca śītāśca sarvāḥ sametya saṃbhūya /
40.10.[3]	taccāvanaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ savitā cānumanyatāmabhyupagacchatu /
40.10.[4]	kīdṛśaḥ /
40.10.[5]	satyadharmā satyameva hyasya dharmaḥ, satyasaṃkalpo hyata evāyam /
40.10.[6]	he āpaḥ ārdradānavaḥ ārdrabhāvasya dātryaḥ stha bhavatha /
40.10.[7]	dadāti iti dānuḥ, auṇādiko dānuśabdaḥ /
40.10.[8]	evaṃ jīvadānavo jīvadātryaḥ stha bhavatha /
40.10.[9]	undatīḥ kledayantyaḥ /
40.10.[10]	āpa undantu jīvase jīvanāya dīrghāyutvāya ca āyuṣe tvapatyoriti salopaḥ /
40.10.[11]	varcase brahmavarcasāya rūpaviśeṣāya // 10 //
40.11.[1]	śiraso dakṣiṇe bhāge oṣadhe trāyasvainamiti mantreṇa darbhamantardhāya svadhite mainaṃ hiṃsīrityanena kṣureṇābhinidhāyāvaṣṭabhya sadarbhān keśān yenāvapadityādibhiścatasṛbhiranuṣṭubbhiḥ dakṣiṇabhāgādārabhya pradakṣiṇaṃ yathā bhavati, tathā pratidiśaṃ pratimantraṃ darbhakṣurakarma kartavyamṛtvijā ādyayā dakṣiṇe bhāge, dvitīyayā paścime bhāge, tṛtīyayottarasmin, caturthyā tvagre //
40.11.[2]	he oṣadhe enaṃ māṇavakaṃ trāyasva gopāya /
40.11.[3]	he svadhite kṣura enaṃ māṇavakaṃ mā hiṃsīḥ /
40.11.[4]	yenāvapadyena kṣureṇa savitā somasya rājño varuṇasyāvapaduptavān śiraḥ, tena he brahmāṇa adyāsminnahani vapata muṇḍayata idaṃ bālakasyāsya śiraḥ /
40.11.[5]	kīdṛśaḥ savitā /
40.11.[6]	vidvān jānan /
40.11.[7]	tathā vapata yathāyaṃ bāla āyuṣmān dīrghāyurjarāmaśnute vyāpnoti jaradaṣṭiścāsau bhavati /
40.11.[8]	asāviti nāmaviśeṣo lakṣyate /
40.11.[9]	yena dhātā, yena kṣureṇa prajāpatirbṛhaspateragnerindrasya ca śira uptavān dīrghāyutvāya, tenaivāsya kṣureṇa bālasya śiro vapa dīrghāyutvāya ca suślokatvāya kīrtaye tathā svastaye'vināśāya /
40.11.[10]	yena pūṣeti anantarakhyākhyayā gatārthaḥ /
40.11.[11]	yena bhūyaśca rātrī jyokpaśyā ca sūryaṃ, yena kṣureṇa rātriḥ sūryamavapat bhūyaḥ punaḥpunaḥ /
40.11.[12]	jyok cirakālaṃ, paśyatīti paśyā jyokpaśyā bahudarśanā rātriḥ /
40.11.[13]	tenetyādi samānam // 11 //
40.12.[1]	yatkṣureṇetyādiyajuṣā nāpitāya kṣuraṃ dadāti lohāyasamiti śastrāntarajātiviśeṣasya saṃjñā nāpitaprasiddhā /
40.12.[2]	anye tu kṣuragrahaṇenaiva lohatvasya siddhatvāt stutyarthaṃ lohagrahaṇamityāhuḥ /
40.12.[3]	yatkṣureṇa yena kṣureṇa atitaikṣṇyādiguṇabhājā praśastatamenetyarthaḥ yaditi luptatṛtīyaikavacanāntam, he vaptaḥ muṇḍayitaḥ nāpita yena kṣureṇa keśānvapasi supeśasā surūpeṇa, tena vartayatā parivartamānena asya āyurmā pramoṣīḥ mainaṃ vadhīrityarthaḥ, kiṃ tarhi, śundhi śiro'sya, śodhaya śiro'sya // 12 //
40.13.[1]	anayā purastādbṛhatyā keśān patato'numantrayate /
40.13.[2]	tava etatprasiddhaṃ rūpādikaṃ tejaḥ keśānanu keśānāṃ paścāt mā gāt /
40.13.[3]	tathā dhātā prajāpatiste tubhyaṃ tejo dadātu /
40.13.[4]	tathā tubhyamindro bṛhaspatiḥ savitā varco rūpaviśeṣādikaṃ ādadhuḥ dadatu // 13 //
40.14.[1]	suhṛdaiva patantaḥ keśā grāhyā iti niyamaḥ /
40.14.[2]	tānupyamānān muṇḍyamānān patataḥ haritagomaye samavacinoti samyagavacinoti pratīcchati haritagomaye saṃmiśrīkṛtya piṇḍīkarotīti kvacidācāraḥ // 14 //
40.15.[1]	anayā vaiśvadevyā triṣṭubhā mitreṇa prāgudīcīṃ diśaṃ nīyamānān keśānanumantrayate kartā /
40.15.[2]	uptvāya uptvā muṇḍayitvā varuṇasya rājñaḥ sambandhinaḥ keśāṃstebhyastadarthaṃ yannidhānaṃ sthānaṃ, tadbahudhā anvavindan jñātavantaḥ /
40.15.[3]	kutra /
40.15.[4]	dyāvyāpṛthivyorantarāle madhye /
40.15.[5]	ke te /
40.15.[6]	somaścandro, dhātā prajāpatiḥ, savitā ādityaḥ, viṣṇuragniḥ /
40.15.[7]	avasyuriti pratyekamabhisambadhyate /
40.15.[8]	avanamavaḥ rakṣaṇam /
40.15.[9]	avanamicchati ‘supa ātmanaḥ kyac’ ‘kyācchandasi’ iti upratyayaḥ avanakāma ityarthaḥ // 15 //
40.16.[1]	arikte dūrvālatāvanaspatiprabhṛtau śītapradeśe samāśleṣayate keśānmitramiti śrutyā pratipāditaṃ śrutimūlametatkarmeti pradarśitaṃ ‘yatra bāṇā niṣpatanti kumārā viśikhā iva /’ ityādinā // 16 //
40.17.[1]	ṛtvije varaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ yathāśakti dadāti yajamānaḥ /
40.17.[2]	caturvarṣā gaurdakṣiṇātretyāhuḥ // 17 //
40.18.[1]	sūkṣmairūrṇāguṇairveṣṭitaṃ tilapātraṃ nāpitāya dadāti // 18 //
40.19.[1]	gatārtham /
40.19.[2]	cūḍākaraṇe'ṅganirdeśātpradhānānabhidhānātpradhānamājyenāgneyyā vaiśvadevyā vā kartavyamityāhuḥ /
40.19.[3]	yadvopasamādhāyetyanenājyabhāgāntaramuktaṃ tadeva pradhānam /
40.19.[4]	yeṣāṃ tvagnisaṃskāramātramupasamādhānaṃ, teṣāṃ pūrvaṃ pradhānam // 19 //
40.19.[5]	iti cūḍākaraṇavivṛtiḥ samāptā //
41.1.[1]	janmanaḥ prabhṛti saptame varṣe garbhādaṣṭame brāhmaṇasyopāyanamācāryasamīpagamanamekhalābandhanasaṃskāraḥ pradhānabhūtaḥ /
41.1.[2]	tasminhi sati śrutismṛtyadhikāro bhavati /
41.1.[3]	ata eva dvitīyaṃ janma smaryate 'prathamaṃ mātṛto janma dvitīyaṃ mauñjibandhanāt /
41.1.[4]	atra mātā ca sāvitrī pitā tvācārya ucyate //' iti // 1 //
41.2.[1]	aveṣṭyadhikaraṇanayena rājā kṣatriyastasyāpatyaṃ rājanyaḥ kṣatriyadārakaḥ /
41.2.[2]	tasya janmanaḥ prabhṛti navame garbhāddaśame upanayanam // 2 //
41.3.[1]	samānaṃ pūrveṇa // 3 //
41.4.[1]	sarvatrābhividhāvāṅ /
41.4.[2]	brāhmaṇasya ṣoḍaśavarṣāntaṃ yāvadupanayanakālānatikramaḥ, evaṃ dvāviṃśāntaṃ yāvat kṣatriyasya, ā caturviṃśādvaidyasya // 4 //
41.5.[1]	snātaścāsāvuptakeśo muṇḍitaśirāstasmin māṇavake upasthite sati yathāvidhi upasamādhānamagnisaṃskāramuddhatasitopalipte bhūviśeṣe sthāpanaṃ parisaṃvahanaṃ paryukṣaṇaṃ paristaraṇaṃ ca kṛtvājyaṃ copanidhāya vilāpya saṃvīkṣya daṇḍamekhalādikaṃ yathopayogamānīyopanetā jayaprabhṛtibhirṛtunakṣatrādyantairhutvā revatīstvetyādikayā śakvaryā ahatamabhuktaṃ navaṃ vāso haste nidhāyābhimantrayate /
41.5.[2]	kila vāsaso’yamutpattikramaḥ ādau tāvadrevatībhiḥ karpāso loṣṭhanikābhirabhihanyate vidhūyate ca, tataḥ kṛtyate veṣṭayate sūtratāmāpādyate ityarthaḥ, tatastantuvāyena ātānāyate, tataḥ kūrcena parāmṛjyate /
41.5.[3]	tato vastraṃ vayati tantuvāyaḥ, sampanne ca vastre pallavadvaye daśāḥ saṃyojayati /
41.5.[4]	evaṃkramo’tra mantre karpāsādīnāṃ hananādau devatāviśeṣāṇāṃ kartṛtāropaṇena stūyate /
41.5.[5]	he vastra tvāṃ revatīḥ devatāḥ vyakṣṇanviśeṣeṇākṣiṇvan karpāsāvasthāyāṃ loṣṭhanikādibhirhatavatyaḥ /
41.5.[6]	kṛttikāḥ 'kṛtī veṣṭane' kartaryo veṣṭikāścakratuḥ cakruḥ sūtraṃ kṛtavatyastadvāreṇa saṃpāditavatyaḥ /
41.5.[7]	apaso’pāpā marutastvāṃ vyatanvata viśeṣeṇātanvata ātānarūpatāṃ kṛtavanta ityarthaḥ /
41.5.[8]	dhiyo’vayan buddhiviśeṣeṇa hi vastraviśeṣasya vānaṃ sampadyate /
41.5.[9]	ava gnāḥ amṛjan 'vyavahitāśca' ityavaśabdo mṛjinā sambadhyate /
41.5.[10]	gnāḥ devatāḥ avāmṛjan 'mṛjū śuddhau' kūrcena ātatasya sūtrasya mārjanaṃ kṛtavatya ityarthaḥ /
41.5.[11]	sahasramantānabhitodayacchan, abhita ubhayataḥ pallavadvaye uditi nipātastathāśabdasyārthe, sahasraśabdo bāhulyārthaḥ, sahasramantānāṃ daśānāmayacchan babandhuḥ /
41.5.[12]	kāḥ /
41.5.[13]	gnā iti yojanīyam /
41.5.[14]	aśītirmadhyamavayannu nārīḥ, nuśabdaḥ kṣipravacanaḥ, madhyaṃ vastrasyāśītirnāryo nāgadevatā avayan utavatyaḥ // 5 //
41.6.[1]	anena yajuṣā vāsaḥ paridhāpayati /
41.6.[2]	he devyo revatyādyā idaṃ vāsaḥ paridhatta paridhāpayata /
41.6.[3]	kasmai /
41.6.[4]	devāya dyotamānāya māṇavakāya /
41.6.[5]	tvamapi he māṇavaka paridhatta paridhatsva /
41.6.[6]	savitā vyatyayena he savitaḥ idaṃ vāsaḥ paridhāpaya savitre devatārthābhijñānasya janayitre māṇavakāya /
41.6.[7]	tvamapi he māṇavaka paridhatta paridhatsva savitā bhūtvā /
41.6.[8]	he vāsaḥ naya prāpaya imaṃ māṇavakaṃ kaṃ brahmāṇaṃ brāhmaṇatvaṃ prāpaya vedasamṛddhiyuktaṃ kurvityarthaḥ, śatāyuṣaṃ kṛṇuhi kuru //
41.6.[9]	eṣa mantratrayāṇāṃ varṇānāṃ paridhāpane sādhāraṇo’dhovāsasaḥ /
41.6.[10]	uttarīyaṃ vakṣyate’jinam /
41.6.[11]	jarāṃ gacchetyādibhiḥ parihitavāsasamanumantrayate ityādityadarśanaḥ /
41.6.[12]	natvevamācāra ācāryāṇām, nāpi mantraliṅgamevamiti yojanānyathā kāryā /
41.6.[13]	ekaikasyāsādhāraṇa ityekaikasya vāsasaḥ paridhāpane mantratrayam /
41.6.[14]	tatra devīrdevāyetyeko varṇatrayasādhāraṇaḥ, jarāṃ gaccheti dvitīyaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ paridhāpane, paramamityādīnāṃ trayāṇāmekaiko yathākramamekaikasyāsādhāraṇa ityekaikasya trayaḥ paridhāpane mantrāḥ // 6 //
41.7-8.[1]	mantraliṅgādayamapi paridhāpane /
41.7-8.[2]	upanetā bravīti he māṇavaka vāsaḥ paridhatsva /
41.7-8.[3]	āśiṣamāha jarāṃ gaccha jarājarjaritatanurbhava /
41.7-8.[4]	āpīvābhūḥ 'sphāyī opyāyī vṛddhau' āṅpūrvaḥ 'āto maninkvanibvanipaśca' iti kvanip pravṛddho bhavetyarthaḥ /
41.7-8.[5]	anabhiśastipāvā abhūrityanuṣajyate, abhiśaso’bhiśastiḥ pāpayogastatpratiṣedho’nabhiśastiḥ pāpābhāvaḥ prasajyapratiṣedhaṃ kṛtvā paryudāsena ca dharmasaṃbandhaḥ, anabhiśastiṃ pātīti anabhiśastipāvā /
41.7-8.[6]	śataṃ jīva śaradaḥ śataṃ śaradāṃ ca tvaṃ prāṇān dhāraya /
41.7-8.[7]	purucīriti śarado viśeṣaṇaṃ puruśabdo bhūrivacanaḥ bahūn puruṣānañcanti sādhayanti iti purūcyaḥ, purūcīnāṃ rāyo dhanasya ca poṣaṃ puṣṭiṃ paridhatsva samantāddhāraya // 7 //
41.7-8.[8]	eṣa brāhmaṇasya paridhāpane mantraḥ somapadālliṅgāditarayoḥ somasaṃbandhābhāvāt 'yadi rājanyaṃ vaiśyaṃ vā yājayennyagrodhatatīrāhṛtya tāḥ saṃpiṣya dadhnyutsṛjya tadasmai bhakṣaṃ prayacchenna somam' iti śruteḥ //
41.7-8.[9]	he māṇavaka etadvāsaḥ paridadhmasi 'idanto masi' itīdantaḥ paridadhmaḥ paridhāpayāmaḥ, somameva cemaṃ paridhāpayāmaḥ, tvayā anenopanayanadvāreṇa soma eva hi parihito dhṛto vedastadarthābhyāsadvāreṇa bhaviṣyati /
41.7-8.[10]	kimarthaṃ paridhāpayāmaḥ /
41.7-8.[11]	tejase mahe, mahate, pūjārthaṃ vā maha pūjāyāmityasya rūpam /
41.7-8.[12]	śrotrāya śrūyate iti śrotraṃ vedaḥ tadarthaṃ vedavedārthādhigamāya, athavā śrotrāya śrotrayuktāya śiṣyāya vedapāraṅgamastvamupādhyāyaḥ śrotriyebhyo hitaḥ sampadyasveti tātparyam /
41.7-8.[13]	yathainaṃ vāsoviśeṣaṃ jarasaṃ nayat jarāṃ nayati māṇavakaḥ tathā ca paridhāpanena paridhāpayāmaḥ, yathā bahūni vastrāṇi bhogena jarayiṣyati tathāhaṃ paridhāpayāmīti yāvat /
41.7-8.[14]	jyok cirakālaṃ śrotrāya vedāya jāgarat jāgṛhi bahukālaṃ vedatadarthajāgaraṇaṃ paṭhanabodhānuṣṭhānātmakaṃ tavāstvityarthaḥ /
41.7-8.[15]	jyok śrotre’dhijāgarat bahukālaṃ śiṣyebhyo jāgṛhi upadiśa atiśayena paropakāraprakṛṣṭadharmakatvāt // 8 //
41.7-8.[16]	he brahmacārin vāsaḥ paridadhmasi vāsaḥ paridhāpayāmaḥ indramindreṇa saha bāhubhyāṃ jātatvādindro rājanyastaṃ parameśvaraṃ svayameva prajāpālanasāmarthyāt /
41.7-8.[17]	kimartham /
41.7-8.[18]	ojase balāya /
41.7-8.[19]	mahe mahate pūjitāya vā /
41.7-8.[20]	kṣatrāya sādhūnāṃ trāṇāya utsāhāya ca /
41.7-8.[21]	gatārthamanyat // 9 //
41.7-8.[22]	manumiti mānuṣatvānmanum /
41.7-8.[23]	poṣo dhanapuṣṭistadartham /
41.7-8.[24]	śiṣṭaṃ samānam // 10 //
41.7-8.[25]	trayāṇāmapi varṇānāṃ parihitavāsasāmanenānumantraṇaṃ karotyupanetā /
41.7-8.[26]	pariśabdaḥ pūrvavadihāpi vyavahitānvayaḥ /
41.7-8.[27]	he māṇavaka tvamidaṃ vāsaḥ pari adhidhāḥ paryadhyadhāḥ ādhikyenotkarṣeṇa parihitavānasi svastaye’vināśāya yat, tattvamāpīvā āpīnaḥ pravṛddho bhava, anabhiśastyanabhiśastaṃ pāti rakṣatītyanabhiśastipāvā, śataṃ ca śaradāṃ jīva, suvīraśca śobhanaputrayukto bhava, tathā vasūni dhanāni udāraḥ sanvibhaja viśeṣeṇa bhajasva dehi vā parijanartvikprabhṛtibhyaḥ /
41.7-8.[28]	suṣṭhu jīvan sujīvan sukhādinā jīvan // 11 //
41.7-8.[29]	yoge yoge ityanena yuvā suvāsa ityanena ca mantreṇāgniṃ lakṣaṇīkṛtya pradakṣiṇaṃ yathā bhavati, tathā māṇavakamānīya ehyaśmānamātiṣṭheti mantreṇāśmānaṃ dakṣiṇena padā āsthāpayati adhiṣṭhāpayatyācāryaḥ //
41.7-8.[30]	yoge yoge tavastaraṃ vāje vāje havāmahe /
41.7-8.[31]	sakhāyamindramūtaye //
41.7-8.[32]	vyākhyāteyam /
41.7-8.[33]	atra vahnipradakṣiṇe tu yogaḥ sambandho viśeṣyate /
41.7-8.[34]	yoge yoge sarvatra brahmacārikriyāsambandhe kartavye, vāje vāje haviṣi haviṣi, indraṃ havāmahe āhvayāmaḥ ūtaye’vanāya, tavastaraṃ balavattaraṃ, sakhāyaṃ sahāyam //
41.7-8.[35]	yuvā suvāsaḥ parivīta āgātsa ucchreyānbhavati jāyamānaḥ /
41.7-8.[36]	taṃ dhīrāsaḥ kavaya unnayanti svādhyo manasā devayantaḥ //
41.7-8.[37]	eṣa yūpocchrāyane viniyukto’nyatra mantraḥ /
41.7-8.[38]	tatraiṣa mantrārthaḥ yūpa eva yuvā navaḥ sadyaśchinnaḥ, śobhanena vāsasā raśanayā ca parito veṣṭita āgāt āgataḥ /
41.7-8.[39]	taṃ dhīrāso dhīrāḥ paṇḍitā ṛtvijaḥ unnayanti ucchriyanti manasā devayantaḥ devān yaṣṭukāmāḥ paśuyāgaṃ cikīrṣantaḥ /
41.7-8.[40]	prakṛto’trāyamarthaḥ brahmacārī yuvā suvāsāḥ parihitaśobhanavastraḥ parivītaḥ saṃvṛto brahmacāryātmā sahi yuvā nityataruṇaḥ saṃvītaśca śaṇavāsasā, āgāt āgataḥ idaṃ śarīraṃ karmavaśātprāptaḥ /
41.7-8.[41]	prāṇo vyākhyātavyo brahmacārisaṃbandhī /
41.7-8.[42]	so’pi hi śarīreṇa vāsaseva saṃvṛta āgato brahmacāriśarīram /
41.7-8.[43]	nityataruṇaśca yuvā sa brahmacārī ucchrita unnato jāyamāno vardhamāno bhavati ātmā vāyurgagana iva kṣudhādibhiḥ pravṛddho bhavati /
41.7-8.[44]	taṃ dhīrāso dhīrāḥ paṇḍitāḥ kavayaḥ krāntadarśanā unnayanti ūrdhvaṃ nayanti ātmānaṃ mokṣaṃ prāpayanti prāṇamutkrāmayanti ūrdhvaṃ brahmadvāraṃ prāpayanti brahmacāriśarīramapyunnayanti kriyājñānakāṇḍānuṣṭhānenotkṛṣṭaṃ sampādayanti, svādhyaḥ śobhanadhiyaḥ sukarmāṇaḥ, ekāgreṇa manasonnayanti //
41.7-8.[45]	ehyaśmānamiti, he māṇavaka ehi āgaccha aśmānaṃ pāṣāṇamātiṣṭhādhitiṣṭha, aśmeva sthiro bhava, viśve sarve devā āyuṣṭe kṛṇvantu śaradaḥ śataṃ samāḥ śatam // 12 //
41.9.[1]	mama vrata ityādinā mantreṇa nābhimārabhya śikhāntaṃ yāvadbrahmacāriṇaṃ ācārya unmārṣṭi /
41.9.[2]	vratamiti karmanāma /
41.9.[3]	he brahmacārin mama karmaṇi te tava hṛdayaṃ dadāmi tvadīyaṃ hṛdayaṃ maccikīrṣitakarmasahāyamastvityarthaḥ /
41.9.[4]	mama sambandhi cittaṃ te tavānucittamastu madīyacittānugataṃ tava cittamastvityarthaḥ /
41.9.[5]	mama sambandhinīṃ vācaṃ tvamekavrato bhūtvā juṣasva yadahamadhyāpayāmi, tadekacitto bhūtvā adhīṣvetyarthaḥ /
41.9.[6]	vāgvai bṛhatī, tasyāḥ patirbṛhaspatirātmā /
41.9.[7]	sa tvāṃ niyunaktu samyaksaṃkalpadvāreṇa matsevādau pravartayatu, mahyaṃ madarthaṃ, mamāpi tathā sati ācāryakasampattirupakāro bhaviṣyatītyarthaḥ // 13 //
41.10.[1]	brahmacārī vakti /
41.10.[2]	tamācāryo vācayati brahmacaryamityādi svarityantam /
41.10.[3]	kiṃ kṛtvā /
41.10.[4]	dadhikrāvṇa ityādinā trirdadhi bhakṣayitvā bhakṣaṇe brahmacāriṇaṃ prayujya /
41.10.[5]	khāditvā ācānto brahmacaryamityādi brahmacārī paṭhati gurupāṭhitaḥ sanniti tātparyam //
41.10.[6]	dadhikrāvṇo akāriṣaṃ jiṣṇoraśvasya vājinaḥ /
41.10.[7]	surabhi no mukhā karatpra ṇa āyūṃṣi tāriṣat //
41.10.[8]	eṣā vyākhyātā /
41.10.[9]	brahmacaryamityādi brahmacārī bravīti /
41.10.[10]	he guro ahaṃ brahmacaryamāgām, brahmaṇo vedasya caraṇamāgāmāgataḥ prāptaḥ brahmacaryaṃ mayā avaśyakartavyatayā saṃkalpitam /
41.10.[11]	ata upanayasva māṃ saṃskurvityarthaḥ /
41.10.[12]	adhyeṣaṇe loṭ /
41.10.[13]	he upanetastavāpyācāryakasiddhiḥ phalaṃ bhaviṣyati māṃ saṃskurvata ityātmanepadena bodhayati ādityadarśanastu vyākhyātavān gururidamāha brahmā prajāpatistasya caraṇaṃ brahmabhāvamahamāgāmāgataḥ, ato māmupanayasva brahmasamīpaṃ prāpaya he brahmacārinnatyādi /
41.10.[14]	etat vicintyam /
41.10.[15]	omiti brahmaṇo’bhidhānamomiti brahma khaṃ brahmeti śruteḥ /
41.10.[16]	bhūriti bhūlokasthā devatā agnirūpocyate /
41.10.[17]	bhuvarityantarikṣadevatā pūrvavattātsthyāt, saca vāyuḥ /
41.10.[18]	svariti svarlokasthā devatā ādityātmikoktā // 14 //
41.11.[1]	iyaṃ duruktādityādikāstriṣṭubho vācayannācāryo mekhalāmābadhnīte /
41.11.[2]	brahmacārī vakti /
41.11.[3]	gururvācayati /
41.11.[4]	iyaṃ mekhalā duruktādduṣṭādasatyabhāṣaṇādikāduktādvacanātparibādhamānā vārayantī tasyāṃ baddhāyāṃ vākpāṇipādacāpalavāraṇānniyamacodanādvarṇaṃ brāhmaṇādijātitrayaṃ punatī pāvayantī adhyayanādiyogyatāpādanadvāreṇa, rūpādikaṃ vā varṇaṃ punatī, svabhāvapavitraṃ pāvanayogyaṃ vā /
41.11.[5]	sā me mamāgādāgatā prāṇāpānābhyāṃ balamābhajantī dadatī svādhyāyādidvāreṇa /
41.11.[6]	'bhañjo āmardane" ityasya, varṇātmakaṃ rūpamābhajantī vināśayantī tasyāṃ hi satyāṃ adhyayanaṃ kriyate /
41.11.[7]	tacca kriyamāṇaṃ prāṇāpānau niruddhya kriyata iti prāṇāpānabalamapahataṃ tayā bhavati /
41.11.[8]	sakhā samānakhyānā /
41.11.[9]	devī dyotanādiguṇayuktā /
41.11.[10]	subhagā hṛdyā navakomalamuñjasaṃgatā /
41.11.[11]	ṛtasya satyasya goptrī pālayitrī tasyāṃ satyāṃ yatheṣṭavācitvanivāraṇāt, ṛtasya yajñasya vā rakṣikā baddhamekhalena vedatīrthādigamanāt /
41.11.[12]	tapaso vrataniyamasahitasya vedādhyayanasya tarutrī tārayitrī pāraṃ nayatrī /
41.11.[13]	ghnatī rakṣaḥ, yātudhānānnāśayantī vajro vai mekhaleti śruteḥ /
41.11.[14]	sahamānā arātiṃ, śatrumadānaṃ vā prasahamānā abhibhavantī kārpaṇyaṃ śatrūṃśca nivārayantītyarthaḥ /
41.11.[15]	sā no’smākaṃ samantaṃ samantādanuparehi āgaccha bhadrayā vṛttyā /
41.11.[16]	he mekhale tava bhartāro dhārayitāraḥ santo vayaṃ mā riṣāma riṣirhiṃsākarmā tvāṃ dhārayatāmasmākaṃ hiṃsā mā bhūt /
41.11.[17]	śraddhāyā āstikyasya duhitā śraddhāsya mātā /
41.11.[18]	tapaso’dhijātā, tapo’syāḥ pitā /
41.11.[19]	mantrakṛtāṃ samyagjñānavidāmṛṣīṇāṃ svasā bhaginī babhūva bhūtā /
41.11.[20]	he mekhale saivaṃbhūtā tvaṃ māṃ parirerihasva 'liha āsvādane' chāndaso varṇavyatyayaḥ māṃ samāśliṣya, mayi tapo niyamayuktādhyayanaṃ dhehi nidhehi, indriyaṃ ca me indriyaṣaṭkapāṭavaṃ ca dehi // 15 //
41.12.[1]	mauñjīṃ saptamuñjanirmitām /
41.12.[2]	trivṛtaṃ triguṇaveṣṭitām /
41.12.[3]	trivṛdvajraḥ /
41.12.[4]	trivṛnnavakam /
41.12.[5]	tatra trivṛtā yūpaṃ paricīyādityādau rajjau trivṛcchandaḥ /
41.12.[6]	trivṛtstoma ityādau trivṛcchabdo navake /
41.12.[7]	ihāpi rajjau triguṇāyāṃ trivṛcchandaḥ tathā sadācārāt /
41.12.[8]	tena bhrāntyā kecinnavaguṇāṃ mekhalāṃ vyācakṣate /
41.12.[9]	murvo nāma tṛṇaviśeṣastasya vikāro maurvī, tāṃ dhanurjyāṃ dhanuṣaḥ prasāryaṃ guṇaṃ rājanyāya prayacchati /
41.12.[10]	sautrīṃ vaiśyāya, sāmānyābhidhāne’pi smṛtyanusāreṇa karpāsasūtramayīm /
41.12.[11]	ādau prayacchati, tata ābadhnīyāditi kramo boddhavyaḥ //
41.13.[1]	cittasya samo’sītyanena mantreṇa mekhalāgranthiṃ kṛtvā śikhāvat yathākulaprasiddhi 'trivṛtā granthinaikena tribhiḥ pañcabhireva vā /' ityādismaraṇāt mitrasyetyādi vācayannaiṇeyaṃ kṛṣṇamṛgasya sambandhi carma brāhmaṇāya prayacchatyupanetā, rājanyāya vyāghracarma, rurucarma vaiśyāya /
41.13.[2]	mekhalāgranthau carmadāne ca trayāṇāṃ sādhāraṇau mantrau //
41.13.[3]	cittasyeti /
41.13.[4]	he granthe tvaṃ cittasya samaścittena tulyo yathā brahmacāriṇaścittaṃ na calati vratādhyayanādiśuddhaṃ tiṣṭhati tathā tvamapi na calasi yāvadbrahmacaryamavasthānāt /

41.13.[12]	dharuṇaṃ brahmacaryādikasya dhāraṇam /
41.13.[13]	balāya brahmacaryasāmarthyārthaṃ paridadhe tejaḥ brahmavarcasasya tejaso nimittatvāt /
41.13.[14]	yaśasvi yaśaskaram /
41.13.[15]	sthaviraṃ vṛddhamiva gauravapātraṃ sthirataraṃ vā /
41.13.[16]	samṛddhaṃ samṛddhikāri /
41.13.[17]	anāhanasyaṃ āhantīti āhanāḥ 'sarvadhātubhyo’sun' ityasun, āhanasi sādhu āhanasyaṃ tatpratiṣedho’nāhanasyam /
41.13.[18]	vasanamācchādanam /

41.13.[20]	vāji vājamannaṃ tadvidyate’syeti vāji, tasminparihite brahmacaryāvasthāya bhaktyānnaṃ prayacchantīti tasyānnatvamupacaryate // 17 //
41.14.[1]	taccakṣurityādinā ādityopasthānaṃ kārayati //
41.14.[2]	taccakṣurdevahitaṃ purastācchukramuccarat /
