41.14.[6]	tat śaradāṃ śataṃ paśyema paśyantaśca varṣaśataṃ jīvemeti brahmacārī śaṃsatyupatiṣṭhamāna ādityam //
41.15.[1]	gururāha ko nāmāsīti /
41.15.[2]	ka iti prajāpatināma /
41.15.[3]	tathāca brāhmaṇaṃ 'ko nāmāsīti prajāpatirvai ko nāmeti /' vedagrahaṇābhimukhatvātprajāpatirivāsīti stuticchalena sākṣāt praśno’yaṃ prativacanavidhānāt /
41.15.[4]	guruṇā pṛṣṭaḥ śiṣyo’bhivādayate /
41.15.[5]	svanāmoccāraṇenāsāvityukte nāma pratīyāt viṣṇumitro’hamabhivādaye bho iti brahmacāriṇābhivādito guruḥ pratyabhivādanamāha plutāntaṃ 'pratyabhivāde’śudre' iti smṛterāyuṣmānedhi saumya viṣṇumitra3 iti /
41.15.[6]	smṛterapi 'āyuṣmānbhava saumyeti vaktavyo ’ntyākṣare plutaḥ /' iti // 19 //
41.16.[1]	ācāryo brahmacāriṇo dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ dakṣiṇena hastena vivāhoktavidhinā gṛhṇāti devasya ta ityādinā /
41.16.[2]	he brahmacārin viṣṇumitra ahamācāryo hariśarmābhidhānastvāmupanaye iti śiṣyaṃ svanāmnā saṃbodhya svanāmoccārya gṛhītahasto gururbravīti, eko’sāviti śabdaḥ śiṣyabodhane, dvitīya ācāryanāmopalakṣaṇārthaḥ, te tava hastaṃ gṛhṇāmi /
41.16.[3]	kīdṛśasya /

41.16.[5]	kimartham /
41.16.[6]	prasave prakṛṣṭajñānādijananāya /
41.16.[7]	stutyarthamāha naivaṃ bhramaṇīyaṃ yaduta carmamayābhyāmātmīyābhyāṃ bāhubhyāṃ hastābhyāṃ vā hastaṃ gṛhṇāmyahamiti /
41.16.[8]	kiṃ tarhi /
41.16.[9]	aśvinordevabhiṣajorbāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇaśca hastābhyām //20// gṛhītahasta evācārya āha /
41.16.[10]	savitābhimatasya janayitā ādityaste tava hastamagrahīt, ātmānameva savitṛtvenopacarati guruḥ /
41.16.[11]	agnirācāryastava, nāham, ahamevāgnistavācāryo vedārthajñānatadanuṣṭhānatapaḥprabhṛtibhirjājvalyamānatvāt kaḥ prajāpatiḥ sannahaṃ gururātmarūpeṇa kaṃ prajāpatimeva santaṃ tvāmahamupanaye asau viṣṇumitranāmā /
41.16.[12]	sarveṣāmevāntaramekaḥ /
41.16.[13]	sa eva ca saṃsthānairaupādhikadoṣanivṛttyā saṃskriyate /
41.16.[14]	kāya prajāpataye tvāmahaṃ paridadāmi parirakṣārthaṃ brahmaṇe tvāṃ samarpayāmītyarthaḥ // 21 //
41.16.[15]	kasya prajāpaterbrahmacāryasīti bhaṅgipraśne ācāryeṇa kṛte sati śiṣyaḥ pratyāha prāṇasya brahmacārī asmi bhavāmītyabhyupagamabhaṅgyaiva pratyuttaram /
41.16.[16]	prāṇo hi prajāpatireva jagatsūtrabhūtaḥ /
41.16.[17]	tathāca śrutiḥ 'hiraṇyagarbhaḥ puruṣo mahāṃstvaṃ prāṇo jagatsūtramanādirindraḥ /
41.16.[18]	bodhaḥ śucirdharmatarāntarātmā tathā vidhātā jagato’sya deva //' iti // 22 //
41.17.[1]	he brahmacārin prajāpataye parirakṣārthamahaṃ tvāṃ dadāmi devāya savitre’ntarātmane bṛhaspataye vāgvai bṛhatī, tasyāḥ patirātmā tasmai dadāmīti samānam /
41.17.[2]	asāviti ācāryanāmapradarśanārtham /
41.17.[3]	he deva svaprakāśatayā dyotamāna /
41.17.[4]	he savitaḥ abhimatavratādijanayitaḥ eṣa brahmacārī te tava sambandhī, taṃ gopāyasva pālaya /
41.17.[5]	dīrghāyuḥ so’stu mā mṛta maraṇaṃ mā bhūdasya /
41.17.[6]	pratyakṣe’pi parokṣanirdeśo vaidiko vyatyayaḥ // 23 //
41.17.[7]	agneḥ putraḥ ṛgvedaḥ /
41.17.[8]	vāyoḥ putro yajurvedaḥ /
41.17.[9]	sūryasya putraḥ sāmavedaḥ /
41.17.[10]	he ṛgveda yajurveda sāmaveda eṣa brahmacārī tubhyaṃ parirakṣārthaṃ datta iti te tava pratyekaṃ sambandhī, atastaṃ gopāyasva /
41.17.[11]	tathāca brāhmaṇamagnyādiputratvamṛgvedādīnāṃ darśayati 'prajāpatirvā eka āsītsa tapo’tapyata tatastapastepānena trayo devā asṛjanta agnirvāyurādityaste tapo’tapyanta tebhyastapastepānebhyastrayo vedā asṛjantāgnerṛgvedo vāyoryajurveda ādityātsāmavedaḥ' iti /
41.17.[12]	viṣṇuputro brahmaputraśceti sambhūtagrāmaḥ /
41.17.[13]	athavā agneḥ putro bhūlokaḥ, asyādhiṣṭhātrī devatā agniḥ /
41.17.[14]	evaṃ vāyuputro’ntarikṣalokaḥ, sūryaputro dyulokaḥ /
41.17.[15]	yadvā puru bahu trāyate iti putraḥ, agniścāsau putro’gniputraḥ /
41.17.[16]	evamanyatrāpi yojanā // 24 //
41.17.[17]	idānīṃ grahīta hastamenamanuśāsti /
41.17.[18]	gururāha he brahmacārin tvaṃ saṃprati yato brahmacārī saṃpanno’ta etāni pañca kartavyāni buddhyasva /
41.17.[19]	apo’śāna nimittopanatāvācamanādikaṃ kuru /
41.17.[20]	tathā guruparicaryāvedādhyayanādikaṃ karma kuru /
41.17.[21]	divāsvapnaṃ ca varjaya, matprasādena śarīrādyapāṭavadaśāyāmabhyupagaccha divāsvāpamicchāyāḥ svatantrāyā niṣedhāt /
41.17.[22]	vāksaṃyamanaṃ ca kuru anṛtaparuṣabhāṣaṇādikaṃ mā kurvityarthaḥ //
41.18.[1]	medhāṃ mahyamityādikāḥ pañca ṛcaḥ, ṣaṣṭhaṃ yajuḥ śiṣyo vakti, gururvācayati /
41.18.[2]	kuśāgrīyā buddhirmedhā /
41.18.[3]	tāmaṅgiraso vāyavaḥ prāṇāpānasamānavyānodānāḥ dadurdadatu mām /
41.18.[4]	aṅgāni rasayantītyaṅgirasaḥ āntarā vāyavastathā saptarṣayo vasiṣṭhādyā mahyaṃ medhāṃ dadatu /
41.18.[5]	etatsamānamṛgdvaye /
41.18.[6]	apsarassu yā medhā, yacca gandharveṣu mano’ntaḥkaraṇaṃ, yāca daivī vedārthādisākṣātkāriṇī, manuṣyeṣu medhā sthitā ihaloke, sā sarvā māmāviśatu praviśatu /
41.18.[7]	mama śarīraṃ vicakṣaṇaṃ paṇḍitamastu adhiṣṭhātṛdvāreṇa /
41.18.[8]	vāk ca vedādirūpā madhumat madhuraphalaṃ duhe dugdhām /
41.18.[9]	yacca mayi śrutaṃ sthitaṃ niśāmitaṃ, tanniśāmaye cintayeyaṃ samyak /
41.18.[10]	yacca mamānūktaṃ guruṇoktaṃ, tadramatām /
41.18.[11]	yaccānubruve gurūktamanuvadāmi, tacchakeyaṃ śaknuyām /
41.18.[12]	vayaṃ ca śrutasya priyā bhūyāsma śrutamasmākaṃ paryavasitamastu /
41.18.[13]	medhayā saṃvidhīmahi saṃbaddhyemahi /
41.18.[14]	ātmānamuddiśya yajuṣā śiṣya idamāha he antarātman prāṇādika asau viṣṇumitro’hamavṛdhaṃ vardhiṣye /
41.18.[15]	tvamapi cāvṛdhaḥ asau prāṇādikaḥ, tasyāpi hi vedādhyayanādinātiśayo bhaviṣyati /
41.18.[16]	he saumya prāṇastvaṃ jagatsūtramato me māṃ gopāya /
41.18.[17]	tvaṃ brahmaṇa āṇī sāraṃ stha bhavasi /
41.18.[18]	śrutaṃ me mā prahāsīt śrutaṃ me mā tyākṣīt mama saṃbandhi yacchrutaṃ tanmāṃ mā tyākṣīdityarthaḥ /

41.19.[1]	anupravacanaṃ prayojanaṃ yeṣāṃ te’nupravacanīyā homā ityanvarthā saṃjñā /
41.19.[2]	anu uttarakālaṃ hi sāvitryāḥ pravacanaṃ kārayiṣyate guruṇā /
41.19.[3]	athavānupravacanamarhantītyanupravacanīyāḥ /
41.19.[4]	atra hi mantrānupādhyāyo vakti, śiṣyo’nupravakti /
41.19.[5]	anupravacanīyasaṃjñakān homānetābhireva prakṛtābhiścatasṛbhirṛgbhiḥ kapiñjalādhikaraṇanyāyena medhāṃ mahyamityādyābhirjuhuyāt /
41.19.[6]	tena catvāro homāḥ /
41.19.[7]	pañcamamāha yajuṣottamām, avṛdhamityādinā yajuṣottamāmāhutiṃ pañcamīṃ juhuyāditi kecit /
41.19.[8]	anye tvāhuḥ atra pakṣe pañcamyā ṛco viniyogābhāvaḥ prāpnoti /
41.19.[9]	uttamāmiti strīliṅganirdeśo na yujyate prakṛtasyānupravacanīyasya puṃstvāt, tadapekṣayottamamiti prasaṅgāt /
41.19.[10]	nacāhutiśabdaḥ prakṛto’sti /
41.19.[11]	tasmāduttamāmṛcaṃ yajuṣā saha saṃyojya pañcamamanupravacanīyaṃ juhuyādityarthaḥ // 28 //
41.19.[12]	ṣaṣṭhamanupravacanīyahomamāha /
41.19.[13]	ṛturiha karma /
41.19.[14]	karmanāmadheyena ca juhuyāt /
41.19.[15]	eṣa saptamo’nupravacanīyahomaḥ /
41.19.[16]	kathaṃ kratunāmadheyena hotavyam /
41.19.[17]	yathopācaritaḥ kraturbhavati, yena prakāreṇa prakṛtaṃ karmopācaritamiṣṭaṃ bhavati, tathā hotavyam /
41.19.[18]	caturthīyogena svāhākāreṇa cābhidhānaśaktiyoginā ca karmanāmadheyena upāyanāya svāhetyupanayanāya svāheti vā /
41.19.[19]	evaṃ sarvāṇi vedoktāni, anenaiva prakāreṇa sarvāṇi vedoktāni karmāṇi svanāmadheyena chandobhyaḥ svāheti hutvā hotavyāni traividyakāya svāhetyādiprakāreṇa // 29 //
41.20.[1]	paścādagnerdarbheṣūpaviṣṭaḥ prāṅmukho guruḥ pratyaṅmukhāsīnāyācāryasaṃmukhopaviṣṭāya śiṣyāya sāvitrīṃ savitṛdevatāṃ tatsaviturityādikāṃ gāyatrīṃ trīn vārānanvāha /
41.20.[2]	brāhmaṇāyeti jñeyam /
41.20.[3]	upalakṣaṇametadrājanyavaiśyayorhi sāvitryāvanye smṛtisadācārābhyāṃ boddhavye’dabdhebhiḥ savitariti rājanyāya, viśvā rūpāṇīti vaiśyāya /
41.20.[4]	kathamanvāha /
41.20.[5]	pacchaḥ pādaṃ pādaṃ pacchaḥ prathamoccāraṇe pādaśo’nubrūyāt /
41.20.[6]	dvitīyoccāraṇe ardharcaśaḥ ṛco’rdhamardharcamardharcamardharcamardharcaśaḥ /
41.20.[7]	ante’ntataḥ sarvām, tṛtīyoccāraṇe yathāśaktyanusāraṃ vā sarvāmṛcamanubrūyāt /
41.20.[8]	yaśca medhāṃ śiṣyasya kāmayate, sopi paccho’rdharcaśaḥ sarvāmantato’nubrūyāt /
41.20.[9]	tatsavituriti vyākhyāteyam //
41.20.[10]	adabdhebhiḥ savitā pāyubhiṣṭuṃ śivebhiradya paripāhi no gayam /
41.20.[11]	hiraṇyajihvaḥ suvitāya navyase rakṣa mā kirno aghaśaṃsa īśata //
41.20.[12]	viśvā rūpāṇi pratimuñcate kaviḥ prāsāvīdbhadraṃ dvipade catuṣpade /
41.20.[13]	vi nākamakhyatsavitā vareṇyo’prayāṇamuṣaso virājati //
41.20.[14]	ete yathāsaṃkhyaṃ rājanyavaiśyayoranubrūyāt /
41.20.[15]	he savitarāditya adyāsminnahani no’smākaṃ gayaṃ gṛhaṃ pāhi rakṣa pāyubhiḥ pālakaiḥ raśmibhiradabdhebhiranupahiṃsitaiḥ, śivebhiḥ sukhakāribhiḥ /
41.20.[16]	yatastvaṃ hiraṇyajihvaḥ dīprakiraṇaḥ /
41.20.[17]	suvitāya havirādidātre navyase stotrādikartre naurivācarasi tārayiṣyasi āpatsamudrāditi vā /
41.20.[18]	ato’smān rakṣa /
41.20.[19]	mā kiḥ kaścinno’smānaghaṃ pāpaṃ śaṃsati yaḥ, sa caurādiḥ īśata prabhūt //
41.20.[20]	savitā viśvā rūpāṇi sarvānbhāvān pratimuñcate prakāśayati, kavirmedhāvī krāntadarśanaḥ /
41.20.[21]	prāsāvīt prasūte janayati bhadraṃ sukhaṃ dvipade catuṣpade ca /
41.20.[22]	nākaṃ svargaṃ vyākhyātaṃ vyakhyat prakāśayati /
41.20.[23]	vareṇyo varaṇīyaḥ prārthanīyaḥ /
41.20.[24]	uṣaso rātrīṇāṃ prayāṇamanu lakṣaṇīkṛtya hīnīkṛtya vā virājati rātritamaso’pahatatvāt prakāśate // 30 //
41.21.[1]	palāśasyāyaṃ pālāśo daṇḍaḥ /
41.21.[2]	tamekasaramavāntaraśākhārahitamṛjuṃ satvacamavraṇaṃ navanītenābhyajya svahastena gṛhītvā gurustasya daṇḍasya sambandhinyāṃ chāyāyāṃ śiṣyaṃ vyavasthāpya suśrava ityādi pāṭhayati //
41.21.[3]	pālāśa ucyate he suśravaḥ suśravā asi śobhanaṃ śravaṇaṃ yasya sa suśravāḥ /
41.21.[4]	tasminhi karmāṅgatvenopādīyamāne duṣṭasyākīrtyātmakasya śabdasya śravaṇaṃ na bhavati /
41.21.[5]	anuvādamāha 'yasya parṇamayī juhūrbhavati na sa pāpaṃ ślokaṃ śṛṇoti' /
41.21.[6]	brāhmaṇamapi /
41.21.[7]	'devā vai brahmansamavadanta tatastadbrahma parṇa upāśṛṇotsuśravā vai nāma eṣa' iti, brahmaṇi vede devā avadanta tatastadbrahma parṇe palāśe samāśritaṃ palāśamāśritamityarthaḥ /
41.21.[8]	ata eva palāśaḥ suśravā iti nāmnā prasiddha iti brāhmaṇatātparyam /
41.21.[9]	he suśravaḥ sauśravasaṃ kuru suśravā eva sauśravasastaṃ sauśravasam /
41.21.[10]	yathā tvaṃ suśravo devānāṃ vivadamānānāṃ vedasya nidhigopaḥ vedānāṃ nidheḥ samūhasya rakṣako’si bhavasi, evamahaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ sambandhino brahmaṇo vedasya nidhigopo bhūyāsam // 31 //
41.22.[1]	evaṃ prakṛtaṃ daṇḍaṃ pālāśaṃ brāhmaṇāya brahmacāriṇe’nuvacanānte prayacchatyācāryaḥ // 32 //
41.22.[2]	aśvattho vaṭaḥ // 33 //
41.22.[3]	vaiśyāya nyagrodhasambandhinaṃ prayacchati daṇḍam // 34 //
41.22.[4]	tacchāyāyāṃ pūrvatantrasyānuvacanaṃ kārayitvā, daṇḍaṃ dattvā kiṃ kārayatyācārya ityāha
41.23-24.[1]	yanmanvādibhiḥ smṛtaṃ yaccāsmṛtamanuṣṭheyatvena varjanīyatvena ca yathāsaṃkhyaṃ vratamavaśyaṃ pālanīyam /
41.23-24.[2]	evaṃ nindā ca me’nindā ca me iti ninditaṃ varjanīyamaninditamupādeyam /
41.23-24.[3]	athavā paranindā varjanīyā, anindā ca praśaṃsāvasare kartavyā paropakāraparyavasāyinī /
41.23-24.[4]	evaṃ vidyāvidye jñātavye hānopādānārtham /
41.23-24.[5]	śraddhā āstikyaṃ nāstikyamaśraddhā /
41.23-24.[6]	tathā satyānṛte /
41.23-24.[7]	amṛtamamaraṇakāri jñānakarmasamuccayānujñānāt jñeyaṃ mama vratam /
41.23-24.[8]	mṛtaṃ maraṇakāri kāmyaṃ saṃsārakāraṇaṃ, tadapi hānāya parapuruṣārthārthinā jñeyaṃ, svargādyarthinā tūpādānāya /
41.23-24.[9]	śrutaṃ mīmāṃsādiśravaṇam, aśrutaṃ kutsitaśrutaṃ lokāyatādiśāstrābhāsaviṣayam /
41.23-24.[10]	vrataṃ sadvratam, avrataṃ vratābhāsaḥ kartavyābhāsa ityarthaḥ /
41.23-24.[11]	yat brāhmaṇasya brahmaṇi vede vratamadhyayanādyarthaṃ tat mamāvaśyakartavyaṃ jñānapūrvam /
41.23-24.[12]	agneḥ prajāpatyādisahitasya yadvrataṃ karma, tat mayā jñeyamanuṣṭheyaṃ ca krameṇa /
41.23-24.[13]	sarvatra guro anugrahaṃ kurviti pratīyamānam /
41.23-24.[14]	janaskasyeti sakārāgamaśchāndasaḥ // 35 //
41.23-24.[15]	mantraliṅgādidamahamityanena samidhamagnau prakṣipati /
41.23-24.[16]	idamiti liṅgavyatyayaḥ /
41.23-24.[17]	imāṃ samidhamahamagnāvādadhāmi /
41.23-24.[18]	abhirābhyamukhyārthaḥ /
41.23-24.[19]	he agne tvatprasādāt sarvavrato bhavāmi bhūyāsam /
41.23-24.[20]	adhīte hetyādikamupanetṛstutyartham /
41.23-24.[21]	ya eva vidvān mantrabrāhmaṇajñaḥ sannupanayate sa evopanetṛtve’dhikṛto, nānyaḥ /
41.23-24.[22]	sa hi yamupanayate sa eteṣāṃ prasiddhānāṃ vedānāmanantaśākhāyuktānāṃ madhye yathecchamekaṃ dvau vā trīnvādhīte sarvān sarvaśākhākhacitān /
41.23-24.[23]	haśabda itihāse /
41.23-24.[24]	ato’nena saṃstutatvācchrautamupanayanaṃ, na saṃskārāntaravat smārtamata evopanayanāsamarthā apyavaśyaṃ kurvantīti kecit /
41.23-24.[25]	tadasat, smārtasyāpyanumitaśrutimūlatvāt /
41.23-24.[26]	apratyakṣaṃ tatra vidhiriti cet, arthavāde’pi samānatā /
41.23-24.[27]	yadapi bhaṇati mantragato na vidhāyaka ākhyātaśabda iti kṛtvā nedamahamityanena samitprakṣepaḥ kartavya iti, tadapyamīmāṃsakabhaṇitamākhyātasyāvidhāyakatve’pi liṅgātprakṣepasiddheḥ // 36 //
41.25.[1]	upanetre dakṣiṇāṃ dadāti brahmacāriṇaḥ svāmī pitā, tadabhāve jyeṣṭhabhrātrādiḥ // 37 //
41.26.[1]	nopaveśayet, nāpi saṃcārayet // 38 //
41.27.[1]	brahmacaryamupakrama eva 'upanayanaprabhṛti vratacārī syāt' ityādinoktamato na bhūya ucyate //
41.27.[2]	ityupanayanam //
42.1.[1]	tisṛṣu vidyāsu vedatrayātmikāsu bhavaṃ grahaṇaṃ prayojanaṃ vā vrataṃ traividyakam /
42.1.[2]	vakṣyāma iti śeṣaḥ // 1 //
42.1.[3]	yaṃ prati kathyate, so’prabuddho brahmacārī /
42.1.[4]	tena vyartha upadeśa ityāśaṅkyāha
42.2.[1]	ācāryeṇānuṣṭhātavya ityarthaḥ // 2 //
42.3.[1]	adhyayanasyārambhe samāptau cāṃhomugbhistisraḥ samidho’gnāvabhyādadhyāt svāhākāramātraśūnyaṃ prakṣepamātraṃ kuryādityarthaḥ, anyathā juhuyāditi brūyāt /
42.3.[2]	aṃhasaḥ pāpādvimocayantītyaṃhomuco mantrāḥ /
42.3.[3]	te punaḥ /
42.3.[4]	yaddevā devaheḻanaṃ devāsaścakṛmā vayam /
42.3.[5]	agnirmā tasmādenaso viśvānmuñcatvaṃhasaḥ //
42.3.[6]	yadi divā yadi naktamenāṃsi cakṛmā vayam /
42.3.[7]	vāyurmā tasmādenaso viśvānmuñcatvaṃhasaḥ //
42.3.[8]	yadi jāgradyadi svapna enāṃsi cakṛmā vayam /
42.3.[9]	sūryo mā tasmādenaso viśvānmuñcatvaṃhasaḥ //
42.3.[10]	devā eva devāsaḥ 'ājjaserasuk' he devā devāso’tiśayārthaṃ punaḥ sambodhanam, yadvayaṃ devaheḻanaṃ cakṛmā 'heḍṛ anādare' anādareṇāvalepena yaddevānāṃ pāpaṃ kṛtavanto vayam, tasmādenaso’ṃhasaḥ pāpāt viśvāt samastādagnirmāṃ vimuñcatu /
42.3.[11]	aṃhasa enasa iti duḥkhapīḍitasya punarvacanam /
42.3.[12]	enaḥśabdo vā pāpakṛte duḥkhātiśaye vartate /
42.3.[13]	anenaiva dvitīyatṛtīyau gatārthau /
42.3.[14]	divānaktaṃśabdābhyāṃ madhyavartinyau sandhye api saṃgṛhīte // 3 //
42.4.[1]	vratasyopāyanaṃ grahaṇaṃ, vimocanaṃ ca parityāgaḥ /
42.4.[2]	tadvayamapi darśapūrṇamāsayoruktam /
42.4.[3]	tathāca tatratyaṃ sūtraṃ 'pāṇī prakṣālya dakṣiṇato’gnestiṣṭhan brūyādagne vratapate vāyo vratapate sūrya vratapate' iti //
42.4.[4]	agne vratapate vratamālabhe tatte prabravīmi tacchakeyaṃ tenardhyāsam /
42.4.[5]	vāyo vratapate° /
42.4.[6]	sūrya vratapate° /
42.4.[7]	agne vratapate vratamacāriṣaṃ tadaśakaṃ tatte prabrūmastanno gopāya /
42.4.[8]	vāyo vrata° /
42.4.[9]	sūrya vrata° //
42.4.[10]	amī ṣaṭ kṛcchravidhau vyākhyātāḥ /
42.4.[11]	iha ca vratagrahaṇe mocane ca samānāḥ kartavyāḥ /
42.4.[12]	iyāṃstu viśeṣaḥ vimocane daṇḍamagnau prāsyedapsu mekhalāṃ vāsaśca hutasamāptiṃ yāvat /
42.4.[13]	tata eva daṇḍādayo mantrāvṛttibhājaḥ /
42.4.[14]	tathāca manuḥ 'yadyasya vihitaṃ carma yatsūtraṃ yā ca mekhalā /
42.4.[15]	yo daṇḍo yacca vasanaṃ tattatsarvaṃ teṣvapi //' iti // 4 //
42.4.[16]	iti traividyakamapavargasahitam //
42.4.[17]	iti dvācatvāriṃśī kāṇḍikā // 42 //
43.1-2.[1]	cittiḥ srugityādayo mantrāścaturhotāra ucyante teṣu bhavaṃ cāturhautṛkaṃ vrataṃ brahmacārikalpena brahmacāridharmopadeśinā vedabhāgena coditamupeyāt // 1 //
43.3.[1]	saṃvatsarametadvratamupeyāditi mukhyaḥ kalpaḥ /
43.3.[2]	aṣṭau caturo māsānvetyanukalpaḥ // 2 //
43.4.[1]	agneryaḥ pūrvadeśastatra darbhastambhaṃ nihatyādhītavedamanyaṃ brahmacāriṇamagnerdakṣiṇabhāge upaveśya agneḥ paścārdhe avasthitaḥ san 'hiraṇyavarṇā' ityādibhiścatasṛbhiścatasraḥ samidho’gnau pūrvavadabhyādadhyāt /
43.4.[2]	'hiraṇyavarṇā' ityādayaścatasraḥ saṃmārjane vyākhyātāḥ // 3 //
43.5.[1]	yadetatprastutaṃ brahmacāriṇo nityamavaśyakartavyaṃ vratagrahaṇaṃ, tatra 'brāhmaṇā vratapatayo vratamālabhe tadvaḥ prabravīmi tacchakeyaṃ tenardhyāsam' iti mantraṃ caturthaṃ kuryāt /
43.5.[2]	trayastu pūrvaṃ vyākhyātā atrāpi sthitā agne vratapate° vāyo vratapate° sūrya vratapate° iti // 4 //
43.6-8.[1]	vakṣyāma iti śeṣaḥ // 5 //
43.6-8.[2]	sapta caturhotāro’tra mantrāḥ /
43.6-8.[3]	śrapayitvetyetadantaṃ spaṣṭam /
43.6-8.[4]	ekaikaṃ caturhotāraṃ hutaṃ mantraṃ manasānumantrayate mantrāgamamanusandadhīta mantradvāreṇetyarthaḥ /
43.6-8.[5]	yadvedavihitaṃ vrataṃ, tat paripūrṇamastvatra mama vratamiti vācayet // 6 //
43.10.[1]	apavargaḥ samāptirvratasya tatra // 8 //
43.11.[1]	vastraṃ dakṣiṇāmācāryāya dakṣiṇata upaviṣṭāya dadyāt // 9 //
43.11.[2]	caturhotṛmantrān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ bhaktyā brahma vivartaṃ vā pariṇāmamupāśritān /
43.11.[3]	ādhyātmikaikarūpārthāṃścaturhotṝnnamāmyaham //
43.11.[4]	cittiḥ sruk cittamājyaṃ vāgvedirādhītaṃ barhiḥ keto agnirvijñātamagnidvācaspatirhotā mana upavaktā prāṇo haviḥ sāmādhvaryurindraṃ gaccha svāhā //
43.11.[5]	caturhotṝṇāmārtham /
43.11.[6]	indro devatā /
43.11.[7]	'hu dānādanayoḥ' juhvati dadatīti hotāraḥ /
43.11.[8]	caturṇāṃ dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ dātāraścaturhotāraḥ pradyumnāniruddhavāsudevasaṅkarṣaṇāḥ prathamabrahmavivartāḥ /
43.11.[9]	tathāca brāhmaṇaṃ 'brahma vai caturhotāraḥ' iti, prajāpatirakāmayata bahu syāmityādi ca /
43.11.[10]	evaṃ ca paramātmaiva yajñarūpaḥ stūyate /
43.11.[11]	yajño vai prajāpatiriti, viṣṇuryajña ityādirapi śrutiḥ /
43.11.[12]	ato’dhyātmayajñasvarūpaṃ rūpakeṇāha cetanaṃ cittirjñānaṃ sruk /
43.11.[13]	cittaṃ manaḥ svāntamantaḥkaraṇaṃ ceto mānasamiti paryāyaḥ, cittamājyaṃ yathāhi srucā ājyaṃ prakṣipyate’gnau tathā vivekajñānena manaḥ paramānandadhyānavahnau prakṣipyate /
43.11.[14]	yathāhi kṣiptamājyaṃ dahyate, tadvanmano’pyadhyātmadhyāne prakṣiptaṃ sat svayaṃ vilīyate sarvāvidyābhedāntarāṇi ca vilāpayati katakaphalarajovat /
43.11.[15]	vāgvediryajñāśrayatvāt /
43.11.[16]	yathāhi vedimāśritya yajñapātrāṇi srugādīni nijakāryeṣu vyāpriyante, tadvadvaidikīṃ vācamupaniṣadrūpāmāśritya manaḥprabhṛti adhyātmayajñasādhanaṃ nijakāryaṃ janayati /
43.11.[17]	ādhītaṃ barhiḥ, ādhyānamādhītiḥ cittadhyātṝṇāṃ tat barhistadāśritatvāccittisrugādīnāṃ 'prastare juhū sādhayati sarvāśca srucaḥ' iti śruteḥ /
43.11.[18]	keto agniḥ 'citī saṃjñāne' asun, chāndaso varṇavyatyayaḥ, ketaḥ prajñāviśeṣaḥ, sa evāgnistenaiva yogayogāṅgādisamidhāṃ sandīpanāt /
43.11.[19]	vijñātamagnit, viśiṣṭaṃ jñānaṃ vedārthagrāhi, agnit chāndaso hrasvaḥ, yathāhi ṛtvigviśeṣeṇaidhasāgniḥ sandīpyate, tathā vedārthajñānenottarottaramadhyātmacittāgniḥ /
43.11.[20]	vācaspatirhotā, vācaspatirantarātmā, sa hotā cittisrugādipreraṇāt, athavā āhvātā manaḥprabhṛtīnāmṛtvijāṃ preṣayitādhvaryuḥ /
43.11.[21]	mana upavaktā, manyate’numanyate iti mano’ntaryāmī, sa upavaktā brahmā /
43.11.[22]	sa hi yat jīvātmā jānāti karoti vā, tat sarvamanuvadatyanupaśyatītyādirūpeṇa anumanyate /
43.11.[23]	prāṇo haviḥ, sa hi paramātmāgnau hūyate niruddhyotkrāntikāle brahmadvāreṇa parabrahmaṇi prakṣipyate /
43.11.[24]	sāmādhvaryuḥ, sāmaśabdo vyānavacanaḥ, yathāhi adhvaryuḥ sarvartvijo nijanijakarmasu praiṣairniyacchati, tathā vyānākhyo vāyurnābherupari daśasvaṅguleṣu puruṣasthāne sthitaḥ prāṇāpānau svamaryādāyāṃ sthāpayati parasparaviruddhagatī /
43.11.[25]	etacca yogasāre nirṇītamasmābhiḥ /
43.11.[26]	yadeva puruṣasya sthānaṃ, tadeva vyānasya prāṇāpānayorniyantuḥ /
43.11.[27]	yadā hotṛpadena āhvātā adhvaryurucyate, tadā bhūtayajñādadhyātmayajñasya vailakṣaṇyapratītiḥ prayojanamadhvaryudvayapradarśanasya /
43.11.[28]	itthaṃ prajāpatinā indrādiśabdavācyena pradyumnādyavasthācatuṣṭayavivartena caturhotrā ca daśavidhamātmānaṃ kṛtvā paramātmani samarpaṇaṃ kṛtam /
43.11.[29]	tadāha indraṃ gaccha svāhā, he prāṇa indraṃ paramātmānaṃ gaccha, suhutamastu vāhūtaṃ vā /
43.11.[30]	āhvānasya ca śobhanatvamanuṣṭhāpanaparyavasānam /
43.11.[31]	evamasmadādayo’pi brahmavivartā brahmapariṇāmā vā saṃsāranivṛttikāmā anutiṣṭhanti, karmakāṇḍasyāpi ca advaitaprāptau paryavasānamityuktamasmābhiḥ sāṃkhyasāraśārīrakayoḥ /
43.11.[32]	evaṃ tāvadekaścaturhotā vyākhyātaḥ //
43.11.[33]	atha dvitīyaḥ /
43.11.[34]	pṛthivī hotā dyauradhvaryustvaṣṭāninmitra upavaktā vācaspate vāco vīryeṇa sambhṛtatamenāyakṣyase yajñapataye vāryamā svaskaro vācaspatiḥ somaṃ pibatu jajanadindramindriyāya svāhā //
43.11.[35]	anena prajāpatirūpayajñasyādhidaivikāni yajñasādhanānyucyante /
43.11.[36]	pṛthivī hotā, sā hi ādhibhautikayajñaprajāpaterannādihavirdānenāpyāyanaṃ karoti /
43.11.[37]	dyauradhvaryuḥ vṛṣṭyādipreṣaṇāt /
43.11.[38]	tvaṣṭā ādityaḥ agnit paktṛtvāt /
43.11.[39]	mitro ha upavaktā brahmā trayyarthabodhenaiva nirmalenālaṃkṛtatvāt /
43.11.[40]	he vācaspate prajāpate caturhotṛrūpa vāco mantrabrāhmaṇātmikāyā vīryeṇa arthatattvāvabodhabalena atiśayasambhṛtena mayā tvamāyakṣyase pūjayiṣyase /
43.11.[41]	sa tvamiṣṭaḥ san yajñapataye yajamānārthaṃ svaḥ svargamākaraḥ ābhimukhyena kuru /
43.11.[42]	kīdṛśaṃ svargam /
43.11.[43]	vāryaṃ varaṇārham /
43.11.[44]	vācaspatiḥ prajāpatiḥ somaṃ pibatu somaśabdena havirmātramatra lakṣyate, pibatinā ca upayogaḥ /
43.11.[45]	jajanadindram, anena cāturhotṛkeṇa karmaṇā prajāpatirjanitavānindramindravivartam /
43.11.[46]	tathāca śrutiḥ /
43.11.[47]	'te cāturhotrāḥ somaṃ gṛhapataye nyaṣīdannindraṃ janayāma' iti, te pṛthivyādayaḥ somaṃ gṛhapatiṃ kṛtvā caturhotrā mantreṇa niṣaṇṇā vedyāmindraṃ janayāmeti /
43.11.[48]	indriyāyeti vratavīryasampattyarthamityarthaḥ /
43.11.[49]	svāheti vyākhyātam //
43.11.[50]	atha tṛtīyaḥ /
43.11.[51]	kimarthaṃ caturhotā /
43.11.[52]	somaḥ somasya purogāḥ śukraḥ śukrasya purogāḥ śrātāsta indra somā vātāpe havanaśrutaḥ svāhā //
43.11.[53]	somo latārūpaḥ somasya candrasya purogāḥ agresaraḥ /
43.11.[54]	śukraḥ pradarśyaḥ somo vā śukraḥ śukrasya grahasyāsuragurorvā purogāḥ /
43.11.[55]	somāḥ śrātāḥ pakvāḥ āśritā vā /
43.11.[56]	somaśabdo havirmātra upacārāt /
43.11.[57]	upacāranimittaṃ tu vratasampattau krameṇa somayāgayogyatāpattiḥ /
43.11.[58]	he vātāpe vātāhāra havanaśrutaḥ āhvānasya śrotustava suhutaṃ svāhūtaṃ vā astu /
43.11.[59]	bahukarmaviniyogabhājo’mī caturhotāro yathāyogyaṃ bahvarthayujo yojyāḥ //
43.11.[60]	agnirhotāśvinādhvaryū rudro’gnidbṛhaspatirupavaktā vācaspate hṛdvidhe nāmanvācaspatiḥ somamapādāsmāsu nṛmṇaṃ dhāḥ svāhā //
43.11.[61]	ayaṃ pañcahotā 'te pāñcahotrā varuṇabṛhaspatayo nyaṣīdannindraṃ janayāma' iti hyasya brāhmaṇam /
43.11.[62]	atra cādhidaivikenādhiyajñiyānāmekatvamucyate mantre /
43.11.[63]	agnirhotā tathāca śrutiḥ 'agnirvai devānāṃ hotā' iti, mantraliṅgamapi 'agnimīḻe purohitam' iti /
43.11.[64]	aśvinau devabhiṣajau adhvaryū adhvaryupratiprasthātārau /
43.11.[65]	rudro’gnit, agnīdho rudraḥ /
43.11.[66]	bṛhaspatirupavaktā /
43.11.[67]	he vācaspate hṛdvidhe nāman hṛdi vidhirhṛdvidhirantaryāmī, tasya sambodhanaṃ he hṛdvidhe, nāman nāmnā antaryāmin tvaṃ vācaspatiḥ somamapāt somapaḥ ataḥ piba somamihāsmāsu asmabhyaṃ nṛmṇaṃ balaṃ ca dhāḥ dehi //
43.11.[68]	vāgghotā vāto’dhvaryurdīkṣā patnyāpo’bhigaro mano havistapasi juhomi vācaspate’cchidrayā vācācchidrayā jihvā divi devāvṛdhotrā mairayasva svāhā //
43.11.[69]	ayaṃ ṣaḍḍhotā /
43.11.[70]	adhyātmani yā vāk, saiva hotā /
43.11.[71]	vāto’dhvaryuḥ prāṇo’ntarikṣagatirvā /
43.11.[72]	dīkṣā vratasiddhirūpā patnī /
43.11.[73]	āpo’bhigaraḥ, śaṃsanamabhigarastatrāpa eva kartryo’nnādisaṃpādanadvāreṇa /
43.11.[74]	mano havirātmāgnau hūyamānatvāt tapasi brahmaṇi juhomi manaḥprabhṛtikaṃ brahmaṇi prakṣipāmi /
43.11.[75]	he vācaspate’cchidrayā avināśinyā vācā antaḥprakāśarūpayā acchidrayā jihvayā he divi deva me mama īrayasva prerayasva sampādaya karma /
43.11.[76]	kīdṛśyā vācā /
43.11.[77]	avṛdhoddhotrādṛṣṭahomādisampādanabhūtayetyarthaḥ //
43.11.[78]	mahāhavirhotā satyahaviradhvaryuracittapājā agnidacittamanā upavaktānāvṛṣyaścāpratidhṛṣyaścābhigarā ayāsya udgātā vācaspate vidhe nāmanvidhema te nāma vidhestvamasmākaṃ nāma mā devānāṃ tantuśchedi mā manuṣyāṇāṃ svāhā //
43.11.[79]	ayaṃ saptahotā mantraḥ /
43.11.[80]	'te sāptahotrā aryamagṛhapatayo nyaṣīdansantarāmi' iti hyasya brāhmaṇaṃ, saṃtaraṇaṃ brahmasaṃprāptiḥ /
43.11.[81]	mahāhaviścandraḥ sarvairupajīvyamānatvādata evāsya kalākṣayaḥ kṛṣṇapakṣe, sa hotā devānāṃ havirdānenāpyāyakatvāt /
43.11.[82]	satyahavirādityaḥ satatapreraṇāt, so’dhvaryuḥ /
43.11.[83]	acittapājā agnit, cittaprajñāśūnyo’gnīdvāyuragnīdhra ityarthaḥ /
43.11.[84]	evamacittamanā jñānamanovihīno vanyaphalaśākādirupavaktā /
43.11.[85]	kīdṛśaḥ /
43.11.[86]	anādhṛṣyaścāpratidhṛṣyaśca, anabhibhavanīyaḥ, atiśayāya bhūyovacanam /
43.11.[87]	abhigarāḥ, gṛṇātiḥ stutyarthaḥ /
43.11.[88]	ayāsya udgātā 'yasu prayatne' aprayatnasiddho vedopaniṣadrūpa udgātā, sa udgāyati tattvam /
43.11.[89]	he vācaspate vidhe nāman vidhema te tava nāma tvannāmārthaṃ yajñaṃ kurma ityarthaḥ /
43.11.[90]	yataśca tvamevāsmākaṃ nāma svarūpaṃ, tenāsmākaṃ devānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ ca mā tantuśchedi saṃtatiṃ mā cchetsīḥ /
43.11.[91]	suhutamastu tava //
43.11.[92]	iti cāturhautṛkamantrāḥ //
43.11.[93]	jñānānandamayaṃ nutvā paramātmānamacyutam /
43.11.[94]	pravargyavratamantrāṇāṃ bhāṣyaṃ prastūyate’dhunā //
43.11.[95]	tatra 'namo vāce' ityādyanuvākena 'prācyā tvā' ityādinā yajuścatuṣṭayarahitena 'divyo gandharvo bhuvanasya' iti 'āhuste bhaga' iti ca dvābhyāmanuvākābhyāṃ śāntibandhanaṃ kriyate /
43.11.[96]	tasya punaḥ kuṇḍe samabhimantrya sthāpanaṃ pradarśitānuvākaiḥ /
43.11.[97]	tataḥ śāntivimoko’vaśyakartavyaḥ /
43.11.[98]	ete ca mantrā mantrarahasyādau saṃmārjane ca kuśalā apīha tāvacchāntibandhāya yojyante //
43.11.[99]	namo vāce namo vācaspataye yā vāguditā yā cānuditā tasyai vāce namaḥ nama ṛṣibhyo maṃtro maṃtravidyo mā māmṛṣayo mantrakṛto maṃtravidaḥ parādurdaivīṃ vācamudyāsaṃ śivāmajasrāṃ juṣṭāṃ devebhyaḥ svadhāvatīṃ pitṛbhyaḥ śuśrūṣeṇyāṃ manuṣyebhyastaṃ māṃ devā avantu śobhāyai pitaro’numadantu sucakṣā ahamakṣibhyāṃ suvarcā mukhena suśrutkarṇābhyāṃ bhūyāsamoṃ bhūrbhuvaḥ svaḥ //
43.11.[100]	rudrasyārtham /
43.11.[101]	abhidheyo’rtho devatā /
43.11.[102]	yā mantramayī vāk tasyai vāce namo’stu /
43.11.[103]	vācaspataye vācāṃ vacanarūpāṇāṃ patistasmai uccārayitre namaḥ /
43.11.[104]	yā vāgupadiśantī sūkṣmā ca tasyai vāce namo namaḥ /
43.11.[105]	namaḥ śabdasya punaruccāraṇamatiśayārtham /
43.11.[106]	ābhyāṃ hi bhūyāṃsamarthaṃ manyante yathā aho ramaṇīyā aho ramaṇīyeti /
43.11.[107]	ye ca ṛṣayo mantravido mantrakṛtaśca tebhyo namo namaḥ /
43.11.[108]	tatra mantravido brahmavaktracatuṣṭayatūrṇavinirgatān mantrān sakṛdeva gṛhṇanti granthato’rthataśca sanakādayaste mantravidaḥ /
43.11.[109]	tathā cāraṇyakam /
43.11.[110]	'yathārdraidhāgnerabhyāhitasya pṛthagdhūmā viniścarantyevaṃ vā are’sya mahato bhūtasya viniḥśvasitametadyadyagvedo yajurvedaḥ sāmaveda' iti /
43.11.[111]	anyatrāpi 'ye sākṣātkṛtadharmāṇa ṛṣayo babhūvuste parebhyo’sākṣātkṛtadharmabhyo mantrān saṃprāduḥ' ityādi /
43.11.[112]	mā māmṛṣayo mantrakṛto mantravidaḥ parādurdaivīṃ vācam iti, ye mantrakṛto mantravidaśca ṛṣayaste devīṃ vācaṃ māṃ mā parāduḥ, māmiti pañcamyarthe dvitīyā, matsakāśāt parāṅmukhīṃ mā kārṣuḥ mantrarūpāṃ vācam /
43.11.[113]	kintarhi /
43.11.[114]	daivīṃ vācamahamudyāsaṃ 'yā prāpaṇe' utkarṣeṇa prāpnuyāmityarthaḥ /
43.11.[115]	śivāṃ śreyaskarīm, ajasrāṃ nityāṃ, juṣṭāṃ devebhyaḥ, devebhyaḥ prītijananīṃ 'juṣī prītisevanayoḥ' /
43.11.[116]	svadhāvatīṃ pitṛbhyaḥ, pitṛbhyo’nnavatīm, mantrairhi devāḥ prīyante pitaraśca svadhāṃ bhajante /
43.11.[117]	śuśrūṣeṇyāṃ manuṣyebhyaḥ, śravaṇārhāṃ śuśrūṣeṇyām /
43.11.[118]	tamevaṃbhūtaṃ māṃ stotāraṃ devā avantu, śobhāyai śobhayopalakṣitaṃ santaṃ pitaraścāvantu anumadantu anumādyantu, śobhāyai devāḥ pitaraśca hṛṣṭā bhavantu /
43.11.[119]	kiṃca devapitṛprasādādahamakṣibhyāṃ sucakṣā bhūyāsamakṣibhyāṃ sudarśanaḥ syāmityarthaḥ, sukhena ca suvarcā sudīptirbhūyāsam /
43.11.[120]	oṃbhūrbhuvaḥ svariti saṃkṣepeṇa vāgvibhava uktaḥ bhuvanatrayasya vāgvibhavavivartatvāt //
43.11.[121]	prācyā vā diśāgninā devatayā gāyatreṇa cchandasā vasantamṛtuṃ praviśāmi //
43.11.[122]	dakṣiṇayā tvā diśendreṇa devatayā traiṣṭubhena cchandasā grīṣmamṛtuṃ praviśāmi //
43.11.[123]	pratīcyā vā diśā savitrā devatayā jāgatena cchandasā varṣā ṛtuṃ praviśāmi //
43.11.[124]	udīcyā vā diśā mitrāvaruṇābhyāṃ devatayānuṣṭubhena cchandasā śaradamṛtuṃ praviśāmi //
43.11.[125]	ūrdhvayā tvā diśā bṛhaspatinā devatayā pāṃktena cchandasā hemantamṛtuṃ praviśāmi //
43.11.[126]	anayā tvā diśā prajāpatinā devatayā anāptena cchandasā śiśiramṛtuṃ praviśāmi //
43.11.[127]	gāyatrīṃ cchandaḥ praviśāmi /
43.11.[128]	triṣṭubhaṃ cchandaḥ pra0 /
43.11.[129]	jagatīṃ chandaḥ pra0 /
43.11.[130]	anuṣṭubhaṃ cchandaḥ pra0 /
43.11.[131]	paktiṃ cchandaḥ pra0 /
43.11.[132]	aticchandasāṃ cchandaḥ pra0 /
43.11.[133]	cchandāṃsi praviśāmi /
43.11.[134]	tāni naḥ pārayantu tāni no’vantu tāni sa ṛcchatu yo’smāndveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ //
43.11.[135]	āpo’smān praviśantvāpo’smāsu jāgrata /
43.11.[136]	āyurviśvāyurviśvamāyurvyaśnavai sarvamāyurvyaśnavai //
43.11.[137]	udakāvamarṣaṇapravṛtta eva tu chandaḥprabhṛtīnāmudakena sahābhinnatvamāropyodakamāha he udaka, tvāṃ vasantartubhūtamahaṃ praviśāmi prastutakarmaṇā tvāmārādhya tvanmayaphalāni labheyamityarthaḥ /
43.11.[138]	kena praviśāmi /
43.11.[139]	prācyā diśāgninā devatayā gāyatreṇa cchandasā /
43.11.[140]	evamṛtupañcakapraveśe vākyāni yojayitavyāni /
43.11.[141]	evaṃ gāyatrīṃ chandaḥ praviśāmītyādi /
43.11.[142]	cchandaḥ praveśavacanamātmādirakṣārthaṃ nirbhayasthānapraveśaparatvena yojayitavyam /
43.11.[143]	tāni cchandāṃsi no’smān pārayantu prastutasamāptiṃ kurvantu /
43.11.[144]	tāni no’vantu rakṣantu tarpayantu ca /
43.11.[145]	tāni sa ṛcchatu yo’smāndveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ, yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmo yaścāsmāndveṣṭi, sa tāni cchandāṃsi ṛcchatu, tāni chandaḥprabhṛtīni prāpya līyatāmityarthaḥ //
43.11.[146]	āpaḥ asmān praviśantu, adhiṣṭhātrī devatā rakṣakatvena māmadhitiṣṭhatvityarthaḥ /
43.11.[147]	āpo’smāsu jāgrata, he āpaḥ asmāsu jāgrata /
43.11.[148]	āyurviśvāyurviśvamāyurvyaśnavai sarvamāyurvyaśnavai, apāṃ prasādāt āyurvyaśnavai viśeṣeṇa vyāpnuyāṃ viśvāyurviśvamāyurityādi punarvacanamatiśayārthaṃ pūrvavat /
43.11.[149]	divyo gandharvo bhuvanasya yaspatirekāvyo manasā vikṣvīḍyaḥ /
43.11.[150]	taṃ tvā yāmi brahmaṇā deva devī namaste’stu divi te sadhastham //
43.11.[151]	divi pṛṣṭo yajata sūryatvagavayāto haraso divyasya /
43.11.[152]	ekāvyo manuṣyaḥ suśevaḥ /
43.11.[153]	mṛḻād gandharvo bhuvanasya yaspatiranavadyābhiḥ samajagmābhirapsaraḥsvapi gandharva āsītsamudra āsāṃ sadanaṃ va āhustataḥ sadhyā ca parācarantyabhriye didyunnakṣatriye yā viśvāvasuṃ gandharvaṃ sasadhre tābhyo namo astu tā no mṛḍayantu tā naḥ śarma yacchantu tā yaṃ dviṣmo yaśca no dveṣṭi tamāsāṃ jambhe dadmaḥ //
43.11.[154]	divi bhavo divyaḥ, gā raśmīndhārayatīti gandharvaḥ, sa eva rudraḥ iṣṭaḥ /
43.11.[155]	sa eva bhuvanasya patiḥ /
43.11.[156]	śrūyate hi 'ime vai lokā bhuvanaṃ teṣāmeṣo’dhipatiryo rudra iti' eka eva avati sarvaṃ rakṣatītyekāvyaḥ /
43.11.[157]	manasā vikṣvīḍyaḥ, vikṣu devasenāsu madhye sa eva īḍyaḥ stutyaḥ manasā mananadhyānādinā ārādhanīya ityarthaḥ, athavā vikṣviti vibhaktivyatyayaḥ viśāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ manasaiveḍyaḥ yo’sāvantarāditye puruṣa aupaniṣadaḥ /
43.11.[158]	he deva dyotanādikarmaka tamevaṃbhūtaṃ tvā bhuvanādhipatibhūtatvāt ahaṃ yāmi prāpnomi brahmaṇā mantrātmakena vedena vandamānaḥ stuvāna āyāmi vā prāptumicchāmītyarthaḥ /
43.11.[159]	ato namaste’stu yasya te divi sadhasthaṃ sthānaṃ tasmai /
43.11.[160]	'divi pṛṣṭaḥ' pravargyavratahomārambhārthamidamṛtvija uddiśyocyate /
43.11.[161]	he ṛtvijaḥ divi svarge pṛṣṭabhūto’yamādityaḥ sarvadevottama ityarthaḥ /
43.11.[162]	sūryatvak sūryasya tvagiva tvak yasya sa sūryatvak sūryāntarvatī puruṣa ityarthaḥ /
43.11.[163]	avayāḥ bālyādyavasthāśūnyo brahmaṇo’nādyantatvāt /
43.11.[164]	ato’sya divyasya harasastejorūpasya yajata he ṛtvijaḥ, ekāvyaḥ, manuṣṣu manuṣyeṣu mumukṣuṣu sādhurmanuṣyaḥ, suśevaḥ, śeva iti sukhanāma, nityānandasvabhāva ityarthaḥ, sukhasevyo vā chāndaso varṇavyatyayaḥ, suśevā iti kecitpaṭhanti mṛḍāt mṛḍaṃ sukhamattīti mṛḍāt nityasukhasya bhoktā /
43.11.[165]	gandharva iti vyākhyātam /
43.11.[166]	kābhiryajata /
43.11.[167]	anavadyābhirāhutibhiḥ samajagmābhiḥ samaṃ kṛtvā agniṃ yatantībhiḥ /
43.11.[168]	anekavikartṛkatvādbhāktaṃ yaugapadyam /
43.11.[169]	apsu saratītyapsarāstāsvapi gandharva āditya āsīdasti /
43.11.[170]	ayamatra vivekaḥ yadi kaścidāśaṅkate tretāyā abhāvādāhavanīyāḥ kathaṃ brahmacārivratāhutayastatredamuktam /
43.11.[171]	jalacāriṇīṣvapyāhutiṣvādityosti sarvatrago’sāvityarthaḥ /
43.11.[172]	ato he ṛtvija āsāṃ vo yuṣmākaṃ sambandhinīnāmāhutīnāṃ samudro mantrarūpo vedaḥ sadanamāśrayo gṛhamāhuḥ atastadbalena laukikāgnau hūyantām /
43.11.[173]	kāstāḥ /
43.11.[174]	yā hutāḥ satyastata eva mantrabalātsadhryā ca sahaiva yajamānena parācaranti /
43.11.[175]	kutra /
43.11.[176]	abhriye’bhracchanne’ndhatamase avidyāvṛta ityarthaḥ /
43.11.[177]	nakṣatriye prakāśe tattvāloke jñāna ityarthaḥ /
43.11.[178]	didyut atiśayena dyotamānā ajñānābhrapaṭalamapasārayantya ityarthaḥ /
43.11.[179]	viśvaṃ sarvaṃ vāsayati viśvāvasustaṃ gandharvamādityaṃ sasadhre gacchante yūyamapi he ṛtvija iti protsāhanā /
43.11.[180]	tābhyo vratāhutibhyo namo’stu mahāprabhāvābhyaḥ /
43.11.[181]	tāścāsmān mṛḍayantu sukhayantu tathā śarma sukhaṃ yacchantu /
43.11.[182]	punarabhidhānaṃ niratiśayamuktisukhārtham /
43.11.[183]	yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmo yaścāsmāndveṣṭi, taṃ vayamāsāmāhutīnāṃ jambhe sthāne vahnau dadmaḥ kṣipāmaḥ //
43.11.[184]	āhuste bhaga cakṣuṣī tābhyāṃ vipaśya māmabhi /
43.11.[185]	yadetatsāraghaṃ madhu tena rūpamanajmi te tena rūpamanagdhi me //
43.11.[186]	devasya tvā savituḥ prasave’śvinorbāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ devānāṃ kratubhirdevābhyañjanairabhyañje bhagavannāmāsi tasya ta ṛcaśca yajūṃṣi ca sāmāni ca vāgagnā anyaccakṣuḥ sūrye’nyadagnā anyadbhagavānbhūyāsam //
43.11.[187]	airosi cakṣurasi śrotramasi purandhirnāma vāgasi /
43.11.[188]	yena śatakraturbhāgamupajuhve tena tvopahvaye bhaga //
43.11.[189]	tadvāṃ narā sanaye daṃsa ugramāviṣkṛṇomi tanyaturna vṛṣṭim /
43.11.[190]	dadhyaṅ ha yanmadhvātharvaṇo vāmaśvasya śīrṣṇā sumatiravocat //
43.11.[191]	agnirīśo vāsavyasyāgnirmahaḥ saubhagasya tānyasmabhyaṃ rāsati //
43.11.[192]	atrāpi ca paramātmaiva rudrarūpa ādityo’śvināgnirūpeṇa stūyate /
43.11.[193]	bhajanīyaḥ sevanīyo bhago rudraḥ paramātmā tasya sambodhanam, he bhaga, tava cakṣuṣī āhurvedavidaḥ cakṣuṣmantaṃ tvāṃ vedavida āhuḥ /
43.11.[194]	'tasya sūryācandramasāveva cakṣuṣī' iti śrutestābhyāṃ cakṣurbhyāṃ viśeṣeṇa māmābhimukhyena cānukūlyena paśya atiśayārthaṃ punarvacanam /
43.11.[195]	saraghā madhumakṣikā /
43.11.[196]	tāsāmidaṃ sāraghaṃ yadetatprasiddhaṃ madhu, tena tava rūpaṃ tejomayamanajma te iti kecit /
43.11.[197]	sāraṃ dṛḍhaṃ saṃsāraṃ hantīti sāraghaṃ madhuraphalatvāt madhu tattvajñānaṃ, tena te cakṣuṣī candrādityarūpe’najmi kṛtāñjane saṃskṛte saṃpādayāmi tattvajñānaviṣayatvamāpādayāmītyarthaḥ /
43.11.[198]	tena rūpamanagdhi me, tvamapi ca mayā viśodhitacakṣurjñānakarmabhirmama yadrūpaṃ pāramārthikabrahmatattvātmakaṃ tadanagdhi añjanena saṃskuru vilīnāvidyopaplavaṃ kurvityarthaḥ /
43.11.[199]	devasyeti /
43.11.[200]	he rudra tvāmahamabhyañje devānāṃ sambandhibhirabhyañjanairdevairdyotanādiguṇakaiḥ ṛṣibhirvedārthābhyāsakuśalairyaistvamabhyakto jñānāhutiprabhṛtibhirityarthaḥ, devasya savituḥ prasave ājñāyāṃ vartamānaḥ, aśvinordevabhiṣajorbāhubhyāṃ na tu svābhyāṃ carmamayābhyāṃ sūryācandramasāvaśvinau aśvarathasaṃcāritvāt, pūṣṇaḥ ādityasya hastābhyāṃ devānāṃ ca /
43.11.[201]	kratubhirāhutibhiḥ pravargyavratahomasambandhinībhiḥ /
43.11.[202]	krāmantīti ṛtavo nityakarmajñānānīti sādhāraṇī vyākhyā /
43.11.[203]	he rudra bhagavannāmāsi sarvasyādhipatistvamityarthaḥ /
43.11.[204]	tasyaivaṃbhūtasya tatra ṛca ṛgvedaḥ, yajūṃṣi yajurvedaḥ, sāmāni sāmavedo vāk vaktīti vāk trayī tava vācikā ityarthaḥ /
43.11.[205]	tvayā vā pratisargādisuptapratibuddhanayena smṛtatvāttava trayī, tathā vāk /
43.11.[206]	agnā anyaccakṣuḥ sūrye cānyat, kāmyakarmāhutibhiḥ saṃtarpyate’gnau yā dṛṣṭistava, sānyā svargādiphalasya dātrī /
43.11.[207]	sūrye tu prakāśakaikasvarūpe dhyānādinā sākṣātkṛte’nyā mokṣasya dātrī yāpi kāmyaniṣiddharahitanityanaimittikakarmāhutibhiḥ saṃtarpyategnau tvadīyasvabhāvāntare dṛṣṭiḥ sūrye ca pūrvoktā sāpyanyā, jñānakarmasamuccayādapi tvaṃ mokṣaṃ sādhayasi gṛhamedhināmityarthaḥ, naiṣṭhikabrahmacaryāpekṣayā tu kevalajñānakṛtā muktirvyaktatayoktā /
43.11.[208]	ato’nena vratena bhagavānbhūyāsaṃ brahmabhūyaṃ prāpnuyāmityarthaḥ /
43.11.[209]	airosi, irā annaṃ tasyāyamairo’nnādhipatirasītyarthaḥ /
43.11.[210]	cakṣurasi /
43.11.[211]	śrotramasi /
43.11.[212]	purāṇi lokatrayasamūhāndhārayatīti puraṃdhristannāmikā vāgasi trayīmayosītyarthaḥ, yāvantaḥ prakāśakā bhāvāstāvanta ityarthaḥ /
43.11.[213]	he bhaga rudra tena mantreṇāhaṃ tvāmupahvaye āhvayāmi, yena śatakraturindro bhāgaṃ somādihaviṣo dānamupajuhve 'hu dānādanayoḥ' dadau cakhāda vetyarthaḥ /
43.11.[214]	tadvāmiti tat tasmāt he narāvaśvinau sūryācandramasau vā kalpitabhedau sanaye vibhajanāya idaṃ bhāgarūpaṃ haviṣa āviṣkaromi /
43.11.[215]	ugraṃ bahubalam /
43.11.[216]	ka iva kim /
43.11.[217]	tanyaturna vṛṣṭiṃ, na śabda upamāyām, tanyaturvāyurmeghādisaṃtānabhedatvāt, yathā vāyurvṛṣṭimāviṣkaroti vaidyutāditejaḥ saṃkṣobhaṇena /
43.11.[218]	dadhyaṅ ha yanmadhvātharvaṇa iti, atharvaṇo’patyaṃ dadhyaṅṅiti yasya saṃjñā, sa tathā vāṃ yuvāmaśvasya śīrṇāśvaśīrṣo bhūtvā āhūtavān sumatiyuktaḥ /
43.11.[219]	kimartham /
43.11.[220]	madhu madhune mokṣāyetyarthaḥ, mokṣasya nityānandasundaramadhumayatvāt, tadvadahamapi sumatiravocat yuvāmāhvaye ityarthaḥ //
43.11.[221]	agnirīśa iti, agnirvasavyasya īśaḥ, vasuni sādhu vasavyam hiraṇyaprabhṛtikaṃ tasyāgnirīśvaraḥ svāmītyarthaḥ /
43.11.[222]	agnirmahaḥ, saubhagasyeśa iti saṃbandhaḥ, mahataḥ saubhāgyasyāgniḥ prabhurityarthaḥ /
43.11.[223]	tāni vasavyasaubhāgyāni asmabhyaṃ rāsati dadātyagniḥ //
43.11.[224]	agne vratapate samrāḍasi vratapā asi vratabhṛdasi vratapatirasi vratamālabhe tatte prabravīmi tacchakeyaṃ tenardhyāsam //
43.11.[225]	vāyo vratapate° /
43.11.[226]	sūrya vratapate° /
43.11.[227]	agne vratapate iti tribhiragnimupatiṣṭhamāno vratamālabhate /
43.11.[228]	he agne vratapate vratasya prakṛtasya gopāyitaḥ, asi tvaṃ samrāḍ samyagrājase, vratapā vratasya pālayitā /
43.11.[229]	vratabhṛdasi vratasya poṣako bhavasi /
43.11.[230]	vratapatirasi vratasya svāmī bhavasi /
43.11.[231]	yata evaṃbhūtastvamata ucyate ahaṃ vratamālabhe ārabhe, tattasmātte prabravīmi tadvrataṃ tvatprasādādahaṃ kartuṃ śaknuyām tena ca karmaṇaḥ samṛddhiṃ phalalakṣaṇāṃ prāpnuyām /
43.11.[232]	vāyo vratapa° sūrya vratapate° ityetāvapi gatārthāvanenaiva //
43.11.[233]	pṛthivī samittāmagniḥ samindhe tāmahaṃ samindhe sā mā samiddhā suṣamiddhā tejasā varcasā yaśasā brahmavarcasena samindhyāt //
43.11.[234]	antarikṣaṃ samittāṃ vāyuḥ samindhe tāmahaṃ° //
43.11.[235]	dyauḥ samittāṃ sūrya samindhe tāmahaṃ° //
43.11.[236]	etaistribhiryathākramamagnau tisraḥ samidha ādadhāti vratasāhacaryāttiṣṭhanneva, nāsīnaḥ /
43.11.[237]	iyaṃ prathamā /
43.11.[238]	samit pṛthvī pārthivatvāt /
43.11.[239]	tāṃ samidhamagniḥ samindhe vyatyayenottamapuruṣaḥ samindhate /
43.11.[240]	tāmahaṃ samindhe dīpayāmi /
43.11.[241]	sā samiddhā suṣṭhu samiddhā satī māṃ brahmavarcasādibhiḥ samindhyāt samindhet /
43.11.[242]	evaṃ dvitīyā antarikṣamiva, tṛtīyā dyauriveti samānam //
43.11.[243]	sūrya vratapate samrāḍasi vratapā asi vratabhṛdasi vratapatirasi vratamacāriṣaṃ tadaśakaṃ tatte prabrūmastanno gopāya //
43.11.[244]	vāyo vratapate0 agne vratapate0 //
43.11.[245]	etaistribhiścūlikākramāpūtairvrataṃ vimucyate /
43.11.[246]	arthastūkta eva, kramamātrameva bhidyate sādhāraṇapadeṣu, tadacāriṣaṃ tadaśakamiti tu viśeṣaḥ /
43.11.[247]	tadvrataṃ caritaṃ tvatprasādānmayā, śaktiṃ ca tat sampannaṃ sat rakṣāmātramevāpekṣate /
43.11.[248]	tasmāt he sūrya vāyo agne tadvrataṃ nosmākaṃ gopāya rakṣa /
43.11.[249]	vratavimoke samittrayadānaṃ kartavyam /
43.11.[250]	tatrāpi ca mantrāḥ samidityādicūlikākrameṇeṣṭāḥ samidādānaṃ ca vratasāhacaryāttiṣṭhataḥ //
43.11.[251]	udu tyamiti daśarcenānuvākena homaḥ /
43.11.[252]	udutyaṃ jātavedasaṃ devaṃ vahanti ketavaḥ /
43.11.[253]	dṛśe viśvāya sūryam //
43.11.[254]	saṃdhyopāsane vyākhyāteyam /
43.11.[255]	imamūṣu tvamasmabhyaṃ saniṃ gāyatraṃ navīyāṃsam /
43.11.[256]	agne deveṣu pravocāt //
43.11.[257]	pravocādityākhyāpane loḍarthe leṭ, 'itaśca lopaḥ parasmaipadeṣu' itīkāralopaḥ, 'leṭo’ḍāṭa' /
43.11.[258]	ū ityanarthakaḥ, ṣu iti suśabda upasargaḥ saniśabdena sambadhyate /
43.11.[259]	he agne imaṃ homamasmabhyamasmākaṃ sambandhinaṃ gāyatraṃ anayā gāyatryā saṃpāditaṃ homaṃ tvaṃ deveṣu pravocāt prabrūhi, yaduta yuṣmākamayaṃ homo yuṣmadbhogya ityarthaḥ /
43.11.[260]	susaniṃ 'vana ṣaṇa saṃbhaktau' śobhanasaṃvibhāgaṃ, navīyāṃsamatiśayena navam //
43.11.[261]	samindra no manasā neṣi gobhiḥ saṃ sūribhirharivaḥ saṃ svastyā /
43.11.[262]	saṃ brahmaṇā devakṛtaṃ yadasti saṃ devānāṃ sumatyā yajñiyānām //
43.11.[263]	he indra harivaḥ haritavarṇāśvayukta no’smākaṃ manasā saṃneṣi saṃnayasi saṃvibhajasi śobhanamananadhyānādikaṃ saṃprayacchasītyarthaḥ /
43.11.[264]	evaṃ gobhiḥ saṃnayasi, sūribhirvidvadbhiḥ ṛtvigbhiryajñasahāyaiḥ saṃnayasi, svastyā avināśena mokṣaprāptilakṣaṇena saṃnayasi, tathā brahmaṇā vedena paramātmanā ca saṃnayasi brahmabhūyaṃ gamayasi devakṛtaṃ yadanyadapyutkṛṣṭamasti tena saṃnayasi, devānāṃ bṛhaspatiprabhṛtīnāṃ sambandhinyā sumatyā śobhanayā buddhyā saṃnayasyasmākam /
43.11.[265]	kīdṛśānām /
43.11.[266]	yajñiyānāṃ yajñārhāṇām /
43.11.[267]	yajñiyānāṃ devānāṃ sumatyā saṃnayasīti vā sambandhaḥ //
43.11.[268]	saṃ varcasā payasā saṃ tanūbhiraganmahi manasā saṃ śivena /
43.11.[269]	tvaṣṭā sudatro vidadhātu rāyo’nu no mārṣṭu tanvo yadviliṣṭam //
43.11.[270]	he indra vayaṃ tvatprasādādvarcasā dīptyā, payasā tanūbhiḥ śarīraiḥ svaputrādisambandhibhiḥ samaganmahi saṃgatāḥ bhūyāsma, śivena śāntena ca manasā samaganmahi /
43.11.[271]	tathā tvaṣṭā rāyo dhanaṃ vidhadātu naḥ sudatraḥ śobhanadātā suṣṭhu vā dātā, yastvaṣṭā anu anantaraṃ no’smākaṃ mārṣṭu saṃśodhayatu anumārṣṭviti vā saṃbandhaḥ /
43.11.[272]	kimanumārṣṭu /
43.11.[273]	yadanumārjanayogyaṃ kilbiṣamarthāt /
43.11.[274]	kīdṛśam /
43.11.[275]	viliṣṭaṃ vilagnamityarthaḥ iti kecit /
43.11.[276]	ayaṃ tvatrārthaḥ 'liśa alpībhāve' nityanaimittikādyanuṣṭhānena yadviśeṣeṇālpībhūtaṃ, tadeva helayaivānumārṣṭu tvaṣṭeti //
43.11.[277]	anvagniruṣasāmagramakhyadanvahāni prathamo jātavedāḥ /
43.11.[278]	anu sūryasya purutrā ca raśmīnanu dyāvāpṛthivī ātatantha //
43.11.[279]	agniḥ prathamo jātavedāḥ sargādāvutpanno vinā tadrūpeṇa jātadhano jātaprajñānaśca uṣasāṃ rātrīṇāmagramārambhamanvakhyadanuprakāśitavān nirmitavānityarthaḥ /
43.11.[280]	tato’hāni divasānanvakhyat /
43.11.[281]	tataḥ sūryasya raśmīnanvakhyatprakhyāpitavān /
43.11.[282]	kīdṛśo’gniḥ /
43.11.[283]	purutrā purūṇāṃ bahūnāṃ trātā, yadvā purureva purutrā 'purudevamanuṣyebhyastrā' iti trāpratyayastaddhitaḥ /
43.11.[284]	dyāvāpṛthivyau cānvātatantha vistāritavān //
43.11.[285]	yā vāṃ kaśā madhumatyaśvinā sūnṛtāvatī /
43.11.[286]	tayā yajñaṃ mimikṣatam //
43.11.[287]	he aśvinau yā vāṃ yuvayoḥ kaśā vāk, sā hi kaśeva niyantrī cittāśvānāṃ madhumatī madhupariṇāmā sūnṛtāvatī satyavatī tayā yajñaṃ vratāṅgabhūtaṃ mimikṣataṃ saṃmiśrīkurutamiti kecit /
43.11.[288]	ayaṃ tvarthaḥ 'miha secane' siñcatamāpyāyatamityarthaḥ //
43.11.[289]	dhātā dadhātu no rayimīśāno jagataspatiḥ /
43.11.[290]	sa naḥ pūrṇena vāvanat //
43.11.[291]	dhātā prajāpatirno’smabhyaṃ rayiṃ dhanaṃ dadhātu dhārayatu vā /
43.11.[292]	sa hi īśānaḥ prabhuḥ jagato jaṃgamasya trilokyā vā, jagataspatirjagatāṃ pātā /
43.11.[293]	sa dhātā no’smākaṃ pūrṇena anyūnena saṃvibhāgena vāvanat 'vana ṣaṇa saṃbhaktau' atiśayena saṃvibhajatu //
43.11.[294]	dhātā prajānāmuta rāya īśiṣe dhātedaṃ viśvaṃ bhuvanaṃ jajāna /
43.11.[295]	saṃdāśuṣe kirati bhūrivāṃsaṃ vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīṇām //
43.11.[296]	dhātā prajānāmīśiṣe īṣṭe /
43.11.[297]	kiṃ vā alpoktyā dhātaivedaṃ viśvaṃ samayaṃ bhuvanatrayaṃ jajāna janitavān jātavāṃśca /
43.11.[298]	dhātaiva dāśuṣe dattavate yajamānāya saṃkirati saṃdadāti /
43.11.[299]	kim /
43.11.[300]	bhūrivāṃsaṃ prabhūtameva nīraṃ saṃvibhajanīyaṃ yajñaphalādikam /
43.11.[301]	ato dhātuḥ prasādādvayaṃ rayīṇāṃ dhanānāṃ patayaḥ syāma //
43.11.[302]	trayastriṃśattantavo yānvitanvata imaṃ yajñaṃ svadhayā ye dadante /
43.11.[303]	teṣāṃ cchidraṃ pratidadhmo yadatra svāhāyaṃ yajño apyetu devān //
43.11.[304]	yajñaṃ tanvanti ye te tantavo yajamānartvikprabhṛtayaḥ /
43.11.[305]	trayastriṃśaditi tantraṃ yathāsambhavopalakṣaṇārthatvāt /
43.11.[306]	yāniti vyatyayaḥ /
43.11.[307]	ya imaṃ yajñaṃ tanvate svadhayā annena, ye dadate yajñaṃ, vyatyayena vā svadhāmannaṃ dadate devebhyo ye, teṣāṃ cchidraṃ vratavighnavidhāyiphalācaritādikaṃ tatpratidadhmaḥ pratividadhmahe vinivārayāmo’nena homena, yadatra vrate kiṃcidvighnakāri vastvanena homena vinivārayāma ityarthaḥ /
43.11.[308]	svāhā suhutamastu /
43.11.[309]	ayamapi yajño devānetu gacchatu //
43.11.[310]	idaṃ viṣṇurvicakrame tredhā nidadhe padam /
43.11.[311]	samūḍhamasya pāṃsure //
43.11.[312]	viṣṇuḥ prajāpatiryajñādirūpamidaṃ trailokyaṃ vicakrame vikrāntavān /
43.11.[313]	tredhā nidadhe padaṃ, tribhiḥ padaistrilokīrūpeṇa vivṛttaḥ pariṇato vetyarthaḥ /
43.11.[314]	samūḍhamasya pāṃsure, caturthaṃ padaṃ caturthacaraṇarūpamavivṛttamapariṇataṃ ca yadasya tāttvikaṃ brahmaṇo rūpaṃ tat pāṃsure’vidyayā succhanne samūḍhaṃ samyag bruḍitaṃ nāyogibhirgamyate ityarthaḥ //
43.11.[315]	atra ca vratāpavarge 'mā no gharma' ityanuvākena pratyṛcamekonatriṃśadāhutayo hotavyāḥ /
43.11.[316]	mā no gharma vyathito vivyatho no mā naḥ paramadhāmāhruto naiḥ /
43.11.[317]	moṣvasmāṃstamasyantarādhā mā rudriyāso abhikurvato naḥ //
43.11.[318]	he gharma pravargyavrata no’smān vyathitaḥ san mā vivyathaḥ pramādajenāparādhena vaiguṇyamāpāditopi sannasmākaṃ vyathāṃ mā kārṣīrityarthaḥ /
43.11.[319]	mā naḥ paramadhāmāhruto naiḥ, 'hvṛ kauṭilye', ahrutaḥ akuṭilaḥ san paramadhāma paramaṃ sthānaṃ mṛtyugṛhaṃ mā naiḥ mā naiṣīḥ /
43.11.[320]	moṣvasmāṃstamasyantarādhāḥ, mā u su māśabdo niṣedhārthaḥ, uśabdaścārthe, suśabdaḥ tamaḥśabdena sambadhyate /
43.11.[321]	mā cāsmānsutamasi andhatamase narake ādhāḥ kṣaipsīḥ antarmadhye /
43.11.[322]	mā rudriyāso abhikurvato naḥ, rudriyāso rudrasambandhinyaḥ krūrāḥ śaktayo no’smākamabhikurvato’smadābhimukhyena svakāryāṇi mā kārṣuḥ, akrūrabhāvo’stu //
43.11.[323]	mā naḥ kratubhirīḻate’bhidviṣo asmānsunīte māparādhāḥ /
43.11.[324]	mā no agniṃ nirṛtimarātiṃ mā no dyāvāpṛthivī heḻate heḻayethām //
43.11.[325]	rudraḥ prārthyate /
43.11.[326]	no’smānye ’bhidviṣo’bhimukhāḥ śatravaste kratubhirmā īḻate kratukaraṇe pravṛttāḥ santaḥ stutiṃ mā kārṣuḥ, yathā prahṛṣṭo rudrastacchatrutvādasmāsu virūpaṃ kaṃcidādadhītāniṣṭamityarthaḥ /
43.11.[327]	asmadviṣo yājñikā mā bhūvannityarthaḥ /
43.11.[328]	kiṃ tarhi /
43.11.[329]	kukarmācaraṇena svayaṃ kṣīyantāmityarthaḥ /
43.11.[330]	asmānsunīte māparādhāḥ /
43.11.[331]	he sunīte sunītiriti bahuvrīhiḥ, he śobhananayayukte’smān māparādhā aparādhayogino mā kṛthā ityarthaḥ /
43.11.[332]	mā no agnimityādi dvitīyā prathamārthe, no’smānagnirmā heḻate 'heḍṛ anādare' anādaraṃ kopamasmāsu mā kārṣīt /
43.11.[333]	evaṃ nirṛtirarātirmā heḻate iti yojyam /
43.11.[334]	evaṃ dyāvāpṛthivyau mā heḻayethāmiti samanvayaḥ kāryaḥ //
43.11.[335]	anu no mitrāvaruṇā ihāvatāmanudīdhyānā abhi naḥ sakhāyau /
43.11.[336]	ādityānāṃ prasṛtirhṛtirugrā śivā pāṣṭā haviṣaḥ pariṇo vṛṇaktu //
43.11.[337]	mitramahaḥ sarvaprāṇyupakāritvāt, varuṇo rātrikālaḥ varaṇāt tamasāvaraṇāt /
43.11.[338]	iha vratasamāptikarmaṇi mitrāvaruṇāvanvavatāṃ rakṣatāṃ no’smākam /
43.11.[339]	kīdṛśau /
43.11.[340]	anudīdhyānau dīpyamānau tejasābhimukhau, asmākañca sakhāyau /
43.11.[341]	tathā ādityānāṃ sambandhī prasṛtiḥ prasāraḥ karanikaro no’smākaṃ haviṣaḥ parivṛṇaktu haviṣyānnādi varjayatu atidīptatvātsasyaprabhṛtīnmā dhākṣīdityarthaḥ /
43.11.[342]	yato’sau hṛtiḥ, harati balaṃ tīvratayeti hṛtiḥ, śivā śāntā bhūyāt, yataḥ sā pāṣṭā praṣṭhā pradhānabhūtā /
43.11.[343]	'praṣṭho’gragāmini' ityanuśāsanāt, ataḥ ugrāpi satī prārthanāvaśācchāntā syādityarthaḥ //
43.11.[344]	vidhuṃ dadrāṇaṃ samane bahūnāṃ yuvānaṃ santaṃ palito jagāra /
43.11.[345]	devasya paśya kāvyaṃ mahitvā dyāṃ mamāra sahyaḥ samānaḥ //
43.11.[346]	rudra evādityarūpeṇa stūyate /
43.11.[347]	tasmādābhyāṃ juhuma iti śeṣaḥ /
43.11.[348]	devasya dyotanādādityasya paśya kāvyaṃ krāntikarma mahitvā mahat, yadetadīyena vikrameṇa sahyaḥ sahanārhaḥ sahabhāvo vā samānaśca ojorūpeṇa candramāḥ dyāṃ divi mamāra prāṇatyāgaṃ kṛtavānamāvasyāyām /
43.11.[349]	tathā hyayamādityaḥ palito vṛddhaḥ parito vā sarvataḥ yuvānamapi kalāparipūrṇaṃ samarthaṃ jagāra bhakṣitavān candraṃ vidhuṃ vidhāvanakriyāyuktaṃ ataeva dadrāṇaṃ gacchantaṃ satatagatim /
43.11.[350]	samane bahūnāṃ, ādityaraśmīnāṃ svakalānāṃ saṃgame sati paurṇamāsyām /
43.11.[351]	yuvānamapītyanvayaḥ //
43.11.[352]	oṃ bhūḥ svāhā /
43.11.[353]	oṃ bhuvaḥ svāhā /
43.11.[354]	oṃ svaḥ svāhā /
43.11.[355]	oṃ bhūrbhuvaḥ svaḥ svāhā //
43.11.[356]	udu tyaṃ jātavedasaṃ devaṃ vahanti ketavaḥ /
43.11.[357]	dṛśe viśvāya sūryam //
43.11.[358]	vyākhyāteyam /
43.11.[359]	udvayantamasaspari jyotiṣpaśyanta uttaram /
43.11.[360]	devaṃ devatrā sūryamaganma jyotiruttamam //
43.11.[361]	iyamapi vyākhyātā /
43.11.[362]	udu tiṣṭha svadhvarāvā no devyā kṛpā dṛśe ca bhāsā /
43.11.[363]	bṛhatā suśukvabhiragne yāhi suśastibhiḥ //
43.11.[364]	he svadhvara śobhanādhvara pravargyavrata udu tiṣṭha, ut u tiṣṭha, uśabdaḥ pādapūraṇārthaḥ, uttiṣṭha, no’smān ava rakṣa devyā devasambandhinyā kṛpā sāmarthyena, bṛhatā mahatyā bhāsā dīptyā, dṛśe darśanāya /
43.11.[365]	he agne tvamapi yāhi gaccha suśukvabhiḥ śobhanābhiḥ śauryādibhirjyālābhiḥ, suśastibhiḥ śobhanapraśaṃsāyuktābhiḥ śubhasūcikābhirupalakṣita ityarthaḥ //
43.11.[366]	ūrdhva ū ṣu ṇa ūtaye tiṣṭhā devo na savitā /
43.11.[367]	ūrdhvo vājasya sanitā yadañjibhirvāghadbhiḥ vihvayāmahe //
43.11.[368]	he agne tvāṃ vayaṃ vihvayāmahe vividhamāhvayāmaḥ /
43.11.[369]	kaiḥ /
43.11.[370]	añjibhirabhivyaktairvākyaiḥ /
43.11.[371]	kīdṛśaiḥ vāghadbhiḥ voḍhṛtamaiḥ saṃśodhanādisamathairityarthaḥ /
43.11.[372]	yaditi yasmādarthe /
43.11.[373]	yata ūrdhvastiṣṭha ūrdhvo bhava /
43.11.[374]	ū iti nipāto’narthakaḥ /
43.11.[375]	suśabda upasargaḥ ūtaye ityanena saṃbadhyate /
43.11.[376]	kimarthamūrdhvo bhava /
43.11.[377]	sūtaye śobhanāvanāya no’smākam /
43.11.[378]	devo na savitā, naśabda upamāyāṃ, deva iva savitā tvamūrdhvo vājasya annasya sanitā 'vana ṣaṇa saṃbhaktau' saṃvibhaktā //
43.11.[379]	punarūrjā nivartasva punaragna iṣāyuṣā /
43.11.[380]	punarnaḥ pāhyaṃhasaḥ //
43.11.[381]	he agne ūrjā ājyalakṣaṇena anneneṣṭaḥ sanpunarnivartasva punarapi iṣā odanalakṣaṇena anneneṣṭaḥ sannivartasva āyuṣā yuktaḥ san haviṣā vṛddha ityarthaḥ, punarapi ca no’smān pāhi rakṣa aṃhasaḥ pāpāt //
43.11.[382]	saha rayyā nivartasva agne pinvasva dhārayā /
43.11.[383]	viśvapnyā viśvataspari //
43.11.[384]	he agne nivartasva samāpteṣvapi vrateṣu mā gāḥ rayyā dhanena saha, kiṃca pinvasva asmān prīṇīhi /
43.11.[385]	kayā /
43.11.[386]	dhārayā dhārayitryā śaktayā /
43.11.[387]	kīdṛśyā /
43.11.[388]	viśvapnyā sarvasyotpattau sphītayā viśvataspari sarvasyopari sthitayā //
43.11.[389]	dhātā dadhātu no rayimīśāno jagataspatiḥ sa naḥ pūrṇena vāvanat //
43.11.[390]	dhātā prajānāmuta rāya īśiṣe dhātedaṃ viśvaṃ bhuvanaṃ jajāna /
43.11.[391]	saṃ dāśuṣe kirati bhūrivāṃsaṃ vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīṇām //
43.11.[392]	agna āyūṃṣi0 /
43.11.[393]	agne pavasva0 /
43.11.[394]	tvaṃ no agne0 /
43.11.[395]	sa tvaṃ no agne0 //
43.11.[396]	vāyuragre gā0 /
43.11.[397]	ete sapta mantrāḥ vyākhyātāḥ //
43.11.[398]	pra yābhiryāsi dāśvāṃsamacchā niyudbhirvāyaviṣṭaye duroṇe /
43.11.[399]	ni no rayiṃ subhojasaṃ yuvasva ni vīraṃ gavyamaśvyaṃ ca rādhaḥ //
43.11.[400]	he vāyo yābhirniyudbhiraśvaistvaṃ prayāsi gacchasi dāśvāṃsaṃ haviṣo dātāraṃ yajamānam /
43.11.[401]	kimartham /
43.11.[402]	iṣṭaye yajanāya, accheti nipāto’bhiśabdasyārthe vartate, abhiprayāsi /
43.11.[403]	tvaṃ tābhirniyudbhirduroṇe gṛhe no’smānniyuvasva 'yu miśraṇe' niyojaya, rayiṃ dhanaṃ subhojasaṃ śobhanānnaṃ ca no gṛhe niyuvasva, vīraṃ ca putraṃ niyuvasva /
43.11.[404]	kīdṛśam /
43.11.[405]	gavyaṃ goṣu sādhuṃ tathāśvyaṃ rādhaśca dhanamaśvyam /
43.11.[406]	punarvacanamatiśayārtham /
43.11.[407]	abhyāse hi bhūyāṃsamarthaṃ manyante yathāho ramaṇīyāho ramaṇīyeti //
43.11.[408]	hiraṇyagarbhaḥ0 //
43.11.[409]	yaḥ prāṇataḥ° //
43.11.[410]	ya ojodā0 //
43.11.[411]	yena dyaurugrā0 //
43.11.[412]	ya ime dyāvā0 //
43.11.[413]	yasya me viśva0 //
43.11.[414]	etāḥ ṣaṭ vyākhyātāḥ //
43.11.[415]	yaṃ krandasī apasā tastabhāne abhyaikṣetāṃ manasārejamāne /
43.11.[416]	yatrādhi sūra udito vibhāti kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema //
43.11.[417]	yaṃ krandasītyasyāḥ ayamarthaḥ /
43.11.[418]	dyāvāpṛthivyabhidhānā prasiddheyaṃ yājñikānām /
43.11.[419]	yatra sūra ādityo’bhyudito vibhāti, tasmai kasmai prajāpataye sarvātmane haviṣā vidhema havirdadhmaḥ haviṣopacarāmastamityarthaḥ /
43.11.[420]	yaṃ yatra krandasī krandanayukte ghanastanitavedādhyayanaśabdavatyau dyāvāpṛthivyāvapasā pāpavihīne’bhyaikṣetām yadadhiṣṭhāne satyau kāryāṇi nirūpayataḥ manasā mananena tastabhāne’vaṣṭambhana yukte arejamāne cākampamāne ca sthāvararūpe iti yāvat /
43.11.[421]	yatra sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ, tasmai prajāpataye havirājyalakṣaṇaṃ juhuma iti tātparyam //
43.11.[422]	ata ūrdhvaṃ pravargyavrate śāntivimokaḥ siddhaḥ /
43.11.[423]	sa ihāpi kartavyaḥ /
43.11.[424]	taṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ /
43.11.[425]	āyurdā āyurme dehi prāṇadāḥ prāṇaṃ me dehi vyānadā vyānaṃ me dehi apānadā apānaṃ me dehi cakṣurdāścakṣurme dehi śrotradāḥ śrotraṃ me dehi varcodā varco me dehi āyuṣe naḥ punardehi //
43.11.[426]	etāni sapta yajūṃṣi /
43.11.[427]	saptānāmapica 'āyuṣe naḥ punardehi' iti sādhāraṇo’nuṣaṅgaḥ //
43.11.[428]	pravargyavrataṃ, sarvakarmako vā prajāpatirucyate /
43.11.[429]	he pravargyavrata prajāpate vā, āyuṣo dātā tvaṃ, ata āyurme mahyaṃ dehi /
43.11.[430]	āyuṣe naḥ punardehi, āyuṣa iti tādarthyacaturthyantena āyurlakṣaṇajīvananimittāni nityakarmāṇyupalakṣyante, nityanaimittikakarmānuṣṭhānārthaṃ punarāyurmahyaṃ dehītyarthaḥ /
43.11.[431]	eṣāṃ ṣaṇṇāmapi yajuṣāṃ tulyā dik //
43.11.[432]	namo rudrāya diviṣade yasya varṣamiṣavastasmai namaste namaḥ samare sa mā mā hiṃsīḥ //
43.11.[433]	ādityo’tra rudraḥ /
43.11.[434]	ādityāya namaḥ /
43.11.[435]	divi sīdatīti diviṣat tasmai /
43.11.[436]	yasya varṣamiṣavaḥ, vṛṣṭirvarṣaṃ dhārāsāro yasya śarāstasmai punaḥpunarnamaskāro’stu /
43.11.[437]	tena ca namaskāreṇa prasāditaḥ saṃstvaṃ rudro mā mā hiṃsīḥ māṃ mā vadhīḥ /
43.11.[438]	dvitīyasya mā ityasya yuṣmadādeśasya prayogo’smadīyopalakṣaṇārthaḥ, asmadīyāṃśca putraprabhṛtīn mā hiṃsīrityarthaḥ /
43.11.[439]	samare saṃgrāme //
43.11.[440]	namo rudrāyāntarikṣasade yasya vāta iṣavastasmai0 //
43.11.[441]	namo rudrāya pṛthivīṣade yasyānnamiṣavastasmai0 //
43.11.[442]	samānaṃ pūrveṇa //
43.11.[443]	'brahmaṇa upastaraṇamasi' ityanuvākaṃ japanti /
43.11.[444]	te japanto 'mitrasya carṣaṇīdhṛta' iti maitryā prathamayādityamavekṣante abliṅgābhiścāpa upaspṛśanti /
43.11.[445]	brahmaṇa upastaraṇamasi brahmaṇe tvopastṛṇāmīḻāyai vāstvasi vāstumadvāstumānbhūyā vāstuḥ sa bhūyādyo’smāndveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ //
43.11.[446]	he udaka asi tvaṃ brahmaṇa upastaraṇaṃ, brahmā tvāmupastīrya bījabhūtamuptvā lokān sṛjati /
43.11.[447]	yathoktam 'apa eva sasarjādau tāsu vīryamathākṣipat /' iti vīryaṃ śaktirudakasyaiva tu sarvakāryanimittatvam /
43.11.[448]	brahmaṇe tvopastṛṇāmi, brahmapadaprāptaye tvāmahamupaspṛśāmi /
43.11.[449]	iḻāyai ca tvāmupaspṛśāmi iḻā annaṃ tacca brahmapadārthināpyabhyarthanīyaṃ taddhetukanityakarmādisādhyatvād apavargasya /
43.11.[450]	vāstvasi gṛhamasi sarvāśrayatvāt, vāstumat brahmā hi tava gṛhamāśrayabhūtaṃ vartate /
43.11.[451]	vāstumān bhūyāḥ puruṣavyatyayo’tra /
43.11.[452]	tvatprasādādahaṃ vāstumān bhūyāsam gṛhavānsyāṃ brahmabhūyaṃ prāpnuyāmityarthaḥ /
43.11.[453]	avāstuḥ sa bhūyādyo’smāndveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ so’pratiṣṭho bhūyāt //
43.11.[454]	pratiṣṭhāsi pratiṣṭhā me bhūyādapratiṣṭhaḥ sa bhūyādyo’smāndveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ //
43.11.[455]	pratiṣṭhante yatra lokāḥ sa pratiṣṭhā asi bhavasi udaka tvamato mama pratiṣṭhā bhūyāt /
43.11.[456]	yastu asmān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ so’pratiṣṭho bhūyāt //
43.11.[457]	ā vāta vāhi bheṣajaṃ vi vāta vāhi yadrapaḥ /
43.11.[458]	tvaṃ hi viśvasya bheṣajo devānāṃ dūta īyase //
43.11.[459]	he vāta bheṣajaṃ satkarmaphalaṃ brahmaprāptilakṣaṇamāvāhi prāpaya, yadrapaḥ pāpamavidyālakṣaṇaṃ tadvivāhi apasāraya /
43.11.[460]	yatastvaṃ sarvasya bheṣajaḥ auṣadhaṃ saṃsāravyādhibādhakatvāt tathā devānāṃ dūtaśca īyase sañcarasi karmānuṣṭhānarūpaiḥ phalairyojayasi /
43.11.[461]	yata evaṃbhūtastvaṃ tasmāducyase //
43.11.[462]	yatado vāta te gṛhe nihitasya nidhihitaḥ /
43.11.[463]	tato no dhehi jīvase tato no abhayaṃ kṛdhi //
43.11.[464]	he vāta tava nidhihito nidhimato gṛhe nihitasya sarvakarmaphalasya yataḥ saṃbhavaḥ, tenātaḥ karmaṇo yadbhāgadheyaṃ, tannastato nidhehi /
43.11.[465]	yatada iti dakārasya takāraśchāndasaḥ /
43.11.[466]	kecittu yadata iti paṭhanti /
43.11.[467]	śatādhyayanasyādhyetāraḥ nidhirhi sa ityapi paṭhanti /
43.11.[468]	sa tava gṛhe tvanāśrayatvena vyavasthitaḥ prajāpatiḥ sarvaphalavidhānabhūta iti tatrārthaḥ /
43.11.[469]	kimarthaṃ dehi bhāgadheyam /
43.11.[470]	jīvase jīvanāya cirataropabhogyasvargādiphalopabhogāyetyarthaḥ /
43.11.[471]	tato no’bhayaṃ kṛdhi, yadasmābhiḥ karma kriyate tato’smākamabhayaṃ kṛdhi saṃsāratamo’vidyāsmitārāgadveṣābhiniveśalakṣaṇakleśabhayanivāraṇaṃ kurvityarthaḥ /
43.11.[472]	evamapi vyācakṣate he vāta tava yatato yatamānasya gṛhe yadvyavasthitaṃ phalaṃ tato nidhehi kiṃcijjīvanāya abhayāya iti //
43.11.[473]	dyubhiraktubhiḥ paripātamasmānariṣṭebhiraśvinā saubhagebhiḥ /
43.11.[474]	tanno mitro varuṇo māmahantāmaditiḥ sindhuḥ pṛthivī uta dyauḥ //
43.11.[475]	he aśvinau asmān paripātaṃ samantādrakṣatam /
43.11.[476]	kaiḥ /
43.11.[477]	dyubhirdivasaiḥ /
43.11.[478]	kīdṛśaiḥ /
43.11.[479]	aktubhirabhivyaktaiḥ nirabhrairata eva subhagaiḥ, riṣṭaṃ hiṃsakaṃ tadrahitairariṣṭaiḥ /
43.11.[480]	yacca kiñcana vayaṃ kurmastanmāmahantāmatiśayena pūjayantu /
43.11.[481]	ke te /
43.11.[482]	mitro varuṇo’ditiḥ sindhurnadīsamudralakṣaṇaḥ pṛthivī uta dyauḥ //
43.11.[483]	pṛthivī śāntirantarikṣaṃ śāntirdyauḥ śāntirdiśaḥ śāntirāpaḥ śāntiroṣadhayaḥ śāntirvanaspatayaḥ śāntistvayāhaṃ śāntyā sarvaśāntyā mahyaṃ dvipade catuṣpade śāntiṃ karomi śāntirno astu śāntirasi śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ //
43.11.[484]	pṛthivī no’smākaṃ śāntiḥ 'astu' iti sarvatrānuṣaṅgaḥ /
43.11.[485]	astvityasya cānuṣaktasya bahuvacanānteṣu vanaspatiprabhṛtiṣu vipariṇāmaḥ /
43.11.[486]	he udaka tvayā śāntyātmakena sarvaśāntyātmakenāhaṃ 'śāntiyukto bhūyāsam' iti śeṣaḥ /
43.11.[487]	ato’haṃ mahyaṃ svārthaṃ dvipade putrādyarthaṃ catuṣpade gavādyarthaṃ śāntiṃ karomi /
43.11.[488]	yato’si tvaṃ śāntirataḥ śāntirno astu, avidyādikleśāḥ śāmyantu naḥ ityarthaḥ /
43.11.[489]	mumukṣuṃ prati śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiriti abhyāso’tiśayārthaḥ saṃsārakleśakamayatvapradarśanārthaḥ //
43.11.[490]	yā vāguditā yā cānuditā śivā naḥ śaṃtamā bhava sumṛḍīkā sarasvati mā te vyoma saṃdṛśi //
43.11.[491]	he vāk sarasvati yā tvamuditoccāritā vaikharīrūpā, yā ca anuditā antaḥsaṃjalpādirūpā madhyamā paśyantī sūkṣmā ca sā no’smākaṃ śivā kṣemakāriṇī bhava śaṃtamā sukhatamā, sumṛḻīkā śobhanasukhā /
43.11.[492]	abhyāso’tiśayārthaḥ /
43.11.[493]	mā te vyoma saṃdṛśi, vyoma cchidraṃ te tava vyoma cchedaṃ mā drākṣaṃ tvadvihīnaḥ kadācidapi mā bhūvamityarthaḥ, avicchinnasthitiṃ ca tvāṃ divyena cakṣuṣā jānīyāmityarthaḥ //
43.11.[494]	mitrasya tvā cakṣuṣā prekṣe mitrasya tvā cakṣuṣānvīkṣe /
43.11.[495]	sūryasya tvā cakṣuṣā prekṣe sūryasya tvā cakṣuṣābhivīkṣe //
43.11.[496]	he vāk tvāmahaṃ mitrasya cakṣuṣā prekṣe, mitrasya cakṣuṣānvīkṣe mitradṛṣṭyā anupaśyāmītyarthaḥ /
43.11.[497]	evaṃ sūryasyeti vyākhyeyam /
43.11.[498]	abhiśabda ābhimukhye’tra //
43.11.[499]	'mitrasya carṣaṇīdhṛta' iti maitrīṃ japannādityamīkṣate /
43.11.[500]	mitrasya carṣaṇīdhṛtaḥ śravo devasya sānasi /
43.11.[501]	dyumnaṃ citraśravastamam //
43.11.[502]	mitrasya sarvaprītikāriṇa ādityasya śravo dhanaṃ raśmilakṣaṇaṃ annādihetutvāt 'ahaṃ vīkṣe' iti śeṣaḥ /
43.11.[503]	kīdṛśasya mitrasya /
43.11.[504]	carṣaṇīdhṛtaḥ carṣaṇayo manuṣyāsteṣāṃ dhārakasya, devasya dyotanādidharmakasya /
43.11.[505]	kīdṛśaṃ śravaḥ /
43.11.[506]	sānasi snehakāri, uṇādiṣu snehārtha eva sānasiśabdo nipātitaḥ /
43.11.[507]	dyumnaṃ dyotamānaṃ yaśoyuktamannayuktaṃ vā /
43.11.[508]	tathā ca 'dyumnaṃ dyotateryaśo vānnaṃ vā' iti niruktakāraḥ /
43.11.[509]	citraśravastamaṃ āścaryabhūtatamadhanamityarthaḥ //
43.11.[510]	mitrasya carṣaṇīdhṛtaḥ śravo devasya sānasi /
43.11.[511]	satyaṃ citraśravastamam //
43.11.[512]	ātmanaivaitāṃ paṭhati /
43.11.[513]	atra satyametāvanmātraṃ viśeṣaḥ //
43.11.[514]	'āpo hi ṣṭhā' ityādayastisraḥ /
43.11.[515]	tāśca saṃmārjane vyākhyātāḥ //
43.11.[516]	āpaḥ pṛṇīta bheṣajaṃ varūthaṃ tanvo mama /
43.11.[517]	jyok ca sūryaṃ dṛśe /
43.11.[518]	he āpaḥ mama bheṣajaṃ hitakāri karma vedādhyayanādikaṃ karma pṛṇīta pūrayata /
43.11.[519]	varūthaṃ tanvo mama, madīyāyāstanoḥ śarīrasya yūyameva varūthaṃ gṛhamāśrayaḥ /
43.11.[520]	jyok cirakālaṃ ca tvatprasādādahaṃ sūryaṃ dṛśe paśyan bhūyāsam //
43.11.[521]	śaṃ no devīrabhīṣṭaya /
43.11.[522]	iti vyākhyātā //
43.11.[523]	śaṃ no mitraḥ śaṃ varuṇaḥ śaṃ no bhavatvaryamā /
43.11.[524]	śaṃ na indro bṛhaspatiḥ śaṃ no viṣṇururukramaḥ //
43.11.[525]	mitrādayo’smākaṃ sukharūpāḥ sukhakarā bhavantvityarthaḥ /
43.11.[526]	viṣṇururukramaḥ trailokyasya kramaṇe vitatakrama ityarthaḥ //
43.11.[527]	śaṃ no mitraḥ śaṃ varuṇaḥ śaṃ no astvaryamā /
43.11.[528]	śaṃ na indraścāgniśca śaṃ no viṣṇururukramaḥ //
43.11.[529]	atrāstvitiviśeṣo devatāviśeṣaśca //
43.11.[530]	tyamūṣu vājinaṃ devajūtaṃ sahovānaṃ tarutāraṃ rathānām /
43.11.[531]	ariṣṭanemiṃ pṛtanājamāśuṃ svastaye tārkṣyamihāhvayema //
43.11.[532]	tyaṃ taṃ tārkṣyaṃ garuḍamiha svasannidhau āhvayema āhvayāmaḥ, ū iti nipāto’narthakaḥ /
43.11.[533]	ṣu iti suśabdaḥ, suvājinaṃ śobhanakampanaṃ devajūtaṃ devānāṃ prītikāraṇamabhimataṃ sahovānaṃ, saha iti balanāma, balavantaṃ rathānāmapi tarutāraṃ tārayitāramariṣṭanemimahiṃsitagatiṃ, pṛtanājaṃ pṛtanānāṃ parasenānāṃ jetāraṃ, āśuṃ śīghragatim /
43.11.[534]	kimarthamāhvayāmaḥ, svastaye’vināśāya //
43.11.[535]	'kayā naścitra' iti vāmadevyastṛcaḥ śāntyartha evoccāryate /
43.11.[536]	kayā nacitra ā bhuvadūtī sadāvṛdhaḥ sakhā /
43.11.[537]	kayā śaciṣṭhayā vṛtā //
43.11.[538]	he indra yā vṛtā vartanena karmaṇā ūtiravanaṃ saṃsārakleśanivāraṇamābhuvat ā samantādbhavati /
43.11.[539]	citraḥ, citrā āścaryabhūtā parapuruṣārtharūpetyarthaḥ /
43.11.[540]	sadāvṛdhaḥ sarvakālāśca samṛddhayaḥ kayā vṛtā bhavanti /
43.11.[541]	sakhā, etadūterviśeṣaṇam /
43.11.[542]	śaciṣṭhayeti vṛtetyasya viśeṣaṇaṃ śaktatamayetyarthaḥ //
43.11.[543]	kastvā satyo madānāṃ maṃhiṣṭho matsadaṃhasaḥ /
43.11.[544]	dṛḍhā cidāruje vasu //
43.11.[545]	he indra tvā tvāṃ, 'muktvā' ityadhyāhāraḥ, tvāṃ varjayitvā kaḥ satyaḥ satyasaṃkalpaḥ /
43.11.[546]	madānāṃ maṃhiṣṭhaḥ nityānandātmakaharṣayogyatayā hṛṣṭānāṃ madhye maṃhiṣṭho’tiśayena pūjanīyaḥ /
43.11.[547]	atastvāṃ muktvā kaḥ satyaḥ, yo aṃhasaḥ matsadaṃhasaḥ mādyatpāpasya saṃsārakleśakāriṇaḥ saṃbandhi vasu dhanamanādyavidyāvāsanātmakaṃ sāmarthyaṃ āruje ārujati vināśayati, dṛḍhā cit, sudṛḍhayā citā caitanyena vidyārūpeṇetyarthaḥ //
43.11.[548]	abhī ṣu ṇaḥ sakhīnāmavitā jaritṝṇāṃ śataṃ bhavāsyūtibhiḥ //
43.11.[549]	he indra nosmākaṃ susakhīnāṃ śobhanasamānakhyānānāmavitā, jaritṝṇāṃ stotṝṇāmabhyavitā ābhimukhyena rakṣitā bhavāsi bhava ūtibhiḥ, śataśabdo’tibāhulyalakṣaṇārthaḥ, atibahvībhirūtibhiravanakriyābhiravitā bhavetyarthaḥ /
43.11.[550]	bhavāsīti loḍarthe leṭ //
43.11.[551]	ya udagātpurastānmahato’rṇavādvibhrājamānaḥ sarirasya madhye /
43.11.[552]	sa mā vṛṣabho rohitākṣaḥ sūryo vipaścinmanasā punātu //
43.11.[553]	sa sūryo vipaścidvidyāmayo manasā mananenānudhyānena māṃ punātu pāvayatu, yaḥ purastātpūrvasyāṃ diśi udagāduditaḥ mahato’rṇavātsamudrāt /
43.11.[554]	viśeṣeṇa bhrājamāno dīpyamānaḥ sarirasya saraṇamārgasyāntarikṣasya madhye /
43.11.[555]	vṛṣabhaḥ kāmānāṃ varṣayitā, vṛṣabho vā sarvajyotiṣāmutkṛṣṭaḥ /
43.11.[556]	rohitākṣaḥ lohitalocanaḥ kanakanayanaḥ //
43.11.[557]	yadbrahmāvādiṣma tanmā mā hāsītsūryāya vibhrājāya vai namo namaḥ //
43.11.[558]	yadbrahma vedamavādiṣma paṭhitavanto vayaṃ tanmā mā hāsīnmātyākṣīt /
43.11.[559]	sūryāya viśeṣeṇa bhrājamānāya punaḥ punaḥ namaskāro’stu //
43.11.[560]	śāntivimokaḥ //
43.11.[561]	āpamāpamapaḥ sarvā asmādasmādito’mutaḥ /
43.11.[562]	agnirvāyuśca sūryaśca saha sañcaskarurdhiyā //
43.11.[563]	aupaniṣadāḥ paramarahasyamantrā amī paramāḥ pāvanāḥ saṃsāraghorasāgarasantaraṇopāyāḥ prāyaḥ sarvatra samarthāḥ, pravargyavrate’pi śāntiprastāvopayogina āpamāpamityādaya itīhāvaśyaṃ vivaraṇīyāḥ /
43.11.[564]	apaḥ pātre nidhāyopastauti sarvā apa ahamāpamāpaṃ prāptavān /
43.11.[565]	abhyāso’tiśayārthaḥ /
43.11.[566]	asmādasmādito’mutaḥ asmāditi pratyakṣanadyādijalāśayanirdeśaḥ, amṛta iti parokṣādhārābhidhānam /
43.11.[567]	abhyāsaḥ sākalyārthaḥ /
43.11.[568]	etā apaḥ sarvā agnivāyusūryāḥ sañcaskaruḥ saṃstambhavantaḥ /
43.11.[569]	dhiyā prajñayā //
43.11.[570]	vāyvaśvā raśmipatayo marīcyātmāno adruhaḥ /
43.11.[571]	devīrbhuvanasūvarīḥ putravattvā ime’suvaḥ //
43.11.[572]	vāyuvadaśvā vyāpakāḥ /
43.11.[573]	ke /
43.11.[574]	raśmipatayaḥ raśmayaśca te patayaḥ pālakāḥ apāṃ, raśmaya eva hyabgarbhāḥ santo meghā bhavanti /
43.11.[575]	ataśca marīcyātmānaḥ, āpo marīcyantarvartitvena sthitā ityarthaḥ /
43.11.[576]	adruhaḥ sūkṣmarūpeṇa marīcimadhyagatā api drohaśūnyā anupahiṃsikā ityarthaḥ /
43.11.[577]	devīḥ devya āpaḥ /
43.11.[578]	bhuvanasya bhuvanānāṃ suvarīḥ sūvaryaḥ prasavaśīlāḥ /
43.11.[579]	ime imān lokān asuvaḥ sūtavatyaḥ /
43.11.[580]	putravat putrāṇāṃ jīvātmanāmavatvai avanāya saṃsārakleśaśāntaye //
43.11.[581]	mahānāmnīrmahāmānā mahāyāmā mahāsomāsaḥ /
43.11.[582]	devīḥ parjanyasūvarīḥ putravattvā imaṃ suva //
43.11.[583]	mahānāmnībhirṛgbhirudakamucyate /
43.11.[584]	ṛcaśca mahānāmnyaḥ tadabhidhānādāpastathā, mahadyato nāma āsāmapāmiti, mahāprabhāvā ityarthaḥ /
43.11.[585]	ata eva ca mahāmānā, bṛhatyā pūjayā yuktāḥ /
43.11.[586]	mahāyāmā mahāparimāṇāḥ /
43.11.[587]	tathā mahāsomāsaḥ, tābhireva hyabhiṣutaḥ somo yāgayogyo bhavati /
43.11.[588]	evaṃbhūtāśca parjanyasūvarīḥ parjanyasya meghasya savitryaḥ /
43.11.[589]	putravattvā imaṃ suva, imaṃ brahmacāriṇaṃ putravattvāya suva putrajananayogyaṃ saṃpādaya //
43.11.[590]	apāśnuṣṭimapārakṣamapāśnuṣṭimapārasam /
43.11.[591]	apāghamanujāvarti mama devīṛte hitāḥ //
43.11.[592]	apa iti ṣaṣṭhībahuvacanasya supāṃ subityādeśaḥ /
43.11.[593]	snuṣṭirekadeśaḥ /
43.11.[594]	spṛśāmītyadhyāhāraḥ /
43.11.[595]	apāmekadeśaṃ spṛśāmītyarthaḥ /
43.11.[596]	uddhṛtya hi jalaikadeśo’trābhimanyata ityuktam /
43.11.[597]	evamapāṃ rakṣakamaṃśamuddhṛtaṃ spṛśāmi, apāṃ rasaṃ sāram /
43.11.[598]	apāghamanujāvarti, apāmaghaṃ pāpaṃ spṛśāmyapasārayāmi /
43.11.[599]	sadbhāve’psu pāpasya pramāṇamāha anujāvarti, apāmanujā jīvātmānastajjanyatvāt, teṣvāvartamānamaghamaśucitvaṃ kāraṇe’pyanuvṛttiṃ gamayati, ghaṭādigatamiva gandhādi mṛtpiṇḍādike /
43.11.[600]	ato vartamānaṃ aghaṃ āsāmuddhṛtya mantraiḥ pāvanaṃ śāntyādau /
43.11.[601]	mama devīrṛte hitāḥ, mama ṛte hitā mama ṛte yajñe satye ca hitāḥ /
43.11.[602]	athavā mama devyo hitā āpaḥ, yathā ṛto yajño hito mama, ṛtaḥ satyaśabdo vā //
43.11.[603]	vajraṃ devīruditāḥ stha varuṇaṃ devasūvarīḥ /
43.11.[604]	ādityānuditaṃ devīryoninordhvamudīṣata //
43.11.[605]	yūyaṃ pāpanivāraṇāya vajramivoditāḥ stha bhavatha /
43.11.[606]	yato varuṇasya doṣanivārakasya devasya sūryo yūyam /
43.11.[607]	ādityānuditaṃ karma vratādikaṃ kāmyaṃ ca tasya kartāraṃ he devya ūrdhvamudīṣata sarvotkṛṣṭaṃ saṃpādayatetyarthaḥ yoninā svajanmanimittena parabrahmaśaktyetyarthaḥ //
43.11.[608]	evamādayo mantrā bahuśaktayaḥ śāntivimoke’pyupayoginaḥ //
43.11.[609]	bhadraṃ karṇebhiḥ śṛṇuyāma devā bhadraṃ paśyemākṣabhiryajatrāḥ /
43.11.[610]	sthirairaṅgaistuṣṭuvāṃsastanūbhirvyaśema devahitaṃ yadāyuḥ //
43.11.[611]	evamādayo japamantrāḥ śāntyupayoginaḥ /
43.11.[612]	he devā vayaṃ karṇairbhadraṃ bhandanīyaṃ kalyāṇaṃ śṛṇuyāmaḥ brahmaprāptiparyavasāyi vedāntādikam /
43.11.[613]	he yajatrāḥ yaṣṭṛṛṇāṃ trātāro’kṣibhirnetrairbhadraṃ paśyema /
43.11.[614]	tathā sthirairavināśibhiraṅgaiḥ karacaraṇādibhirupalakṣitāḥ santastuṣṭuvāṃsastuvanto devahitaṃ deveṣu nihitaṃ yadāyuḥ, tat vyaśema viśeṣeṇāśnuvāma tanūbhiḥ śarīraiḥ //
43.11.[615]	svasti na indro vṛddhaśravāḥ svasti naḥ pūṣā viśvavedāḥ /
43.11.[616]	svasti nastārkṣyo ariṣṭanemiḥ svasti no bṛhaspatirdadhātu //
43.11.[617]	indro vṛddhaśravāḥ vṛddhadhanaḥ bahudhano no’smabhyaṃ svasti avināśaṃ dadhātu dadātu dhārayatu vā /
43.11.[618]	evaṃ pūṣā ādityo viśvavedāḥ sarvajñaḥ svasti no dadātu /
43.11.[619]	tārkṣyo garutmānariṣṭanemiḥ, 'riṣṭirhiṃsākarmā', ariṣṭo’nupahiṃsitaḥ nemirāspadaṃ sthānaṃ yasya saḥ, anupahiṃsitāspadaḥ /
43.11.[620]	prānto vā nemirahiṃsitamaryādaḥ kenāpyanullaṅghita ityarthaḥ /
43.11.[621]	bṛhaspatirdevaguruścāsmabhyaṃ svasti dadhātu dhārayatu vā //
43.11.[622]	ketavo’ruṇāḥ saścarṣaṇayo vātaraśanāḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ śatadhāya samāhitā atho sahasradhāyasam //
43.11.[623]	ketusaṃjñakā aruṇavarṇā jñātāro vātamekhalā śatadhāya samāhitā samāśritāḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ samādhisthairyādikaṃ śarīragateṣvanubhūya tato mokṣaṃ gatā ityarthaḥ /
43.11.[624]	śatadhāyeti yakāro’narthakaḥ /
43.11.[625]	atho sahasradhāyasaṃ sahasradhā ityarthaḥ, cirataralabhyo mokṣa ityarthaḥ /
43.11.[626]	tathā ca smṛtiḥ 'mahāyajñaiśca yajñaiśca brāhmīyaṃ kriyate tanuḥ /' iti //
43.11.[627]	śivā naḥ śaṃtamā bhavātha divyā āpa oṣadhayo vanaspatayaḥ //
43.11.[628]	no’smākaṃ śivāḥ kṣemakāriṇyaḥ śaṃtamāśca sukhatamā yūyaṃ bhavatha //
43.11.[629]	sumṛḻīkā sarasvati mā te vyoma saṃdṛśi //
43.11.[630]	anena bhūmimālabhate /
43.11.[631]	he sarasvati udakavati sumṛḻīkā susukhadā bhava, mā te tava vyoma vicchedaviplavaṃ dasyuprabhṛtikṛtaṃ drākṣam //
43.11.[632]	ityaruṇamantravivṛtiḥ //
43.11.[633]	naiṣṭhikabrahmacāriṇo vratamuktamadhunā mantrārtho vivriyate /
43.11.[634]	tatra śatādhyayana upaniṣattvena prasiddheṣvanuvākeṣu pañcadaśasu prathamaikādaśadvādaśānāmihopayogo’sti /
43.11.[635]	prathamasya vighnaśāntau, ekādaśasya śiṣyānuśāsane, dvādaśasyāpi śāntau /
43.11.[636]	tatra prathamadvādaśau tāvat śaṃ no mitraḥ śaṃ varuṇaḥ śaṃ no bhavatvaryamā /
43.11.[637]	śaṃ na indro bṛhaspatiḥ śaṃ no viṣṇururukramaḥ //
43.11.[638]	namo brahmaṇe namo vāyave namaste vāyo tvameva pratyakṣaṃ brahmāsi tvāmeva pratyakṣaṃ brahma vadiṣyāmyṛtaṃ vadiṣyāmi satyaṃ vadiṣyāmi tanmāmavatu tadvaktāramavatvavatu māmavatu vaktāraṃ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ //
43.11.[639]	mitrādayo’trādhyātmikyo devatāḥ /
43.11.[640]	tathā ca śrutiḥ 'prāṇo vai mitro’pāno varuṇaḥ' iti /
43.11.[641]	paramātmavivartāstatpariṇāmā vā jagatsūtraprāṇaprabhṛtayastadadhiṣṭhātryo devatā mitrādayaḥ /
43.11.[642]	evaṃ cakṣuṣo’dhiṣṭhātā devatāviśeṣaḥ aryamā /
43.11.[643]	arīn svādhyāyādivirodhinaḥ niyacchati yaḥ so’ryamā /
43.11.[644]	no’smākaṃ mitraḥ śaṃ sukhaṃ bhavatu sukhamasmākaṃ bhāvayatvityarthaḥ /
43.11.[645]	evaṃ varuṇādiṣvapi yojyam /
43.11.[646]	viṣṇurvyāpako’ntaryāmī urukramo bṛhatkramaḥ /
43.11.[647]	namo brahmaṇe, paramātmane namaskāro’stu /
43.11.[648]	evaṃ vāyave vāyurūpāya jagatsūtrabhūtāya namaskāro’stu /
43.11.[649]	he vāyo namaste’stu /
43.11.[650]	parokṣeṇa stutvā pratyakṣeṇa stauti he vāyo tvameva pratyakṣaṃ brahmāsi bhavasi nābherutthitastvameva vedarūpeṇa pratyakṣeṇa vivartase vipariṇamase vetyarthaḥ /
43.11.[651]	atastvāmeva pratyakṣaṃ brahma vadiṣyāmi yatastvameva pratyakṣaṃ brahma /
43.11.[652]	tvāmeva ṛtaṃ vadiṣyāmi satyaṃ ca /
43.11.[653]	iha samuccīyamāne mokṣopāyabhūte jñānakarmaṇī ṛtaśabdenokte, taditikartavyatā tu satyaśabdena /
43.11.[654]	athavā ṛtasatyaśabdayorekārthatvātpunarvacanamatiśayārtham /
43.11.[655]	tadṛtaṃ ca satyaṃ ca māmavatu vaktāramavatu /
43.11.[656]	punarvacanaṃ pūrvavat /
43.11.[657]	athavā māmavatu vaktāraṃ, pravaktāraṃ copādhyāyam /
43.11.[658]	śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntirityastu vighnānāmiti śeṣaḥ /
43.11.[659]	trirvacanaṃ saṃsārasya vighnabhūyastvādatiśayārtham /
43.11.[660]	eṣa prathamo’nuvākaḥ //
43.11.[661]	śaṃ no mitraḥ śaṃ varuṇaḥ śaṃ no astvaryamā śaṃ na indravāgniśca śaṃ no viṣṇururukramaḥ //
43.11.[662]	namo brahmaṇe namo vāyave namaste vāyo tvameva pratyakṣaṃ brahmāsi tvāmeva pratyakṣaṃ brahmāvādiṣamṛtamavādiṣaṃ satyamavādiṣaṃ tanmāmāvīttadvaktāramāvīdāvīnmāmāvīdvaktāraṃ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ //
43.11.[663]	atra prathamāddevatāmātraṃ viśiṣyate’tītakālatā ca //
43.11.[664]	saha nā avatu saha nau bhunaktu saha vīryaṃ karavāvahai /
43.11.[665]	tejasvinā adhītamastu mā vidviṣāvahai śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ //
43.11.[666]	idaṃ śiṣyopādhyāya saha brūtaḥ, anyatra tu dampatī api /
43.11.[667]	mitrādidevatāgaṇo nau āvāṃ śiṣyopādhyāyau karmabhūtāvavatu rakṣatu saha sthitau tathā bhunaktu pālayatu bhojayatu vā nityānandarūpamapavargaphalam /
43.11.[668]	sahaiva ca sthitau vīryaṃ vedābhyāsasamudbhūtamatinairmalyalakṣaṇaṃ karavāvahai kurvahe /
43.11.[669]	tejasvinau abhibhavituṃ kenāpyaśakyau /
43.11.[670]	yadadhītaṃ, tadāvayorastu sthiram /
43.11.[671]	mā vidviṣāvahai, āvayoranyonyaṃ vidveṣo mā bhūt /
43.11.[672]	śāntiriti vyākhyātam /
43.11.[673]	evamāvāpasthāne śāntiṃ kṛtvā, śiṣyaṃ medhāvitvamanirākariṣṇutvaṃ ca kāmayamānamācāryo vācayedṛgdvayam //
43.11.[674]	yacchandasāmṛṣabho viśvavedāśchandobhyodhyamṛtātsaṃbabhūva /
43.11.[675]	sa māmindro medhayā spṛṇotvamṛtasya vedadhāraṇo bhūyāsam //
43.11.[676]	śarīraṃ me vicakṣaṇaṃ vā madhumaduhe /
43.11.[677]	karṇābhyāṃ bhūri suśravaṃ brahmaṇaḥ kośosmi medhayā pihitaḥ śrutaṃ me gopāya //
43.11.[678]	mantravarṇājjapamātrādeva medhādiphalaṃ dhāraṇaśaktiranirākariṣṇutā tāṃ ca prāpnoti /
43.11.[679]	yaḥ chandasāṃ vedānāṃ ṛṣabho varṣitā kāmānāṃ pradhānabhūto vā oṃkāraḥ viśvavedāḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvadhano vā, chandobhyo vedāntebhyo’mṛtarūpo’dhibabhūva /
43.11.[680]	avidyāvaśena dvaitāpanno vedāntārthānuṣṭhānena sarvavedārthānuṣṭhānena vā jñānakarmasamuccayenādhikāmṛtarūpo nityānandādvaitarūpo bhavatītyarthaḥ /
43.11.[681]	sa indraḥ prajāpatiḥ mā māṃ medhayā spṛṇotu prīṇātu /
43.11.[682]	amṛtasyāmṛtatvāya mokṣāyāhaṃ vedadhāraṇaśaktiyuktaḥ syām /
43.11.[683]	anirākariṣṇutāpyatroktā /
43.11.[684]	tathā mama śarīraṃ vicakṣaṇaṃ mokṣopāyānuṣṭhānacaturaṃ bhūyāt /
43.11.[685]	vāk ca vedayuktā madhumat madhurarasayuktaṃ karmaphalaṃ duhe dogdhu /
43.11.[686]	karṇābhyāṃ bhūri bahu ciraṃ suśravaṃ śobhanaṃ śṛṇuyāṃ vedāntarūpam /
43.11.[687]	brahmaṇo vedasyāhaṃ kośo vedārthajñānaratnanicayabhāṇḍāgāraṃ bhūyāsam /
43.11.[688]	bhāṇḍāgāraṃ ca pidhānena sthagitaṃ bhavatītyāha medhayā prajñājanitasaṃskāreṇa pihita ācchādito rakṣitaḥ dṛḍhasaṃskāravaśena vedārthasyāvismaraṇāt /
43.11.[689]	śrutaṃ me gopāya, mama śrutaṃ ca rakṣa paraprayojanayuktaṃ kurvityarthaḥ //
43.11.[690]	śrīkāmaḥ 'āvahantī vitanvānā' ityādibhirjuhuyāt /
43.11.[691]	āvahantī vitanvānā kurvāṇā varamātmanaḥ /
43.11.[692]	vāsāṃsi mama gāvaścānnapānena vardhaya //
43.11.[693]	ato me śriyamāvaha lomaśāṃ paśubhiḥ saha svāhā //
43.11.[694]	ṛgyajuṣābhyāmābhyāṃ dve āhutī juhuyāt /
43.11.[695]	ekāmityeke, ṛgyajuṣānta ekasvāhākārāt /
43.11.[696]	anyāścāhutayo’tra pūrvavyākhyātaiḥ strīliṅgakairmantrairhotavyāḥ /
43.11.[697]	he śrīḥ mama vāsāṃsi gāścā’nnapānena saha vardhaya /
43.11.[698]	kiṃ kurvatī /
43.11.[699]	āvahantī prāpayantī ḍhaukayantī /
43.11.[700]	vitanvānā vividhaṃ viśeṣeṇa vā vistārayantī /
43.11.[701]	ātmanaśca varaṃ kurvāṇā varaṇīyaṃ varamutkṛṣṭaṃ maṇikanakādikamātmasambandhitayā kurvāṇā /
43.11.[702]	ato me śriyamāvaha, yasmātsamyagadhītavedo’hamupādhyāyāvaśyadeyadakṣiṇāyogyatopanatārthiviśeṣo vā, tato hetorlomaśāṃ lomaśājāviprabhṛtibhirvibhūṣitāṃ paśubhiraśvādibhiḥ saha /
43.11.[703]	upakurvāṇakasyaitaduktamityāhuḥ //
43.11.[704]	yaśaskāma 'ā mā yantu' ityaṣṭābhirjuhuyāt /
43.11.[705]	yadyācāryo juhoti, athāpi brahmacārī, ubhayathā brahmacāriṇaḥ phalaṃ taduddeśena karmakaraṇāt /
43.11.[706]	ā mā yantu brahmacāriṇaḥ svāhā /
43.11.[707]	saṃ mā yantu brahmacāriṇaḥ svāhā /
43.11.[708]	tapoyaśoyaśāni svāhā /
43.11.[709]	janoyaśoyaśāni svāhā /
43.11.[710]	taṃ tvā bhaga praviśāmi svāhā /
43.11.[711]	sa mā bhaga praviśa svāhā /
43.11.[712]	śreyānvaso yaśoyaśāni svāhā /
43.11.[713]	asminsahasraśākhe vibhajāhaṃ tvayi mṛje svāhā //
43.11.[714]	ye brahmacāriṇo dharmāḥ siddhayaśca te mā māṃ āyāntu /
43.11.[715]	prajāpatirevamabhyarthyate /
43.11.[716]	tadarthaṃ ca suhutamastu /
43.11.[717]	evaṃ samyagāyāntu māṃ ye brahmacāriṇaḥ sambandhino yamaniyamādayaḥ /
43.11.[718]	tapoyaśoyaśāni svāhā, tapāṃsyeva yaśaḥprakārāḥ tapoyaśoyaśāni tapoyaśoyaśāṃsi samāyāntu, 'prakāre guṇavacanasya' iti dvirvacanam /
43.11.[719]	tadarthaṃ ca suhutamastu /
43.11.[720]	tapoloke vā svargaviśeṣe ye yaśaḥprakārāste samāyāntvityarthaḥ /
43.11.[721]	evaṃ janoyaśoyaśāni svāheti vyākhyeyam /
43.11.[722]	taṃ tvā bhageti, he bhaga bhajanīya brahman tvāmahaṃ praviśāmi /
43.11.[723]	sa mā bhageti, sa tvaṃ he bhaga māṃ praviśa /
43.11.[724]	śreyānvaso yaśoyaśāni svāhā, he vaso vāsayitaḥ dhanada tvaṃ śreyān praśasyo’tiśayena, atastvatprasādānmāṃ yaśāṃsi praviśantu tadarthaṃ ca suhutamastu /
43.11.[725]	asminsahasreti, asminbahuśākhe yajurvede brahmavibhavopaniṣatpathe vā vibhaja vibhāgayoginaṃ kuru /
43.11.[726]	ahaṃ tvayi viṣayabhūte he brahman mṛje ātmānaṃ śodhayāmi, vigatanikhilamalaṃ sampādayāmi brahmaṇi kṣīṇaṃ, tadarthaṃ tu suhutamastu /
43.11.[727]	āraṇyakavratapaddhatiparyavasāne tvidaṃ kāryam //
43.11.[728]	vedamanūcyācāryo’ntevāsinamanuśāsti idaṃ kartavyamidamakartavyamityaupaniṣadaikādaśānuvākena /
43.11.[729]	ekādaśānuvākastu /
43.11.[730]	satyaṃ vada /
43.11.[731]	dharmaṃ cara /
43.11.[732]	svādhyāyānmā pramada /
43.11.[733]	ācāryāya priyaṃ dhanamāhṛtya prajātantuṃ mā vyavacchaitsīḥ /
43.11.[734]	satyānna pramaditavyam /
43.11.[735]	dharmānna pramaditavyam /
43.11.[736]	yatnānna pramaditavyam /
43.11.[737]	kuśalānna pramaditavyam /
43.11.[738]	svādhyāyapravacanābhyāṃ na pramaditavyam /
43.11.[739]	yajñāddevapitṛkāryebhyo na pramaditavyam /
43.11.[740]	mātṛdevo bhava /
43.11.[741]	pitṛdevo bhava /
43.11.[742]	ācāryadevo bhava /
43.11.[743]	atithidevo bhava /
43.11.[744]	yānyanavadyāni karmāṇi tāni tvayā kartavyāni no itarāṇi /
43.11.[745]	atha yānyasmākaṃ sucaritāni tāni tvayā kartavyāni no itarāṇi /
43.11.[746]	atha ye kecanāsmacchreyāṃso brāhmaṇā āgaccheran teṣāṃ tvayāsanena praśrayitavyam /
43.11.[747]	śraddhayā deyamaśraddhayā deyam /
43.11.[748]	saṃvidā deyamasaṃvidā deyam /
43.11.[749]	hriyā deyam /
43.11.[750]	bhiyā deyam /
43.11.[751]	vittyai deyam /
43.11.[752]	avittyai deyam /
43.11.[753]	bhūtyai deyam /
43.11.[754]	abhūtyai deyam /
43.11.[755]	atha yadi te karmavicikitsā vṛttivicikitsā vā syādye tatra brāhmaṇāḥ saṃmarśino yuktā āyuktā alakṣā alubdhā dharmakāmā vā syuryathā te tatra varteraṃstathā tvaṃ teṣu vartethāḥ /
43.11.[756]	athābhyākhyāteṣu ye tatra brāhmaṇāḥ saṃmarśino yuktā āyuktā alakṣā alubdhā dharmakāmā vā syuryathā te tatra varteraṃstathā tvaṃ tatra vartethāḥ /
43.11.[757]	eṣa ādeśa eṣa upadeśa eṣā vedopaniṣadetadanuśāsanametadupāsyam //
43.11.[758]	upaniṣatsaṃhitāmadhītyaivedamucyate /
43.11.[759]	ācārya ekādaśānuvākābhihitāṃ nītimupaniṣadadhyayanānte grāhayati, ata eva “vedādhyayanānantarameva dharmajijñāsā kartavyā" iti jaiminimuninā nigaditam /
43.11.[760]	yata ekādaśānuvākārambha eva 'vedamanūcya' iti śrutirapyasti mūlabhūtā /
43.11.[761]	vedasamuttha eva hi nyāyaḥ pramāṇam /
43.11.[762]	yatrocyate "āpa dharmopadeśaṃ ca vedaśāstrāvirodhinā /
43.11.[763]	yastarkeṇānusandhatte sa dharmaṃ veda netaraḥ " //
43.11.[764]	iti /
43.11.[765]	avedamūlastu mānuṣamatimātrakalpitaḥ kutarko dharmādharmau prati na pramāṇaṃ, yathā saugatabārhaspatyakalpaḥ /
43.11.[766]	yatredamucyate "purāṇaṃ mānavo dharmaḥ sāṃgo vedaścikitsitam /
43.11.[767]	ājñāsiddhāni catvāri na hantavyāni hetubhiḥ" //
43.11.[768]	"tarko’pratiṣṭaḥ smṛtayo vibhinnā nāsāvṛṣiryasya mataṃ na bhinnam /
43.11.[769]	dharmasya tattvaṃ nihitaṃ guhāyāṃ mahājano yena gataḥ sa panthāḥ" //
43.11.[770]	"hastasparśādivāndhena" iti //
43.11.[771]	he brahmacārin satyaṃ vada, satyaṃ punaḥ paropakāraparyavasāyi, asatyamapi satyaphalaṃ kadācidvaktavyaṃ yena brāhmaṇavadhādikaṃ rakṣyate /
43.11.[772]	yathoktaṃ "satyaṃ brūyāt priyaṃ brūyānna brūyātsatyamapriyam /
43.11.[773]	asatyaṃ ca priyaṃ brūyādeṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ" /
43.11.[774]	dharmaṃ cara, vihitakarmācārasaṃgrahādikamanutiṣṭha /
43.11.[775]	svādhyāyānmā pramada, svādhyāyaviṣayaṃ pramādamālasyādinānadhyayanaṃ mā kṛthāḥ /
43.11.[776]	ācāryadakṣiṇārthamabhimataṃ dhanamāhṛtya putrapautrādisantānavicchedaṃ mā kārṣīḥ, gurave dakṣiṇāṃ dattvā vivāhaṃ kuryādityarthaḥ /
43.11.[777]	satyasyāsatyabhāṣaṇaṃ pramādaḥ /
43.11.[778]	dharmasya nityanaimittikalakṣaṇasyākaraṇaṃ pramādaḥ /
43.11.[779]	kāmyasya tu viguṇasya karaṇamakaraṇaṃ ca /
43.11.[780]	evaṃ yatnasya pramādaḥ ālasyādyupahatatā /
43.11.[781]	kuśalaṃ śarīrarakṣādikaṃ tatra pramādaḥ svāsthye-’ pyabhayena tacchāntyādikaraṇaṃ, svastyayanaṃ hi pratyahaṃ śāntirūpaṃ vaiśvadevādāvāmnātam /
43.11.[782]	svādhyāyapramādo na kartavyaḥ, pravacane cādhyāpane āvṛtto’pi vedo guṇitavyo’dhyāpayitavyaśca /
43.11.[783]	evaṃ yajñeṣu pākayajñādiṣu pramādo’nanuṣṭhānalakṣaṇo na kartavyaḥ /
43.11.[784]	mātā deva iva yasya sa mātṛdevo bhava /
43.11.[785]	tvayā’navadyāni agarhitānyeva karmāṇi kartavyāni, na kadāciditarāṇi /
